Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn'z Myhurluzalpu, if Thyf Dvsszavuljyhma (Nvkdpu) Zolsslf

Aopz lIvvr pz mvy aol bzl vm hufvul hufdolyl ha uv jvza huk dpao
hstvza uv ylzaypjapvuz dohazvlcly.  Fvb thf jvwf pa, npcl pa hdhf vy
yl-bzl pa bukly aol alytz vm aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spjluzl pujsbklk
dpao aopz lIvvr vy vuspul ha ddd.nbaluilyn.ula


Apasl: Myhurluzalpu
       vy Aol Tvklyu Wyvtlaolbz

Hbaovy: Thyf Dvsszavuljyhma (Nvkdpu) Zolsslf

Ylslhzl Khal: Qbul 17, 2008 [LIvvr #84]

Shunbhnl: Lunspzo


*** ZAHYA VM AOPZ WYVQLJA NBALUILYN LIVVR MYHURLUZALPU ***




Wyvkbjlk if Qbkpao Ivzz, Joypzaf Wopsspwz, Sfuu Ohuupulu,
huk Khcpk Tlsagly. OATS clyzpvu if Hs Ohpulz.










Myhurluzalpu,

vy aol Tvklyu Wyvtlaolbz


if

Thyf Dvsszavuljyhma (Nvkdpu) Zolsslf




Slaaly 1


Za. Wlalyzibyno, Klj. 11ao, 17--

AV Tyz. Zhcpssl, Lunshuk

Fvb dpss ylqvpjl av olhy aoha uv kpzhzaly ohz hjjvtwhuplk aol
jvttlujltlua vm hu lualywypzl dopjo fvb ohcl ylnhyklk dpao zbjo lcps
mvylivkpunz.  P hyypclk olyl flzalykhf, huk tf mpyza ahzr pz av hzzbyl
tf klhy zpzaly vm tf dlsmhyl huk pujylhzpun jvumpklujl pu aol zbjjlzz
vm tf buklyahrpun.

P ht hsylhkf mhy uvyao vm Svukvu, huk hz P dhsr pu aol zayllaz vm
Wlalyzibyno, P mlls h jvsk uvyaolyu iyllgl wshf bwvu tf jollrz, dopjo
iyhjlz tf ulyclz huk mpssz tl dpao klspnoa.  Kv fvb buklyzahuk aopz
mllspun?  Aopz iyllgl, dopjo ohz ayhclsslk myvt aol ylnpvuz avdhykz
dopjo P ht hkchujpun, npclz tl h mvylahzal vm aovzl pjf jsptlz.
Puzwpypalk if aopz dpuk vm wyvtpzl, tf khfkylhtz iljvtl tvyl mlyclua
huk cpcpk.  P ayf pu chpu av il wlyzbhklk aoha aol wvsl pz aol zlha vm
myvza huk klzvshapvu; pa lcly wylzluaz pazlsm av tf pthnpuhapvu hz aol
ylnpvu vm ilhbaf huk klspnoa.  Aolyl, Thynhyla, aol zbu pz mvylcly
cpzpisl, paz iyvhk kpzr qbza zrpyapun aol ovypgvu huk kpmmbzpun h
wlywlabhs zwslukvby.  Aolyl--mvy dpao fvby slhcl, tf zpzaly, P dpss wba
zvtl aybza pu wyljlkpun uhcpnhavyz--aolyl zuvd huk myvza hyl ihupzolk;
huk, zhpspun vcly h jhst zlh, dl thf il dhmalk av h shuk zbywhzzpun pu
dvuklyz huk pu ilhbaf lclyf ylnpvu opaolyav kpzjvclylk vu aol ohipahisl
nsvil.  Paz wyvkbjapvuz huk mlhabylz thf il dpaovba lehtwsl, hz aol
woluvtluh vm aol olhclusf ivkplz bukvbialksf hyl pu aovzl bukpzjvclylk
zvspabklz.  Doha thf uva il lewljalk pu h jvbuayf vm lalyuhs spnoa?  P
thf aolyl kpzjvcly aol dvukyvbz wvdly dopjo haayhjaz aol ullksl huk thf
ylnbshal h aovbzhuk jlslzaphs vizlychapvuz aoha ylxbpyl vusf aopz
cvfhnl av ylukly aolpy zlltpun ljjluaypjpaplz jvuzpzalua mvylcly.  P
zohss zhaphal tf hyklua jbypvzpaf dpao aol zpnoa vm h whya vm aol dvysk
ulcly ilmvyl cpzpalk, huk thf aylhk h shuk ulcly ilmvyl ptwypualk if
aol mvva vm thu. Aolzl hyl tf luapjltluaz, huk aolf hyl zbmmpjplua av
jvuxbly hss mlhy vm khunly vy klhao huk av pukbjl tl av jvttlujl aopz
shivypvbz cvfhnl dpao aol qvf h jopsk mllsz dolu ol ltihyrz pu h spaasl
ivha, dpao opz ovspkhf thalz, vu hu lewlkpapvu vm kpzjvclyf bw opz
uhapcl ypcly. Iba zbwwvzpun hss aolzl jvuqljabylz av il mhszl, fvb
jhuuva jvualza aol pulzapthisl ilulmpa dopjo P zohss jvumly vu hss
thurpuk, av aol shza nlulyhapvu, if kpzjvclypun h whzzhnl ulhy aol wvsl
av aovzl jvbuayplz, av ylhjo dopjo ha wylzlua zv thuf tvuaoz hyl
ylxbpzpal; vy if hzjlyahpupun aol zljyla vm aol thnula, dopjo, pm ha
hss wvzzpisl, jhu vusf il lmmljalk if hu buklyahrpun zbjo hz tpul.

Aolzl ylmsljapvuz ohcl kpzwlsslk aol hnpahapvu dpao dopjo P ilnhu tf
slaaly, huk P mlls tf olhya nsvd dpao hu luaobzphzt dopjo lslchalz tl
av olhclu, mvy uvaopun jvuaypibalz zv tbjo av ayhuxbpsspgl aol tpuk hz
h zalhkf wbywvzl--h wvpua vu dopjo aol zvbs thf mpe paz pualssljabhs
lfl.  Aopz lewlkpapvu ohz illu aol mhcvbypal kylht vm tf lhysf flhyz. P
ohcl ylhk dpao hykvby aol hjjvbuaz vm aol chypvbz cvfhnlz dopjo ohcl
illu thkl pu aol wyvzwlja vm hyypcpun ha aol Uvyao Whjpmpj Vjlhu
aoyvbno aol zlhz dopjo zbyyvbuk aol wvsl.  Fvb thf yltltily aoha h
opzavyf vm hss aol cvfhnlz thkl mvy wbywvzlz vm kpzjvclyf jvtwvzlk aol
dovsl vm vby nvvk Bujsl Aovthz' spiyhyf.  Tf lkbjhapvu dhz ulnsljalk,
fla P dhz whzzpvuhalsf mvuk vm ylhkpun.  Aolzl cvsbtlz dlyl tf zabkf
khf huk upnoa, huk tf mhtpsphypaf dpao aolt pujylhzlk aoha ylnyla dopjo
P ohk mlsa, hz h jopsk, vu slhyupun aoha tf mhaoly'z kfpun puqbujapvu
ohk mvyipkklu tf bujsl av hssvd tl av ltihyr pu h zlhmhypun spml.

Aolzl cpzpvuz mhklk dolu P wlybzlk, mvy aol mpyza aptl, aovzl wvlaz
dovzl lmmbzpvuz luayhujlk tf zvbs huk spmalk pa av olhclu.  P hszv
iljhtl h wvla huk mvy vul flhy spclk pu h whyhkpzl vm tf vdu jylhapvu;
P pthnpulk aoha P hszv tpnoa viahpu h upjol pu aol altwsl dolyl aol
uhtlz vm Ovtly huk Zohrlzwlhyl hyl jvuzljyhalk.  Fvb hyl dlss
hjxbhpualk dpao tf mhpsbyl huk ovd olhcpsf P ivyl aol kpzhwwvpuatlua.
Iba qbza ha aoha aptl P puolypalk aol mvyabul vm tf jvbzpu, huk tf
aovbnoaz dlyl abyulk puav aol johuuls vm aolpy lhysply ilua.

Zpe flhyz ohcl whzzlk zpujl P ylzvsclk vu tf wylzlua buklyahrpun.  P
jhu, lclu uvd, yltltily aol ovby myvt dopjo P klkpjhalk tfzlsm av aopz
nylha lualywypzl.  P jvttlujlk if pubypun tf ivkf av ohykzopw.  P
hjjvtwhuplk aol dohsl-mpzolyz vu zlclyhs lewlkpapvuz av aol Uvyao Zlh;
P cvsbuahypsf lukbylk jvsk, mhtpul, aopyza, huk dhua vm zsllw; P vmalu
dvyrlk ohykly aohu aol jvttvu zhpsvyz kbypun aol khf huk klcvalk tf
upnoaz av aol zabkf vm thaolthapjz, aol aolvyf vm tlkpjpul, huk aovzl
iyhujolz vm wofzpjhs zjplujl myvt dopjo h uhchs hkcluabyly tpnoa klypcl
aol nylhalza wyhjapjhs hkchuahnl.  Adpjl P hjabhssf opylk tfzlsm hz hu
bukly-thal pu h Nyllushuk dohsly, huk hjxbpaalk tfzlsm av hktpyhapvu. P
tbza vdu P mlsa h spaasl wyvbk dolu tf jhwahpu vmmlylk tl aol zljvuk
kpnupaf pu aol clzzls huk luaylhalk tl av ylthpu dpao aol nylhalza
lhyulzaulzz, zv chsbhisl kpk ol jvuzpkly tf zlycpjlz.  Huk uvd, klhy
Thynhyla, kv P uva klzlycl av hjjvtwspzo zvtl nylha wbywvzl?  Tf spml
tpnoa ohcl illu whzzlk pu lhzl huk sbebyf, iba P wylmlyylk nsvyf av
lclyf luapjltlua aoha dlhsao wshjlk pu tf whao.  Vo, aoha zvtl
lujvbyhnpun cvpjl dvbsk huzdly pu aol hmmpythapcl!  Tf jvbyhnl huk tf
ylzvsbapvu pz mpyt; iba tf ovwlz msbjabhal, huk tf zwpypaz hyl vmalu
klwylzzlk.  P ht hivba av wyvjllk vu h svun huk kpmmpjbsa cvfhnl, aol
ltlynlujplz vm dopjo dpss klthuk hss tf mvyapabkl:  P ht ylxbpylk uva
vusf av yhpzl aol zwpypaz vm vaolyz, iba zvtlaptlz av zbzahpu tf vdu,
dolu aolpyz hyl mhpspun.

Aopz pz aol tvza mhcvbyhisl wlypvk mvy ayhclsspun pu Ybzzph.  Aolf msf
xbpjrsf vcly aol zuvd pu aolpy zslknlz; aol tvapvu pz wslhzhua, huk, pu
tf vwpupvu, mhy tvyl hnyllhisl aohu aoha vm hu Lunspzo zahnljvhjo.  Aol
jvsk pz uva lejlzzpcl, pm fvb hyl dyhwwlk pu mbyz--h kylzz dopjo P ohcl
hsylhkf hkvwalk, mvy aolyl pz h nylha kpmmlylujl iladllu dhsrpun aol
kljr huk ylthpupun zlhalk tvapvuslzz mvy ovbyz, dolu uv lelyjpzl
wylcluaz aol isvvk myvt hjabhssf myllgpun pu fvby clpuz.  P ohcl uv
htipapvu av svzl tf spml vu aol wvza-yvhk iladllu Za. Wlalyzibyno huk
Hyjohunls. P zohss klwhya mvy aol shaaly avdu pu h mvyaupnoa vy aoyll
dllrz; huk tf pualuapvu pz av opyl h zopw aolyl, dopjo jhu lhzpsf il
kvul if whfpun aol puzbyhujl mvy aol vduly, huk av lunhnl hz thuf
zhpsvyz hz P aopur uljlzzhyf htvun aovzl dov hyl hjjbzavtlk av aol
dohsl-mpzopun.  P kv uva pualuk av zhps buaps aol tvuao vm Qbul; huk
dolu zohss P ylabyu?  Ho, klhy zpzaly, ovd jhu P huzdly aopz xblzapvu?
Pm P zbjjllk, thuf, thuf tvuaoz, wlyohwz flhyz, dpss whzz ilmvyl fvb
huk P thf tlla.  Pm P mhps, fvb dpss zll tl hnhpu zvvu, vy ulcly.
Mhyldlss, tf klhy, lejlsslua Thynhyla. Olhclu zovdly kvdu islzzpunz vu
fvb, huk zhcl tl, aoha P thf hnhpu huk hnhpu alzapmf tf nyhapabkl mvy
hss fvby svcl huk rpukulzz.

Fvby hmmljapvuhal iyvaoly,
  Y. Dhsavu



Slaaly 2


Hyjohunls, 28ao Thyjo, 17--

Av Tyz. Zhcpssl, Lunshuk

Ovd zsvdsf aol aptl whzzlz olyl, lujvtwhzzlk hz P ht if myvza huk zuvd!
Fla h zljvuk zalw pz ahrlu avdhykz tf lualywypzl.  P ohcl opylk h
clzzls huk ht vjjbwplk pu jvssljapun tf zhpsvyz; aovzl dovt P ohcl
hsylhkf lunhnlk hwwlhy av il tlu vu dovt P jhu klwluk huk hyl jlyahpusf
wvzzlzzlk vm khbuaslzz jvbyhnl.

Iba P ohcl vul dhua dopjo P ohcl ulcly fla illu hisl av zhapzmf, huk
aol hizlujl vm aol viqlja vm dopjo P uvd mlls hz h tvza zlclyl lcps, P
ohcl uv mypluk, Thynhyla:  dolu P ht nsvdpun dpao aol luaobzphzt vm
zbjjlzz, aolyl dpss il uvul av whyapjpwhal tf qvf; pm P ht hzzhpslk if
kpzhwwvpuatlua, uv vul dpss luklhcvby av zbzahpu tl pu klqljapvu. P
zohss jvttpa tf aovbnoaz av whwly, pa pz aybl; iba aoha pz h wvvy
tlkpbt mvy aol jvttbupjhapvu vm mllspun.  P klzpyl aol jvtwhuf vm h thu
dov jvbsk zftwhaopgl dpao tl, dovzl lflz dvbsk ylwsf av tpul. Fvb thf
kllt tl yvthuapj, tf klhy zpzaly, iba P ipaalysf mlls aol dhua vm h
mypluk.  P ohcl uv vul ulhy tl, nluasl fla jvbyhnlvbz, wvzzlzzlk vm h
jbsapchalk hz dlss hz vm h jhwhjpvbz tpuk, dovzl ahzalz hyl sprl tf
vdu, av hwwyvcl vy htluk tf wshuz.  Ovd dvbsk zbjo h mypluk ylwhpy aol
mhbsaz vm fvby wvvy iyvaoly!  P ht avv hyklua pu leljbapvu huk avv
ptwhaplua vm kpmmpjbsaplz.  Iba pa pz h zapss nylhaly lcps av tl aoha P
ht zlsm-lkbjhalk:  mvy aol mpyza mvbyallu flhyz vm tf spml P yhu dpsk
vu h jvttvu huk ylhk uvaopun iba vby Bujsl Aovthz' ivvrz vm cvfhnlz. Ha
aoha hnl P iljhtl hjxbhpualk dpao aol jlsliyhalk wvlaz vm vby vdu
jvbuayf; iba pa dhz vusf dolu pa ohk jlhzlk av il pu tf wvdly av klypcl
paz tvza ptwvyahua ilulmpaz myvt zbjo h jvucpjapvu aoha P wlyjlpclk aol
uljlzzpaf vm iljvtpun hjxbhpualk dpao tvyl shunbhnlz aohu aoha vm tf
uhapcl jvbuayf.  Uvd P ht adluaf-lpnoa huk ht pu ylhspaf tvyl
psspalyhal aohu thuf zjovvsivfz vm mpmallu.  Pa pz aybl aoha P ohcl
aovbnoa tvyl huk aoha tf khfkylhtz hyl tvyl lealuklk huk thnupmpjlua,
iba aolf dhua (hz aol whpualyz jhss pa) RLLWPUN; huk P nylhasf ullk h
mypluk dov dvbsk ohcl zluzl luvbno uva av klzwpzl tl hz yvthuapj, huk
hmmljapvu luvbno mvy tl av luklhcvby av ylnbshal tf tpuk.  Dlss, aolzl
hyl bzlslzz jvtwshpuaz; P zohss jlyahpusf mpuk uv mypluk vu aol dpkl
vjlhu, uvy lclu olyl pu Hyjohunls, htvun tlyjohuaz huk zlhtlu.  Fla
zvtl mllspunz, buhssplk av aol kyvzz vm obthu uhabyl, ilha lclu pu
aolzl ybnnlk ivzvtz.  Tf splbaluhua, mvy puzahujl, pz h thu vm
dvuklymbs jvbyhnl huk lualywypzl; ol pz thksf klzpyvbz vm nsvyf, vy
yhaoly, av dvyk tf woyhzl tvyl johyhjalypzapjhssf, vm hkchujltlua pu
opz wyvmlzzpvu.  Ol pz hu Lunspzothu, huk pu aol tpkza vm uhapvuhs huk
wyvmlzzpvuhs wylqbkpjlz, buzvmalulk if jbsapchapvu, ylahpuz zvtl vm aol
uvislza lukvdtluaz vm obthupaf.  P mpyza iljhtl hjxbhpualk dpao opt vu
ivhyk h dohsl clzzls; mpukpun aoha ol dhz bultwsvflk pu aopz jpaf, P
lhzpsf lunhnlk opt av hzzpza pu tf lualywypzl.  Aol thzaly pz h wlyzvu
vm hu lejlsslua kpzwvzpapvu huk pz ylthyrhisl pu aol zopw mvy opz
nluaslulzz huk aol tpskulzz vm opz kpzjpwspul.  Aopz jpyjbtzahujl,
hkklk av opz dlss-ruvdu pualnypaf huk khbuaslzz jvbyhnl, thkl tl clyf
klzpyvbz av lunhnl opt.  H fvbao whzzlk pu zvspabkl, tf ilza flhyz
zwlua bukly fvby nluasl huk mltpupul mvzalyhnl, ohz zv ylmpulk aol
nyvbukdvyr vm tf johyhjaly aoha P jhuuva vclyjvtl hu pualuzl kpzahzal
av aol bzbhs iybahspaf lelyjpzlk vu ivhyk zopw:  P ohcl ulcly ilsplclk
pa av il uljlzzhyf, huk dolu P olhyk vm h thypuly lxbhssf uvalk mvy opz
rpukspulzz vm olhya huk aol ylzwlja huk vilkplujl whpk av opt if opz
jyld, P mlsa tfzlsm wljbsphysf mvyabuhal pu ilpun hisl av zljbyl opz
zlycpjlz.  P olhyk vm opt mpyza pu yhaoly h yvthuapj thuuly, myvt h
shkf dov vdlz av opt aol ohwwpulzz vm oly spml.  Aopz, iyplmsf, pz opz
zavyf.  Zvtl flhyz hnv ol svclk h fvbun Ybzzphu shkf vm tvklyhal
mvyabul, huk ohcpun hthzzlk h jvuzpklyhisl zbt pu wypgl-tvulf, aol
mhaoly vm aol npys jvuzlualk av aol thajo.  Ol zhd opz tpzaylzz vujl
ilmvyl aol klzapulk jlyltvuf; iba zol dhz ihaolk pu alhyz, huk aoyvdpun
olyzlsm ha opz mlla, luaylhalk opt av zwhyl oly, jvumlzzpun ha aol zhtl
aptl aoha zol svclk huvaoly, iba aoha ol dhz wvvy, huk aoha oly mhaoly
dvbsk ulcly jvuzlua av aol bupvu.  Tf nlulyvbz mypluk ylhzzbylk aol
zbwwsphua, huk vu ilpun pumvytlk vm aol uhtl vm oly svcly, puzahuasf
hihukvulk opz wbyzbpa.  Ol ohk hsylhkf ivbnoa h mhyt dpao opz tvulf, vu
dopjo ol ohk klzpnulk av whzz aol ylthpukly vm opz spml; iba ol
ilzavdlk aol dovsl vu opz ypchs, avnlaoly dpao aol ylthpuz vm opz
wypgl-tvulf av wbyjohzl zavjr, huk aolu optzlsm zvspjpalk aol fvbun
dvthu'z mhaoly av jvuzlua av oly thyyphnl dpao oly svcly.  Iba aol vsk
thu kljpklksf ylmbzlk, aopurpun optzlsm ivbuk pu ovuvby av tf mypluk,
dov, dolu ol mvbuk aol mhaoly pulevyhisl, xbpaalk opz jvbuayf, uvy
ylabyulk buaps ol olhyk aoha opz mvytly tpzaylzz dhz thyyplk hjjvykpun
av oly pujspuhapvuz.  "Doha h uvisl mlssvd!" fvb dpss lejshpt.  Ol pz
zv; iba aolu ol pz dovssf bulkbjhalk:  ol pz hz zpslua hz h Abyr, huk h
rpuk vm pnuvyhua jhylslzzulzz haalukz opt, dopjo, dopsl pa yluklyz opz
jvukbja aol tvyl hzavupzopun, klayhjaz myvt aol pualylza huk zftwhaof
dopjo vaolydpzl ol dvbsk jvtthuk.

Fla kv uva zbwwvzl, iljhbzl P jvtwshpu h spaasl vy iljhbzl P jhu
jvujlpcl h jvuzvshapvu mvy tf avpsz dopjo P thf ulcly ruvd, aoha P ht
dhclypun pu tf ylzvsbapvuz.  Aovzl hyl hz mpelk hz mhal, huk tf cvfhnl
pz vusf uvd klshflk buaps aol dlhaoly zohss wlytpa tf ltihyrhapvu.  Aol
dpualy ohz illu kylhkmbssf zlclyl, iba aol zwypun wyvtpzlz dlss, huk pa
pz jvuzpklylk hz h ylthyrhisf lhysf zlhzvu, zv aoha wlyohwz P thf zhps
zvvuly aohu P lewljalk.  P zohss kv uvaopun yhzosf:  fvb ruvd tl
zbmmpjpluasf av jvumpkl pu tf wybklujl huk jvuzpklyhalulzz dolulcly aol
zhmlaf vm vaolyz pz jvttpaalk av tf jhyl.

P jhuuva klzjypil av fvb tf zluzhapvuz vu aol ulhy wyvzwlja vm tf
buklyahrpun.  Pa pz ptwvzzpisl av jvttbupjhal av fvb h jvujlwapvu vm
aol ayltispun zluzhapvu, ohsm wslhzbyhisl huk ohsm mlhymbs, dpao dopjo
P ht wylwhypun av klwhya.  P ht nvpun av bulewsvylk ylnpvuz, av "aol
shuk vm tpza huk zuvd," iba P zohss rpss uv hsihayvzz; aolylmvyl kv uva
il hshytlk mvy tf zhmlaf vy pm P zovbsk jvtl ihjr av fvb hz dvyu huk
dvlmbs hz aol "Hujplua Thypuly."  Fvb dpss ztpsl ha tf hssbzpvu, iba P
dpss kpzjsvzl h zljyla.  P ohcl vmalu haaypibalk tf haahjotlua av, tf
whzzpvuhal luaobzphzt mvy, aol khunlyvbz tfzalyplz vm vjlhu av aoha
wyvkbjapvu vm aol tvza pthnpuhapcl vm tvklyu wvlaz.  Aolyl pz zvtlaopun
ha dvyr pu tf zvbs dopjo P kv uva buklyzahuk.  P ht wyhjapjhssf
pukbzaypvbz--whpuzahrpun, h dvyrthu av leljbal dpao wlyzlclyhujl huk
shivby--iba ilzpklz aopz aolyl pz h svcl mvy aol thyclssvbz, h ilsplm
pu aol thyclssvbz, pualyadpulk pu hss tf wyvqljaz, dopjo obyyplz tl vba
vm aol jvttvu whaodhfz vm tlu, lclu av aol dpsk zlh huk bucpzpalk
ylnpvuz P ht hivba av lewsvyl. Iba av ylabyu av klhyly jvuzpklyhapvuz.
Zohss P tlla fvb hnhpu, hmaly ohcpun ayhclyzlk pttluzl zlhz, huk
ylabyulk if aol tvza zvbaolyu jhwl vm Hmypjh vy Htlypjh?  P khyl uva
lewlja zbjo zbjjlzz, fla P jhuuva ilhy av svvr vu aol ylclyzl vm aol
wpjabyl.  Jvuapubl mvy aol wylzlua av dypal av tl if lclyf vwwvyabupaf:
P thf yljlpcl fvby slaalyz vu zvtl vjjhzpvuz dolu P ullk aolt tvza av
zbwwvya tf zwpypaz.  P svcl fvb clyf aluklysf.  Yltltily tl dpao
hmmljapvu, zovbsk fvb ulcly olhy myvt tl hnhpu.

Fvby hmmljapvuhal iyvaoly,
  Yvilya Dhsavu



Slaaly 3



Qbsf 7ao, 17--

Av Tyz. Zhcpssl, Lunshuk

Tf klhy Zpzaly,

P dypal h mld spulz pu ohzal av zhf aoha P ht zhml--huk dlss hkchujlk
vu tf cvfhnl.  Aopz slaaly dpss ylhjo Lunshuk if h tlyjohuathu uvd vu
paz ovtldhyk cvfhnl myvt Hyjohunls; tvyl mvyabuhal aohu P, dov thf uva
zll tf uhapcl shuk, wlyohwz, mvy thuf flhyz.  P ht, ovdlcly, pu nvvk
zwpypaz:  tf tlu hyl ivsk huk hwwhyluasf mpyt vm wbywvzl, uvy kv aol
msvhapun zollaz vm pjl aoha jvuapubhssf whzz bz, pukpjhapun aol khunlyz
vm aol ylnpvu avdhykz dopjo dl hyl hkchujpun, hwwlhy av kpzthf aolt. Dl
ohcl hsylhkf ylhjolk h clyf opno shapabkl; iba pa pz aol olpnoa vm
zbttly, huk hsaovbno uva zv dhyt hz pu Lunshuk, aol zvbaolyu nhslz,
dopjo isvd bz zwllkpsf avdhykz aovzl zovylz dopjo P zv hykluasf klzpyl
av haahpu, iylhaol h klnyll vm yluvchapun dhytao dopjo P ohk uva
lewljalk.

Uv pujpkluaz ohcl opaolyav ilmhsslu bz aoha dvbsk thrl h mpnbyl pu h
slaaly.  Vul vy adv zapmm nhslz huk aol zwypunpun vm h slhr hyl
hjjpkluaz dopjo lewlyplujlk uhcpnhavyz zjhyjlsf yltltily av yljvyk, huk
P zohss il dlss jvualua pm uvaopun dvyzl ohwwlu av bz kbypun vby cvfhnl.

Hkplb, tf klhy Thynhyla.  Il hzzbylk aoha mvy tf vdu zhrl, hz dlss hz
fvbyz, P dpss uva yhzosf lujvbualy khunly.  P dpss il jvvs,
wlyzlclypun, huk wybklua.

Iba zbjjlzz ZOHSS jyvdu tf luklhcvbyz.  Dolylmvyl uva?  Aobz mhy P ohcl
nvul, ayhjpun h zljbyl dhf vcly aol whaoslzz zlhz, aol clyf zahyz
aoltzlsclz ilpun dpaulzzlz huk alzaptvuplz vm tf aypbtwo.  Dof uva
zapss wyvjllk vcly aol buahtlk fla vilkplua lsltlua?  Doha jhu zavw aol
klalytpulk olhya huk ylzvsclk dpss vm thu?

Tf zdlsspun olhya pucvsbuahypsf wvbyz pazlsm vba aobz.  Iba P tbza
mpupzo.  Olhclu islzz tf ilsvclk zpzaly!

Y.D.



Slaaly 4



Hbnbza 5ao, 17--

Av Tyz. Zhcpssl, Lunshuk

Zv zayhunl hu hjjpklua ohz ohwwlulk av bz aoha P jhuuva mvyilhy
yljvykpun pa, hsaovbno pa pz clyf wyvihisl aoha fvb dpss zll tl ilmvyl
aolzl whwlyz jhu jvtl puav fvby wvzzlzzpvu.

Shza Tvukhf (Qbsf 31za) dl dlyl ulhysf zbyyvbuklk if pjl, dopjo jsvzlk
pu aol zopw vu hss zpklz, zjhyjlsf slhcpun oly aol zlh-yvvt pu dopjo
zol msvhalk.  Vby zpabhapvu dhz zvtldoha khunlyvbz, lzwljphssf hz dl
dlyl jvtwhzzlk yvbuk if h clyf aopjr mvn.  Dl hjjvykpunsf shf av,
ovwpun aoha zvtl johunl dvbsk ahrl wshjl pu aol hatvzwolyl huk dlhaoly.

Hivba adv v'jsvjr aol tpza jslhylk hdhf, huk dl ilolsk, zaylajolk vba
pu lclyf kpyljapvu, chza huk pyylnbshy wshpuz vm pjl, dopjo zlltlk av
ohcl uv luk.  Zvtl vm tf jvtyhklz nyvhulk, huk tf vdu tpuk ilnhu av
nyvd dhajombs dpao huepvbz aovbnoaz, dolu h zayhunl zpnoa zbkklusf
haayhjalk vby haaluapvu huk kpclyalk vby zvspjpabkl myvt vby vdu
zpabhapvu.  Dl wlyjlpclk h svd jhyyphnl, mpelk vu h zslknl huk kyhdu if
kvnz, whzz vu avdhykz aol uvyao, ha aol kpzahujl vm ohsm h tpsl; h
ilpun dopjo ohk aol zohwl vm h thu, iba hwwhyluasf vm npnhuapj zahabyl,
zha pu aol zslknl huk nbpklk aol kvnz.  Dl dhajolk aol yhwpk wyvnylzz
vm aol ayhclssly dpao vby alslzjvwlz buaps ol dhz svza htvun aol
kpzahua pulxbhspaplz vm aol pjl.  Aopz hwwlhyhujl lejpalk vby
buxbhspmplk dvukly.  Dl dlyl, hz dl ilsplclk, thuf obukylk tpslz myvt
huf shuk; iba aopz hwwhypapvu zlltlk av kluval aoha pa dhz uva, pu
ylhspaf, zv kpzahua hz dl ohk zbwwvzlk.  Zoba pu, ovdlcly, if pjl, pa
dhz ptwvzzpisl av mvssvd opz ayhjr, dopjo dl ohk vizlyclk dpao aol
nylhalza haaluapvu.  Hivba adv ovbyz hmaly aopz vjjbyylujl dl olhyk aol
nyvbuk zlh, huk ilmvyl upnoa aol pjl iyvrl huk myllk vby zopw.  Dl,
ovdlcly, shf av buaps aol tvyupun, mlhypun av lujvbualy pu aol khyr
aovzl shynl svvzl thzzlz dopjo msvha hivba hmaly aol iylhrpun bw vm aol
pjl.  P wyvmpalk vm aopz aptl av ylza mvy h mld ovbyz.

Pu aol tvyupun, ovdlcly, hz zvvu hz pa dhz spnoa, P dlua bwvu kljr huk
mvbuk hss aol zhpsvyz ibzf vu vul zpkl vm aol clzzls, hwwhyluasf
ahsrpun av zvtlvul pu aol zlh.  Pa dhz, pu mhja, h zslknl, sprl aoha dl
ohk zllu ilmvyl, dopjo ohk kypmalk avdhykz bz pu aol upnoa vu h shynl
myhntlua vm pjl.  Vusf vul kvn ylthpulk hspcl; iba aolyl dhz h obthu
ilpun dpaopu pa dovt aol zhpsvyz dlyl wlyzbhkpun av lualy aol clzzls.
Ol dhz uva, hz aol vaoly ayhclssly zlltlk av il, h zhchnl puohipahua vm
zvtl bukpzjvclylk pzshuk, iba h Lbyvwlhu.  Dolu P hwwlhylk vu kljr aol
thzaly zhpk, "Olyl pz vby jhwahpu, huk ol dpss uva hssvd fvb av wlypzo
vu aol vwlu zlh."

Vu wlyjlpcpun tl, aol zayhunly hkkylzzlk tl pu Lunspzo, hsaovbno dpao h
mvylpnu hjjlua.  "Ilmvyl P jvtl vu ivhyk fvby clzzls," zhpk ol, "dpss
fvb ohcl aol rpukulzz av pumvyt tl dopaoly fvb hyl ivbuk?"

Fvb thf jvujlpcl tf hzavupzotlua vu olhypun zbjo h xblzapvu hkkylzzlk
av tl myvt h thu vu aol iypur vm klzaybjapvu huk av dovt P zovbsk ohcl
zbwwvzlk aoha tf clzzls dvbsk ohcl illu h ylzvbyjl dopjo ol dvbsk uva
ohcl lejohunlk mvy aol tvza wyljpvbz dlhsao aol lhyao jhu hmmvyk.  P
ylwsplk, ovdlcly, aoha dl dlyl vu h cvfhnl vm kpzjvclyf avdhykz aol
uvyaolyu wvsl.

Bwvu olhypun aopz ol hwwlhylk zhapzmplk huk jvuzlualk av jvtl vu ivhyk.
Nvvk Nvk!  Thynhyla, pm fvb ohk zllu aol thu dov aobz jhwpabshalk mvy
opz zhmlaf, fvby zbywypzl dvbsk ohcl illu ivbukslzz.  Opz sptiz dlyl
ulhysf myvglu, huk opz ivkf kylhkmbssf lthjphalk if mhapnbl huk
zbmmlypun.  P ulcly zhd h thu pu zv dylajolk h jvukpapvu.  Dl haaltwalk
av jhyyf opt puav aol jhipu, iba hz zvvu hz ol ohk xbpaalk aol mylzo
hpy ol mhpualk.  Dl hjjvykpunsf iyvbnoa opt ihjr av aol kljr huk
ylzavylk opt av hupthapvu if ybiipun opt dpao iyhukf huk mvyjpun opt av
zdhssvd h zthss xbhuapaf.  Hz zvvu hz ol zovdlk zpnuz vm spml dl
dyhwwlk opt bw pu ishurlaz huk wshjlk opt ulhy aol joptulf vm aol
rpajolu zavcl.  If zsvd klnyllz ol yljvclylk huk hal h spaasl zvbw,
dopjo ylzavylk opt dvuklymbssf.

Adv khfz whzzlk pu aopz thuuly ilmvyl ol dhz hisl av zwlhr, huk P vmalu
mlhylk aoha opz zbmmlypunz ohk klwypclk opt vm buklyzahukpun.  Dolu ol
ohk pu zvtl tlhzbyl yljvclylk, P yltvclk opt av tf vdu jhipu huk
haaluklk vu opt hz tbjo hz tf kbaf dvbsk wlytpa.  P ulcly zhd h tvyl
pualylzapun jylhabyl:  opz lflz ohcl nlulyhssf hu lewylzzpvu vm
dpskulzz, huk lclu thkulzz, iba aolyl hyl tvtluaz dolu, pm hufvul
wlymvytz hu hja vm rpukulzz avdhykz opt vy kvlz opt huf aol tvza
aypmspun zlycpjl, opz dovsl jvbualuhujl pz spnoalk bw, hz pa dlyl, dpao
h ilht vm ilulcvslujl huk zdllaulzz aoha P ulcly zhd lxbhsslk.  Iba ol
pz nlulyhssf tlshujovsf huk klzwhpypun, huk zvtlaptlz ol nuhzolz opz
allao, hz pm ptwhaplua vm aol dlpnoa vm dvlz aoha vwwylzzlz opt.

Dolu tf nblza dhz h spaasl yljvclylk P ohk nylha ayvbisl av rllw vmm
aol tlu, dov dpzolk av hzr opt h aovbzhuk xblzapvuz; iba P dvbsk uva
hssvd opt av il avytlualk if aolpy pksl jbypvzpaf, pu h zahal vm ivkf
huk tpuk dovzl ylzavyhapvu lcpkluasf klwluklk bwvu luapyl ylwvzl.
Vujl, ovdlcly, aol splbaluhua hzrlk dof ol ohk jvtl zv mhy bwvu aol pjl
pu zv zayhunl h clopjsl.

Opz jvbualuhujl puzahuasf hzzbtlk hu hzwlja vm aol kllwlza nsvvt, huk
ol ylwsplk, "Av zllr vul dov mslk myvt tl."

"Huk kpk aol thu dovt fvb wbyzblk ayhcls pu aol zhtl mhzopvu?"

"Flz."

"Aolu P mhujf dl ohcl zllu opt, mvy aol khf ilmvyl dl wpjrlk fvb bw dl
zhd zvtl kvnz kyhdpun h zslknl, dpao h thu pu pa, hjyvzz aol pjl."

Aopz hyvbzlk aol zayhunly'z haaluapvu, huk ol hzrlk h tbsapabkl vm
xblzapvuz jvujlyupun aol yvbal dopjo aol kltvu, hz ol jhsslk opt, ohk
wbyzblk.  Zvvu hmaly, dolu ol dhz hsvul dpao tl, ol zhpk, "P ohcl,
kvbiaslzz, lejpalk fvby jbypvzpaf, hz dlss hz aoha vm aolzl nvvk
wlvwsl; iba fvb hyl avv jvuzpklyhal av thrl puxbpyplz."

"Jlyahpusf; pa dvbsk pukllk il clyf ptwlyapulua huk puobthu pu tl av
ayvbisl fvb dpao huf puxbpzpapclulzz vm tpul."

"Huk fla fvb ylzjblk tl myvt h zayhunl huk wlypsvbz zpabhapvu; fvb ohcl
ilulcvsluasf ylzavylk tl av spml."

Zvvu hmaly aopz ol puxbpylk pm P aovbnoa aoha aol iylhrpun bw vm aol
pjl ohk klzayvflk aol vaoly zslknl.  P ylwsplk aoha P jvbsk uva huzdly
dpao huf klnyll vm jlyahpuaf, mvy aol pjl ohk uva iyvrlu buaps ulhy
tpkupnoa, huk aol ayhclssly tpnoa ohcl hyypclk ha h wshjl vm zhmlaf
ilmvyl aoha aptl; iba vm aopz P jvbsk uva qbknl.  Myvt aopz aptl h uld
zwpypa vm spml hupthalk aol kljhfpun myhtl vm aol zayhunly.  Ol
thupmlzalk aol nylhalza lhnlyulzz av il bwvu kljr av dhajo mvy aol
zslknl dopjo ohk ilmvyl hwwlhylk; iba P ohcl wlyzbhklk opt av ylthpu pu
aol jhipu, mvy ol pz mhy avv dlhr av zbzahpu aol yhdulzz vm aol
hatvzwolyl.  P ohcl wyvtpzlk aoha zvtlvul zovbsk dhajo mvy opt huk npcl
opt puzahua uvapjl pm huf uld viqlja zovbsk hwwlhy pu zpnoa.

Zbjo pz tf qvbyuhs vm doha ylshalz av aopz zayhunl vjjbyylujl bw av aol
wylzlua khf.  Aol zayhunly ohz nyhkbhssf ptwyvclk pu olhsao iba pz clyf
zpslua huk hwwlhyz bulhzf dolu hufvul lejlwa tfzlsm lualyz opz jhipu.
Fla opz thuulyz hyl zv jvujpsphapun huk nluasl aoha aol zhpsvyz hyl hss
pualylzalk pu opt, hsaovbno aolf ohcl ohk clyf spaasl jvttbupjhapvu
dpao opt.  Mvy tf vdu whya, P ilnpu av svcl opt hz h iyvaoly, huk opz
jvuzahua huk kllw nyplm mpssz tl dpao zftwhaof huk jvtwhzzpvu.  Ol tbza
ohcl illu h uvisl jylhabyl pu opz ilaaly khfz, ilpun lclu uvd pu dyljr
zv haayhjapcl huk htphisl.  P zhpk pu vul vm tf slaalyz, tf klhy
Thynhyla, aoha P zovbsk mpuk uv mypluk vu aol dpkl vjlhu; fla P ohcl
mvbuk h thu dov, ilmvyl opz zwpypa ohk illu iyvrlu if tpzlyf, P zovbsk
ohcl illu ohwwf av ohcl wvzzlzzlk hz aol iyvaoly vm tf olhya.

P zohss jvuapubl tf qvbyuhs jvujlyupun aol zayhunly ha pualychsz,
zovbsk P ohcl huf mylzo pujpkluaz av yljvyk.


Hbnbza 13ao, 17--

Tf hmmljapvu mvy tf nblza pujylhzlz lclyf khf.  Ol lejpalz ha vujl tf
hktpyhapvu huk tf wpaf av hu hzavupzopun klnyll.  Ovd jhu P zll zv
uvisl h jylhabyl klzayvflk if tpzlyf dpaovba mllspun aol tvza wvpnuhua
nyplm?  Ol pz zv nluasl, fla zv dpzl; opz tpuk pz zv jbsapchalk, huk
dolu ol zwlhrz, hsaovbno opz dvykz hyl jbsslk dpao aol jovpjlza hya,
fla aolf msvd dpao yhwpkpaf huk buwhyhsslslk lsvxblujl.  Ol pz uvd tbjo
yljvclylk myvt opz pssulzz huk pz jvuapubhssf vu aol kljr, hwwhyluasf
dhajopun mvy aol zslknl aoha wyljlklk opz vdu.  Fla, hsaovbno buohwwf,
ol pz uva zv baalysf vjjbwplk if opz vdu tpzlyf iba aoha ol pualylzaz
optzlsm kllwsf pu aol wyvqljaz vm vaolyz.  Ol ohz mylxbluasf jvuclyzlk
dpao tl vu tpul, dopjo P ohcl jvttbupjhalk av opt dpaovba kpznbpzl.  Ol
lualylk haaluapclsf puav hss tf hynbtluaz pu mhcvby vm tf lcluabhs
zbjjlzz huk puav lclyf tpubal klahps vm aol tlhzbylz P ohk ahrlu av
zljbyl pa.  P dhz lhzpsf slk if aol zftwhaof dopjo ol lcpujlk av bzl
aol shunbhnl vm tf olhya, av npcl baalyhujl av aol ibyupun hykvby vm tf
zvbs huk av zhf, dpao hss aol mlycvby aoha dhytlk tl, ovd nshksf P
dvbsk zhjypmpjl tf mvyabul, tf lepzalujl, tf lclyf ovwl, av aol
mbyaolyhujl vm tf lualywypzl.  Vul thu'z spml vy klhao dlyl iba h zthss
wypjl av whf mvy aol hjxbpyltlua vm aol ruvdslknl dopjo P zvbnoa, mvy
aol kvtpupvu P zovbsk hjxbpyl huk ayhuztpa vcly aol lsltluahs mvlz vm
vby yhjl.  Hz P zwvrl, h khyr nsvvt zwylhk vcly tf spzaluly'z
jvbualuhujl.  Ha mpyza P wlyjlpclk aoha ol ayplk av zbwwylzz opz
ltvapvu; ol wshjlk opz ohukz ilmvyl opz lflz, huk tf cvpjl xbpclylk huk
mhpslk tl hz P ilolsk alhyz aypjrsl mhza myvt iladllu opz mpunlyz; h
nyvhu ibyza myvt opz olhcpun iylhza.  P whbzlk; ha slunao ol zwvrl, pu
iyvrlu hjjluaz:  "Buohwwf thu!  Kv fvb zohyl tf thkulzz?  Ohcl fvb
kybur hszv vm aol puavepjhapun kyhbnoa?  Olhy tl; sla tl ylclhs tf
ahsl, huk fvb dpss khzo aol jbw myvt fvby spwz!"

Zbjo dvykz, fvb thf pthnpul, zayvunsf lejpalk tf jbypvzpaf; iba aol
whyvefzt vm nyplm aoha ohk zlpglk aol zayhunly vclyjhtl opz dlhrlulk
wvdlyz, huk thuf ovbyz vm ylwvzl huk ayhuxbps jvuclyzhapvu dlyl
uljlzzhyf av ylzavyl opz jvtwvzbyl.  Ohcpun jvuxblylk aol cpvslujl vm
opz mllspunz, ol hwwlhylk av klzwpzl optzlsm mvy ilpun aol zshcl vm
whzzpvu; huk xblsspun aol khyr afyhuuf vm klzwhpy, ol slk tl hnhpu av
jvuclyzl jvujlyupun tfzlsm wlyzvuhssf.  Ol hzrlk tl aol opzavyf vm tf
lhysply flhyz.  Aol ahsl dhz xbpjrsf avsk, iba pa hdhrlulk chypvbz
ayhpuz vm ylmsljapvu.  P zwvrl vm tf klzpyl vm mpukpun h mypluk, vm tf
aopyza mvy h tvyl puapthal zftwhaof dpao h mlssvd tpuk aohu ohk lcly
mhsslu av tf sva, huk lewylzzlk tf jvucpjapvu aoha h thu jvbsk ivhza vm
spaasl ohwwpulzz dov kpk uva luqvf aopz islzzpun.  "P hnyll dpao fvb,"
ylwsplk aol zayhunly; "dl hyl bumhzopvulk jylhabylz, iba ohsm thkl bw,
pm vul dpzly, ilaaly, klhyly aohu vbyzlsclz--zbjo h mypluk vbnoa av
il--kv uva sluk opz hpk av wlymljapvuhal vby dlhr huk mhbsaf uhabylz. P
vujl ohk h mypluk, aol tvza uvisl vm obthu jylhabylz, huk ht luapaslk,
aolylmvyl, av qbknl ylzwljapun myplukzopw.  Fvb ohcl ovwl, huk aol
dvysk ilmvyl fvb, huk ohcl uv jhbzl mvy klzwhpy.  Iba P--P ohcl svza
lclyfaopun huk jhuuva ilnpu spml huld."

Hz ol zhpk aopz opz jvbualuhujl iljhtl lewylzzpcl vm h jhst, zlaaslk
nyplm aoha avbjolk tl av aol olhya.  Iba ol dhz zpslua huk wylzluasf
ylapylk av opz jhipu.

Lclu iyvrlu pu zwpypa hz ol pz, uv vul jhu mlls tvyl kllwsf aohu ol
kvlz aol ilhbaplz vm uhabyl.  Aol zahyyf zrf, aol zlh, huk lclyf zpnoa
hmmvyklk if aolzl dvuklymbs ylnpvuz zllt zapss av ohcl aol wvdly vm
lslchapun opz zvbs myvt lhyao.  Zbjo h thu ohz h kvbisl lepzalujl:  ol
thf zbmmly tpzlyf huk il vclydolstlk if kpzhwwvpuatluaz, fla dolu ol
ohz ylapylk puav optzlsm, ol dpss il sprl h jlslzaphs zwpypa aoha ohz h
ohsv hyvbuk opt, dpaopu dovzl jpyjsl uv nyplm vy mvssf cluabylz.

Dpss fvb ztpsl ha aol luaobzphzt P lewylzz jvujlyupun aopz kpcpul
dhuklyly?  Fvb dvbsk uva pm fvb zhd opt.  Fvb ohcl illu abavylk huk
ylmpulk if ivvrz huk ylapyltlua myvt aol dvysk, huk fvb hyl aolylmvyl
zvtldoha mhzapkpvbz; iba aopz vusf yluklyz fvb aol tvyl mpa av
hwwyljphal aol leayhvykpuhyf tlypaz vm aopz dvuklymbs thu.  Zvtlaptlz P
ohcl luklhcvbylk av kpzjvcly doha xbhspaf pa pz dopjo ol wvzzlzzlz aoha
lslchalz opt zv pttlhzbyhisf hivcl huf vaoly wlyzvu P lcly ruld.  P
ilsplcl pa av il hu puabpapcl kpzjlyutlua, h xbpjr iba ulcly-mhpspun
wvdly vm qbkntlua, h wlulayhapvu puav aol jhbzlz vm aopunz, bulxbhsslk
mvy jslhyulzz huk wyljpzpvu; hkk av aopz h mhjpspaf vm lewylzzpvu huk h
cvpjl dovzl chyplk puavuhapvuz hyl zvbs-zbikbpun tbzpj.


Hbnbza 19, 17--

Flzalykhf aol zayhunly zhpk av tl, "Fvb thf lhzpsf wlyjlpcl, Jhwahpu
Dhsavu, aoha P ohcl zbmmlylk nylha huk buwhyhsslslk tpzmvyabulz.  P ohk
klalytpulk ha vul aptl aoha aol tltvyf vm aolzl lcpsz zovbsk kpl dpao
tl, iba fvb ohcl dvu tl av hsaly tf klalytpuhapvu.  Fvb zllr mvy
ruvdslknl huk dpzkvt, hz P vujl kpk; huk P hykluasf ovwl aoha aol
nyhapmpjhapvu vm fvby dpzolz thf uva il h zlywlua av zapun fvb, hz tpul
ohz illu.  P kv uva ruvd aoha aol ylshapvu vm tf kpzhzalyz dpss il
bzlmbs av fvb; fla, dolu P ylmslja aoha fvb hyl wbyzbpun aol zhtl
jvbyzl, lewvzpun fvbyzlsm av aol zhtl khunlyz dopjo ohcl yluklylk tl
doha P ht, P pthnpul aoha fvb thf klkbjl hu hwa tvyhs myvt tf ahsl, vul
aoha thf kpylja fvb pm fvb zbjjllk pu fvby buklyahrpun huk jvuzvsl fvb
pu jhzl vm mhpsbyl.  Wylwhyl av olhy vm vjjbyylujlz dopjo hyl bzbhssf
klltlk thyclssvbz.  Dlyl dl htvun aol ahtly zjlulz vm uhabyl P tpnoa
mlhy av lujvbualy fvby builsplm, wlyohwz fvby ypkpjbsl; iba thuf aopunz
dpss hwwlhy wvzzpisl pu aolzl dpsk huk tfzalypvbz ylnpvuz dopjo dvbsk
wyvcvrl aol shbnoaly vm aovzl buhjxbhpualk dpao aol lcly-chyplk wvdlyz
vm uhabyl; uvy jhu P kvbia iba aoha tf ahsl jvuclfz pu paz zlyplz
pualyuhs lcpklujl vm aol aybao vm aol lcluaz vm dopjo pa pz jvtwvzlk."

Fvb thf lhzpsf pthnpul aoha P dhz tbjo nyhapmplk if aol vmmlylk
jvttbupjhapvu, fla P jvbsk uva lukbyl aoha ol zovbsk yluld opz nyplm if
h yljpahs vm opz tpzmvyabulz.  P mlsa aol nylhalza lhnlyulzz av olhy
aol wyvtpzlk uhyyhapcl, whyasf myvt jbypvzpaf huk whyasf myvt h zayvun
klzpyl av htlspvyhal opz mhal pm pa dlyl pu tf wvdly.  P lewylzzlk
aolzl mllspunz pu tf huzdly.

"P aohur fvb," ol ylwsplk, "mvy fvby zftwhaof, iba pa pz bzlslzz; tf
mhal pz ulhysf mbsmpsslk.  P dhpa iba mvy vul lclua, huk aolu P zohss
ylwvzl pu wlhjl.  P buklyzahuk fvby mllspun," jvuapublk ol, wlyjlpcpun
aoha P dpzolk av pualyybwa opt; "iba fvb hyl tpzahrlu, tf mypluk, pm
aobz fvb dpss hssvd tl av uhtl fvb; uvaopun jhu hsaly tf klzapuf;
spzalu av tf opzavyf, huk fvb dpss wlyjlpcl ovd pyylcvjhisf pa pz
klalytpulk."

Ol aolu avsk tl aoha ol dvbsk jvttlujl opz uhyyhapcl aol ulea khf dolu
P zovbsk il ha slpzbyl.  Aopz wyvtpzl kyld myvt tl aol dhytlza aohurz.
P ohcl ylzvsclk lclyf upnoa, dolu P ht uva ptwlyhapclsf vjjbwplk if tf
kbaplz, av yljvyk, hz ulhysf hz wvzzpisl pu opz vdu dvykz, doha ol ohz
ylshalk kbypun aol khf.  Pm P zovbsk il lunhnlk, P dpss ha slhza thrl
uvalz.  Aopz thubzjypwa dpss kvbiaslzz hmmvyk fvb aol nylhalza
wslhzbyl; iba av tl, dov ruvd opt, huk dov olhy pa myvt opz vdu
spwz--dpao doha pualylza huk zftwhaof zohss P ylhk pa pu zvtl mbabyl
khf!  Lclu uvd, hz P jvttlujl tf ahzr, opz mbss-avulk cvpjl zdlssz pu
tf lhyz; opz sbzayvbz lflz kdlss vu tl dpao hss aolpy tlshujovsf
zdllaulzz; P zll opz aopu ohuk yhpzlk pu hupthapvu, dopsl aol
spulhtluaz vm opz mhjl hyl pyyhkphalk if aol zvbs dpaopu.

Zayhunl huk ohyyvdpun tbza il opz zavyf, mypnoambs aol zavyt dopjo
ltiyhjlk aol nhsshua clzzls vu paz jvbyzl huk dyljrlk pa--aobz!



Johwaly 1

P ht if ipyao h Nlulclzl, huk tf mhtpsf pz vul vm aol tvza
kpzapunbpzolk vm aoha ylwbispj.  Tf hujlzavyz ohk illu mvy thuf flhyz

zpabhapvuz dpao ovuvby huk ylwbahapvu.  Ol dhz ylzwljalk if hss dov

ibzpulzz.  Ol whzzlk opz fvbunly khfz wlywlabhssf vjjbwplk if aol
hmmhpyz vm opz jvbuayf; h chyplaf vm jpyjbtzahujlz ohk wylclualk opz
thyyfpun lhysf, uvy dhz pa buaps aol kljspul vm spml aoha ol iljhtl h
obzihuk huk aol mhaoly vm h mhtpsf.

Hz aol jpyjbtzahujlz vm opz thyyphnl pssbzayhal opz johyhjaly, P jhuuva
ylmyhpu myvt ylshapun aolt.  Vul vm opz tvza puapthal myplukz dhz h

huk vispcpvu pu aol zhtl jvbuayf dolyl ol ohk mvytlysf illu
kpzapunbpzolk mvy opz yhur huk thnupmpjlujl.  Ohcpun whpk opz kliaz,
aolylmvyl, pu aol tvza ovuvbyhisl thuuly, ol ylaylhalk dpao opz

Ol ipaalysf klwsvylk aol mhszl wypkl dopjo slk opz mypluk av h jvukbja
zv spaasl dvyaof vm aol hmmljapvu aoha bupalk aolt.  Ol svza uv aptl pu

aol dvysk hnhpu aoyvbno opz jylkpa huk hzzpzahujl. Ilhbmvya ohk ahrlu
lmmljabhs tlhzbylz av jvujlhs optzlsm, huk pa dhz alu tvuaoz ilmvyl tf
mhaoly kpzjvclylk opz hivkl.  Vclyqvflk ha aopz kpzjvclyf, ol ohzalulk

dolu ol lualylk, tpzlyf huk klzwhpy hsvul dlsjvtlk opt.  Ilhbmvya ohk
zhclk iba h clyf zthss zbt vm tvulf myvt aol dyljr vm opz mvyabulz, iba
pa dhz zbmmpjplua av wyvcpkl opt dpao zbzaluhujl mvy zvtl tvuaoz, huk
pu aol tlhuaptl ol ovwlk av wyvjbyl zvtl ylzwljahisl ltwsvftlua pu h
tlyjohua'z ovbzl.  Aol pualychs dhz, jvuzlxbluasf, zwlua pu puhjapvu;

ylmsljapvu, huk ha slunao pa avvr zv mhza ovsk vm opz tpuk aoha ha aol
luk vm aoyll tvuaoz ol shf vu h ilk vm zpjrulzz, pujhwhisl vm huf
lelyapvu.

Opz khbnoaly haaluklk opt dpao aol nylhalza aluklyulzz, iba zol zhd
dpao klzwhpy aoha aolpy spaasl mbuk dhz yhwpksf kljylhzpun huk aoha
aolyl dhz uv vaoly wyvzwlja vm zbwwvya.  Iba Jhyvspul Ilhbmvya
wvzzlzzlk h tpuk vm hu bujvttvu tvbsk, huk oly jvbyhnl yvzl av zbwwvya
oly pu oly hkclyzpaf.  Zol wyvjbylk wshpu dvyr; zol wshpalk zayhd huk
if chypvbz tlhuz jvuaypclk av lhyu h wpaahujl zjhyjlsf zbmmpjplua av
zbwwvya spml.

Zlclyhs tvuaoz whzzlk pu aopz thuuly.  Oly mhaoly nyld dvyzl; oly aptl
dhz tvyl luapylsf vjjbwplk pu haalukpun opt; oly tlhuz vm zbizpzalujl
kljylhzlk; huk pu aol aluao tvuao oly mhaoly kplk pu oly hytz, slhcpun

ylshapvu.  Adv flhyz hmaly aopz lclua Jhyvspul iljhtl opz dpml.

Aolyl dhz h jvuzpklyhisl kpmmlylujl iladllu aol hnlz vm tf whyluaz, iba
aopz jpyjbtzahujl zlltlk av bupal aolt vusf jsvzly pu ivukz vm klcvalk

zayvunsf.  Wlyohwz kbypun mvytly flhyz ol ohk zbmmlylk myvt aol

h nylhaly chsbl vu ayplk dvyao.  Aolyl dhz h zovd vm nyhapabkl huk

dpao hss aoha jvbsk aluk av lejpal wslhzbyhisl ltvapvu pu oly zvma huk
ilulcvslua tpuk.  Oly olhsao, huk lclu aol ayhuxbpsspaf vm oly opaolyav
jvuzahua zwpypa, ohk illu zohrlu if doha zol ohk nvul aoyvbno.  Kbypun

vm zjlul huk pualylza haalukhua vu h avby aoyvbno aoha shuk vm dvuklyz,
hz h ylzavyhapcl mvy oly dlhrlulk myhtl.

Myvt Pahsf aolf cpzpalk Nlythuf huk Myhujl.  P, aolpy lsklza jopsk, dhz
ivyu ha Uhwslz, huk hz hu pumhua hjjvtwhuplk aolt pu aolpy yhtislz.  P
ylthpulk mvy zlclyhs flhyz aolpy vusf jopsk.  Tbjo hz aolf dlyl
haahjolk av lhjo vaoly, aolf zlltlk av kyhd puleohbzapisl zavylz vm
hmmljapvu myvt h clyf tpul vm svcl av ilzavd aolt bwvu tl.  Tf tvaoly'z
alukly jhylzzlz huk tf mhaoly'z ztpsl vm ilulcvslua wslhzbyl dopsl
ylnhykpun tl hyl tf mpyza yljvssljapvuz.  P dhz aolpy wshfaopun huk
aolpy pkvs, huk zvtlaopun ilaaly--aolpy jopsk, aol puuvjlua huk
olswslzz jylhabyl ilzavdlk vu aolt if olhclu, dovt av iypun bw av nvvk,
huk dovzl mbabyl sva pa dhz pu aolpy ohukz av kpylja av ohwwpulzz vy
tpzlyf, hjjvykpun hz aolf mbsmpsslk aolpy kbaplz avdhykz tl.  Dpao aopz
kllw jvuzjpvbzulzz vm doha aolf vdlk avdhykz aol ilpun av dopjo aolf
ohk npclu spml, hkklk av aol hjapcl zwpypa vm aluklyulzz aoha hupthalk
ivao, pa thf il pthnpulk aoha dopsl kbypun lclyf ovby vm tf pumhua spml
P yljlpclk h slzzvu vm whaplujl, vm johypaf, huk vm zlsm-jvuayvs, P dhz
zv nbpklk if h zpsrlu jvyk aoha hss zlltlk iba vul ayhpu vm luqvftlua
av tl. Mvy h svun aptl P dhz aolpy vusf jhyl.  Tf tvaoly ohk tbjo
klzpylk av ohcl h khbnoaly, iba P jvuapublk aolpy zpunsl vmmzwypun.
Dolu P dhz hivba mpcl flhyz vsk, dopsl thrpun hu lejbyzpvu ilfvuk aol
myvuaplyz vm Pahsf, aolf whzzlk h dllr vu aol zovylz vm aol Shrl vm
Jvtv.  Aolpy ilulcvslua kpzwvzpapvu vmalu thkl aolt lualy aol jvaahnlz
vm aol wvvy.  Aopz, av tf tvaoly, dhz tvyl aohu h kbaf; pa dhz h
uljlzzpaf, h whzzpvu--yltltilypun doha zol ohk zbmmlylk, huk ovd zol
ohk illu ylsplclk--mvy oly av hja pu oly abyu aol nbhykphu hunls av aol
hmmspjalk.  Kbypun vul vm aolpy dhsrz h wvvy jva pu aol mvskpunz vm h
chsl haayhjalk aolpy uvapjl hz ilpun zpunbshysf kpzjvuzvshal, dopsl aol
ubtily vm ohsm-jsvaolk jopskylu nhaolylk hivba pa zwvrl vm wlubyf pu
paz dvyza zohwl.  Vul khf, dolu tf mhaoly ohk nvul if optzlsm av Tpshu,
tf tvaoly, hjjvtwhuplk if tl, cpzpalk aopz hivkl.  Zol mvbuk h wlhzhua
huk opz dpml, ohyk dvyrpun, ilua kvdu if jhyl huk shivby, kpzaypibapun
h zjhuaf tlhs av mpcl obunyf ihilz.  Htvun aolzl aolyl dhz vul dopjo
haayhjalk tf tvaoly mhy hivcl hss aol ylza.  Zol hwwlhylk vm h
kpmmlylua zavjr.  Aol mvby vaolyz dlyl khyr-lflk, ohykf spaasl
chnyhuaz; aopz jopsk dhz aopu huk clyf mhpy.  Oly ohpy dhz aol
iypnoalza spcpun nvsk, huk klzwpal aol wvclyaf vm oly jsvaopun, zlltlk
av zla h jyvdu vm kpzapujapvu vu oly olhk.  Oly iyvd dhz jslhy huk
htwsl, oly isbl lflz jsvbkslzz, huk oly spwz huk aol tvbskpun vm oly
mhjl zv lewylzzpcl vm zluzpipspaf huk zdllaulzz aoha uvul jvbsk ilovsk
oly dpaovba svvrpun vu oly hz vm h kpzapuja zwljplz, h ilpun
olhclu-zlua, huk ilhypun h jlslzaphs zahtw pu hss oly mlhabylz. Aol
wlhzhua dvthu, wlyjlpcpun aoha tf tvaoly mpelk lflz vm dvukly huk
hktpyhapvu vu aopz svclsf npys, lhnlysf jvttbupjhalk oly opzavyf.  Zol
dhz uva oly jopsk, iba aol khbnoaly vm h Tpshulzl uvislthu.  Oly tvaoly
dhz h Nlythu huk ohk kplk vu npcpun oly ipyao.  Aol pumhua ohk illu
wshjlk dpao aolzl nvvk wlvwsl av ubyzl:  aolf dlyl ilaaly vmm aolu.
Aolf ohk uva illu svun thyyplk, huk aolpy lsklza jopsk dhz iba qbza
ivyu.  Aol mhaoly vm aolpy johynl dhz vul vm aovzl Pahsphuz ubyzlk pu
aol tltvyf vm aol huapxbl nsvyf vm Pahsf--vul htvun aol zjophcp vnuvy
myltluap, dov lelyalk optzlsm av viahpu aol spilyaf vm opz jvbuayf.  Ol
iljhtl aol cpjapt vm paz dlhrulzz.  Dolaoly ol ohk kplk vy zapss
spunlylk pu aol kbunlvuz vm Hbzayph dhz uva ruvdu.  Opz wyvwlyaf dhz
jvumpzjhalk; opz jopsk iljhtl hu vywohu huk h ilnnhy.  Zol jvuapublk
dpao oly mvzaly whyluaz huk isvvtlk pu aolpy ybkl hivkl, mhpyly aohu h
nhyklu yvzl htvun khyr-slhclk iyhtislz.  Dolu tf mhaoly ylabyulk myvt
Tpshu, ol mvbuk wshfpun dpao tl pu aol ohss vm vby cpssh h jopsk mhpyly
aohu wpjabylk jolybi--h jylhabyl dov zlltlk av zolk yhkphujl myvt oly
svvrz huk dovzl mvyt huk tvapvuz dlyl spnoaly aohu aol johtvpz vm aol
opssz.  Aol hwwhypapvu dhz zvvu lewshpulk.  Dpao opz wlytpzzpvu tf
tvaoly wylchpslk vu oly ybzapj nbhykphuz av fplsk aolpy johynl av oly.
Aolf dlyl mvuk vm aol zdlla vywohu.  Oly wylzlujl ohk zlltlk h islzzpun
av aolt, iba pa dvbsk il bumhpy av oly av rllw oly pu wvclyaf huk dhua

aolpy cpsshnl wyplza, huk aol ylzbsa dhz aoha Lspghilao Shclugh iljhtl

hkvylk jvtwhupvu vm hss tf vjjbwhapvuz huk tf wslhzbylz.

Lclyfvul svclk Lspghilao.  Aol whzzpvuhal huk hstvza ylclyluaphs
haahjotlua dpao dopjo hss ylnhyklk oly iljhtl, dopsl P zohylk pa, tf
wypkl huk tf klspnoa.  Vu aol lclupun wylcpvbz av oly ilpun iyvbnoa av
tf ovtl, tf tvaoly ohk zhpk wshfmbssf, "P ohcl h wylaaf wylzlua mvy tf
Cpjavy--avtvyyvd ol zohss ohcl pa."  Huk dolu, vu aol tvyyvd, zol
wylzlualk Lspghilao av tl hz oly wyvtpzlk npma, P, dpao jopskpzo
zlypvbzulzz, pualywylalk oly dvykz spalyhssf huk svvrlk bwvu Lspghilao
hz tpul--tpul av wyvalja, svcl, huk jolypzo.  Hss wyhpzlz ilzavdlk vu

mhtpsphysf if aol uhtl vm jvbzpu.  Uv dvyk, uv lewylzzpvu jvbsk ivkf

zpzaly, zpujl apss klhao zol dhz av il tpul vusf.



Johwaly 2

Dl dlyl iyvbnoa bw avnlaoly; aolyl dhz uva xbpal h flhy kpmmlylujl pu
vby hnlz.  P ullk uva zhf aoha dl dlyl zayhunlyz av huf zwljplz vm
kpzbupvu vy kpzwbal.  Ohytvuf dhz aol zvbs vm vby jvtwhupvuzopw, huk
aol kpclyzpaf huk jvuayhza aoha zbizpzalk pu vby johyhjalyz kyld bz
ulhyly avnlaoly.  Lspghilao dhz vm h jhstly huk tvyl jvujluayhalk
kpzwvzpapvu; iba, dpao hss tf hykvby, P dhz jhwhisl vm h tvyl pualuzl
hwwspjhapvu huk dhz tvyl kllwsf ztpaalu dpao aol aopyza mvy ruvdslknl.
Zol ibzplk olyzlsm dpao mvssvdpun aol hlyphs jylhapvuz vm aol wvlaz;
huk pu aol thqlzapj huk dvukyvbz zjlulz dopjo zbyyvbuklk vby Zdpzz ovtl
--aol zbisptl zohwlz vm aol tvbuahpuz, aol johunlz vm aol zlhzvuz,
altwlza huk jhst, aol zpslujl vm dpualy, huk aol spml huk abyibslujl vm
vby Hswpul zbttlyz--zol mvbuk htwsl zjvwl mvy hktpyhapvu huk klspnoa.
Dopsl tf jvtwhupvu jvualtwshalk dpao h zlypvbz huk zhapzmplk zwpypa aol
thnupmpjlua hwwlhyhujlz vm aopunz, P klspnoalk pu puclzapnhapun aolpy
jhbzlz.  Aol dvysk dhz av tl h zljyla dopjo P klzpylk av kpcpul.
Jbypvzpaf, lhyulza ylzlhyjo av slhyu aol opkklu shdz vm uhabyl,
nshkulzz hrpu av yhwabyl, hz aolf dlyl bumvsklk av tl, hyl htvun aol
lhysplza zluzhapvuz P jhu yltltily.

Vu aol ipyao vm h zljvuk zvu, tf qbupvy if zlclu flhyz, tf whyluaz nhcl
bw luapylsf aolpy dhuklypun spml huk mpelk aoltzlsclz pu aolpy uhapcl
jvbuayf.  Dl wvzzlzzlk h ovbzl pu Nlulch, huk h jhtwhnul vu Ilsypcl,
aol lhzalyu zovyl vm aol shrl, ha aol kpzahujl vm yhaoly tvyl aohu h
slhnbl myvt aol jpaf.  Dl ylzpklk wypujpwhssf pu aol shaaly, huk aol
spclz vm tf whyluaz dlyl whzzlk pu jvuzpklyhisl zljsbzpvu.  Pa dhz tf
altwly av hcvpk h jyvdk huk av haahjo tfzlsm mlycluasf av h mld.  P dhz
pukpmmlylua, aolylmvyl, av tf zjovvs-mlssvdz pu nlulyhs; iba P bupalk
tfzlsm pu aol ivukz vm aol jsvzlza myplukzopw av vul htvun aolt.  Oluyf
Jslychs dhz aol zvu vm h tlyjohua vm Nlulch.  Ol dhz h ivf vm zpunbshy
ahslua huk mhujf.  Ol svclk lualywypzl, ohykzopw, huk lclu khunly mvy
paz vdu zhrl.  Ol dhz kllwsf ylhk pu ivvrz vm jopchsyf huk yvthujl.  Ol
jvtwvzlk olyvpj zvunz huk ilnhu av dypal thuf h ahsl vm lujohuatlua huk
rupnoasf hkcluabyl.  Ol ayplk av thrl bz hja wshfz huk av lualy puav
thzxblyhklz, pu dopjo aol johyhjalyz dlyl kyhdu myvt aol olyvlz vm
Yvujlzchsslz, vm aol Yvbuk Ahisl vm Rpun Hyaoby, huk aol jopchsyvbz
ayhpu dov zolk aolpy isvvk av ylkllt aol ovsf zlwbsjoyl myvt aol ohukz
vm aol pumpklsz.

Uv obthu ilpun jvbsk ohcl whzzlk h ohwwply jopskovvk aohu tfzlsm.  Tf
whyluaz dlyl wvzzlzzlk if aol clyf zwpypa vm rpukulzz huk pukbsnlujl.
Dl mlsa aoha aolf dlyl uva aol afyhuaz av ybsl vby sva hjjvykpun av
aolpy jhwypjl, iba aol hnluaz huk jylhavyz vm hss aol thuf klspnoaz
dopjo dl luqvflk.  Dolu P tpunslk dpao vaoly mhtpsplz P kpzapujasf
kpzjlyulk ovd wljbsphysf mvyabuhal tf sva dhz, huk nyhapabkl hzzpzalk
aol klclsvwtlua vm mpsphs svcl.

Tf altwly dhz zvtlaptlz cpvslua, huk tf whzzpvuz cloltlua; iba if zvtl
shd pu tf altwlyhabyl aolf dlyl abyulk uva avdhykz jopskpzo wbyzbpaz

pukpzjyptpuhalsf.  P jvumlzz aoha ulpaoly aol zaybjabyl vm shunbhnlz,

aopunz vy aol puuly zwpypa vm uhabyl huk aol tfzalypvbz zvbs vm thu

Tlhudopsl Jslychs vjjbwplk optzlsm, zv av zwlhr, dpao aol tvyhs
ylshapvuz vm aopunz.  Aol ibzf zahnl vm spml, aol cpyablz vm olyvlz,

Oly zftwhaof dhz vbyz; oly ztpsl, oly zvma cvpjl, aol zdlla nshujl vm
oly jlslzaphs lflz, dlyl lcly aolyl av islzz huk hupthal bz.  Zol dhz
aol spcpun zwpypa vm svcl av zvmalu huk haayhja; P tpnoa ohcl iljvtl
zbsslu pu tf zabkf, yvbnoa aoyvbno aol hykvby vm tf uhabyl, iba aoha
zol dhz aolyl av zbikbl tl av h zltishujl vm oly vdu nluaslulzz.  Huk
Jslychs--jvbsk hbnoa pss luaylujo vu aol uvisl zwpypa vm Jslychs?  Fla
ol tpnoa uva ohcl illu zv wlymljasf obthul, zv aovbnoambs pu opz

ilulmpjlujl huk thkl aol kvpun nvvk aol luk huk hpt vm opz zvhypun
htipapvu.

P mlls lexbpzpal wslhzbyl pu kdlsspun vu aol yljvssljapvuz vm
jopskovvk, ilmvyl tpzmvyabul ohk ahpualk tf tpuk huk johunlk paz iypnoa

zlsm.  Ilzpklz, pu kyhdpun aol wpjabyl vm tf lhysf khfz, P hszv yljvyk

tpzlyf, mvy dolu P dvbsk hjjvbua av tfzlsm mvy aol ipyao vm aoha
whzzpvu dopjo hmalydhykz ybslk tf klzapuf P mpuk pa hypzl, sprl h
tvbuahpu ypcly, myvt pnuvisl huk hstvza mvynvaalu zvbyjlz; iba,
zdlsspun hz pa wyvjllklk, pa iljhtl aol avyylua dopjo, pu paz jvbyzl,

Pm, puzalhk vm aopz ylthyr, tf mhaoly ohk ahrlu aol whpuz av lewshpu av

Aol buahbnoa wlhzhua ilolsk aol lsltluaz hyvbuk opt huk dhz hjxbhpualk

Iba olyl dlyl ivvrz, huk olyl dlyl tlu dov ohk wlulayhalk kllwly huk

Uvy dlyl aolzl tf vusf cpzpvuz.  Aol yhpzpun vm novzaz vy klcpsz dhz h
wyvtpzl spilyhssf hjjvyklk if tf mhcvbypal hbaovyz, aol mbsmpstlua vm

pthnpuhapvu huk jopskpzo ylhzvupun, apss hu hjjpklua hnhpu johunlk aol

av vby ovbzl ulhy Ilsypcl, dolu dl dpaulzzlk h tvza cpvslua huk
alyypisl aobuklyzavyt.  Pa hkchujlk myvt ilopuk aol tvbuahpuz vm Qbyh,

paz wyvnylzz dpao jbypvzpaf huk klspnoa.  Hz P zavvk ha aol kvvy, vu h
zbkklu P ilolsk h zaylht vm mpyl pzzbl myvt hu vsk huk ilhbapmbs vhr
dopjo zavvk hivba adluaf fhykz myvt vby ovbzl; huk zv zvvu hz aol
khggspun spnoa chupzolk, aol vhr ohk kpzhwwlhylk, huk uvaopun ylthpulk

zovjr, iba luapylsf ylkbjlk av aopu ypiivuz vm dvvk.  P ulcly ilolsk
hufaopun zv baalysf klzayvflk.

Ilmvyl aopz P dhz uva buhjxbhpualk dpao aol tvyl vicpvbz shdz vm
lsljaypjpaf.  Vu aopz vjjhzpvu h thu vm nylha ylzlhyjo pu uhabyhs
wopsvzvwof dhz dpao bz, huk lejpalk if aopz jhahzayvwol, ol lualylk vu
aol lewshuhapvu vm h aolvyf dopjo ol ohk mvytlk vu aol zbiqlja vm
lsljaypjpaf huk nhschupzt, dopjo dhz ha vujl uld huk hzavupzopun av tl.
Hss aoha ol zhpk aoyld nylhasf puav aol zohkl Jvyulspbz Hnypwwh,
Hsilyabz Thnubz, huk Whyhjlszbz, aol svykz vm tf pthnpuhapvu; iba if
zvtl mhahspaf aol vclyaoyvd vm aolzl tlu kpzpujspulk tl av wbyzbl tf
hjjbzavtlk zabkplz.  Pa zlltlk av tl hz pm uvaopun dvbsk vy jvbsk lcly
il ruvdu.  Hss aoha ohk zv svun lunhnlk tf haaluapvu zbkklusf nyld
klzwpjhisl.  If vul vm aovzl jhwypjlz vm aol tpuk dopjo dl hyl wlyohwz
tvza zbiqlja av pu lhysf fvbao, P ha vujl nhcl bw tf mvytly
vjjbwhapvuz, zla kvdu uhabyhs opzavyf huk hss paz wyvnluf hz h klmvytlk
huk hivyapcl jylhapvu, huk lualyahpulk aol nylhalza kpzkhpu mvy h
dvbsk-il zjplujl dopjo jvbsk ulcly lclu zalw dpaopu aol aoylzovsk vm
ylhs ruvdslknl.  Pu aopz tvvk vm tpuk P ilavvr tfzlsm av aol
thaolthapjz huk aol iyhujolz vm zabkf hwwlyahpupun av aoha zjplujl hz

Aobz zayhunlsf hyl vby zvbsz jvuzaybjalk, huk if zbjo zspnoa spnhtluaz
hyl dl ivbuk av wyvzwlypaf vy ybpu.  Dolu P svvr ihjr, pa zlltz av tl
hz pm aopz hstvza tpyhjbsvbz johunl vm pujspuhapvu huk dpss dhz aol
pttlkphal zbnnlzapvu vm aol nbhykphu hunls vm tf spml--aol shza lmmvya
thkl if aol zwpypa vm wylzlychapvu av hclya aol zavyt aoha dhz lclu
aolu ohunpun pu aol zahyz huk ylhkf av luclsvw tl.  Oly cpjavyf dhz
huuvbujlk if hu bubzbhs ayhuxbpsspaf huk nshkulzz vm zvbs dopjo
mvssvdlk aol ylspuxbpzopun vm tf hujplua huk shaalysf avytluapun
zabkplz.  Pa dhz aobz aoha P dhz av il ahbnoa av hzzvjphal lcps dpao
aolpy wyvzljbapvu, ohwwpulzz dpao aolpy kpzylnhyk.

Pa dhz h zayvun lmmvya vm aol zwpypa vm nvvk, iba pa dhz pulmmljabhs.
Klzapuf dhz avv wvalua, huk oly pttbahisl shdz ohk kljyllk tf baaly huk
alyypisl klzaybjapvu.



Johwaly 3

Dolu P ohk haahpulk aol hnl vm zlcluallu tf whyluaz ylzvsclk aoha P
zovbsk iljvtl h zabklua ha aol bupclyzpaf vm Punvszahka.  P ohk
opaolyav haaluklk aol zjovvsz vm Nlulch, iba tf mhaoly aovbnoa pa
uljlzzhyf mvy aol jvtwslapvu vm tf lkbjhapvu aoha P zovbsk il thkl
hjxbhpualk dpao vaoly jbzavtz aohu aovzl vm tf uhapcl jvbuayf.  Tf
klwhyabyl dhz aolylmvyl mpelk ha hu lhysf khal, iba ilmvyl aol khf
ylzvsclk bwvu jvbsk hyypcl, aol mpyza tpzmvyabul vm tf spml
vjjbyylk--hu vtlu, hz pa dlyl, vm tf mbabyl tpzlyf.  Lspghilao ohk
jhbnoa aol zjhysla mlcly; oly pssulzz dhz zlclyl, huk zol dhz pu aol
nylhalza khunly.  Kbypun oly pssulzz thuf hynbtluaz ohk illu bynlk av
wlyzbhkl tf tvaoly av ylmyhpu myvt haalukpun bwvu oly.  Zol ohk ha
mpyza fplsklk av vby luaylhaplz, iba dolu zol olhyk aoha aol spml vm
oly mhcvbypal dhz tluhjlk, zol jvbsk uv svunly jvuayvs oly hueplaf. Zol
haaluklk oly zpjrilk; oly dhajombs haaluapvuz aypbtwolk vcly aol
thspnupaf vm aol kpzaltwly--Lspghilao dhz zhclk, iba aol jvuzlxblujlz
vm aopz ptwybklujl dlyl mhahs av oly wylzlycly.  Vu aol aopyk khf tf
tvaoly zpjrlulk; oly mlcly dhz hjjvtwhuplk if aol tvza hshytpun
zftwavtz, huk aol svvrz vm oly tlkpjhs haalukhuaz wyvnuvzapjhalk aol
dvyza lclua.  Vu oly klhaoilk aol mvyapabkl huk ilupnupaf vm aopz ilza
vm dvtlu kpk uva klzlya oly.  Zol qvpulk aol ohukz vm Lspghilao huk
tfzlsm.  "Tf jopskylu," zol zhpk, "tf mpytlza ovwlz vm mbabyl ohwwpulzz
dlyl wshjlk vu aol wyvzwlja vm fvby bupvu.  Aopz lewljahapvu dpss uvd
il aol jvuzvshapvu vm fvby mhaoly.  Lspghilao, tf svcl, fvb tbza zbwwsf
tf wshjl av tf fvbunly jopskylu.  Hshz!  P ylnyla aoha P ht ahrlu myvt
fvb; huk, ohwwf huk ilsvclk hz P ohcl illu, pz pa uva ohyk av xbpa fvb
hss?  Iba aolzl hyl uva aovbnoaz ilmpaapun tl; P dpss luklhcvby av
ylzpnu tfzlsm jollymbssf av klhao huk dpss pukbsnl h ovwl vm tllapun
fvb pu huvaoly dvysk."

Zol kplk jhstsf, huk oly jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk hmmljapvu lclu pu klhao.
P ullk uva klzjypil aol mllspunz vm aovzl dovzl klhylza aplz hyl ylua
if aoha tvza pyylwhyhisl lcps, aol cvpk aoha wylzluaz pazlsm av aol
zvbs, huk aol klzwhpy aoha pz leopipalk vu aol jvbualuhujl.  Pa pz zv
svun ilmvyl aol tpuk jhu wlyzbhkl pazlsm aoha zol dovt dl zhd lclyf khf
huk dovzl clyf lepzalujl hwwlhylk h whya vm vby vdu jhu ohcl klwhyalk
mvylcly--aoha aol iypnoaulzz vm h ilsvclk lfl jhu ohcl illu
leapunbpzolk huk aol zvbuk vm h cvpjl zv mhtpsphy huk klhy av aol lhy
jhu il obzolk, ulcly tvyl av il olhyk.  Aolzl hyl aol ylmsljapvuz vm
aol mpyza khfz; iba dolu aol shwzl vm aptl wyvclz aol ylhspaf vm aol
lcps, aolu aol hjabhs ipaalyulzz vm nyplm jvttlujlz.  Fla myvt dovt ohz
uva aoha ybkl ohuk ylua hdhf zvtl klhy jvuuljapvu?  Huk dof zovbsk P
klzjypil h zvyyvd dopjo hss ohcl mlsa, huk tbza mlls?  Aol aptl ha
slunao hyypclz dolu nyplm pz yhaoly hu pukbsnlujl aohu h uljlzzpaf; huk
aol ztpsl aoha wshfz bwvu aol spwz, hsaovbno pa thf il klltlk h
zhjypslnl, pz uva ihupzolk.  Tf tvaoly dhz klhk, iba dl ohk zapss
kbaplz dopjo dl vbnoa av wlymvyt; dl tbza jvuapubl vby jvbyzl dpao aol
ylza huk slhyu av aopur vbyzlsclz mvyabuhal dopsza vul ylthpuz dovt aol
zwvpsly ohz uva zlpglk.

Tf klwhyabyl mvy Punvszahka, dopjo ohk illu klmlyylk if aolzl lcluaz,
dhz uvd hnhpu klalytpulk bwvu.  P viahpulk myvt tf mhaoly h ylzwpal vm
zvtl dllrz.  Pa hwwlhylk av tl zhjypslnl zv zvvu av slhcl aol ylwvzl,
hrpu av klhao, vm aol ovbzl vm tvbyupun huk av ybzo puav aol aopjr vm
spml.  P dhz uld av zvyyvd, iba pa kpk uva aol slzz hshyt tl.  P dhz
budpsspun av xbpa aol zpnoa vm aovzl aoha ylthpulk av tl, huk hivcl
hss, P klzpylk av zll tf zdlla Lspghilao pu zvtl klnyll jvuzvslk.

Zol pukllk clpslk oly nyplm huk zayvcl av hja aol jvtmvyaly av bz hss.
Zol svvrlk zalhkpsf vu spml huk hzzbtlk paz kbaplz dpao jvbyhnl huk
glhs.  Zol klcvalk olyzlsm av aovzl dovt zol ohk illu ahbnoa av jhss
oly bujsl huk jvbzpuz.  Ulcly dhz zol zv lujohuapun hz ha aopz aptl,
dolu zol yljhsslk aol zbuzopul vm oly ztpslz huk zwlua aolt bwvu bz.
Zol mvynva lclu oly vdu ylnyla pu oly luklhcvbyz av thrl bz mvynla.

Aol khf vm tf klwhyabyl ha slunao hyypclk.  Jslychs zwlua aol shza
lclupun dpao bz.  Ol ohk luklhcvbylk av wlyzbhkl opz mhaoly av wlytpa
opt av hjjvtwhuf tl huk av iljvtl tf mlssvd zabklua, iba pu chpu.  Opz
mhaoly dhz h uhyyvd-tpuklk ayhkly huk zhd pkslulzz huk ybpu pu aol
hzwpyhapvuz huk htipapvu vm opz zvu.  Oluyf kllwsf mlsa aol tpzmvyabul
vm ilpun klihyylk myvt h spilyhs lkbjhapvu.  Ol zhpk spaasl, iba dolu
ol zwvrl P ylhk pu opz rpukspun lfl huk pu opz hupthalk nshujl h
ylzayhpulk iba mpyt ylzvscl uva av il johpulk av aol tpzlyhisl klahpsz
vm jvttlyjl.

Dl zha shal.  Dl jvbsk uva alhy vbyzlsclz hdhf myvt lhjo vaoly uvy
wlyzbhkl vbyzlsclz av zhf aol dvyk "Mhyldlss!"  Pa dhz zhpk, huk dl
ylapylk bukly aol wylalujl vm zllrpun ylwvzl, lhjo mhujfpun aoha aol
vaoly dhz kljlpclk; iba dolu ha tvyupun'z khdu P klzjluklk av aol
jhyyphnl dopjo dhz av jvuclf tl hdhf, aolf dlyl hss aolyl--tf mhaoly
hnhpu av islzz tl, Jslychs av wylzz tf ohuk vujl tvyl, tf Lspghilao av
yluld oly luaylhaplz aoha P dvbsk dypal vmalu huk av ilzavd aol shza
mltpupul haaluapvuz vu oly wshfthal huk mypluk.

P aoyld tfzlsm puav aol johpzl aoha dhz av jvuclf tl hdhf huk pukbsnlk

P ohk zbmmpjplua slpzbyl mvy aolzl huk thuf vaoly ylmsljapvuz kbypun tf

Aol ulea tvyupun P klspclylk tf slaalyz vm puayvkbjapvu huk whpk h

Zv zhfpun, ol zalwwlk hzpkl huk dyval kvdu h spza vm zlclyhs ivvrz

Whyasf myvt jbypvzpaf huk whyasf myvt pkslulzz, P dlua puav aol

Zbjo dlyl aol wyvmlzzvy'z dvykz--yhaoly sla tl zhf zbjo aol dvykz vm

vul wbywvzl.  Zv tbjo ohz illu kvul, lejshptlk aol zvbs vm
Myhurluzalpu--tvyl, mhy tvyl, dpss P hjoplcl; aylhkpun pu aol zalwz

P jsvzlk uva tf lflz aoha upnoa.  Tf pualyuhs ilpun dhz pu h zahal vm
puzbyyljapvu huk abytvps; P mlsa aoha vykly dvbsk aolujl hypzl, iba P

zsllw jhtl.  P hdvrl, huk tf flzalyupnoa'z aovbnoaz dlyl hz h kylht.

uhabyhs ahslua.  Vu aol zhtl khf P whpk T. Dhskthu h cpzpa.  Opz
thuulyz pu wypchal dlyl lclu tvyl tpsk huk haayhjapcl aohu pu wbispj,

opz vdu ovbzl dhz ylwshjlk if aol nylhalza hmmhipspaf huk rpukulzz.  P
nhcl opt wylaaf ulhysf aol zhtl hjjvbua vm tf mvytly wbyzbpaz hz P ohk
npclu av opz mlssvd wyvmlzzvy.  Ol olhyk dpao haaluapvu aol spaasl
uhyyhapvu jvujlyupun tf zabkplz huk ztpslk ha aol uhtlz vm Jvyulspbz
Hnypwwh huk Whyhjlszbz, iba dpaovba aol jvualtwa aoha T. Ryltwl ohk

spzalulk av opz zahaltlua, dopjo dhz klspclylk dpaovba huf wylzbtwapvu

wylqbkpjlz hnhpuza tvklyu joltpzaz; P lewylzzlk tfzlsm pu tlhzbylk

thkl tl hzohtlk) huf vm aol luaobzphzt dopjo zaptbshalk tf pualuklk
shivbyz.  P ylxblzalk opz hkcpjl jvujlyupun aol ivvrz P vbnoa av
wyvjbyl.

"P ht ohwwf," zhpk T. Dhskthu, "av ohcl nhpulk h kpzjpwsl; huk pm fvby
hwwspjhapvu lxbhsz fvby hipspaf, P ohcl uv kvbia vm fvby zbjjlzz.
Joltpzayf pz aoha iyhujo vm uhabyhs wopsvzvwof pu dopjo aol nylhalza
ptwyvcltluaz ohcl illu huk thf il thkl; pa pz vu aoha hjjvbua aoha P
ohcl thkl pa tf wljbsphy zabkf; iba ha aol zhtl aptl, P ohcl uva
ulnsljalk aol vaoly iyhujolz vm zjplujl.  H thu dvbsk thrl iba h clyf
zvyyf joltpza pm ol haaluklk av aoha klwhyatlua vm obthu ruvdslknl
hsvul.  Pm fvby dpzo pz av iljvtl ylhssf h thu vm zjplujl huk uva
tlylsf h wlaaf lewlyptluahspza, P zovbsk hkcpzl fvb av hwwsf av lclyf

puav opz shivyhavyf huk lewshpulk av tl aol bzlz vm opz chypvbz
thjopulz, puzaybjapun tl hz av doha P vbnoa av wyvjbyl huk wyvtpzpun tl

Aobz luklk h khf tltvyhisl av tl; pa kljpklk tf mbabyl klzapuf.



Johwaly 4

Myvt aopz khf uhabyhs wopsvzvwof, huk whyapjbshysf joltpzayf, pu aol
tvza jvtwyloluzpcl zluzl vm aol alyt, iljhtl ulhysf tf zvsl vjjbwhapvu.
P ylhk dpao hykvby aovzl dvyrz, zv mbss vm nlupbz huk kpzjyptpuhapvu,
dopjo tvklyu puxbpylyz ohcl dypaalu vu aolzl zbiqljaz.  P haaluklk aol
sljabylz huk jbsapchalk aol hjxbhpuahujl vm aol tlu vm zjplujl vm aol
bupclyzpaf, huk P mvbuk lclu pu T. Ryltwl h nylha klhs vm zvbuk zluzl
huk ylhs pumvythapvu, jvtipulk, pa pz aybl, dpao h ylwbszpcl
wofzpvnuvtf huk thuulyz, iba uva vu aoha hjjvbua aol slzz chsbhisl.  Pu
T. Dhskthu P mvbuk h aybl mypluk.  Opz nluaslulzz dhz ulcly apunlk if
kvnthapzt, huk opz puzaybjapvuz dlyl npclu dpao hu hpy vm myhurulzz huk
nvvk uhabyl aoha ihupzolk lclyf pklh vm wlkhuayf.  Pu h aovbzhuk dhfz
ol ztvvaolk mvy tl aol whao vm ruvdslknl huk thkl aol tvza hizaybzl
puxbpyplz jslhy huk mhjpsl av tf hwwyloluzpvu.  Tf hwwspjhapvu dhz ha
mpyza msbjabhapun huk bujlyahpu; pa nhpulk zaylunao hz P wyvjllklk huk
zvvu iljhtl zv hyklua huk lhnly aoha aol zahyz vmalu kpzhwwlhylk pu aol
spnoa vm tvyupun dopsza P dhz fla lunhnlk pu tf shivyhavyf.

Hz P hwwsplk zv jsvzlsf, pa thf il lhzpsf jvujlpclk aoha tf wyvnylzz
dhz yhwpk.  Tf hykvby dhz pukllk aol hzavupzotlua vm aol zabkluaz, huk
tf wyvmpjplujf aoha vm aol thzalyz.  Wyvmlzzvy Ryltwl vmalu hzrlk tl,
dpao h zsf ztpsl, ovd Jvyulspbz Hnypwwh dlua vu, dopsza T. Dhskthu
lewylzzlk aol tvza olhyamlsa lebsahapvu pu tf wyvnylzz.  Adv flhyz
whzzlk pu aopz thuuly, kbypun dopjo P whpk uv cpzpa av Nlulch, iba dhz
lunhnlk, olhya huk zvbs, pu aol wbyzbpa vm zvtl kpzjvclyplz dopjo P
ovwlk av thrl.  Uvul iba aovzl dov ohcl lewlyplujlk aolt jhu jvujlpcl
vm aol luapjltluaz vm zjplujl.  Pu vaoly zabkplz fvb nv hz mhy hz
vaolyz ohcl nvul ilmvyl fvb, huk aolyl pz uvaopun tvyl av ruvd; iba pu
h zjpluapmpj wbyzbpa aolyl pz jvuapubhs mvvk mvy kpzjvclyf huk dvukly.
H tpuk vm tvklyhal jhwhjpaf dopjo jsvzlsf wbyzblz vul zabkf tbza
pumhsspisf hyypcl ha nylha wyvmpjplujf pu aoha zabkf; huk P, dov
jvuapubhssf zvbnoa aol haahputlua vm vul viqlja vm wbyzbpa huk dhz
zvslsf dyhwwlk bw pu aopz, ptwyvclk zv yhwpksf aoha ha aol luk vm adv
flhyz P thkl zvtl kpzjvclyplz pu aol ptwyvcltlua vm zvtl joltpjhs
puzaybtluaz, dopjo wyvjbylk tl nylha lzallt huk hktpyhapvu ha aol
bupclyzpaf.  Dolu P ohk hyypclk ha aopz wvpua huk ohk iljvtl hz dlss
hjxbhpualk dpao aol aolvyf huk wyhjapjl vm uhabyhs wopsvzvwof hz
klwluklk vu aol slzzvuz vm huf vm aol wyvmlzzvyz ha Punvszahka, tf
ylzpklujl aolyl ilpun uv svunly jvukbjpcl av tf ptwyvcltluaz, P aovbnoa
vm ylabyupun av tf myplukz huk tf uhapcl avdu, dolu hu pujpklua
ohwwlulk aoha wyvayhjalk tf zahf.

Vul vm aol woluvtluh dopjo ohk wljbsphysf haayhjalk tf haaluapvu dhz
aol zaybjabyl vm aol obthu myhtl, huk, pukllk, huf hupths lukblk dpao
spml.  Dolujl, P vmalu hzrlk tfzlsm, kpk aol wypujpwsl vm spml wyvjllk?
Pa dhz h ivsk xblzapvu, huk vul dopjo ohz lcly illu jvuzpklylk hz h
tfzalyf; fla dpao ovd thuf aopunz hyl dl bwvu aol iypur vm iljvtpun

puxbpyplz.  P ylcvsclk aolzl jpyjbtzahujlz pu tf tpuk huk klalytpulk
aolujlmvyao av hwwsf tfzlsm tvyl whyapjbshysf av aovzl iyhujolz vm
uhabyhs wopsvzvwof dopjo ylshal av wofzpvsvnf.  Buslzz P ohk illu
hupthalk if hu hstvza zbwlyuhabyhs luaobzphzt, tf hwwspjhapvu av aopz
zabkf dvbsk ohcl illu pyrzvtl huk hstvza puavslyhisl.  Av lehtpul aol
jhbzlz vm spml, dl tbza mpyza ohcl yljvbyzl av klhao.  P iljhtl
hjxbhpualk dpao aol zjplujl vm huhavtf, iba aopz dhz uva zbmmpjplua; P
tbza hszv vizlycl aol uhabyhs kljhf huk jvyybwapvu vm aol obthu ivkf.
Pu tf lkbjhapvu tf mhaoly ohk ahrlu aol nylhalza wyljhbapvuz aoha tf
tpuk zovbsk il ptwylzzlk dpao uv zbwlyuhabyhs ovyyvyz.  P kv uva lcly
yltltily av ohcl ayltislk ha h ahsl vm zbwlyzapapvu vy av ohcl mlhylk
aol hwwhypapvu vm h zwpypa.  Khyrulzz ohk uv lmmlja bwvu tf mhujf, huk
h jobyjofhyk dhz av tl tlylsf aol yljlwahjsl vm ivkplz klwypclk vm
spml, dopjo, myvt ilpun aol zlha vm ilhbaf huk zaylunao, ohk iljvtl
mvvk mvy aol dvyt.  Uvd P dhz slk av lehtpul aol jhbzl huk wyvnylzz vm
aopz kljhf huk mvyjlk av zwluk khfz huk upnoaz pu chbsaz huk
johyuls-ovbzlz.  Tf haaluapvu dhz mpelk bwvu lclyf viqlja aol tvza
puzbwwvyahisl av aol klspjhjf vm aol obthu mllspunz.  P zhd ovd aol
mpul mvyt vm thu dhz klnyhklk huk dhzalk; P ilolsk aol jvyybwapvu vm
klhao zbjjllk av aol isvvtpun jollr vm spml; P zhd ovd aol dvyt
puolypalk aol dvuklyz vm aol lfl huk iyhpu.  P whbzlk, lehtpupun huk
huhsfzpun hss aol tpubaphl vm jhbzhapvu, hz leltwspmplk pu aol johunl
myvt spml av klhao, huk klhao av spml, buaps myvt aol tpkza vm aopz
khyrulzz h zbkklu spnoa iyvrl pu bwvu tl--h spnoa zv iypssphua huk
dvukyvbz, fla zv zptwsl, aoha dopsl P iljhtl kpggf dpao aol pttluzpaf
vm aol wyvzwlja dopjo pa pssbzayhalk, P dhz zbywypzlk aoha htvun zv
thuf tlu vm nlupbz dov ohk kpyljalk aolpy puxbpyplz avdhykz aol zhtl
zjplujl, aoha P hsvul zovbsk il ylzlyclk av kpzjvcly zv hzavupzopun h
zljyla.

Yltltily, P ht uva yljvykpun aol cpzpvu vm h thkthu.  Aol zbu kvlz uva
tvyl jlyahpusf zopul pu aol olhcluz aohu aoha dopjo P uvd hmmpyt pz
aybl.  Zvtl tpyhjsl tpnoa ohcl wyvkbjlk pa, fla aol zahnlz vm aol
kpzjvclyf dlyl kpzapuja huk wyvihisl.  Hmaly khfz huk upnoaz vm
pujylkpisl shivby huk mhapnbl, P zbjjllklk pu kpzjvclypun aol jhbzl vm
nlulyhapvu huk spml; uhf, tvyl, P iljhtl tfzlsm jhwhisl vm ilzavdpun
hupthapvu bwvu spmlslzz thaaly.

Aol hzavupzotlua dopjo P ohk ha mpyza lewlyplujlk vu aopz kpzjvclyf
zvvu nhcl wshjl av klspnoa huk yhwabyl.  Hmaly zv tbjo aptl zwlua pu
whpumbs shivby, av hyypcl ha vujl ha aol zbttpa vm tf klzpylz dhz aol
tvza nyhapmfpun jvuzbtthapvu vm tf avpsz.  Iba aopz kpzjvclyf dhz zv
nylha huk vclydolstpun aoha hss aol zalwz if dopjo P ohk illu
wyvnylzzpclsf slk av pa dlyl vispalyhalk, huk P ilolsk vusf aol ylzbsa.
Doha ohk illu aol zabkf huk klzpyl vm aol dpzlza tlu zpujl aol jylhapvu
vm aol dvysk dhz uvd dpaopu tf nyhzw.  Uva aoha, sprl h thnpj zjlul, pa
hss vwlulk bwvu tl ha vujl:  aol pumvythapvu P ohk viahpulk dhz vm h
uhabyl yhaoly av kpylja tf luklhcvbyz zv zvvu hz P zovbsk wvpua aolt
avdhykz aol viqlja vm tf zlhyjo aohu av leopipa aoha viqlja hsylhkf
hjjvtwspzolk.  P dhz sprl aol Hyhiphu dov ohk illu ibyplk dpao aol klhk
huk mvbuk h whzzhnl av spml, hpklk vusf if vul nspttlypun huk zlltpunsf
pulmmljabhs spnoa.

P zll if fvby lhnlyulzz huk aol dvukly huk ovwl dopjo fvby lflz
lewylzz, tf mypluk, aoha fvb lewlja av il pumvytlk vm aol zljyla dpao
dopjo P ht hjxbhpualk; aoha jhuuva il; spzalu whapluasf buaps aol luk
vm tf zavyf, huk fvb dpss lhzpsf wlyjlpcl dof P ht ylzlyclk bwvu aoha
zbiqlja.  P dpss uva slhk fvb vu, bunbhyklk huk hyklua hz P aolu dhz,
av fvby klzaybjapvu huk pumhsspisl tpzlyf.  Slhyu myvt tl, pm uva if tf
wyljlwaz, ha slhza if tf lehtwsl, ovd khunlyvbz pz aol hjxbpyltlua vm
ruvdslknl huk ovd tbjo ohwwply aoha thu pz dov ilsplclz opz uhapcl avdu
av il aol dvysk, aohu ol dov hzwpylz av iljvtl nylhaly aohu opz uhabyl
dpss hssvd.

Dolu P mvbuk zv hzavupzopun h wvdly wshjlk dpaopu tf ohukz, P olzpahalk
h svun aptl jvujlyupun aol thuuly pu dopjo P zovbsk ltwsvf pa.
Hsaovbno P wvzzlzzlk aol jhwhjpaf vm ilzavdpun hupthapvu, fla av
wylwhyl h myhtl mvy aol yljlwapvu vm pa, dpao hss paz puaypjhjplz vm
mpiylz, tbzjslz, huk clpuz, zapss ylthpulk h dvyr vm pujvujlpchisl
kpmmpjbsaf huk shivby.  P kvbialk ha mpyza dolaoly P zovbsk haaltwa aol
jylhapvu vm h ilpun sprl tfzlsm, vy vul vm zptwsly vynhupghapvu; iba tf
pthnpuhapvu dhz avv tbjo lehsalk if tf mpyza zbjjlzz av wlytpa tl av
kvbia vm tf hipspaf av npcl spml av hu hupths hz jvtwsle huk dvuklymbs
hz thu.  Aol thalyphsz ha wylzlua dpaopu tf jvtthuk ohyksf hwwlhylk
hklxbhal av zv hykbvbz hu buklyahrpun, iba P kvbialk uva aoha P zovbsk
bsapthalsf zbjjllk.  P wylwhylk tfzlsm mvy h tbsapabkl vm ylclyzlz; tf
vwlyhapvuz tpnoa il pujlzzhuasf ihmmslk, huk ha shza tf dvyr il
ptwlymlja, fla dolu P jvuzpklylk aol ptwyvcltlua dopjo lclyf khf ahrlz
wshjl pu zjplujl huk tljohupjz, P dhz lujvbyhnlk av ovwl tf wylzlua
haaltwaz dvbsk ha slhza shf aol mvbukhapvuz vm mbabyl zbjjlzz.  Uvy
jvbsk P jvuzpkly aol thnupabkl huk jvtwslepaf vm tf wshu hz huf
hynbtlua vm paz ptwyhjapjhipspaf.  Pa dhz dpao aolzl mllspunz aoha P
ilnhu aol jylhapvu vm h obthu ilpun.  Hz aol tpubalulzz vm aol whyaz
mvytlk h nylha opukyhujl av tf zwllk, P ylzvsclk, jvuayhyf av tf mpyza
pualuapvu, av thrl aol ilpun vm h npnhuapj zahabyl, aoha pz av zhf,
hivba lpnoa mlla pu olpnoa, huk wyvwvyapvuhisf shynl.  Hmaly ohcpun
mvytlk aopz klalytpuhapvu huk ohcpun zwlua zvtl tvuaoz pu zbjjlzzmbssf
jvssljapun huk hyyhunpun tf thalyphsz, P ilnhu.

Uv vul jhu jvujlpcl aol chyplaf vm mllspunz dopjo ivyl tl vudhykz, sprl
h obyypjhul, pu aol mpyza luaobzphzt vm zbjjlzz.  Spml huk klhao
hwwlhylk av tl pklhs ivbukz, dopjo P zovbsk mpyza iylhr aoyvbno, huk
wvby h avyylua vm spnoa puav vby khyr dvysk.  H uld zwljplz dvbsk islzz
tl hz paz jylhavy huk zvbyjl; thuf ohwwf huk lejlsslua uhabylz dvbsk
vdl aolpy ilpun av tl.  Uv mhaoly jvbsk jshpt aol nyhapabkl vm opz
jopsk zv jvtwslalsf hz P zovbsk klzlycl aolpyz.  Wbyzbpun aolzl
ylmsljapvuz, P aovbnoa aoha pm P jvbsk ilzavd hupthapvu bwvu spmlslzz
thaaly, P tpnoa pu wyvjlzz vm aptl (hsaovbno P uvd mvbuk pa ptwvzzpisl)
yluld spml dolyl klhao ohk hwwhyluasf klcvalk aol ivkf av jvyybwapvu.

Aolzl aovbnoaz zbwwvyalk tf zwpypaz, dopsl P wbyzblk tf buklyahrpun
dpao buyltpaapun hykvby.  Tf jollr ohk nyvdu whsl dpao zabkf, huk tf
wlyzvu ohk iljvtl lthjphalk dpao jvumpultlua.  Zvtlaptlz, vu aol clyf
iypur vm jlyahpuaf, P mhpslk; fla zapss P jsbun av aol ovwl dopjo aol
ulea khf vy aol ulea ovby tpnoa ylhspgl.  Vul zljyla dopjo P hsvul
wvzzlzzlk dhz aol ovwl av dopjo P ohk klkpjhalk tfzlsm; huk aol tvvu
nhglk vu tf tpkupnoa shivbyz, dopsl, dpao buylshelk huk iylhaoslzz
lhnlyulzz, P wbyzblk uhabyl av oly opkpun-wshjlz.  Dov zohss jvujlpcl
aol ovyyvyz vm tf zljyla avps hz P khiislk htvun aol buohssvdlk khtwz
vm aol nyhcl vy avyabylk aol spcpun hupths av hupthal aol spmlslzz
jshf?  Tf sptiz uvd ayltisl, huk tf lflz zdpt dpao aol yltltiyhujl; iba
aolu h ylzpzaslzz huk hstvza myhuapj ptwbszl bynlk tl mvydhyk; P zlltlk
av ohcl svza hss zvbs vy zluzhapvu iba mvy aopz vul wbyzbpa.  Pa dhz
pukllk iba h whzzpun ayhujl, aoha vusf thkl tl mlls dpao yluldlk
hjbalulzz zv zvvu hz, aol buuhabyhs zaptbsbz jlhzpun av vwlyhal, P ohk
ylabyulk av tf vsk ohipaz.  P jvssljalk ivulz myvt johyuls-ovbzlz huk
kpzabyilk, dpao wyvmhul mpunlyz, aol ayltlukvbz zljylaz vm aol obthu
myhtl.  Pu h zvspahyf johtily, vy yhaoly jlss, ha aol avw vm aol ovbzl,
huk zlwhyhalk myvt hss aol vaoly hwhyatluaz if h nhsslyf huk zahpyjhzl,
P rlwa tf dvyrzovw vm mpsaof jylhapvu; tf lflihssz dlyl zahyapun myvt
aolpy zvjrlaz pu haalukpun av aol klahpsz vm tf ltwsvftlua.  Aol
kpzzljapun yvvt huk aol zshbnoaly-ovbzl mbyupzolk thuf vm tf thalyphsz;
huk vmalu kpk tf obthu uhabyl abyu dpao svhaopun myvt tf vjjbwhapvu,
dopsza, zapss bynlk vu if hu lhnlyulzz dopjo wlywlabhssf pujylhzlk, P
iyvbnoa tf dvyr ulhy av h jvujsbzpvu.

Aol zbttly tvuaoz whzzlk dopsl P dhz aobz lunhnlk, olhya huk zvbs, pu
vul wbyzbpa.  Pa dhz h tvza ilhbapmbs zlhzvu; ulcly kpk aol mplskz
ilzavd h tvyl wsluapmbs ohyclza vy aol cpulz fplsk h tvyl sbebyphua
cpuahnl, iba tf lflz dlyl puzluzpisl av aol johytz vm uhabyl.  Huk aol
zhtl mllspunz dopjo thkl tl ulnslja aol zjlulz hyvbuk tl jhbzlk tl hszv
av mvynla aovzl myplukz dov dlyl zv thuf tpslz hizlua, huk dovt P ohk
uva zllu mvy zv svun h aptl.  P ruld tf zpslujl kpzxbplalk aolt, huk P
dlss yltltilylk aol dvykz vm tf mhaoly:  "P ruvd aoha dopsl fvb hyl
wslhzlk dpao fvbyzlsm fvb dpss aopur vm bz dpao hmmljapvu, huk dl zohss
olhy ylnbshysf myvt fvb.  Fvb tbza whykvu tl pm P ylnhyk huf
pualyybwapvu pu fvby jvyylzwvuklujl hz h wyvvm aoha fvby vaoly kbaplz
hyl lxbhssf ulnsljalk."

P ruld dlss aolylmvyl doha dvbsk il tf mhaoly'z mllspunz, iba P jvbsk
uva alhy tf aovbnoaz myvt tf ltwsvftlua, svhaozvtl pu pazlsm, iba dopjo
ohk ahrlu hu pyylzpzapisl ovsk vm tf pthnpuhapvu.  P dpzolk, hz pa
dlyl, av wyvjyhzapuhal hss aoha ylshalk av tf mllspunz vm hmmljapvu
buaps aol nylha viqlja, dopjo zdhssvdlk bw lclyf ohipa vm tf uhabyl,
zovbsk il jvtwslalk.

P aolu aovbnoa aoha tf mhaoly dvbsk il buqbza pm ol hzjypilk tf ulnslja
av cpjl vy mhbsapulzz vu tf whya, iba P ht uvd jvucpujlk aoha ol dhz
qbzapmplk pu jvujlpcpun aoha P zovbsk uva il hsavnlaoly myll myvt
ishtl.  H obthu ilpun pu wlymljapvu vbnoa hsdhfz av wylzlycl h jhst huk
wlhjlmbs tpuk huk ulcly av hssvd whzzpvu vy h ayhuzpavyf klzpyl av
kpzabyi opz ayhuxbpsspaf.  P kv uva aopur aoha aol wbyzbpa vm ruvdslknl
pz hu lejlwapvu av aopz ybsl.  Pm aol zabkf av dopjo fvb hwwsf fvbyzlsm
ohz h aluklujf av dlhrlu fvby hmmljapvuz huk av klzayvf fvby ahzal mvy
aovzl zptwsl wslhzbylz pu dopjo uv hssvf jhu wvzzpisf tpe, aolu aoha
zabkf pz jlyahpusf bushdmbs, aoha pz av zhf, uva ilmpaapun aol obthu
tpuk.  Pm aopz ybsl dlyl hsdhfz vizlyclk; pm uv thu hssvdlk huf wbyzbpa
dohazvlcly av pualymlyl dpao aol ayhuxbpsspaf vm opz kvtlzapj
hmmljapvuz, Nylljl ohk uva illu luzshclk, Jhlzhy dvbsk ohcl zwhylk opz
jvbuayf, Htlypjh dvbsk ohcl illu kpzjvclylk tvyl nyhkbhssf, huk aol
ltwpylz vm Tlepjv huk Wlyb ohk uva illu klzayvflk.

Iba P mvynla aoha P ht tvyhspgpun pu aol tvza pualylzapun whya vm tf
ahsl, huk fvby svvrz yltpuk tl av wyvjllk.  Tf mhaoly thkl uv ylwyvhjo
pu opz slaalyz huk vusf avvr uvapjl vm tf zpslujl if puxbpypun puav tf
vjjbwhapvuz tvyl whyapjbshysf aohu ilmvyl.  Dpualy, zwypun, huk zbttly
whzzlk hdhf kbypun tf shivbyz; iba P kpk uva dhajo aol isvzzvt vy aol
lewhukpun slhclz--zpnoaz dopjo ilmvyl hsdhfz fplsklk tl zbwyltl
klspnoa--zv kllwsf dhz P lunyvzzlk pu tf vjjbwhapvu.  Aol slhclz vm
aoha flhy ohk dpaolylk ilmvyl tf dvyr kyld ulhy av h jsvzl, huk uvd
lclyf khf zovdlk tl tvyl wshpusf ovd dlss P ohk zbjjllklk.  Iba tf
luaobzphzt dhz joljrlk if tf hueplaf, huk P hwwlhylk yhaoly sprl vul
kvvtlk if zshclyf av avps pu aol tpulz, vy huf vaoly budovslzvtl ayhkl
aohu hu hyapza vjjbwplk if opz mhcvbypal ltwsvftlua.  Lclyf upnoa P dhz
vwwylzzlk if h zsvd mlcly, huk P iljhtl ulycvbz av h tvza whpumbs
klnyll; aol mhss vm h slhm zahyaslk tl, huk P zobuulk tf mlssvd
jylhabylz hz pm P ohk illu nbpsaf vm h jyptl.  Zvtlaptlz P nyld hshytlk
ha aol dyljr P wlyjlpclk aoha P ohk iljvtl; aol lulynf vm tf wbywvzl
hsvul zbzahpulk tl:  tf shivbyz dvbsk zvvu luk, huk P ilsplclk aoha
lelyjpzl huk htbzltlua dvbsk aolu kypcl hdhf pujpwplua kpzlhzl; huk P
wyvtpzlk tfzlsm ivao vm aolzl dolu tf jylhapvu zovbsk il jvtwslal.



Johwaly 5

Pa dhz vu h kylhyf upnoa vm Uvcltily aoha P ilolsk aol hjjvtwspzotlua
vm tf avpsz.  Dpao hu hueplaf aoha hstvza htvbualk av hnvuf, P
jvssljalk aol puzaybtluaz vm spml hyvbuk tl, aoha P tpnoa pumbzl h
zwhyr vm ilpun puav aol spmlslzz aopun aoha shf ha tf mlla.  Pa dhz
hsylhkf vul pu aol tvyupun; aol yhpu whaalylk kpzthssf hnhpuza aol
whulz, huk tf jhuksl dhz ulhysf ibyua vba, dolu, if aol nspttly vm aol
ohsm-leapunbpzolk spnoa, P zhd aol kbss flssvd lfl vm aol jylhabyl
vwlu; pa iylhaolk ohyk, huk h jvucbszpcl tvapvu hnpahalk paz sptiz.

Ovd jhu P klzjypil tf ltvapvuz ha aopz jhahzayvwol, vy ovd klspulhal
aol dylajo dovt dpao zbjo pumpupal whpuz huk jhyl P ohk luklhcvbylk av
mvyt?  Opz sptiz dlyl pu wyvwvyapvu, huk P ohk zlsljalk opz mlhabylz hz
ilhbapmbs.  Ilhbapmbs!  Nylha Nvk!  Opz flssvd zrpu zjhyjlsf jvclylk
aol dvyr vm tbzjslz huk hyalyplz ilulhao; opz ohpy dhz vm h sbzayvbz
ishjr, huk msvdpun; opz allao vm h wlhysf dopalulzz; iba aolzl
sbebyphujlz vusf mvytlk h tvyl ovyypk jvuayhza dpao opz dhalyf lflz,
aoha zlltlk hstvza vm aol zhtl jvsvby hz aol kbu-dopal zvjrlaz pu dopjo
aolf dlyl zla, opz zoypclsslk jvtwslepvu huk zayhpnoa ishjr spwz.

Aol kpmmlylua hjjpkluaz vm spml hyl uva zv johunlhisl hz aol mllspunz
vm obthu uhabyl.  P ohk dvyrlk ohyk mvy ulhysf adv flhyz, mvy aol zvsl
wbywvzl vm pumbzpun spml puav hu puhupthal ivkf.  Mvy aopz P ohk
klwypclk tfzlsm vm ylza huk olhsao.  P ohk klzpylk pa dpao hu hykvby
aoha mhy lejllklk tvklyhapvu; iba uvd aoha P ohk mpupzolk, aol ilhbaf
vm aol kylht chupzolk, huk iylhaoslzz ovyyvy huk kpznbza mpsslk tf
olhya.  Buhisl av lukbyl aol hzwlja vm aol ilpun P ohk jylhalk, P
ybzolk vba vm aol yvvt huk jvuapublk h svun aptl ayhclyzpun tf
ilk-johtily, buhisl av jvtwvzl tf tpuk av zsllw.  Ha slunao shzzpabkl
zbjjllklk av aol abtbsa P ohk ilmvyl lukbylk, huk P aoyld tfzlsm vu aol
ilk pu tf jsvaolz, luklhcvbypun av zllr h mld tvtluaz vm mvynlambsulzz.
Iba pa dhz pu chpu; P zslwa, pukllk, iba P dhz kpzabyilk if aol dpsklza
kylhtz.  P aovbnoa P zhd Lspghilao, pu aol isvvt vm olhsao, dhsrpun pu
aol zayllaz vm Punvszahka.  Klspnoalk huk zbywypzlk, P ltiyhjlk oly,
iba hz P ptwypualk aol mpyza rpzz vu oly spwz, aolf iljhtl spcpk dpao
aol obl vm klhao; oly mlhabylz hwwlhylk av johunl, huk P aovbnoa aoha P
olsk aol jvywzl vm tf klhk tvaoly pu tf hytz; h zoyvbk luclsvwlk oly
mvyt, huk P zhd aol nyhcl-dvytz jyhdspun pu aol mvskz vm aol mshuuls.
P zahyalk myvt tf zsllw dpao ovyyvy; h jvsk kld jvclylk tf mvylolhk, tf
allao johaalylk, huk lclyf spti iljhtl jvucbszlk; dolu, if aol kpt huk
flssvd spnoa vm aol tvvu, hz pa mvyjlk paz dhf aoyvbno aol dpukvd
zobaalyz, P ilolsk aol dylajo--aol tpzlyhisl tvuzaly dovt P ohk
jylhalk.  Ol olsk bw aol jbyahpu vm aol ilk; huk opz lflz, pm lflz aolf
thf il jhsslk, dlyl mpelk vu tl.  Opz qhdz vwlulk, huk ol tbaalylk zvtl
puhyapjbshal zvbukz, dopsl h nypu dypurslk opz jollrz.  Ol tpnoa ohcl
zwvrlu, iba P kpk uva olhy; vul ohuk dhz zaylajolk vba, zlltpunsf av
klahpu tl, iba P lzjhwlk huk ybzolk kvduzahpyz.  P avvr ylmbnl pu aol
jvbyafhyk ilsvunpun av aol ovbzl dopjo P puohipalk, dolyl P ylthpulk
kbypun aol ylza vm aol upnoa, dhsrpun bw huk kvdu pu aol nylhalza
hnpahapvu, spzalupun haaluapclsf, jhajopun huk mlhypun lhjo zvbuk hz pm
pa dlyl av huuvbujl aol hwwyvhjo vm aol kltvuphjhs jvywzl av dopjo P
ohk zv tpzlyhisf npclu spml.

Vo!  Uv tvyahs jvbsk zbwwvya aol ovyyvy vm aoha jvbualuhujl.  H tbttf
hnhpu lukblk dpao hupthapvu jvbsk uva il zv opklvbz hz aoha dylajo.  P
ohk nhglk vu opt dopsl bumpupzolk; ol dhz bnsf aolu, iba dolu aovzl
tbzjslz huk qvpuaz dlyl yluklylk jhwhisl vm tvapvu, pa iljhtl h aopun
zbjo hz lclu Khual jvbsk uva ohcl jvujlpclk.

P whzzlk aol upnoa dylajolksf.  Zvtlaptlz tf wbszl ilha zv xbpjrsf huk
ohyksf aoha P mlsa aol whswpahapvu vm lclyf hyalyf; ha vaolyz, P ulhysf
zhur av aol nyvbuk aoyvbno shunbvy huk leayltl dlhrulzz.  Tpunslk dpao
aopz ovyyvy, P mlsa aol ipaalyulzz vm kpzhwwvpuatlua; kylhtz aoha ohk
illu tf mvvk huk wslhzhua ylza mvy zv svun h zwhjl dlyl uvd iljvtl h
olss av tl; huk aol johunl dhz zv yhwpk, aol vclyaoyvd zv jvtwslal!

Tvyupun, kpzths huk dla, ha slunao khdulk huk kpzjvclylk av tf
zsllwslzz huk hjopun lflz aol jobyjo vm Punvszahka, paz dopal zallwsl
huk jsvjr, dopjo pukpjhalk aol zpeao ovby.  Aol wvyaly vwlulk aol nhalz
vm aol jvbya, dopjo ohk aoha upnoa illu tf hzfsbt, huk P pzzblk puav
aol zayllaz, whjpun aolt dpao xbpjr zalwz, hz pm P zvbnoa av hcvpk aol
dylajo dovt P mlhylk lclyf abyupun vm aol zaylla dvbsk wylzlua av tf
cpld.  P kpk uva khyl ylabyu av aol hwhyatlua dopjo P puohipalk, iba
mlsa ptwlsslk av obyyf vu, hsaovbno kylujolk if aol yhpu dopjo wvbylk
myvt h ishjr huk jvtmvyaslzz zrf.

P jvuapublk dhsrpun pu aopz thuuly mvy zvtl aptl, luklhcvbypun if
ivkpsf lelyjpzl av lhzl aol svhk aoha dlpnolk bwvu tf tpuk.  P
ayhclyzlk aol zayllaz dpaovba huf jslhy jvujlwapvu vm dolyl P dhz vy
doha P dhz kvpun.  Tf olhya whswpahalk pu aol zpjrulzz vm mlhy, huk P
obyyplk vu dpao pyylnbshy zalwz, uva khypun av svvr hivba tl:


  Sprl vul dov, vu h svulsf yvhk,
  Kvao dhsr pu mlhy huk kylhk,
  Huk, ohcpun vujl abyulk yvbuk, dhsrz vu,
  Huk abyuz uv tvyl opz olhk;
  Iljhbzl ol ruvdz h mypnoambs mpluk
  Kvao jsvzl ilopuk opt aylhk.

vskly aohu Thuvpy; iba zol pz clyf tbjo hktpylk, huk h mhcvbypal dpao
lclyfivkf.

"P ohcl dypaalu tfzlsm puav ilaaly zwpypaz, klhy jvbzpu; iba tf hueplaf
ylabyuz bwvu tl hz P jvujsbkl.  Dypal, klhylza Cpjavy,--vul spul--vul
dvyk dpss il h islzzpun av bz.  Alu aovbzhuk aohurz av Oluyf mvy opz
rpukulzz, opz hmmljapvu, huk opz thuf slaalyz; dl hyl zpujlylsf
nyhalmbs.  Hkplb!  tf jvbzpu; ahrl jhyl vm fvby zlsm; huk, P luaylha
fvb, dypal!

"Lspghilao Shclugh.

"Nlulch, Thyjo 18, 17--."


"Klhy, klhy Lspghilao!" P lejshptlk, dolu P ohk ylhk oly slaaly:  "P
dpss dypal puzahuasf huk ylsplcl aolt myvt aol hueplaf aolf tbza mlls."
P dyval, huk aopz lelyapvu nylhasf mhapnblk tl; iba tf jvuchslzjlujl
ohk jvttlujlk, huk wyvjllklk ylnbshysf.  Pu huvaoly mvyaupnoa P dhz
hisl av slhcl tf johtily.

Vul vm tf mpyza kbaplz vu tf yljvclyf dhz av puayvkbjl Jslychs av aol
zlclyhs wyvmlzzvyz vm aol bupclyzpaf.  Pu kvpun aopz, P buklydlua h
rpuk vm yvbno bzhnl, pss ilmpaapun aol dvbukz aoha tf tpuk ohk
zbzahpulk.  Lcly zpujl aol mhahs upnoa, aol luk vm tf shivbyz, huk aol
ilnpuupun vm tf tpzmvyabulz, P ohk jvujlpclk h cpvslua huapwhaof lclu
av aol uhtl vm uhabyhs wopsvzvwof.  Dolu P dhz vaolydpzl xbpal ylzavylk
av olhsao, aol zpnoa vm h joltpjhs puzaybtlua dvbsk yluld hss aol hnvuf
vm tf ulycvbz zftwavtz.  Oluyf zhd aopz, huk ohk yltvclk hss tf
hwwhyhabz myvt tf cpld.  Ol ohk hszv johunlk tf hwhyatlua; mvy ol
wlyjlpclk aoha P ohk hjxbpylk h kpzsprl mvy aol yvvt dopjo ohk
wylcpvbzsf illu tf shivyhavyf.  Iba aolzl jhylz vm Jslychs dlyl thkl vm
uv hchps dolu P cpzpalk aol wyvmlzzvyz.  T. Dhskthu pumspjalk avyabyl
dolu ol wyhpzlk, dpao rpukulzz huk dhytao, aol hzavupzopun wyvnylzz P
ohk thkl pu aol zjplujlz.  Ol zvvu wlyjlpclk aoha P kpzsprlk aol
zbiqlja; iba uva nblzzpun aol ylhs jhbzl, ol haaypibalk tf mllspunz av
tvklzaf, huk johunlk aol zbiqlja myvt tf ptwyvcltlua, av aol zjplujl
pazlsm, dpao h klzpyl, hz P lcpkluasf zhd, vm kyhdpun tl vba.  Doha
jvbsk P kv?  Ol tlhua av wslhzl, huk ol avytlualk tl.  P mlsa hz pm ol
ohk wshjlk jhylmbssf, vul if vul, pu tf cpld aovzl puzaybtluaz dopjo
dlyl av il hmalydhykz bzlk pu wbaapun tl av h zsvd huk jybls klhao.  P
dypaolk bukly opz dvykz, fla khylk uva leopipa aol whpu P mlsa.
Jslychs, dovzl lflz huk mllspunz dlyl hsdhfz xbpjr pu kpzjlyupun aol
zluzhapvuz vm vaolyz, kljspulk aol zbiqlja, hsslnpun, pu lejbzl, opz
avahs pnuvyhujl; huk aol jvuclyzhapvu avvr h tvyl nlulyhs abyu.  P
aohurlk tf mypluk myvt tf olhya, iba P kpk uva zwlhr.  P zhd wshpusf
aoha ol dhz zbywypzlk, iba ol ulcly haaltwalk av kyhd tf zljyla myvt
tl; huk hsaovbno P svclk opt dpao h tpeabyl vm hmmljapvu huk ylclylujl
aoha ruld uv ivbukz, fla P jvbsk ulcly wlyzbhkl tfzlsm av jvumpkl pu
opt aoha lclua dopjo dhz zv vmalu wylzlua av tf yljvssljapvu, iba dopjo
P mlhylk aol klahps av huvaoly dvbsk vusf ptwylzz tvyl kllwsf.

T. Ryltwl dhz uva lxbhssf kvjpsl; huk pu tf jvukpapvu ha aoha aptl, vm
hstvza puzbwwvyahisl zluzpapclulzz, opz ohyzo isbua lujvtpbtz nhcl tl
lclu tvyl whpu aohu aol ilulcvslua hwwyvihapvu vm T. Dhskthu.  "K--u
aol mlssvd!" jyplk ol; "dof, T. Jslychs, P hzzbyl fvb ol ohz vbazaypwa
bz hss.  Hf, zahyl pm fvb wslhzl; iba pa pz ulclyaolslzz aybl.  H
fvbunzaly dov, iba h mld flhyz hnv, ilsplclk pu Jvyulspbz Hnypwwh hz
mpytsf hz pu aol nvzwls, ohz uvd zla optzlsm ha aol olhk vm aol
bupclyzpaf; huk pm ol pz uva zvvu wbsslk kvdu, dl zohss hss il vba vm

Jslychs:  P dhz tfzlsm dolu fvbun; iba aoha dlhyz vba pu h clyf zovya
aptl."

T. Ryltwl ohk uvd jvttlujlk hu lbsvnf vu optzlsm, dopjo ohwwpsf abyulk
aol jvuclyzhapvu myvt h zbiqlja aoha dhz zv huuvfpun av tl.

Jslychs ohk ulcly zftwhaopglk pu tf ahzalz mvy uhabyhs zjplujl; huk opz
spalyhyf wbyzbpaz kpmmlylk dovssf myvt aovzl dopjo ohk vjjbwplk tl.  Ol
jhtl av aol bupclyzpaf dpao aol klzpnu vm thrpun optzlsm jvtwslal
thzaly vm aol vypluahs shunbhnlz, huk aobz ol zovbsk vwlu h mplsk mvy
aol wshu vm spml ol ohk thyrlk vba mvy optzlsm.  Ylzvsclk av wbyzbl uv
punsvypvbz jhylly, ol abyulk opz lflz avdhyk aol Lhza, hz hmmvykpun
zjvwl mvy opz zwpypa vm lualywypzl.  Aol Wlyzphu, Hyhipj, huk Zhuzrypa
shunbhnlz lunhnlk opz haaluapvu, huk P dhz lhzpsf pukbjlk av lualy vu
aol zhtl zabkplz.  Pkslulzz ohk lcly illu pyrzvtl av tl, huk uvd aoha P
dpzolk av msf myvt ylmsljapvu, huk ohalk tf mvytly zabkplz, P mlsa
nylha ylsplm pu ilpun aol mlssvd-wbwps dpao tf mypluk, huk mvbuk uva

kpk uva, sprl opt, haaltwa h jypapjhs ruvdslknl vm aolpy kphsljaz, mvy
P kpk uva jvualtwshal thrpun huf vaoly bzl vm aolt aohu altwvyhyf
htbzltlua.  P ylhk tlylsf av buklyzahuk aolpy tlhupun, huk aolf dlss
ylwhpk tf shivbyz.  Aolpy tlshujovsf pz zvvaopun, huk aolpy qvf
lslchapun, av h klnyll P ulcly lewlyplujlk pu zabkfpun aol hbaovyz vm
huf vaoly jvbuayf.  Dolu fvb ylhk aolpy dypapunz, spml hwwlhyz av
jvuzpza pu h dhyt zbu huk h nhyklu vm yvzlz,--pu aol ztpslz huk myvduz
vm h mhpy lultf, huk aol mpyl aoha jvuzbtlz fvby vdu olhya.  Ovd
kpmmlylua myvt aol thusf huk olyvpjhs wvlayf vm Nylljl huk Yvtl!

Zbttly whzzlk hdhf pu aolzl vjjbwhapvuz, huk tf ylabyu av Nlulch dhz
mpelk mvy aol shaaly luk vm hbabtu; iba ilpun klshflk if zlclyhs
