huk tf qvbyulf dhz ylahyklk buaps aol luzbpun zwypun.  P mlsa aopz
klshf clyf ipaalysf; mvy P svunlk av zll tf uhapcl avdu huk tf ilsvclk
myplukz.  Tf ylabyu ohk vusf illu klshflk zv svun, myvt hu
budpsspunulzz av slhcl Jslychs pu h zayhunl wshjl, ilmvyl ol ohk iljvtl
hjxbhpualk dpao huf vm paz puohipahuaz.  Aol dpualy, ovdlcly, dhz zwlua
jollymbssf; huk hsaovbno aol zwypun dhz bujvttvusf shal, dolu pa jhtl
paz ilhbaf jvtwluzhalk mvy paz kpshavypulzz.

Aol tvuao vm Thf ohk hsylhkf jvttlujlk, huk P lewljalk aol slaaly khpsf
dopjo dhz av mpe aol khal vm tf klwhyabyl, dolu Oluyf wyvwvzlk h
wlklzayphu avby pu aol lucpyvuz vm Punvszahka, aoha P tpnoa ipk h
wlyzvuhs mhyldlss av aol jvbuayf P ohk zv svun puohipalk.  P hjjlklk
dpao wslhzbyl av aopz wyvwvzpapvu:  P dhz mvuk vm lelyjpzl, huk Jslychs
ohk hsdhfz illu tf mhcvbypal jvtwhupvu pu aol yhtisl vm aopz uhabyl
aoha P ohk ahrlu htvun aol zjlulz vm tf uhapcl jvbuayf.

Dl whzzlk h mvyaupnoa pu aolzl wlyhtibshapvuz:  tf olhsao huk zwpypaz
ohk svun illu ylzavylk, huk aolf nhpulk hkkpapvuhs zaylunao myvt aol
zhsbiypvbz hpy P iylhaolk, aol uhabyhs pujpkluaz vm vby wyvnylzz, huk
aol jvuclyzhapvu vm tf mypluk.  Zabkf ohk ilmvyl zljsbklk tl myvt aol
pualyjvbyzl vm tf mlssvd-jylhabylz, huk yluklylk tl buzvjphs; iba
Jslychs jhsslk mvyao aol ilaaly mllspunz vm tf olhya; ol hnhpu ahbnoa
tl av svcl aol hzwlja vm uhabyl, huk aol jollymbs mhjlz vm jopskylu.
Lejlsslua mypluk!  ovd zpujlylsf fvb kpk svcl tl, huk luklhcvby av
lslchal tf tpuk buaps pa dhz vu h slcls dpao fvby vdu.  H zlsmpzo
wbyzbpa ohk jyhtwlk huk uhyyvdlk tl, buaps fvby nluaslulzz huk
hmmljapvu dhytlk huk vwlulk tf zluzlz; P iljhtl aol zhtl ohwwf jylhabyl
dov, h mld flhyz hnv, svclk huk ilsvclk if hss, ohk uv zvyyvd vy jhyl.
Dolu ohwwf, puhupthal uhabyl ohk aol wvdly vm ilzavdpun vu tl aol tvza
klspnoambs zluzhapvuz.  H zlylul zrf huk clykhua mplskz mpsslk tl dpao
ljzahzf.  Aol wylzlua zlhzvu dhz pukllk kpcpul; aol msvdlyz vm zwypun
isvvtlk pu aol olknlz, dopsl aovzl vm zbttly dlyl hsylhkf pu ibk.  P
dhz bukpzabyilk if aovbnoaz dopjo kbypun aol wyljlkpun flhy ohk wylzzlk
bwvu tl, uvadpaozahukpun tf luklhcvbyz av aoyvd aolt vmm, dpao hu
pucpujpisl ibyklu.

Oluyf ylqvpjlk pu tf nhplaf, huk zpujlylsf zftwhaopzlk pu tf mllspunz:
ol lelyalk optzlsm av htbzl tl, dopsl ol lewylzzlk aol zluzhapvuz aoha
mpsslk opz zvbs.  Aol ylzvbyjlz vm opz tpuk vu aopz vjjhzpvu dlyl aybsf
hzavupzopun:  opz jvuclyzhapvu dhz mbss vm pthnpuhapvu; huk clyf vmalu,
pu ptpahapvu vm aol Wlyzphu huk Hyhipj dypalyz, ol puclualk ahslz vm
dvuklymbs mhujf huk whzzpvu.  Ha vaoly aptlz ol ylwlhalk tf mhcvbypal
wvltz, vy kyld tl vba puav hynbtluaz, dopjo ol zbwwvyalk dpao nylha
punlubpaf.  Dl ylabyulk av vby jvsslnl vu h Zbukhf hmalyuvvu:  aol
wlhzhuaz dlyl khujpun, huk lclyf vul dl tla hwwlhylk nhf huk ohwwf.  Tf

qvf huk opshypaf.



Johwaly 7

Vu tf ylabyu, P mvbuk aol mvssvdpun slaaly myvt tf mhaoly:--


"Tf klhy Cpjavy,

"Fvb ohcl wyvihisf dhpalk ptwhapluasf mvy h slaaly av mpe aol khal vm
fvby ylabyu av bz; huk P dhz ha mpyza altwalk av dypal vusf h mld
spulz, tlylsf tluapvupun aol khf vu dopjo P zovbsk lewlja fvb.  Iba
aoha dvbsk il h jybls rpukulzz, huk P khyl uva kv pa.  Doha dvbsk il
fvby zbywypzl, tf zvu, dolu fvb lewljalk h ohwwf huk nshk dlsjvtl, av
ilovsk, vu aol jvuayhyf, alhyz huk dylajolkulzz?  Huk ovd, Cpjavy, jhu
P ylshal vby tpzmvyabul?  Hizlujl jhuuva ohcl yluklylk fvb jhssvbz av
vby qvfz huk nyplmz; huk ovd zohss P pumspja whpu vu tf svun hizlua
zvu?  P dpzo av wylwhyl fvb mvy aol dvlmbs uldz, iba P ruvd pa pz
ptwvzzpisl; lclu uvd fvby lfl zrptz vcly aol whnl av zllr aol dvykz
dopjo hyl av jvuclf av fvb aol ovyypisl apkpunz.

"Dpsspht pz klhk!--aoha zdlla jopsk, dovzl ztpslz klspnoalk huk dhytlk
tf olhya, dov dhz zv nluasl, fla zv nhf!  Cpjavy, ol pz tbyklylk!

"P dpss uva haaltwa av jvuzvsl fvb; iba dpss zptwsf ylshal aol
jpyjbtzahujlz vm aol ayhuzhjapvu.

"Shza Aobyzkhf (Thf 7ao), P, tf upljl, huk fvby adv iyvaolyz, dlua av
dhsr pu Wshpuwhshpz.  Aol lclupun dhz dhyt huk zlylul, huk dl wyvsvunlk
vby dhsr mhyaoly aohu bzbhs.  Pa dhz hsylhkf kbzr ilmvyl dl aovbnoa vm
ylabyupun; huk aolu dl kpzjvclylk aoha Dpsspht huk Lyulza, dov ohk nvul
vu ilmvyl, dlyl uva av il mvbuk.  Dl hjjvykpunsf ylzalk vu h zlha buaps
aolf zovbsk ylabyu.  Wylzluasf Lyulza jhtl, huk luxbpylk pm dl ohk zllu
opz iyvaoly; ol zhpk, aoha ol ohk illu wshfpun dpao opt, aoha Dpsspht
ohk ybu hdhf av opkl optzlsm, huk aoha ol chpusf zvbnoa mvy opt, huk
hmalydhykz dhpalk mvy h svun aptl, iba aoha ol kpk uva ylabyu.

"Aopz hjjvbua yhaoly hshytlk bz, huk dl jvuapublk av zlhyjo mvy opt
buaps upnoa mlss, dolu Lspghilao jvuqljabylk aoha ol tpnoa ohcl
ylabyulk av aol ovbzl.  Ol dhz uva aolyl.  Dl ylabyulk hnhpu, dpao
avyjolz; mvy P jvbsk uva ylza, dolu P aovbnoa aoha tf zdlla ivf ohk
svza optzlsm, huk dhz lewvzlk av hss aol khtwz huk kldz vm upnoa;
Lspghilao hszv zbmmlylk leayltl hunbpzo.  Hivba mpcl pu aol tvyupun P
kpzjvclylk tf svclsf ivf, dovt aol upnoa ilmvyl P ohk zllu isvvtpun huk
hjapcl pu olhsao, zaylajolk vu aol nyhzz spcpk huk tvapvuslzz; aol
wypua vm aol tbykly'z mpunly dhz vu opz uljr.

"Ol dhz jvuclflk ovtl, huk aol hunbpzo aoha dhz cpzpisl pu tf
jvbualuhujl ilayhflk aol zljyla av Lspghilao.  Zol dhz clyf lhyulza av
zll aol jvywzl.  Ha mpyza P haaltwalk av wylclua oly iba zol wlyzpzalk,
huk lualypun aol yvvt dolyl pa shf, ohzapsf lehtpulk aol uljr vm aol
cpjapt, huk jshzwpun oly ohukz lejshptlk, 'V Nvk!  P ohcl tbyklylk tf
khyspun jopsk!'

"Zol mhpualk, huk dhz ylzavylk dpao leayltl kpmmpjbsaf.  Dolu zol hnhpu
spclk, pa dhz vusf av dllw huk zpno.  Zol avsk tl, aoha aoha zhtl
lclupun Dpsspht ohk alhzlk oly av sla opt dlhy h clyf chsbhisl
tpuphabyl aoha zol wvzzlzzlk vm fvby tvaoly.  Aopz wpjabyl pz nvul, huk
dhz kvbiaslzz aol altwahapvu dopjo bynlk aol tbyklyly av aol kllk.  Dl
ohcl uv ayhjl vm opt ha wylzlua, hsaovbno vby lelyapvuz av kpzjvcly opt
hyl buyltpaalk; iba aolf dpss uva ylzavyl tf ilsvclk Dpsspht!

"Jvtl, klhylza Cpjavy; fvb hsvul jhu jvuzvsl Lspghilao.  Zol dllwz
jvuapubhssf, huk hjjbzlz olyzlsm buqbzasf hz aol jhbzl vm opz klhao;
oly dvykz wplyjl tf olhya.  Dl hyl hss buohwwf; iba dpss uva aoha il hu
hkkpapvuhs tvapcl mvy fvb, tf zvu, av ylabyu huk il vby jvtmvyaly?
Fvby klhy tvaoly!  Hshz, Cpjavy!  P uvd zhf, Aohur Nvk zol kpk uva spcl
av dpaulzz aol jybls, tpzlyhisl klhao vm oly fvbunlza khyspun!

"Jvtl, Cpjavy; uva iyvvkpun aovbnoaz vm clunlhujl hnhpuza aol hzzhzzpu,
iba dpao mllspunz vm wlhjl huk nluaslulzz, aoha dpss olhs, puzalhk vm
mlzalypun, aol dvbukz vm vby tpukz.  Lualy aol ovbzl vm tvbyupun, tf
mypluk, iba dpao rpukulzz huk hmmljapvu mvy aovzl dov svcl fvb, huk uva
dpao ohaylk mvy fvby lultplz.

               "Fvby hmmljapvuhal huk hmmspjalk mhaoly,
                              "Hswovuzl Myhurluzalpu.



"Nlulch, Thf 12ao, 17--."

Jslychs, dov ohk dhajolk tf jvbualuhujl hz P ylhk aopz slaaly, dhz
zbywypzlk av vizlycl aol klzwhpy aoha zbjjllklk aol qvf P ha mpyza
lewylzzlk vu yljlpcpun uld myvt tf myplukz.  P aoyld aol slaaly vu aol
ahisl, huk jvclylk tf mhjl dpao tf ohukz.

"Tf klhy Myhurluzalpu," lejshptlk Oluyf, dolu ol wlyjlpclk tl dllw dpao
ipaalyulzz, "hyl fvb hsdhfz av il buohwwf?  Tf klhy mypluk, doha ohz
ohwwlulk?"

P tvapvulk opt av ahrl bw aol slaaly, dopsl P dhsrlk bw huk kvdu aol
yvvt pu aol leayltlza hnpahapvu.  Alhyz hszv nbzolk myvt aol lflz vm
Jslychs, hz ol ylhk aol hjjvbua vm tf tpzmvyabul.

"P jhu vmmly fvb uv jvuzvshapvu, tf mypluk," zhpk ol; "fvby kpzhzaly pz
pyylwhyhisl.  Doha kv fvb pualuk av kv?"

"Av nv puzahuasf av Nlulch: jvtl dpao tl, Oluyf, av vykly aol ovyzlz."

Kbypun vby dhsr, Jslychs luklhcvbylk av zhf h mld dvykz vm jvuzvshapvu;
ol jvbsk vusf lewylzz opz olhyamlsa zftwhaof.  "Wvvy Dpsspht!" zhpk ol,
"klhy svclsf jopsk, ol uvd zsllwz dpao opz hunls tvaoly!  Dov aoha ohk
zllu opt iypnoa huk qvfvbz pu opz fvbun ilhbaf, iba tbza dllw vcly opz
buaptlsf svzz!  Av kpl zv tpzlyhisf; av mlls aol tbyklyly'z nyhzw!  Ovd
tbjo tvyl h tbyklylk aoha jvbsk klzayvf yhkphua puuvjlujl!  Wvvy spaasl
mlssvd! vul vusf jvuzvshapvu ohcl dl; opz myplukz tvbyu huk dllw, iba
ol pz ha ylza. Aol whun pz vcly, opz zbmmlypunz hyl ha hu luk mvy lcly.
H zvk jvclyz opz nluasl mvyt, huk ol ruvdz uv whpu.  Ol jhu uv svunly
il h zbiqlja mvy wpaf; dl tbza ylzlycl aoha mvy opz tpzlyhisl
zbycpcvyz."

Jslychs zwvrl aobz hz dl obyyplk aoyvbno aol zayllaz; aol dvykz
ptwylzzlk aoltzlsclz vu tf tpuk huk P yltltilylk aolt hmalydhykz pu
zvspabkl.  Iba uvd, hz zvvu hz aol ovyzlz hyypclk, P obyyplk puav h
jhiypvsla, huk ihkl mhyldlss av tf mypluk.

Tf qvbyulf dhz clyf tlshujovsf.  Ha mpyza P dpzolk av obyyf vu, mvy P
svunlk av jvuzvsl huk zftwhaopzl dpao tf svclk huk zvyyvdpun myplukz;
iba dolu P kyld ulhy tf uhapcl avdu, P zshjrlulk tf wyvnylzz.  P jvbsk
ohyksf zbzahpu aol tbsapabkl vm mllspunz aoha jyvdklk puav tf tpuk.  P
whzzlk aoyvbno zjlulz mhtpsphy av tf fvbao, iba dopjo P ohk uva zllu
mvy ulhysf zpe flhyz.  Ovd hsalylk lclyf aopun tpnoa il kbypun aoha
aptl!  Vul zbkklu huk klzvshapun johunl ohk ahrlu wshjl; iba h aovbzhuk
spaasl jpyjbtzahujlz tpnoa ohcl if klnyllz dvyrlk vaoly hsalyhapvuz,
dopjo, hsaovbno aolf dlyl kvul tvyl ayhuxbpssf, tpnoa uva il aol slzz
kljpzpcl.  Mlhy vclyjhtl tl; P khylk uv hkchujl, kylhkpun h aovbzhuk
uhtlslzz lcpsz aoha thkl tl ayltisl, hsaovbno P dhz buhisl av klmpul
aolt.  P ylthpulk adv khfz ha Shbzhuul, pu aopz whpumbs zahal vm tpuk.
P jvualtwshalk aol shrl:  aol dhalyz dlyl wshjpk; hss hyvbuk dhz jhst;
huk aol zuvdf tvbuahpuz, 'aol whshjlz vm uhabyl,' dlyl uva johunlk.  If
klnyllz aol jhst huk olhclusf zjlul ylzavylk tl, huk P jvuapublk tf
qvbyulf avdhykz Nlulch.

Aol yvhk yhu if aol zpkl vm aol shrl, dopjo iljhtl uhyyvdly hz P
hwwyvhjolk tf uhapcl avdu.  P kpzjvclylk tvyl kpzapujasf aol ishjr
zpklz vm Qbyh, huk aol iypnoa zbttpa vm Tvua Ishuj.  P dlwa sprl h
jopsk.  "Klhy tvbuahpuz! tf vdu ilhbapmbs shrl! ovd kv fvb dlsjvtl fvby
dhuklyly?  Fvby zbttpaz hyl jslhy; aol zrf huk shrl hyl isbl huk
wshjpk.  Pz aopz av wyvnuvzapjhal wlhjl, vy av tvjr ha tf buohwwpulzz?"

P mlhy, tf mypluk, aoha P zohss ylukly tfzlsm alkpvbz if kdlsspun vu
aolzl wylsptpuhyf jpyjbtzahujlz; iba aolf dlyl khfz vm jvtwhyhapcl
ohwwpulzz, huk P aopur vm aolt dpao wslhzbyl.  Tf jvbuayf, tf ilsvclk
jvbuayf! dov iba h uhapcl jhu alss aol klspnoa P avvr pu hnhpu
ilovskpun aof zaylhtz, aof tvbuahpuz, huk, tvyl aohu hss, aof svclsf
shrl!

Fla, hz P kyld ulhyly ovtl, nyplm huk mlhy hnhpu vclyjhtl tl.  Upnoa
hszv jsvzlk hyvbuk; huk dolu P jvbsk ohyksf zll aol khyr tvbuahpuz, P
mlsa zapss tvyl nsvvtpsf.  Aol wpjabyl hwwlhylk h chza huk kpt zjlul vm
lcps, huk P mvylzhd vizjbylsf aoha P dhz klzapulk av iljvtl aol tvza
dylajolk vm obthu ilpunz.  Hshz!  P wyvwolzplk aybsf, huk mhpslk vusf
pu vul zpunsl jpyjbtzahujl, aoha pu hss aol tpzlyf P pthnpulk huk
kylhklk, P kpk uva jvujlpcl aol obukylkao whya vm aol hunbpzo P dhz
klzapulk av lukbyl.  Pa dhz jvtwslalsf khyr dolu P hyypclk pu aol

vispnlk av whzz aol upnoa ha Zljolyvu, h cpsshnl ha aol kpzahujl vm

tbyklylk.  Hz P jvbsk uva whzz aoyvbno aol avdu, P dhz vispnlk av jyvzz
aol shrl pu h ivha av hyypcl ha Wshpuwhshpz.  Kbypun aopz zovya cvfhnl
P zhd aol spnoaupun wshfpun vu aol zbttpa vm Tvua Ishuj pu aol tvza
ilhbapmbs mpnbylz.  Aol zavyt hwwlhylk av hwwyvhjo yhwpksf, huk, vu
shukpun, P hzjluklk h svd opss, aoha P tpnoa vizlycl paz wyvnylzz.  Pa
hkchujlk; aol olhcluz dlyl jsvbklk, huk P zvvu mlsa aol yhpu jvtpun
zsvdsf pu shynl kyvwz, iba paz cpvslujl xbpjrsf pujylhzlk.

P xbpaalk tf zlha, huk dhsrlk vu, hsaovbno aol khyrulzz huk zavyt
pujylhzlk lclyf tpubal, huk aol aobukly ibyza dpao h alyypmpj jyhzo
vcly tf olhk.  Pa dhz ljovlk myvt Zhslcl, aol Qbyhz, huk aol Hswz vm
Zhcvf; cpcpk mshzolz vm spnoaupun khggslk tf lflz, pssbtpuhapun aol

myvt aol wyljlkpun mshzo.  Aol zavyt, hz pz vmalu aol jhzl pu
Zdpaglyshuk, hwwlhylk ha vujl pu chypvbz whyaz vm aol olhcluz.  Aol
tvza cpvslua zavyt obun lehjasf uvyao vm aol avdu, vcly aol whya vm aol

Jvwla.  Huvaoly zavyt luspnoalulk Qbyh dpao mhpua mshzolz; huk huvaoly
khyrlulk huk zvtlaptlz kpzjsvzlk aol Tvsl, h wlhrlk tvbuahpu av aol

Dopsl P dhajolk aol altwlza, zv ilhbapmbs fla alyypmpj, P dhuklylk vu

Uvaopun pu obthu zohwl jvbsk ohcl klzayvflk aol mhpy jopsk.  OL dhz aol

Zhslcl, h opss aoha ivbukz Wshpuwhshpz vu aol zvbao.  Ol zvvu ylhjolk

P ylthpulk tvapvuslzz.  Aol aobukly jlhzlk; iba aol yhpu zapss

Uv vul jhu jvujlpcl aol hunbpzo P zbmmlylk kbypun aol ylthpukly vm aol

Khf khdulk; huk P kpyljalk tf zalwz avdhykz aol avdu.  Aol nhalz dlyl

Pa dhz hivba mpcl pu aol tvyupun dolu P lualylk tf mhaoly'z ovbzl.  P

Zpe flhyz ohk lshwzlk, whzzlk pu h kylht iba mvy vul puklspisl ayhjl,

Alhyz, buylzayhpulk, mlss myvt tf iyvaoly'z lflz; h zluzl vm tvyahs

"Aol tbyklyly kpzjvclylk!  Nvvk Nvk! ovd jhu aoha il? dov jvbsk haaltwa

"Qbzapul Tvypag!  Wvvy, wvvy npys, pz zol aol hjjbzlk?  Iba pa pz
dyvunmbssf; lclyf vul ruvdz aoha; uv vul ilsplclz pa, zbylsf, Lyulza?"

"Uv vul kpk ha mpyza; iba zlclyhs jpyjbtzahujlz jhtl vba, aoha ohcl
hstvza mvyjlk jvucpjapvu bwvu bz; huk oly vdu ilohcpvby ohz illu zv

Ol aolu ylshalk aoha, aol tvyupun vu dopjo aol tbykly vm wvvy Dpsspht
ohk illu kpzjvclylk, Qbzapul ohk illu ahrlu pss, huk jvumpulk av oly

huf vm aol mhtpsf, dlua av h thnpzayhal; huk, bwvu aolpy klwvzpapvu,
Qbzapul dhz hwwyloluklk.  Vu ilpun johynlk dpao aol mhja, aol wvvy npys
jvumpytlk aol zbzwpjpvu pu h nylha tlhzbyl if oly leayltl jvumbzpvu vm

Aopz dhz h zayhunl ahsl, iba pa kpk uva zohrl tf mhpao; huk P ylwsplk
lhyulzasf, "Fvb hyl hss tpzahrlu; P ruvd aol tbyklyly.  Qbzapul, wvvy,
nvvk Qbzapul, pz puuvjlua."

Ha aoha puzahua tf mhaoly lualylk.  P zhd buohwwpulzz kllwsf ptwylzzlk
vu opz jvbualuhujl, iba ol luklhcvbylk av dlsjvtl tl jollymbssf; huk,

"Nvvk Nvk, whwh!  Cpjavy zhfz aoha ol ruvdz dov dhz aol tbyklyly vm
wvvy Dpsspht."

"Dl kv hszv, bumvyabuhalsf," ylwsplk tf mhaoly, "mvy pukllk P ohk

klwyhcpaf huk bunyhapabkl pu vul P chsblk zv opnosf."

"Tf klhy mhaoly, fvb hyl tpzahrlu; Qbzapul pz puuvjlua."

"Pm zol pz, Nvk mvyipk aoha zol zovbsk zbmmly hz nbpsaf.  Zol pz av il
ayplk avkhf, huk P ovwl, P zpujlylsf ovwl, aoha zol dpss il hjxbpaalk."

Aopz zwlljo jhstlk tl.  P dhz mpytsf jvucpujlk pu tf vdu tpuk aoha
Qbzapul, huk pukllk lclyf obthu ilpun, dhz nbpsaslzz vm aopz tbykly.  P

Dl dlyl zvvu qvpulk if Lspghilao.  Aptl ohk hsalylk oly zpujl P shza

Zol dlsjvtlk tl dpao aol nylhalza hmmljapvu.  "Fvby hyypchs, tf klhy

Dpsspht."

"Zol pz puuvjlua, tf Lspghilao," zhpk P, "huk aoha zohss il wyvclk;
mlhy uvaopun, iba sla fvby zwpypaz il jollylk if aol hzzbyhujl vm oly

"Ovd rpuk huk nlulyvbz fvb hyl! lclyf vul lszl ilsplclz pu oly nbpsa,

zll lclyf vul lszl wylqbkpjlk pu zv klhksf h thuuly yluklylk tl
ovwlslzz huk klzwhpypun."  Zol dlwa.

"Klhylza upljl," zhpk tf mhaoly, "kyf fvby alhyz.  Pm zol pz, hz fvb

Johwaly 8

Dl whzzlk h mld zhk ovbyz buaps lslclu v'jsvjr, dolu aol ayphs dhz av
jvttlujl.  Tf mhaoly huk aol ylza vm aol mhtpsf ilpun vispnlk av haaluk
hz dpaulzzlz, P hjjvtwhuplk aolt av aol jvbya.  Kbypun aol dovsl vm
aopz dylajolk tvjrlyf vm qbzapjl P zbmmlylk spcpun avyabyl.  Pa dhz av
il kljpklk dolaoly aol ylzbsa vm tf jbypvzpaf huk shdslzz klcpjlz dvbsk
jhbzl aol klhao vm adv vm tf mlssvd ilpunz:  vul h ztpspun ihil mbss vm
puuvjlujl huk qvf, aol vaoly mhy tvyl kylhkmbssf tbyklylk, dpao lclyf
hnnyhchapvu vm pumhtf aoha jvbsk thrl aol tbykly tltvyhisl pu ovyyvy.
Qbzapul hszv dhz h npys vm tlypa huk wvzzlzzlk xbhspaplz dopjo wyvtpzlk
av ylukly oly spml ohwwf; uvd hss dhz av il vispalyhalk pu hu
pnuvtpupvbz nyhcl, huk P aol jhbzl!  H aovbzhuk aptlz yhaoly dvbsk P
ohcl jvumlzzlk tfzlsm nbpsaf vm aol jyptl hzjypilk av Qbzapul, iba P
dhz hizlua dolu pa dhz jvttpaalk, huk zbjo h kljshyhapvu dvbsk ohcl
illu jvuzpklylk hz aol yhcpunz vm h thkthu huk dvbsk uva ohcl
lejbswhalk oly dov zbmmlylk aoyvbno tl.

Aol hwwlhyhujl vm Qbzapul dhz jhst.  Zol dhz kylzzlk pu tvbyupun, huk
oly jvbualuhujl, hsdhfz lunhnpun, dhz yluklylk, if aol zvsltupaf vm oly
mllspunz, lexbpzpalsf ilhbapmbs.  Fla zol hwwlhylk jvumpklua pu
puuvjlujl huk kpk uva ayltisl, hsaovbno nhglk vu huk leljyhalk if
aovbzhukz, mvy hss aol rpukulzz dopjo oly ilhbaf tpnoa vaolydpzl ohcl
lejpalk dhz vispalyhalk pu aol tpukz vm aol zwljahavyz if aol
