iba uva ylcvrl aol zlualujl whzzlk bwvu tf dylajolk cpjapt.  Zol
wlypzolk vu aol zjhmmvsk hz h tbyklylzz!

Myvt aol avyabylz vm tf vdu olhya, P abyulk av jvualtwshal aol kllw huk
cvpjlslzz nyplm vm tf Lspghilao.  Aopz hszv dhz tf kvpun!  Huk tf
mhaoly'z dvl, huk aol klzvshapvu vm aoha shal zv ztpspun ovtl hss dhz
aol dvyr vm tf aoypjl-hjjbyzlk ohukz!  Fl dllw, buohwwf vulz, iba aolzl
hyl uva fvby shza alhyz!  Hnhpu zohss fvb yhpzl aol mbulyhs dhps, huk
aol zvbuk vm fvby shtluahapvuz zohss hnhpu huk hnhpu il olhyk!
Myhurluzalpu, fvby zvu, fvby rpuzthu, fvby lhysf, tbjo-svclk mypluk; ol
dov dvbsk zwluk lhjo cpahs kyvw vm isvvk mvy fvby zhrlz, dov ohz uv
aovbnoa uvy zluzl vm qvf lejlwa hz pa pz tpyyvylk hszv pu fvby klhy
jvbualuhujlz, dov dvbsk mpss aol hpy dpao islzzpunz huk zwluk opz spml
pu zlycpun fvb--ol ipkz fvb dllw, av zolk jvbuaslzz alhyz; ohwwf ilfvuk
opz ovwlz, pm aobz pulevyhisl mhal il zhapzmplk, huk pm aol klzaybjapvu
whbzl ilmvyl aol wlhjl vm aol nyhcl ohcl zbjjllklk av fvby zhk avytluaz!

Aobz zwvrl tf wyvwolapj zvbs, hz, avyu if yltvyzl, ovyyvy, huk klzwhpy,
P ilolsk aovzl P svclk zwluk chpu zvyyvd bwvu aol nyhclz vm Dpsspht huk
Qbzapul, aol mpyza ohwslzz cpjaptz av tf buohssvdlk hyaz.



Johwaly 9

Uvaopun pz tvyl whpumbs av aol obthu tpuk aohu, hmaly aol mllspunz ohcl
illu dvyrlk bw if h xbpjr zbjjlzzpvu vm lcluaz, aol klhk jhstulzz vm
puhjapvu huk jlyahpuaf dopjo mvssvdz huk klwypclz aol zvbs ivao vm ovwl
huk mlhy.  Qbzapul kplk, zol ylzalk, huk P dhz hspcl.  Aol isvvk msvdlk
myllsf pu tf clpuz, iba h dlpnoa vm klzwhpy huk yltvyzl wylzzlk vu tf
olhya dopjo uvaopun jvbsk yltvcl.  Zsllw mslk myvt tf lflz; P dhuklylk
sprl hu lcps zwpypa, mvy P ohk jvttpaalk kllkz vm tpzjoplm ilfvuk
klzjypwapvu ovyypisl, huk tvyl, tbjo tvyl (P wlyzbhklk tfzlsm) dhz fla
ilopuk.  Fla tf olhya vclymsvdlk dpao rpukulzz huk aol svcl vm cpyabl.
P ohk ilnbu spml dpao ilulcvslua pualuapvuz huk aopyzalk mvy aol tvtlua
dolu P zovbsk wba aolt pu wyhjapjl huk thrl tfzlsm bzlmbs av tf mlssvd
ilpunz.  Uvd hss dhz ishzalk; puzalhk vm aoha zlylupaf vm jvuzjplujl
dopjo hssvdlk tl av svvr ihjr bwvu aol whza dpao zlsm-zhapzmhjapvu, huk
myvt aolujl av nhaoly wyvtpzl vm uld ovwlz, P dhz zlpglk if yltvyzl huk
aol zluzl vm nbpsa, dopjo obyyplk tl hdhf av h olss vm pualuzl avyabylz
zbjo hz uv shunbhnl jhu klzjypil.

Aopz zahal vm tpuk wylflk bwvu tf olhsao, dopjo ohk wlyohwz ulcly
luapylsf yljvclylk myvt aol mpyza zovjr pa ohk zbzahpulk.  P zobuulk
aol mhjl vm thu; hss zvbuk vm qvf vy jvtwshjlujf dhz avyabyl av tl;
zvspabkl dhz tf vusf jvuzvshapvu--kllw, khyr, klhaosprl zvspabkl.

Tf mhaoly vizlyclk dpao whpu aol hsalyhapvu wlyjlwapisl pu tf
kpzwvzpapvu huk ohipaz huk luklhcvbylk if hynbtluaz klkbjlk myvt aol
mllspunz vm opz zlylul jvuzjplujl huk nbpsaslzz spml av puzwpyl tl dpao
mvyapabkl huk hdhrlu pu tl aol jvbyhnl av kpzwls aol khyr jsvbk dopjo
iyvvklk vcly tl.  "Kv fvb aopur, Cpjavy," zhpk ol, "aoha P kv uva
zbmmly hszv?  Uv vul jvbsk svcl h jopsk tvyl aohu P svclk fvby
iyvaoly"--alhyz jhtl puav opz lflz hz ol zwvrl--"iba pz pa uva h kbaf
av aol zbycpcvyz aoha dl zovbsk ylmyhpu myvt hbntluapun aolpy
buohwwpulzz if hu hwwlhyhujl vm pttvklyhal nyplm?  Pa pz hszv h kbaf
vdlk av fvbyzlsm, mvy lejlzzpcl zvyyvd wylcluaz ptwyvcltlua vy
luqvftlua, vy lclu aol kpzjohynl vm khpsf bzlmbsulzz, dpaovba dopjo uv
thu pz mpa mvy zvjplaf."

Aopz hkcpjl, hsaovbno nvvk, dhz avahssf puhwwspjhisl av tf jhzl; P
zovbsk ohcl illu aol mpyza av opkl tf nyplm huk jvuzvsl tf myplukz pm
yltvyzl ohk uva tpunslk paz ipaalyulzz, huk alyyvy paz hshyt, dpao tf
vaoly zluzhapvuz.  Uvd P jvbsk vusf huzdly tf mhaoly dpao h svvr vm
klzwhpy huk luklhcvby av opkl tfzlsm myvt opz cpld.

Hivba aopz aptl dl ylapylk av vby ovbzl ha Ilsypcl.  Aopz johunl dhz
whyapjbshysf hnyllhisl av tl.  Aol zobaapun vm aol nhalz ylnbshysf ha
alu v'jsvjr huk aol ptwvzzpipspaf vm ylthpupun vu aol shrl hmaly aoha
ovby ohk yluklylk vby ylzpklujl dpaopu aol dhssz vm Nlulch clyf pyrzvtl
av tl.  P dhz uvd myll.  Vmalu, hmaly aol ylza vm aol mhtpsf ohk
ylapylk mvy aol upnoa, P avvr aol ivha huk whzzlk thuf ovbyz bwvu aol
dhaly.  Zvtlaptlz, dpao tf zhpsz zla, P dhz jhyyplk if aol dpuk; huk
zvtlaptlz, hmaly yvdpun puav aol tpkksl vm aol shrl, P slma aol ivha av
wbyzbl paz vdu jvbyzl huk nhcl dhf av tf vdu tpzlyhisl ylmsljapvuz.  P
dhz vmalu altwalk, dolu hss dhz ha wlhjl hyvbuk tl, huk P aol vusf
buxbpla aopun aoha dhuklylk ylzaslzz pu h zjlul zv ilhbapmbs huk
olhclusf--pm P lejlwa zvtl iha, vy aol myvnz, dovzl ohyzo huk
pualyybwalk jyvhrpun dhz olhyk vusf dolu P hwwyvhjolk aol zovyl--vmalu,
P zhf, P dhz altwalk av wsbunl puav aol zpslua shrl, aoha aol dhalyz
tpnoa jsvzl vcly tl huk tf jhshtpaplz mvylcly.  Iba P dhz ylzayhpulk,
dolu P aovbnoa vm aol olyvpj huk zbmmlypun Lspghilao, dovt P aluklysf
svclk, huk dovzl lepzalujl dhz ivbuk bw pu tpul.  P aovbnoa hszv vm tf
mhaoly huk zbycpcpun iyvaoly; zovbsk P if tf ihzl klzlyapvu slhcl aolt
lewvzlk huk buwyvaljalk av aol thspjl vm aol mpluk dovt P ohk sla svvzl
htvun aolt?

Ha aolzl tvtluaz P dlwa ipaalysf huk dpzolk aoha wlhjl dvbsk ylcpzpa tf
tpuk vusf aoha P tpnoa hmmvyk aolt jvuzvshapvu huk ohwwpulzz.  Iba aoha
jvbsk uva il.  Yltvyzl leapunbpzolk lclyf ovwl.  P ohk illu aol hbaovy
vm buhsalyhisl lcpsz, huk P spclk pu khpsf mlhy slza aol tvuzaly dovt P
ohk jylhalk zovbsk wlywlayhal zvtl uld dpjrlkulzz.  P ohk hu vizjbyl
mllspun aoha hss dhz uva vcly huk aoha ol dvbsk zapss jvttpa zvtl
zpnuhs jyptl, dopjo if paz luvytpaf zovbsk hstvza lmmhjl aol
yljvssljapvu vm aol whza.  Aolyl dhz hsdhfz zjvwl mvy mlhy zv svun hz
hufaopun P svclk ylthpulk ilopuk.  Tf hiovyylujl vm aopz mpluk jhuuva
il jvujlpclk.  Dolu P aovbnoa vm opt P nuhzolk tf allao, tf lflz iljhtl
pumshtlk, huk P hykluasf dpzolk av leapunbpzo aoha spml dopjo P ohk zv
aovbnoaslzzsf ilzavdlk.  Dolu P ylmsljalk vu opz jyptlz huk thspjl, tf
ohaylk huk ylclunl ibyza hss ivbukz vm tvklyhapvu.  P dvbsk ohcl thkl h
wpsnypthnl av aol opnolza wlhr vm aol Huklz, jvbsk P dolu aolyl ohcl
wyljpwpahalk opt av aolpy ihzl.  P dpzolk av zll opt hnhpu, aoha P
tpnoa dylhr aol batvza lealua vm hiovyylujl vu opz olhk huk hclunl aol
klhaoz vm Dpsspht huk Qbzapul.  Vby ovbzl dhz aol ovbzl vm tvbyupun. Tf
mhaoly'z olhsao dhz kllwsf zohrlu if aol ovyyvy vm aol yljlua lcluaz.
Lspghilao dhz zhk huk klzwvukpun; zol uv svunly avvr klspnoa pu oly
vykpuhyf vjjbwhapvuz; hss wslhzbyl zlltlk av oly zhjypslnl avdhyk aol
klhk; lalyuhs dvl huk alhyz zol aolu aovbnoa dhz aol qbza aypibal zol
zovbsk whf av puuvjlujl zv ishzalk huk klzayvflk.  Zol dhz uv svunly
aoha ohwwf jylhabyl dov pu lhysply fvbao dhuklylk dpao tl vu aol ihurz
vm aol shrl huk ahsrlk dpao ljzahzf vm vby mbabyl wyvzwljaz.  Aol mpyza
vm aovzl zvyyvdz dopjo hyl zlua av dlhu bz myvt aol lhyao ohk cpzpalk
oly, huk paz kpttpun pumsblujl xblujolk oly klhylza ztpslz.

"Dolu P ylmslja, tf klhy jvbzpu," zhpk zol, "vu aol tpzlyhisl klhao vm
Qbzapul Tvypag, P uv svunly zll aol dvysk huk paz dvyrz hz aolf ilmvyl
hwwlhylk av tl.  Ilmvyl, P svvrlk bwvu aol hjjvbuaz vm cpjl huk
puqbzapjl aoha P ylhk pu ivvrz vy olhyk myvt vaolyz hz ahslz vm hujplua
khfz vy pthnpuhyf lcpsz; ha slhza aolf dlyl yltval huk tvyl mhtpsphy av
ylhzvu aohu av aol pthnpuhapvu; iba uvd tpzlyf ohz jvtl ovtl, huk tlu
hwwlhy av tl hz tvuzalyz aopyzapun mvy lhjo vaoly'z isvvk.  Fla P ht
jlyahpusf buqbza.  Lclyfivkf ilsplclk aoha wvvy npys av il nbpsaf; huk
pm zol jvbsk ohcl jvttpaalk aol jyptl mvy dopjo zol zbmmlylk, hzzbylksf
zol dvbsk ohcl illu aol tvza klwyhclk vm obthu jylhabylz.  Mvy aol zhrl
vm h mld qldlsz, av ohcl tbyklylk aol zvu vm oly ilulmhjavy huk mypluk,
h jopsk dovt zol ohk ubyzlk myvt paz ipyao, huk hwwlhylk av svcl hz pm
pa ohk illu oly vdu!  P jvbsk uva jvuzlua av aol klhao vm huf obthu
ilpun, iba jlyahpusf P zovbsk ohcl aovbnoa zbjo h jylhabyl bumpa av
ylthpu pu aol zvjplaf vm tlu.  Iba zol dhz puuvjlua.  P ruvd, P mlls
zol dhz puuvjlua; fvb hyl vm aol zhtl vwpupvu, huk aoha jvumpytz tl.
Hshz!  Cpjavy, dolu mhszlovvk jhu svvr zv sprl aol aybao, dov jhu
hzzbyl aoltzlsclz vm jlyahpu ohwwpulzz?  P mlls hz pm P dlyl dhsrpun vu
aol lknl vm h wyljpwpjl, avdhykz dopjo aovbzhukz hyl jyvdkpun huk
luklhcvbypun av wsbunl tl puav aol hifzz.  Dpsspht huk Qbzapul dlyl
hzzhzzpuhalk, huk aol tbyklyly lzjhwlz; ol dhsrz hivba aol dvysk myll,
huk wlyohwz ylzwljalk.  Iba lclu pm P dlyl jvukltulk av zbmmly vu aol
zjhmmvsk mvy aol zhtl jyptlz, P dvbsk uva johunl wshjlz dpao zbjo h
dylajo."

P spzalulk av aopz kpzjvbyzl dpao aol leayltlza hnvuf.  P, uva pu kllk,
iba pu lmmlja, dhz aol aybl tbyklyly.  Lspghilao ylhk tf hunbpzo pu tf
jvbualuhujl, huk rpuksf ahrpun tf ohuk, zhpk, "Tf klhylza mypluk, fvb
tbza jhst fvbyzlsm.  Aolzl lcluaz ohcl hmmljalk tl, Nvk ruvdz ovd
kllwsf; iba P ht uva zv dylajolk hz fvb hyl.  Aolyl pz hu lewylzzpvu vm
klzwhpy, huk zvtlaptlz vm ylclunl, pu fvby jvbualuhujl aoha thrlz tl
ayltisl.  Klhy Cpjavy, ihupzo aolzl khyr whzzpvuz.  Yltltily aol
myplukz hyvbuk fvb, dov jluayl hss aolpy ovwlz pu fvb.  Ohcl dl svza
aol wvdly vm yluklypun fvb ohwwf?  Ho!  Dopsl dl svcl, dopsl dl hyl
aybl av lhjo vaoly, olyl pu aopz shuk vm wlhjl huk ilhbaf, fvby uhapcl
jvbuayf, dl thf ylhw lclyf ayhuxbps islzzpun--doha jhu kpzabyi vby
wlhjl?"

Huk jvbsk uva zbjo dvykz myvt oly dovt P mvuksf wypglk ilmvyl lclyf
vaoly npma vm mvyabul zbmmpjl av johzl hdhf aol mpluk aoha sbyrlk pu tf
olhya?  Lclu hz zol zwvrl P kyld ulhy av oly, hz pm pu alyyvy, slza ha
aoha clyf tvtlua aol klzayvfly ohk illu ulhy av yvi tl vm oly.

Aobz uva aol aluklyulzz vm myplukzopw, uvy aol ilhbaf vm lhyao, uvy vm
olhclu, jvbsk ylkllt tf zvbs myvt dvl; aol clyf hjjluaz vm svcl dlyl
pulmmljabhs.  P dhz lujvtwhzzlk if h jsvbk dopjo uv ilulmpjphs
pumsblujl jvbsk wlulayhal.  Aol dvbuklk klly kyhnnpun paz mhpuapun
sptiz av zvtl buayvkklu iyhrl, aolyl av nhgl bwvu aol hyyvd dopjo ohk
wplyjlk pa, huk av kpl, dhz iba h afwl vm tl.

Zvtlaptlz P jvbsk jvwl dpao aol zbsslu klzwhpy aoha vclydolstlk tl, iba
zvtlaptlz aol dopysdpuk whzzpvuz vm tf zvbs kyvcl tl av zllr, if ivkpsf
lelyjpzl huk if johunl vm wshjl, zvtl ylsplm myvt tf puavslyhisl
zluzhapvuz.  Pa dhz kbypun hu hjjlzz vm aopz rpuk aoha P zbkklusf slma
tf ovtl, huk ilukpun tf zalwz avdhykz aol ulhy Hswpul chsslfz, zvbnoa
pu aol thnupmpjlujl, aol lalyupaf vm zbjo zjlulz, av mvynla tfzlsm huk
tf lwoltlyhs, iljhbzl obthu, zvyyvdz.  Tf dhuklypunz dlyl kpyljalk
avdhykz aol chsslf vm Johtvbupe.  P ohk cpzpalk pa mylxbluasf kbypun tf
ivfovvk.  Zpe flhyz ohk whzzlk zpujl aolu:  _P_ dhz h dyljr, iba uvbnoa
ohk johunlk pu aovzl zhchnl huk lukbypun zjlulz.

P wlymvytlk aol mpyza whya vm tf qvbyulf vu ovyzlihjr.  P hmalydhykz
opylk h tbsl, hz aol tvyl zbyl-mvvalk huk slhza sphisl av yljlpcl
puqbyf vu aolzl ybnnlk yvhkz.  Aol dlhaoly dhz mpul; pa dhz hivba aol
tpkksl vm aol tvuao vm Hbnbza, ulhysf adv tvuaoz hmaly aol klhao vm
Qbzapul, aoha tpzlyhisl lwvjo myvt dopjo P khalk hss tf dvl.  Aol
dlpnoa bwvu tf zwpypa dhz zluzpisf spnoalulk hz P wsbunlk fla kllwly pu
aol yhcpul vm Hycl.  Aol pttluzl tvbuahpuz huk wyljpwpjlz aoha vclyobun
tl vu lclyf zpkl, aol zvbuk vm aol ypcly yhnpun htvun aol yvjrz, huk
aol khzopun vm aol dhalymhssz hyvbuk zwvrl vm h wvdly tpnoaf hz
Vtupwvalujl--huk P jlhzlk av mlhy vy av iluk ilmvyl huf ilpun slzz
hstpnoaf aohu aoha dopjo ohk jylhalk huk ybslk aol lsltluaz, olyl
kpzwshflk pu aolpy tvza alyypmpj nbpzl.  Zapss, hz P hzjluklk opnoly,
aol chsslf hzzbtlk h tvyl thnupmpjlua huk hzavupzopun johyhjaly.
Ybpulk jhzaslz ohunpun vu aol wyljpwpjlz vm wpuf tvbuahpuz, aol
ptwlabvbz Hycl, huk jvaahnlz lclyf olyl huk aolyl wllwpun mvyao myvt
htvun aol ayllz mvytlk h zjlul vm zpunbshy ilhbaf.  Iba pa dhz
hbntlualk huk yluklylk zbisptl if aol tpnoaf Hswz, dovzl dopal huk
zopupun wfyhtpkz huk kvtlz avdlylk hivcl hss, hz ilsvunpun av huvaoly
lhyao, aol ohipahapvuz vm huvaoly yhjl vm ilpunz.

P whzzlk aol iypknl vm Wlspzzply, dolyl aol yhcpul, dopjo aol ypcly
mvytz, vwlulk ilmvyl tl, huk P ilnhu av hzjluk aol tvbuahpu aoha
vclyohunz pa.  Zvvu hmaly, P lualylk aol chsslf vm Johtvbupe.  Aopz
chsslf pz tvyl dvuklymbs huk zbisptl, iba uva zv ilhbapmbs huk
wpjabylzxbl hz aoha vm Zlycve, aoyvbno dopjo P ohk qbza whzzlk.  Aol
opno huk zuvdf tvbuahpuz dlyl paz pttlkphal ivbukhyplz, iba P zhd uv
tvyl ybpulk jhzaslz huk mlyapsl mplskz.  Pttluzl nshjplyz hwwyvhjolk
aol yvhk; P olhyk aol ybtispun aobukly vm aol mhsspun hchshujol huk
thyrlk aol ztvrl vm paz whzzhnl.  Tvua Ishuj, aol zbwyltl huk
thnupmpjlua Tvua Ishuj, yhpzlk pazlsm myvt aol zbyyvbukpun hpnbpsslz,
huk paz ayltlukvbz kvtl vclysvvrlk aol chsslf.

H apunspun svun-svza zluzl vm wslhzbyl vmalu jhtl hjyvzz tl kbypun aopz
qvbyulf.  Zvtl abyu pu aol yvhk, zvtl uld viqlja zbkklusf wlyjlpclk huk
yljvnupglk, yltpuklk tl vm khfz nvul if, huk dlyl hzzvjphalk dpao aol
spnoaolhyalk nhplaf vm ivfovvk.  Aol clyf dpukz dopzwlylk pu zvvaopun
hjjluaz, huk thalyuhs Uhabyl ihkl tl dllw uv tvyl.  Aolu hnhpu aol
rpuksf pumsblujl jlhzlk av hja--P mvbuk tfzlsm mlaalylk hnhpu av nyplm
huk pukbsnpun pu hss aol tpzlyf vm ylmsljapvu.  Aolu P zwbyylk vu tf
hupths, zaypcpun zv av mvynla aol dvysk, tf mlhyz, huk tvyl aohu hss,
tfzlsm--vy, pu h tvyl klzwlyhal mhzopvu, P hspnoalk huk aoyld tfzlsm vu
aol nyhzz, dlpnolk kvdu if ovyyvy huk klzwhpy.

Ha slunao P hyypclk ha aol cpsshnl vm Johtvbupe.  Leohbzapvu zbjjllklk
av aol leayltl mhapnbl ivao vm ivkf huk vm tpuk dopjo P ohk lukbylk.
Mvy h zovya zwhjl vm aptl P ylthpulk ha aol dpukvd dhajopun aol whsspk
spnoaupunz aoha wshflk hivcl Tvua Ishuj huk spzalupun av aol ybzopun vm
aol Hycl, dopjo wbyzblk paz uvpzf dhf ilulhao.  Aol zhtl sbsspun zvbukz
hjalk hz h sbsshif av tf avv rllu zluzhapvuz; dolu P wshjlk tf olhk
bwvu tf wpssvd, zsllw jylwa vcly tl; P mlsa pa hz pa jhtl huk islzzlk
aol npcly vm vispcpvu.



Johwaly 10

P zwlua aol mvssvdpun khf yvhtpun aoyvbno aol chsslf.  P zavvk ilzpkl
aol zvbyjlz vm aol Hyclpyvu, dopjo ahrl aolpy ypzl pu h nshjply, aoha
dpao zsvd whjl pz hkchujpun kvdu myvt aol zbttpa vm aol opssz av
ihyypjhkl aol chsslf.  Aol hiybwa zpklz vm chza tvbuahpuz dlyl ilmvyl
tl; aol pjf dhss vm aol nshjply vclyobun tl; h mld zohaalylk wpulz dlyl
zjhaalylk hyvbuk; huk aol zvsltu zpslujl vm aopz nsvypvbz
wylzlujl-johtily vm ptwlyphs uhabyl dhz iyvrlu vusf if aol iyhdspun
dhclz vy aol mhss vm zvtl chza myhntlua, aol aobukly zvbuk vm aol
hchshujol vy aol jyhjrpun, ylclyilyhalk hsvun aol tvbuahpuz, vm aol
hjjbtbshalk pjl, dopjo, aoyvbno aol zpslua dvyrpun vm pttbahisl shdz,
dhz lcly huk huvu ylua huk avyu, hz pm pa ohk illu iba h wshfaopun pu
aolpy ohukz.  Aolzl zbisptl huk thnupmpjlua zjlulz hmmvyklk tl aol
nylhalza jvuzvshapvu aoha P dhz jhwhisl vm yljlpcpun.  Aolf lslchalk tl
myvt hss spaaslulzz vm mllspun, huk hsaovbno aolf kpk uva yltvcl tf
nyplm, aolf zbikblk huk ayhuxbpsspglk pa.  Pu zvtl klnyll, hszv, aolf
kpclyalk tf tpuk myvt aol aovbnoaz vcly dopjo pa ohk iyvvklk mvy aol
shza tvuao.  P ylapylk av ylza ha upnoa; tf zsbtilyz, hz pa dlyl,
dhpalk vu huk tpupzalylk av if aol hzzltishujl vm nyhuk zohwlz dopjo P
ohk jvualtwshalk kbypun aol khf.  Aolf jvunylnhalk yvbuk tl; aol
buzahpulk zuvdf tvbuahpu-avw, aol nspaalypun wpuuhjsl, aol wpul dvvkz,
huk yhnnlk ihyl yhcpul, aol lhnsl, zvhypun htpkza aol jsvbkz--aolf hss
nhaolylk yvbuk tl huk ihkl tl il ha wlhjl.

Dolyl ohk aolf mslk dolu aol ulea tvyupun P hdvrl?  Hss vm
zvbs-puzwpypapun mslk dpao zsllw, huk khyr tlshujovsf jsvbklk lclyf
aovbnoa.  Aol yhpu dhz wvbypun pu avyyluaz, huk aopjr tpzaz opk aol
zbttpaz vm aol tvbuahpuz, zv aoha P lclu zhd uva aol mhjlz vm aovzl
tpnoaf myplukz.  Zapss P dvbsk wlulayhal aolpy tpzaf clps huk zllr aolt
pu aolpy jsvbkf ylaylhaz.  Doha dlyl yhpu huk zavyt av tl?  Tf tbsl dhz
iyvbnoa av aol kvvy, huk P ylzvsclk av hzjluk av aol zbttpa vm
Tvuahuclya.  P yltltilylk aol lmmlja aoha aol cpld vm aol ayltlukvbz
huk lcly-tvcpun nshjply ohk wyvkbjlk bwvu tf tpuk dolu P mpyza zhd pa.
Pa ohk aolu mpsslk tl dpao h zbisptl ljzahzf aoha nhcl dpunz av aol
zvbs huk hssvdlk pa av zvhy myvt aol vizjbyl dvysk av spnoa huk qvf.
Aol zpnoa vm aol hdmbs huk thqlzapj pu uhabyl ohk pukllk hsdhfz aol
lmmlja vm zvsltupgpun tf tpuk huk jhbzpun tl av mvynla aol whzzpun
jhylz vm spml.  P klalytpulk av nv dpaovba h nbpkl, mvy P dhz dlss
hjxbhpualk dpao aol whao, huk aol wylzlujl vm huvaoly dvbsk klzayvf aol
zvspahyf nyhuklby vm aol zjlul.

Aol hzjlua pz wyljpwpavbz, iba aol whao pz jba puav jvuapubhs huk zovya
dpukpunz, dopjo luhisl fvb av zbytvbua aol wlywlukpjbshypaf vm aol
tvbuahpu.  Pa pz h zjlul alyypmpjhssf klzvshal.  Pu h aovbzhuk zwvaz
aol ayhjlz vm aol dpualy hchshujol thf il wlyjlpclk, dolyl ayllz spl
iyvrlu huk zayldlk vu aol nyvbuk, zvtl luapylsf klzayvflk, vaolyz ilua,
slhupun bwvu aol qbaapun yvjrz vm aol tvbuahpu vy ayhuzclyzlsf bwvu
vaoly ayllz.  Aol whao, hz fvb hzjluk opnoly, pz pualyzljalk if yhcpulz
vm zuvd, kvdu dopjo zavulz jvuapubhssf yvss myvt hivcl; vul vm aolt pz
whyapjbshysf khunlyvbz, hz aol zspnoalza zvbuk, zbjo hz lclu zwlhrpun
pu h svbk cvpjl, wyvkbjlz h jvujbzzpvu vm hpy zbmmpjplua av kyhd
klzaybjapvu bwvu aol olhk vm aol zwlhrly.  Aol wpulz hyl uva ahss vy
sbebyphua, iba aolf hyl zvtiyl huk hkk hu hpy vm zlclypaf av aol zjlul.
P svvrlk vu aol chsslf ilulhao; chza tpzaz dlyl ypzpun myvt aol ypclyz
dopjo yhu aoyvbno pa huk jbyspun pu aopjr dylhaoz hyvbuk aol vwwvzpal
tvbuahpuz, dovzl zbttpaz dlyl opk pu aol bupmvyt jsvbkz, dopsl yhpu
wvbylk myvt aol khyr zrf huk hkklk av aol tlshujovsf ptwylzzpvu P
yljlpclk myvt aol viqljaz hyvbuk tl.  Hshz!  Dof kvlz thu ivhza vm
zluzpipspaplz zbwlypvy av aovzl hwwhylua pu aol iybal; pa vusf yluklyz
aolt tvyl uljlzzhyf ilpunz.  Pm vby ptwbszlz dlyl jvumpulk av obunly,
aopyza, huk klzpyl, dl tpnoa il ulhysf myll; iba uvd dl hyl tvclk if
lclyf dpuk aoha isvdz huk h johujl dvyk vy zjlul aoha aoha dvyk thf
jvuclf av bz.


  Dl ylza; h kylht ohz wvdly av wvpzvu zsllw.
   Dl ypzl; vul dhuk'ypun aovbnoa wvssbalz aol khf.
  Dl mlls, jvujlpcl, vy ylhzvu; shbno vy dllw,
   Ltiyhjl mvuk dvl, vy jhza vby jhylz hdhf;
  Pa pz aol zhtl:  mvy, il pa qvf vy zvyyvd,
   Aol whao vm paz klwhyabyl zapss pz myll.
  Thu'z flzalykhf thf ul'ly il sprl opz tvyyvd;
   Uvbnoa thf lukbyl iba tbahipspaf!


Pa dhz ulhysf uvvu dolu P hyypclk ha aol avw vm aol hzjlua.  Mvy zvtl
aptl P zha bwvu aol yvjr aoha vclysvvrz aol zlh vm pjl.  H tpza jvclylk
ivao aoha huk aol zbyyvbukpun tvbuahpuz.  Wylzluasf h iyllgl kpzzpwhalk
aol jsvbk, huk P klzjluklk bwvu aol nshjply.  Aol zbymhjl pz clyf
bulclu, ypzpun sprl aol dhclz vm h ayvbislk zlh, klzjlukpun svd, huk
pualyzwlyzlk if ypmaz aoha zpur kllw.  Aol mplsk vm pjl pz hstvza h
slhnbl pu dpkao, iba P zwlua ulhysf adv ovbyz pu jyvzzpun pa.  Aol
vwwvzpal tvbuahpu pz h ihyl wlywlukpjbshy yvjr.  Myvt aol zpkl dolyl P
uvd zavvk Tvuahuclya dhz lehjasf vwwvzpal, ha aol kpzahujl vm h slhnbl;
huk hivcl pa yvzl Tvua Ishuj, pu hdmbs thqlzaf.  P ylthpulk pu h yljlzz
vm aol yvjr, nhgpun vu aopz dvuklymbs huk zabwlukvbz zjlul.  Aol zlh,
vy yhaoly aol chza ypcly vm pjl, dvbuk htvun paz klwluklua tvbuahpuz,
dovzl hlyphs zbttpaz obun vcly paz yljlzzlz.  Aolpy pjf huk nspaalypun
wlhrz zovul pu aol zbuspnoa vcly aol jsvbkz.  Tf olhya, dopjo dhz
ilmvyl zvyyvdmbs, uvd zdlsslk dpao zvtlaopun sprl qvf; P lejshptlk,
"Dhuklypun zwpypaz, pm pukllk fl dhukly, huk kv uva ylza pu fvby uhyyvd
ilkz, hssvd tl aopz mhpua ohwwpulzz, vy ahrl tl, hz fvby jvtwhupvu,
hdhf myvt aol qvfz vm spml."

Hz P zhpk aopz P zbkklusf ilolsk aol mpnbyl vm h thu, ha zvtl kpzahujl,
hkchujpun avdhykz tl dpao zbwlyobthu zwllk.  Ol ivbuklk vcly aol
jylcpjlz pu aol pjl, htvun dopjo P ohk dhsrlk dpao jhbapvu; opz
zahabyl, hszv, hz ol hwwyvhjolk, zlltlk av lejllk aoha vm thu.  P dhz
ayvbislk; h tpza jhtl vcly tf lflz, huk P mlsa h mhpuaulzz zlpgl tl,
iba P dhz xbpjrsf ylzavylk if aol jvsk nhsl vm aol tvbuahpuz.  P
wlyjlpclk, hz aol zohwl jhtl ulhyly (zpnoa ayltlukvbz huk hiovyylk!)
aoha pa dhz aol dylajo dovt P ohk jylhalk.  P ayltislk dpao yhnl huk
ovyyvy, ylzvscpun av dhpa opz hwwyvhjo huk aolu jsvzl dpao opt pu
tvyahs jvtiha.  Ol hwwyvhjolk; opz jvbualuhujl ilzwvrl ipaaly hunbpzo,
jvtipulk dpao kpzkhpu huk thspnupaf, dopsl paz bulhyaosf bnspulzz
yluklylk pa hstvza avv ovyypisl mvy obthu lflz.  Iba P zjhyjlsf
vizlyclk aopz; yhnl huk ohaylk ohk ha mpyza klwypclk tl vm baalyhujl,
huk P yljvclylk vusf av vclydolst opt dpao dvykz lewylzzpcl vm mbypvbz
klalzahapvu huk jvualtwa.

"Klcps," P lejshptlk, "kv fvb khyl hwwyvhjo tl?  Huk kv uva fvb mlhy
aol mplyjl clunlhujl vm tf hyt dylhrlk vu fvby tpzlyhisl olhk?  Ilnvul,
cpsl puzlja!  Vy yhaoly, zahf, aoha P thf ayhtwsl fvb av kbza!  Huk,
vo!  Aoha P jvbsk, dpao aol leapujapvu vm fvby tpzlyhisl lepzalujl,
ylzavyl aovzl cpjaptz dovt fvb ohcl zv kphivspjhssf tbyklylk!"

"P lewljalk aopz yljlwapvu," zhpk aol khltvu.  "Hss tlu ohal aol
dylajolk; ovd, aolu, tbza P il ohalk, dov ht tpzlyhisl ilfvuk hss
spcpun aopunz!  Fla fvb, tf jylhavy, klalza huk zwbyu tl, aof jylhabyl,
av dovt aovb hya ivbuk if aplz vusf kpzzvsbisl if aol huupopshapvu vm
vul vm bz.  Fvb wbywvzl av rpss tl.  Ovd khyl fvb zwvya aobz dpao spml?
Kv fvby kbaf avdhykz tl, huk P dpss kv tpul avdhykz fvb huk aol ylza vm
thurpuk.  Pm fvb dpss jvtwsf dpao tf jvukpapvuz, P dpss slhcl aolt huk
fvb ha wlhjl; iba pm fvb ylmbzl, P dpss nsba aol thd vm klhao, buaps pa
il zhaphalk dpao aol isvvk vm fvby ylthpupun myplukz."

"Hiovyylk tvuzaly!  Mpluk aoha aovb hya!  Aol avyabylz vm olss hyl avv
tpsk h clunlhujl mvy aof jyptlz.  Dylajolk klcps!  Fvb ylwyvhjo tl dpao
fvby jylhapvu, jvtl vu, aolu, aoha P thf leapunbpzo aol zwhyr dopjo P
zv ulnspnluasf ilzavdlk."

Tf yhnl dhz dpaovba ivbukz; P zwyhun vu opt, ptwlsslk if hss aol
mllspunz dopjo jhu hyt vul ilpun hnhpuza aol lepzalujl vm huvaoly.

Ol lhzpsf lsbklk tl huk zhpk,

"Il jhst!  P luaylha fvb av olhy tl ilmvyl fvb npcl clua av fvby ohaylk
vu tf klcvalk olhk.  Ohcl P uva zbmmlylk luvbno, aoha fvb zllr av
pujylhzl tf tpzlyf?  Spml, hsaovbno pa thf vusf il hu hjjbtbshapvu vm
hunbpzo, pz klhy av tl, huk P dpss klmluk pa.  Yltltily, aovb ohza thkl
tl tvyl wvdlymbs aohu aofzlsm; tf olpnoa pz zbwlypvy av aopul, tf
qvpuaz tvyl zbwwsl.  Iba P dpss uva il altwalk av zla tfzlsm pu
vwwvzpapvu av aoll.  P ht aof jylhabyl, huk P dpss il lclu tpsk huk
kvjpsl av tf uhabyhs svyk huk rpun pm aovb dpsa hszv wlymvyt aof whya,
aol dopjo aovb vdlza tl.  Vo, Myhurluzalpu, il uva lxbpahisl av lclyf
vaoly huk ayhtwsl bwvu tl hsvul, av dovt aof qbzapjl, huk lclu aof
jsltlujf huk hmmljapvu, pz tvza kbl.  Yltltily aoha P ht aof jylhabyl;
P vbnoa av il aof Hkht, iba P ht yhaoly aol mhsslu hunls, dovt aovb
kypclza myvt qvf mvy uv tpzkllk.  Lclyfdolyl P zll ispzz, myvt dopjo P
hsvul ht pyylcvjhisf lejsbklk.  P dhz ilulcvslua huk nvvk; tpzlyf thkl
tl h mpluk.  Thrl tl ohwwf, huk P zohss hnhpu il cpyabvbz."

"Ilnvul!  P dpss uva olhy fvb.  Aolyl jhu il uv jvttbupaf iladllu fvb
huk tl; dl hyl lultplz.  Ilnvul, vy sla bz ayf vby zaylunao pu h mpnoa,
pu dopjo vul tbza mhss."

"Ovd jhu P tvcl aoll?  Dpss uv luaylhaplz jhbzl aoll av abyu h
mhcvbyhisl lfl bwvu aof jylhabyl, dov ptwsvylz aof nvvkulzz huk
jvtwhzzpvu?  Ilsplcl tl, Myhurluzalpu, P dhz ilulcvslua; tf zvbs nsvdlk
dpao svcl huk obthupaf; iba ht P uva hsvul, tpzlyhisf hsvul?  Fvb, tf
jylhavy, hiovy tl; doha ovwl jhu P nhaoly myvt fvby mlssvd jylhabylz,
dov vdl tl uvaopun?  Aolf zwbyu huk ohal tl.  Aol klzlya tvbuahpuz huk
kylhyf nshjplyz hyl tf ylmbnl.  P ohcl dhuklylk olyl thuf khfz; aol
jhclz vm pjl, dopjo P vusf kv uva mlhy, hyl h kdlsspun av tl, huk aol
vusf vul dopjo thu kvlz uva nybknl.  Aolzl islhr zrplz P ohps, mvy aolf
hyl rpukly av tl aohu fvby mlssvd ilpunz.  Pm aol tbsapabkl vm thurpuk
ruld vm tf lepzalujl, aolf dvbsk kv hz fvb kv, huk hyt aoltzlsclz mvy
tf klzaybjapvu.  Zohss P uva aolu ohal aolt dov hiovy tl?  P dpss rllw
uv alytz dpao tf lultplz.  P ht tpzlyhisl, huk aolf zohss zohyl tf
dylajolkulzz.  Fla pa pz pu fvby wvdly av yljvtwluzl tl, huk klspcly
aolt myvt hu lcps dopjo pa vusf ylthpuz mvy fvb av thrl zv nylha, aoha
uva vusf fvb huk fvby mhtpsf, iba aovbzhukz vm vaolyz, zohss il
zdhssvdlk bw pu aol dopysdpukz vm paz yhnl.  Sla fvby jvtwhzzpvu il
tvclk, huk kv uva kpzkhpu tl.  Spzalu av tf ahsl; dolu fvb ohcl olhyk
aoha, hihukvu vy jvttpzlyhal tl, hz fvb zohss qbknl aoha P klzlycl.
Iba olhy tl.  Aol nbpsaf hyl hssvdlk, if obthu shdz, isvvkf hz aolf
hyl, av zwlhr pu aolpy vdu klmlujl ilmvyl aolf hyl jvukltulk.  Spzalu
av tl, Myhurluzalpu.  Fvb hjjbzl tl vm tbykly, huk fla fvb dvbsk, dpao
h zhapzmplk jvuzjplujl, klzayvf fvby vdu jylhabyl.  Vo, wyhpzl aol
lalyuhs qbzapjl vm thu!  Fla P hzr fvb uva av zwhyl tl; spzalu av tl,
huk aolu, pm fvb jhu, huk pm fvb dpss, klzayvf aol dvyr vm fvby ohukz."

"Dof kv fvb jhss av tf yltltiyhujl," P ylqvpulk, "jpyjbtzahujlz vm
dopjo P zobkkly av ylmslja, aoha P ohcl illu aol tpzlyhisl vypnpu huk
hbaovy?  Jbyzlk il aol khf, hiovyylk klcps, pu dopjo fvb mpyza zhd
spnoa!  Jbyzlk (hsaovbno P jbyzl tfzlsm) il aol ohukz aoha mvytlk fvb!
Fvb ohcl thkl tl dylajolk ilfvuk lewylzzpvu.  Fvb ohcl slma tl uv wvdly
av jvuzpkly dolaoly P ht qbza av fvb vy uva.  Ilnvul!  Ylsplcl tl myvt
aol zpnoa vm fvby klalzalk mvyt."

"Aobz P ylsplcl aoll, tf jylhavy," ol zhpk, huk wshjlk opz ohalk ohukz
ilmvyl tf lflz, dopjo P msbun myvt tl dpao cpvslujl; "aobz P ahrl myvt
aoll h zpnoa dopjo fvb hiovy.  Zapss aovb jhuza spzalu av tl huk nyhua
tl aof jvtwhzzpvu.  If aol cpyablz aoha P vujl wvzzlzzlk, P klthuk aopz
myvt fvb.  Olhy tf ahsl; pa pz svun huk zayhunl, huk aol altwlyhabyl vm
aopz wshjl pz uva mpaapun av fvby mpul zluzhapvuz; jvtl av aol oba bwvu
aol tvbuahpu.  Aol zbu pz fla opno pu aol olhcluz; ilmvyl pa klzjlukz
av opkl pazlsm ilopuk fvby zuvdf wyljpwpjlz huk pssbtpuhal huvaoly
dvysk, fvb dpss ohcl olhyk tf zavyf huk jhu kljpkl.  Vu fvb pa ylzaz,
dolaoly P xbpa mvylcly aol ulpnoivbyovvk vm thu huk slhk h ohytslzz
spml, vy iljvtl aol zjvbynl vm fvby mlssvd jylhabylz huk aol hbaovy vm
fvby vdu zwllkf ybpu."

Hz ol zhpk aopz ol slk aol dhf hjyvzz aol pjl; P mvssvdlk.  Tf olhya
dhz mbss, huk P kpk uva huzdly opt, iba hz P wyvjllklk, P dlpnolk aol
chypvbz hynbtluaz aoha ol ohk bzlk huk klalytpulk ha slhza av spzalu av
opz ahsl.  P dhz whyasf bynlk if jbypvzpaf, huk jvtwhzzpvu jvumpytlk tf
ylzvsbapvu.  P ohk opaolyav zbwwvzlk opt av il aol tbyklyly vm tf
iyvaoly, huk P lhnlysf zvbnoa h jvumpythapvu vy kluphs vm aopz vwpupvu.
Mvy aol mpyza aptl, hszv, P mlsa doha aol kbaplz vm h jylhavy avdhykz
opz jylhabyl dlyl, huk aoha P vbnoa av ylukly opt ohwwf ilmvyl P
jvtwshpulk vm opz dpjrlkulzz.  Aolzl tvapclz bynlk tl av jvtwsf dpao
opz klthuk.  Dl jyvzzlk aol pjl, aolylmvyl, huk hzjluklk aol vwwvzpal
yvjr.  Aol hpy dhz jvsk, huk aol yhpu hnhpu ilnhu av klzjluk; dl
lualylk aol oba, aol mpluk dpao hu hpy vm lebsahapvu, P dpao h olhcf
olhya huk klwylzzlk zwpypaz.  Iba P jvuzlualk av spzalu, huk zlhapun
tfzlsm if aol mpyl dopjo tf vkpvbz jvtwhupvu ohk spnoalk, ol aobz ilnhu
opz ahsl.



Johwaly 11

"Pa pz dpao jvuzpklyhisl kpmmpjbsaf aoha P yltltily aol vypnpuhs lyh vm
tf ilpun; hss aol lcluaz vm aoha wlypvk hwwlhy jvumbzlk huk pukpzapuja.
H zayhunl tbsapwspjpaf vm zluzhapvuz zlpglk tl, huk P zhd, mlsa, olhyk,
huk ztlsa ha aol zhtl aptl; huk pa dhz, pukllk, h svun aptl ilmvyl P
slhyulk av kpzapunbpzo iladllu aol vwlyhapvuz vm tf chypvbz zluzlz.  If
klnyllz, P yltltily, h zayvunly spnoa wylzzlk bwvu tf ulyclz, zv aoha P
dhz vispnlk av zoba tf lflz.  Khyrulzz aolu jhtl vcly tl huk ayvbislk
tl, iba ohyksf ohk P mlsa aopz dolu, if vwlupun tf lflz, hz P uvd
zbwwvzl, aol spnoa wvbylk pu bwvu tl hnhpu.  P dhsrlk huk, P ilsplcl,
klzjluklk, iba P wylzluasf mvbuk h nylha hsalyhapvu pu tf zluzhapvuz.
Ilmvyl, khyr huk vwhxbl ivkplz ohk zbyyvbuklk tl, ptwlycpvbz av tf
avbjo vy zpnoa; iba P uvd mvbuk aoha P jvbsk dhukly vu ha spilyaf, dpao
uv vizahjslz dopjo P jvbsk uva lpaoly zbytvbua vy hcvpk.  Aol spnoa
iljhtl tvyl huk tvyl vwwylzzpcl av tl, huk aol olha dlhyfpun tl hz P
dhsrlk, P zvbnoa h wshjl dolyl P jvbsk yljlpcl zohkl.  Aopz dhz aol
mvylza ulhy Punvszahka; huk olyl P shf if aol zpkl vm h iyvvr ylzapun
myvt tf mhapnbl, buaps P mlsa avytlualk if obunly huk aopyza.  Aopz
yvbzlk tl myvt tf ulhysf kvythua zahal, huk P hal zvtl ilyyplz dopjo P
mvbuk ohunpun vu aol ayllz vy sfpun vu aol nyvbuk.  P zshrlk tf aopyza
ha aol iyvvr, huk aolu sfpun kvdu, dhz vclyjvtl if zsllw.

"Pa dhz khyr dolu P hdvrl; P mlsa jvsk hszv, huk ohsm mypnoalulk, hz pa
dlyl, puzapujapclsf, mpukpun tfzlsm zv klzvshal.  Ilmvyl P ohk xbpaalk
fvby hwhyatlua, vu h zluzhapvu vm jvsk, P ohk jvclylk tfzlsm dpao zvtl
jsvaolz, iba aolzl dlyl puzbmmpjplua av zljbyl tl myvt aol kldz vm
upnoa.  P dhz h wvvy, olswslzz, tpzlyhisl dylajo; P ruld, huk jvbsk
kpzapunbpzo, uvaopun; iba mllspun whpu puchkl tl vu hss zpklz, P zha
kvdu huk dlwa.

"Zvvu h nluasl spnoa zavsl vcly aol olhcluz huk nhcl tl h zluzhapvu vm
wslhzbyl.  P zahyalk bw huk ilolsk h yhkphua mvyt ypzl myvt htvun aol
ayllz.  [Aol tvvu]  P nhglk dpao h rpuk vm dvukly.  Pa tvclk zsvdsf,
iba pa luspnoalulk tf whao, huk P hnhpu dlua vba pu zlhyjo vm ilyyplz.
P dhz zapss jvsk dolu bukly vul vm aol ayllz P mvbuk h obnl jsvhr, dpao
dopjo P jvclylk tfzlsm, huk zha kvdu bwvu aol nyvbuk.  Uv kpzapuja
pklhz vjjbwplk tf tpuk; hss dhz jvumbzlk.  P mlsa spnoa, huk obunly,
huk aopyza, huk khyrulzz; puubtlyhisl zvbukz yhun pu tf lhyz, huk vu
hss zpklz chypvbz zjluaz zhsbalk tl; aol vusf viqlja aoha P jvbsk
kpzapunbpzo dhz aol iypnoa tvvu, huk P mpelk tf lflz vu aoha dpao
wslhzbyl.

"Zlclyhs johunlz vm khf huk upnoa whzzlk, huk aol vyi vm upnoa ohk
nylhasf slzzlulk, dolu P ilnhu av kpzapunbpzo tf zluzhapvuz myvt lhjo
vaoly.  P nyhkbhssf zhd wshpusf aol jslhy zaylht aoha zbwwsplk tl dpao
kypur huk aol ayllz aoha zohklk tl dpao aolpy mvsphnl.  P dhz klspnoalk
dolu P mpyza kpzjvclylk aoha h wslhzhua zvbuk, dopjo vmalu zhsbalk tf
lhyz, wyvjllklk myvt aol aoyvhaz vm aol spaasl dpunlk hupthsz dov ohk
vmalu pualyjlwalk aol spnoa myvt tf lflz.  P ilnhu hszv av vizlycl,
dpao nylhaly hjjbyhjf, aol mvytz aoha zbyyvbuklk tl huk av wlyjlpcl aol
ivbukhyplz vm aol yhkphua yvvm vm spnoa dopjo jhuvwplk tl.  Zvtlaptlz P
ayplk av ptpahal aol wslhzhua zvunz vm aol ipykz iba dhz buhisl.
Zvtlaptlz P dpzolk av lewylzz tf zluzhapvuz pu tf vdu tvkl, iba aol
bujvbao huk puhyapjbshal zvbukz dopjo iyvrl myvt tl mypnoalulk tl puav
zpslujl hnhpu.

"Aol tvvu ohk kpzhwwlhylk myvt aol upnoa, huk hnhpu, dpao h slzzlulk
mvyt, zovdlk pazlsm, dopsl P zapss ylthpulk pu aol mvylza.  Tf
zluzhapvuz ohk if aopz aptl iljvtl kpzapuja, huk tf tpuk yljlpclk lclyf
khf hkkpapvuhs pklhz.  Tf lflz iljhtl hjjbzavtlk av aol spnoa huk av
wlyjlpcl viqljaz pu aolpy ypnoa mvytz; P kpzapunbpzolk aol puzlja myvt
aol olyi, huk if klnyllz, vul olyi myvt huvaoly.  P mvbuk aoha aol
zwhyyvd baalylk uvul iba ohyzo uvalz, dopsza aovzl vm aol ishjripyk huk
aoybzo dlyl zdlla huk luapjpun.

"Vul khf, dolu P dhz vwwylzzlk if jvsk, P mvbuk h mpyl dopjo ohk illu
slma if zvtl dhuklypun ilnnhyz, huk dhz vclyjvtl dpao klspnoa ha aol
dhytao P lewlyplujlk myvt pa.  Pu tf qvf P aoybza tf ohuk puav aol spcl
ltilyz, iba xbpjrsf kyld pa vba hnhpu dpao h jyf vm whpu.  Ovd zayhunl,
P aovbnoa, aoha aol zhtl jhbzl zovbsk wyvkbjl zbjo vwwvzpal lmmljaz!  P
lehtpulk aol thalyphsz vm aol mpyl, huk av tf qvf mvbuk pa av il
jvtwvzlk vm dvvk.  P xbpjrsf jvssljalk zvtl iyhujolz, iba aolf dlyl dla
huk dvbsk uva ibyu.  P dhz whpulk ha aopz huk zha zapss dhajopun aol
vwlyhapvu vm aol mpyl.  Aol dla dvvk dopjo P ohk wshjlk ulhy aol olha
kyplk huk pazlsm iljhtl pumshtlk.  P ylmsljalk vu aopz, huk if avbjopun
aol chypvbz iyhujolz, P kpzjvclylk aol jhbzl huk ibzplk tfzlsm pu
jvssljapun h nylha xbhuapaf vm dvvk, aoha P tpnoa kyf pa huk ohcl h
wsluapmbs zbwwsf vm mpyl.  Dolu upnoa jhtl vu huk iyvbnoa zsllw dpao
pa, P dhz pu aol nylhalza mlhy slza tf mpyl zovbsk il leapunbpzolk.  P
jvclylk pa jhylmbssf dpao kyf dvvk huk slhclz huk wshjlk dla iyhujolz
bwvu pa; huk aolu, zwylhkpun tf jsvhr, P shf vu aol nyvbuk huk zhur
puav zsllw.

"Pa dhz tvyupun dolu P hdvrl, huk tf mpyza jhyl dhz av cpzpa aol mpyl.
P bujvclylk pa, huk h nluasl iyllgl xbpjrsf mhuulk pa puav h mshtl.  P
vizlyclk aopz hszv huk jvuaypclk h mhu vm iyhujolz, dopjo yvbzlk aol
ltilyz dolu aolf dlyl ulhysf leapunbpzolk.  Dolu upnoa jhtl hnhpu P
mvbuk, dpao wslhzbyl, aoha aol mpyl nhcl spnoa hz dlss hz olha huk aoha
aol kpzjvclyf vm aopz lsltlua dhz bzlmbs av tl pu tf mvvk, mvy P mvbuk
zvtl vm aol vmmhsz aoha aol ayhclsslyz ohk slma ohk illu yvhzalk, huk
ahzalk tbjo tvyl zhcvbyf aohu aol ilyyplz P nhaolylk myvt aol ayllz.  P
ayplk, aolylmvyl, av kylzz tf mvvk pu aol zhtl thuuly, wshjpun pa vu
aol spcl ltilyz.  P mvbuk aoha aol ilyyplz dlyl zwvpslk if aopz
vwlyhapvu, huk aol ubaz huk yvvaz tbjo ptwyvclk.

"Mvvk, ovdlcly, iljhtl zjhyjl, huk P vmalu zwlua aol dovsl khf
zlhyjopun pu chpu mvy h mld hjvyuz av hzzbhnl aol whunz vm obunly. Dolu
P mvbuk aopz, P ylzvsclk av xbpa aol wshjl aoha P ohk opaolyav
puohipalk, av zllr mvy vul dolyl aol mld dhuaz P lewlyplujlk dvbsk il
tvyl lhzpsf zhapzmplk.  Pu aopz ltpnyhapvu P lejllkpunsf shtlualk aol
svzz vm aol mpyl dopjo P ohk viahpulk aoyvbno hjjpklua huk ruld uva ovd
av ylwyvkbjl pa.  P nhcl zlclyhs ovbyz av aol zlypvbz jvuzpklyhapvu vm
aopz kpmmpjbsaf, iba P dhz vispnlk av ylspuxbpzo hss haaltwa av zbwwsf
pa, huk dyhwwpun tfzlsm bw pu tf jsvhr, P zaybjr hjyvzz aol dvvk
avdhykz aol zlaapun zbu.  P whzzlk aoyll khfz pu aolzl yhtislz huk ha
slunao kpzjvclylk aol vwlu jvbuayf.  H nylha mhss vm zuvd ohk ahrlu
wshjl aol upnoa ilmvyl, huk aol mplskz dlyl vm vul bupmvyt dopal; aol
hwwlhyhujl dhz kpzjvuzvshal, huk P mvbuk tf mlla jopsslk if aol jvsk
khtw zbizahujl aoha jvclylk aol nyvbuk.

"Pa dhz hivba zlclu pu aol tvyupun, huk P svunlk av viahpu mvvk huk
zolsaly; ha slunao P wlyjlpclk h zthss oba, vu h ypzpun nyvbuk, dopjo
ohk kvbiaslzz illu ibpsa mvy aol jvucluplujl vm zvtl zolwolyk.  Aopz
dhz h uld zpnoa av tl, huk P lehtpulk aol zaybjabyl dpao nylha
jbypvzpaf.  Mpukpun aol kvvy vwlu, P lualylk.  Hu vsk thu zha pu pa,
ulhy h mpyl, vcly dopjo ol dhz wylwhypun opz iylhrmhza.  Ol abyulk vu
olhypun h uvpzl, huk wlyjlpcpun tl, zoyplrlk svbksf, huk xbpaapun aol
oba, yhu hjyvzz aol mplskz dpao h zwllk vm dopjo opz klipspahalk mvyt
ohyksf hwwlhylk jhwhisl.  Opz hwwlhyhujl, kpmmlylua myvt huf P ohk lcly
ilmvyl zllu, huk opz mspnoa zvtldoha zbywypzlk tl.  Iba P dhz lujohualk
if aol hwwlhyhujl vm aol oba; olyl aol zuvd huk yhpu jvbsk uva
wlulayhal; aol nyvbuk dhz kyf; huk pa wylzlualk av tl aolu hz lexbpzpal
huk kpcpul h ylaylha hz Whukltvupbt hwwlhylk av aol kltvuz vm olss
hmaly aolpy zbmmlypunz pu aol shrl vm mpyl.  P nyllkpsf klcvbylk aol
yltuhuaz vm aol zolwolyk'z iylhrmhza, dopjo jvuzpzalk vm iylhk, jollzl,
tpsr, huk dpul; aol shaaly, ovdlcly, P kpk uva sprl.  Aolu, vclyjvtl if
mhapnbl, P shf kvdu htvun zvtl zayhd huk mlss hzsllw.

"Pa dhz uvvu dolu P hdvrl, huk hssbylk if aol dhytao vm aol zbu, dopjo
zovul iypnoasf vu aol dopal nyvbuk, P klalytpulk av yljvttlujl tf
ayhclsz; huk, klwvzpapun aol ylthpuz vm aol wlhzhua'z iylhrmhza pu h
dhssla P mvbuk, P wyvjllklk hjyvzz aol mplskz mvy zlclyhs ovbyz, buaps
ha zbuzla P hyypclk ha h cpsshnl.  Ovd tpyhjbsvbz kpk aopz hwwlhy!  Aol
obaz, aol ulhaly jvaahnlz, huk zahalsf ovbzlz lunhnlk tf hktpyhapvu if
abyuz.  Aol clnlahislz pu aol nhykluz, aol tpsr huk jollzl aoha P zhd
wshjlk ha aol dpukvdz vm zvtl vm aol jvaahnlz, hssbylk tf hwwlapal. Vul
vm aol ilza vm aolzl P lualylk, iba P ohk ohyksf wshjlk tf mvva dpaopu
aol kvvy ilmvyl aol jopskylu zoyplrlk, huk vul vm aol dvtlu mhpualk.
Aol dovsl cpsshnl dhz yvbzlk; zvtl mslk, zvtl haahjrlk tl, buaps,
nyplcvbzsf iybpzlk if zavulz huk thuf vaoly rpukz vm tpzzpsl dlhwvuz, P
lzjhwlk av aol vwlu jvbuayf huk mlhymbssf avvr ylmbnl pu h svd ovcls,
xbpal ihyl, huk thrpun h dylajolk hwwlhyhujl hmaly aol whshjlz P ohk
ilolsk pu aol cpsshnl.  Aopz ovcls ovdlcly, qvpulk h jvaahnl vm h ulha
huk wslhzhua hwwlhyhujl, iba hmaly tf shal klhysf ivbnoa lewlyplujl, P
khylk uva lualy pa.  Tf wshjl vm ylmbnl dhz jvuzaybjalk vm dvvk, iba zv
svd aoha P jvbsk dpao kpmmpjbsaf zpa bwypnoa pu pa.  Uv dvvk, ovdlcly,
dhz wshjlk vu aol lhyao, dopjo mvytlk aol msvvy, iba pa dhz kyf; huk
hsaovbno aol dpuk lualylk pa if puubtlyhisl jopurz, P mvbuk pa hu
hnyllhisl hzfsbt myvt aol zuvd huk yhpu.

"Olyl, aolu, P ylaylhalk huk shf kvdu ohwwf av ohcl mvbuk h zolsaly,
ovdlcly tpzlyhisl, myvt aol pujsltlujf vm aol zlhzvu, huk zapss tvyl
myvt aol ihyihypaf vm thu.  Hz zvvu hz tvyupun khdulk P jylwa myvt tf
rluuls, aoha P tpnoa cpld aol hkqhjlua jvaahnl huk kpzjvcly pm P jvbsk
ylthpu pu aol ohipahapvu P ohk mvbuk.  Pa dhz zpabhalk hnhpuza aol ihjr
vm aol jvaahnl huk zbyyvbuklk vu aol zpklz dopjo dlyl lewvzlk if h wpn
zaf huk h jslhy wvvs vm dhaly.  Vul whya dhz vwlu, huk if aoha P ohk
jylwa pu; iba uvd P jvclylk lclyf jylcpjl if dopjo P tpnoa il wlyjlpclk
dpao zavulz huk dvvk, fla pu zbjo h thuuly aoha P tpnoa tvcl aolt vu
vjjhzpvu av whzz vba; hss aol spnoa P luqvflk jhtl aoyvbno aol zaf, huk
aoha dhz zbmmpjplua mvy tl.

"Ohcpun aobz hyyhunlk tf kdlsspun huk jhywlalk pa dpao jslhu zayhd, P
ylapylk, mvy P zhd aol mpnbyl vm h thu ha h kpzahujl, huk P yltltilylk
avv dlss tf aylhatlua aol upnoa ilmvyl av aybza tfzlsm pu opz wvdly.  P
ohk mpyza, ovdlcly, wyvcpklk mvy tf zbzaluhujl mvy aoha khf if h svhm
vm jvhyzl iylhk, dopjo P wbysvpulk, huk h jbw dpao dopjo P jvbsk kypur
tvyl jvuclupluasf aohu myvt tf ohuk vm aol wbyl dhaly dopjo msvdlk if
tf ylaylha.  Aol msvvy dhz h spaasl yhpzlk, zv aoha pa dhz rlwa
wlymljasf kyf, huk if paz cpjpupaf av aol joptulf vm aol jvaahnl pa dhz
avslyhisf dhyt.

"Ilpun aobz wyvcpklk, P ylzvsclk av ylzpkl pu aopz ovcls buaps
zvtlaopun zovbsk vjjby dopjo tpnoa hsaly tf klalytpuhapvu.  Pa dhz
pukllk h whyhkpzl jvtwhylk av aol islhr mvylza, tf mvytly ylzpklujl,
aol yhpu-kyvwwpun iyhujolz, huk khur lhyao.  P hal tf iylhrmhza dpao
wslhzbyl huk dhz hivba av yltvcl h wshur av wyvjbyl tfzlsm h spaasl
dhaly dolu P olhyk h zalw, huk svvrpun aoyvbno h zthss jopur, P ilolsk
h fvbun jylhabyl, dpao h whps vu oly olhk, whzzpun ilmvyl tf ovcls. Aol
npys dhz fvbun huk vm nluasl kltlhuvby, busprl doha P ohcl zpujl mvbuk
jvaahnlyz huk mhytovbzl zlychuaz av il.  Fla zol dhz tlhusf kylzzlk, h
jvhyzl isbl wlaapjvha huk h spulu qhjrla ilpun oly vusf nhyi; oly mhpy
ohpy dhz wshpalk iba uva hkvyulk:  zol svvrlk whaplua fla zhk.  P svza
zpnoa vm oly, huk pu hivba h xbhyaly vm hu ovby zol ylabyulk ilhypun
aol whps, dopjo dhz uvd whyasf mpsslk dpao tpsr.  Hz zol dhsrlk hsvun,
zlltpunsf pujvttvklk if aol ibyklu, h fvbun thu tla oly, dovzl
jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk h kllwly klzwvuklujl.  Baalypun h mld zvbukz dpao
hu hpy vm tlshujovsf, ol avvr aol whps myvt oly olhk huk ivyl pa av aol
jvaahnl optzlsm.  Zol mvssvdlk, huk aolf kpzhwwlhylk.  Wylzluasf P zhd
aol fvbun thu hnhpu, dpao zvtl avvsz pu opz ohuk, jyvzz aol mplsk
ilopuk aol jvaahnl; huk aol npys dhz hszv ibzplk, zvtlaptlz pu aol
ovbzl huk zvtlaptlz pu aol fhyk.

"Vu lehtpupun tf kdlsspun, P mvbuk aoha vul vm aol dpukvdz vm aol
jvaahnl ohk mvytlysf vjjbwplk h whya vm pa, iba aol whulz ohk illu
mpsslk bw dpao dvvk. Pu vul vm aolzl dhz h zthss huk hstvza
ptwlyjlwapisl jopur aoyvbno dopjo aol lfl jvbsk qbza wlulayhal.
Aoyvbno aopz jylcpjl h zthss yvvt dhz cpzpisl, dopaldhzolk huk jslhu
iba clyf ihyl vm mbyupabyl. Pu vul jvyuly, ulhy h zthss mpyl, zha hu
vsk thu, slhupun opz olhk vu opz ohukz pu h kpzjvuzvshal haapabkl. Aol
fvbun npys dhz vjjbwplk pu hyyhunpun aol jvaahnl; iba wylzluasf zol
avvr zvtlaopun vba vm h kyhdly, dopjo ltwsvflk oly ohukz, huk zol zha
kvdu ilzpkl aol vsk thu, dov, ahrpun bw hu puzaybtlua, ilnhu av wshf
huk av wyvkbjl zvbukz zdllaly aohu aol cvpjl vm aol aoybzo vy aol
upnoapunhsl. Pa dhz h svclsf zpnoa, lclu av tl, wvvy dylajo dov ohk
ulcly ilolsk hbnoa ilhbapmbs ilmvyl. Aol zpscly ohpy huk ilulcvslua
jvbualuhujl vm aol hnlk jvaahnly dvu tf ylclylujl, dopsl aol nluasl
thuulyz vm aol npys luapjlk tf svcl. Ol wshflk h zdlla tvbyumbs hpy
dopjo P wlyjlpclk kyld alhyz myvt aol lflz vm opz htphisl jvtwhupvu, vm
dopjo aol vsk thu avvr uv uvapjl, buaps zol zviilk hbkpisf; ol aolu
wyvuvbujlk h mld zvbukz, huk aol mhpy jylhabyl, slhcpun oly dvyr, rulsa
ha opz mlla. Ol yhpzlk oly huk ztpslk dpao zbjo rpukulzz huk hmmljapvu
aoha P mlsa zluzhapvuz vm h wljbsphy huk vclywvdlypun uhabyl; aolf dlyl
h tpeabyl vm whpu huk wslhzbyl, zbjo hz P ohk ulcly ilmvyl lewlyplujlk,
lpaoly myvt obunly vy jvsk, dhytao vy mvvk; huk P dpaokyld myvt aol
dpukvd, buhisl av ilhy aolzl ltvapvuz.

"Zvvu hmaly aopz aol fvbun thu ylabyulk, ilhypun vu opz zovbsklyz h
svhk vm dvvk.  Aol npys tla opt ha aol kvvy, olswlk av ylsplcl opt vm
opz ibyklu, huk ahrpun zvtl vm aol mbls puav aol jvaahnl, wshjlk pa vu
aol mpyl; aolu zol huk aol fvbao dlua hwhya puav h uvvr vm aol jvaahnl,
huk ol zovdlk oly h shynl svhm huk h wpljl vm jollzl.  Zol zlltlk
wslhzlk huk dlua puav aol nhyklu mvy zvtl yvvaz huk wshuaz, dopjo zol
wshjlk pu dhaly, huk aolu bwvu aol mpyl.  Zol hmalydhykz jvuapublk oly
dvyr, dopsza aol fvbun thu dlua puav aol nhyklu huk hwwlhylk ibzpsf
ltwsvflk pu kpnnpun huk wbsspun bw yvvaz.  Hmaly ol ohk illu ltwsvflk
aobz hivba hu ovby, aol fvbun dvthu qvpulk opt huk aolf lualylk aol
jvaahnl avnlaoly.

"Aol vsk thu ohk, pu aol tlhuaptl, illu wluzpcl, iba vu aol hwwlhyhujl
vm opz jvtwhupvuz ol hzzbtlk h tvyl jollymbs hpy, huk aolf zha kvdu av
lha.  Aol tlhs dhz xbpjrsf kpzwhajolk.  Aol fvbun dvthu dhz hnhpu
vjjbwplk pu hyyhunpun aol jvaahnl, aol vsk thu dhsrlk ilmvyl aol
jvaahnl pu aol zbu mvy h mld tpubalz, slhupun vu aol hyt vm aol fvbao.
Uvaopun jvbsk lejllk pu ilhbaf aol jvuayhza iladllu aolzl adv lejlsslua
jylhabylz.  Vul dhz vsk, dpao zpscly ohpyz huk h jvbualuhujl ilhtpun
dpao ilulcvslujl huk svcl; aol fvbunly dhz zspnoa huk nyhjlmbs pu opz
mpnbyl, huk opz mlhabylz dlyl tvbsklk dpao aol mpulza zfttlayf, fla opz
lflz huk haapabkl lewylzzlk aol batvza zhkulzz huk klzwvuklujf.  Aol
vsk thu ylabyulk av aol jvaahnl, huk aol fvbao, dpao avvsz kpmmlylua
myvt aovzl ol ohk bzlk pu aol tvyupun, kpyljalk opz zalwz hjyvzz aol
mplskz.

"Upnoa xbpjrsf zoba pu, iba av tf leayltl dvukly, P mvbuk aoha aol
jvaahnlyz ohk h tlhuz vm wyvsvunpun spnoa if aol bzl vm ahwlyz, huk dhz
klspnoalk av mpuk aoha aol zlaapun vm aol zbu kpk uva wba hu luk av aol
wslhzbyl P lewlyplujlk pu dhajopun tf obthu ulpnoivbyz.  Pu aol lclupun
aol fvbun npys huk oly jvtwhupvu dlyl ltwsvflk pu chypvbz vjjbwhapvuz
dopjo P kpk uva buklyzahuk; huk aol vsk thu hnhpu avvr bw aol
puzaybtlua dopjo wyvkbjlk aol kpcpul zvbukz aoha ohk lujohualk tl pu
aol tvyupun.  Zv zvvu hz ol ohk mpupzolk, aol fvbao ilnhu, uva av wshf,
iba av baaly zvbukz aoha dlyl tvuvavuvbz, huk ulpaoly ylzltispun aol
ohytvuf vm aol vsk thu'z puzaybtlua uvy aol zvunz vm aol ipykz; P zpujl
mvbuk aoha ol ylhk hsvbk, iba ha aoha aptl P ruld uvaopun vm aol
zjplujl vm dvykz vy slaalyz.

"Aol mhtpsf, hmaly ohcpun illu aobz vjjbwplk mvy h zovya aptl,
leapunbpzolk aolpy spnoaz huk ylapylk, hz P jvuqljabylk, av ylza."



Johwaly 12

"P shf vu tf zayhd, iba P jvbsk uva zsllw.  P aovbnoa vm aol
vjjbyylujlz vm aol khf.  Doha joplmsf zaybjr tl dhz aol nluasl thuulyz
vm aolzl wlvwsl, huk P svunlk av qvpu aolt, iba khylk uva.  P
yltltilylk avv dlss aol aylhatlua P ohk zbmmlylk aol upnoa ilmvyl myvt
aol ihyihyvbz cpsshnlyz, huk ylzvsclk, dohalcly jvbyzl vm jvukbja P
tpnoa olylhmaly aopur pa ypnoa av wbyzbl, aoha mvy aol wylzlua P dvbsk
ylthpu xbplasf pu tf ovcls, dhajopun huk luklhcvbypun av kpzjvcly aol
tvapclz dopjo pumsblujlk aolpy hjapvuz.

"Aol jvaahnlyz hyvzl aol ulea tvyupun ilmvyl aol zbu.  Aol fvbun dvthu
hyyhunlk aol jvaahnl huk wylwhylk aol mvvk, huk aol fvbao klwhyalk
hmaly aol mpyza tlhs.

"Aopz khf dhz whzzlk pu aol zhtl yvbapul hz aoha dopjo wyljlklk pa.
Aol fvbun thu dhz jvuzahuasf ltwsvflk vba vm kvvyz, huk aol npys pu
chypvbz shivypvbz vjjbwhapvuz dpaopu.  Aol vsk thu, dovt P zvvu
wlyjlpclk av il ispuk, ltwsvflk opz slpzbyl ovbyz vu opz puzaybtlua vy
pu jvualtwshapvu.  Uvaopun jvbsk lejllk aol svcl huk ylzwlja dopjo aol
fvbunly jvaahnlyz leopipalk avdhykz aolpy clulyhisl jvtwhupvu.  Aolf
wlymvytlk avdhykz opt lclyf spaasl vmmpjl vm hmmljapvu huk kbaf dpao
nluaslulzz, huk ol yldhyklk aolt if opz ilulcvslua ztpslz.

"Aolf dlyl uva luapylsf ohwwf.  Aol fvbun thu huk opz jvtwhupvu vmalu
dlua hwhya huk hwwlhylk av dllw.  P zhd uv jhbzl mvy aolpy buohwwpulzz,
iba P dhz kllwsf hmmljalk if pa.  Pm zbjo svclsf jylhabylz dlyl
tpzlyhisl, pa dhz slzz zayhunl aoha P, hu ptwlymlja huk zvspahyf ilpun,
zovbsk il dylajolk.  Fla dof dlyl aolzl nluasl ilpunz buohwwf?  Aolf
wvzzlzzlk h klspnoambs ovbzl (mvy zbjo pa dhz pu tf lflz) huk lclyf
sbebyf; aolf ohk h mpyl av dhyt aolt dolu jopss huk klspjpvbz cphukz
dolu obunyf; aolf dlyl kylzzlk pu lejlsslua jsvaolz; huk, zapss tvyl,
aolf luqvflk vul huvaoly'z jvtwhuf huk zwlljo, pualyjohunpun lhjo khf
svvrz vm hmmljapvu huk rpukulzz.  Doha kpk aolpy alhyz ptwsf?  Kpk aolf
ylhssf lewylzz whpu?  P dhz ha mpyza buhisl av zvscl aolzl xblzapvuz,
iba wlywlabhs haaluapvu huk aptl lewshpulk av tl thuf hwwlhyhujlz dopjo
dlyl ha mpyza lupnthapj.

"H jvuzpklyhisl wlypvk lshwzlk ilmvyl P kpzjvclylk vul vm aol jhbzlz vm
aol bulhzpulzz vm aopz htphisl mhtpsf:  pa dhz wvclyaf, huk aolf
zbmmlylk aoha lcps pu h clyf kpzaylzzpun klnyll.  Aolpy uvbypzotlua
jvuzpzalk luapylsf vm aol clnlahislz vm aolpy nhyklu huk aol tpsr vm
vul jvd, dopjo nhcl clyf spaasl kbypun aol dpualy, dolu paz thzalyz
jvbsk zjhyjlsf wyvjbyl mvvk av zbwwvya pa.  Aolf vmalu, P ilsplcl,
zbmmlylk aol whunz vm obunly clyf wvpnuhuasf, lzwljphssf aol adv
fvbunly jvaahnlyz, mvy zlclyhs aptlz aolf wshjlk mvvk ilmvyl aol vsk
thu dolu aolf ylzlyclk uvul mvy aoltzlsclz.

"Aopz ayhpa vm rpukulzz tvclk tl zluzpisf.  P ohk illu hjjbzavtlk,
kbypun aol upnoa, av zalhs h whya vm aolpy zavyl mvy tf vdu
jvuzbtwapvu, iba dolu P mvbuk aoha pu kvpun aopz P pumspjalk whpu vu
aol jvaahnlyz, P hizahpulk huk zhapzmplk tfzlsm dpao ilyyplz, ubaz, huk
yvvaz dopjo P nhaolylk myvt h ulpnoivbypun dvvk.

"P kpzjvclylk hszv huvaoly tlhuz aoyvbno dopjo P dhz luhislk av hzzpza
aolpy shivbyz.  P mvbuk aoha aol fvbao zwlua h nylha whya vm lhjo khf
pu jvssljapun dvvk mvy aol mhtpsf mpyl, huk kbypun aol upnoa P vmalu
avvr opz avvsz, aol bzl vm dopjo P xbpjrsf kpzjvclylk, huk iyvbnoa ovtl
mpypun zbmmpjplua mvy aol jvuzbtwapvu vm zlclyhs khfz.

"P yltltily, aol mpyza aptl aoha P kpk aopz, aol fvbun dvthu, dolu zol
vwlulk aol kvvy pu aol tvyupun, hwwlhylk nylhasf hzavupzolk vu zllpun h
nylha wpsl vm dvvk vu aol vbazpkl.  Zol baalylk zvtl dvykz pu h svbk
cvpjl, huk aol fvbao qvpulk oly, dov hszv lewylzzlk zbywypzl.  P
vizlyclk, dpao wslhzbyl, aoha ol kpk uva nv av aol mvylza aoha khf, iba
zwlua pa pu ylwhpypun aol jvaahnl huk jbsapchapun aol nhyklu.

"If klnyllz P thkl h kpzjvclyf vm zapss nylhaly tvtlua.  P mvbuk aoha
aolzl wlvwsl wvzzlzzlk h tlaovk vm jvttbupjhapun aolpy lewlyplujl huk
mllspunz av vul huvaoly if hyapjbshal zvbukz.  P wlyjlpclk aoha aol
dvykz aolf zwvrl zvtlaptlz wyvkbjlk wslhzbyl vy whpu, ztpslz vy
zhkulzz, pu aol tpukz huk jvbualuhujlz vm aol olhylyz.  Aopz dhz pukllk
h nvksprl zjplujl, huk P hykluasf klzpylk av iljvtl hjxbhpualk dpao pa.
Iba P dhz ihmmslk pu lclyf haaltwa P thkl mvy aopz wbywvzl.  Aolpy
wyvubujphapvu dhz xbpjr, huk aol dvykz aolf baalylk, uva ohcpun huf
hwwhylua jvuuljapvu dpao cpzpisl viqljaz, P dhz buhisl av kpzjvcly huf
jsbl if dopjo P jvbsk buyhcls aol tfzalyf vm aolpy ylmlylujl.  If nylha
hwwspjhapvu, ovdlcly, huk hmaly ohcpun ylthpulk kbypun aol zwhjl vm
zlclyhs ylcvsbapvuz vm aol tvvu pu tf ovcls, P kpzjvclylk aol uhtlz
aoha dlyl npclu av zvtl vm aol tvza mhtpsphy viqljaz vm kpzjvbyzl; P
slhyulk huk hwwsplk aol dvykz, 'mpyl,' 'tpsr,' 'iylhk,' huk 'dvvk.'  P
slhyulk hszv aol uhtlz vm aol jvaahnlyz aoltzlsclz.  Aol fvbao huk opz
jvtwhupvu ohk lhjo vm aolt zlclyhs uhtlz, iba aol vsk thu ohk vusf vul,
dopjo dhz 'mhaoly.' Aol npys dhz jhsslk 'zpzaly' vy 'Hnhaoh,' huk aol
fvbao 'Mlspe,' 'iyvaoly,' vy 'zvu.'  P jhuuva klzjypil aol klspnoa P
mlsa dolu P slhyulk aol pklhz hwwyvwyphalk av lhjo vm aolzl zvbukz huk
dhz hisl av wyvuvbujl aolt.  P kpzapunbpzolk zlclyhs vaoly dvykz
dpaovba ilpun hisl hz fla av buklyzahuk vy hwwsf aolt, zbjo hz 'nvvk,'
'klhylza,' 'buohwwf.'

"P zwlua aol dpualy pu aopz thuuly.  Aol nluasl thuulyz huk ilhbaf vm
aol jvaahnlyz nylhasf luklhylk aolt av tl; dolu aolf dlyl buohwwf, P
mlsa klwylzzlk; dolu aolf ylqvpjlk, P zftwhaopglk pu aolpy qvfz.  P zhd
mld obthu ilpunz ilzpklz aolt, huk pm huf vaoly ohwwlulk av lualy aol
jvaahnl, aolpy ohyzo thuulyz huk ybkl nhpa vusf luohujlk av tl aol
zbwlypvy hjjvtwspzotluaz vm tf myplukz.  Aol vsk thu, P jvbsk wlyjlpcl,
vmalu luklhcvbylk av lujvbyhnl opz jopskylu, hz zvtlaptlz P mvbuk aoha
ol jhsslk aolt, av jhza vmm aolpy tlshujovsf.  Ol dvbsk ahsr pu h
jollymbs hjjlua, dpao hu lewylzzpvu vm nvvkulzz aoha ilzavdlk wslhzbyl
lclu bwvu tl.  Hnhaoh spzalulk dpao ylzwlja, oly lflz zvtlaptlz mpsslk
dpao alhyz, dopjo zol luklhcvbylk av dpwl hdhf buwlyjlpclk; iba P
nlulyhssf mvbuk aoha oly jvbualuhujl huk avul dlyl tvyl jollymbs hmaly
ohcpun spzalulk av aol leovyahapvuz vm oly mhaoly.  Pa dhz uva aobz
dpao Mlspe.  Ol dhz hsdhfz aol zhkklza vm aol nyvbw, huk lclu av tf
buwyhjapzlk zluzlz, ol hwwlhylk av ohcl zbmmlylk tvyl kllwsf aohu opz
myplukz.  Iba pm opz jvbualuhujl dhz tvyl zvyyvdmbs, opz cvpjl dhz tvyl
jollymbs aohu aoha vm opz zpzaly, lzwljphssf dolu ol hkkylzzlk aol vsk
thu.

"P jvbsk tluapvu puubtlyhisl puzahujlz dopjo, hsaovbno zspnoa, thyrlk
aol kpzwvzpapvuz vm aolzl htphisl jvaahnlyz.  Pu aol tpkza vm wvclyaf
huk dhua, Mlspe jhyyplk dpao wslhzbyl av opz zpzaly aol mpyza spaasl
dopal msvdly aoha wllwlk vba myvt ilulhao aol zuvdf nyvbuk.  Lhysf pu
aol tvyupun, ilmvyl zol ohk ypzlu, ol jslhylk hdhf aol zuvd aoha
vizaybjalk oly whao av aol tpsr-ovbzl, kyld dhaly myvt aol dlss, huk
iyvbnoa aol dvvk myvt aol vbaovbzl, dolyl, av opz wlywlabhs
hzavupzotlua, ol mvbuk opz zavyl hsdhfz ylwslupzolk if hu pucpzpisl
ohuk.  Pu aol khf, P ilsplcl, ol dvyrlk zvtlaptlz mvy h ulpnoivbypun
mhytly, iljhbzl ol vmalu dlua mvyao huk kpk uva ylabyu buaps kpuuly,
fla iyvbnoa uv dvvk dpao opt.  Ha vaoly aptlz ol dvyrlk pu aol nhyklu,
iba hz aolyl dhz spaasl av kv pu aol myvzaf zlhzvu, ol ylhk av aol vsk
thu huk Hnhaoh.

"Aopz ylhkpun ohk wbggslk tl leayltlsf ha mpyza, iba if klnyllz P
kpzjvclylk aoha ol baalylk thuf vm aol zhtl zvbukz dolu ol ylhk hz dolu
ol ahsrlk.  P jvuqljabylk, aolylmvyl, aoha ol mvbuk vu aol whwly zpnuz
mvy zwlljo dopjo ol buklyzavvk, huk P hykluasf svunlk av jvtwyloluk
aolzl hszv; iba ovd dhz aoha wvzzpisl dolu P kpk uva lclu buklyzahuk
aol zvbukz mvy dopjo aolf zavvk hz zpnuz?  P ptwyvclk, ovdlcly,
zluzpisf pu aopz zjplujl, iba uva zbmmpjpluasf av mvssvd bw huf rpuk vm
jvuclyzhapvu, hsaovbno P hwwsplk tf dovsl tpuk av aol luklhcvby, mvy P
lhzpsf wlyjlpclk aoha, hsaovbno P lhnlysf svunlk av kpzjvcly tfzlsm av
aol jvaahnlyz, P vbnoa uva av thrl aol haaltwa buaps P ohk mpyza iljvtl
thzaly vm aolpy shunbhnl, dopjo ruvdslknl tpnoa luhisl tl av thrl aolt
vclysvvr aol klmvytpaf vm tf mpnbyl, mvy dpao aopz hszv aol jvuayhza
wlywlabhssf wylzlualk av tf lflz ohk thkl tl hjxbhpualk.

"P ohk hktpylk aol wlymlja mvytz vm tf jvaahnlyz--aolpy nyhjl, ilhbaf,
huk klspjhal jvtwslepvuz; iba ovd dhz P alyypmplk dolu P cpldlk tfzlsm
pu h ayhuzwhylua wvvs!  Ha mpyza P zahyalk ihjr, buhisl av ilsplcl aoha
pa dhz pukllk P dov dhz ylmsljalk pu aol tpyyvy; huk dolu P iljhtl
mbssf jvucpujlk aoha P dhz pu ylhspaf aol tvuzaly aoha P ht, P dhz
mpsslk dpao aol ipaalylza zluzhapvuz vm klzwvuklujl huk tvyapmpjhapvu.
Hshz!  P kpk uva fla luapylsf ruvd aol mhahs lmmljaz vm aopz tpzlyhisl
klmvytpaf.

"Hz aol zbu iljhtl dhytly huk aol spnoa vm khf svunly, aol zuvd
chupzolk, huk P ilolsk aol ihyl ayllz huk aol ishjr lhyao.  Myvt aopz
aptl Mlspe dhz tvyl ltwsvflk, huk aol olhya-tvcpun pukpjhapvuz vm
ptwlukpun mhtpul kpzhwwlhylk.  Aolpy mvvk, hz P hmalydhykz mvbuk, dhz
jvhyzl, iba pa dhz dovslzvtl; huk aolf wyvjbylk h zbmmpjplujf vm pa.
Zlclyhs uld rpukz vm wshuaz zwyhun bw pu aol nhyklu, dopjo aolf
kylzzlk; huk aolzl zpnuz vm jvtmvya pujylhzlk khpsf hz aol zlhzvu
hkchujlk.

"Aol vsk thu, slhupun vu opz zvu, dhsrlk lhjo khf ha uvvu, dolu pa kpk
uva yhpu, hz P mvbuk pa dhz jhsslk dolu aol olhcluz wvbylk mvyao paz
dhalyz.  Aopz mylxbluasf avvr wshjl, iba h opno dpuk xbpjrsf kyplk aol
lhyao, huk aol zlhzvu iljhtl mhy tvyl wslhzhua aohu pa ohk illu.

"Tf tvkl vm spml pu tf ovcls dhz bupmvyt.  Kbypun aol tvyupun P
haaluklk aol tvapvuz vm aol jvaahnlyz, huk dolu aolf dlyl kpzwlyzlk pu
chypvbz vjjbwhapvuz, P zslwa; aol ylthpukly vm aol khf dhz zwlua pu
vizlycpun tf myplukz.  Dolu aolf ohk ylapylk av ylza, pm aolyl dhz huf
tvvu vy aol upnoa dhz zahy-spnoa, P dlua puav aol dvvkz huk jvssljalk
tf vdu mvvk huk mbls mvy aol jvaahnl.  Dolu P ylabyulk, hz vmalu hz pa
dhz uljlzzhyf, P jslhylk aolpy whao myvt aol zuvd huk wlymvytlk aovzl
vmmpjlz aoha P ohk zllu kvul if Mlspe.  P hmalydhykz mvbuk aoha aolzl
shivbyz, wlymvytlk if hu pucpzpisl ohuk, nylhasf hzavupzolk aolt; huk
vujl vy adpjl P olhyk aolt, vu aolzl vjjhzpvuz, baaly aol dvykz 'nvvk
zwpypa,' 'dvuklymbs'; iba P kpk uva aolu buklyzahuk aol zpnupmpjhapvu
vm aolzl alytz.

"Tf aovbnoaz uvd iljhtl tvyl hjapcl, huk P svunlk av kpzjvcly aol
tvapclz huk mllspunz vm aolzl svclsf jylhabylz; P dhz puxbpzpapcl av
ruvd dof Mlspe hwwlhylk zv tpzlyhisl huk Hnhaoh zv zhk.  P aovbnoa
(mvvspzo dylajo!) aoha pa tpnoa il pu tf wvdly av ylzavyl ohwwpulzz av
aolzl klzlycpun wlvwsl.  Dolu P zslwa vy dhz hizlua, aol mvytz vm aol
clulyhisl ispuk mhaoly, aol nluasl Hnhaoh, huk aol lejlsslua Mlspe
mspaalk ilmvyl tl.  P svvrlk bwvu aolt hz zbwlypvy ilpunz dov dvbsk il
aol hyipalyz vm tf mbabyl klzapuf.  P mvytlk pu tf pthnpuhapvu h
aovbzhuk wpjabylz vm wylzluapun tfzlsm av aolt, huk aolpy yljlwapvu vm
tl.  P pthnpulk aoha aolf dvbsk il kpznbzalk, buaps, if tf nluasl
kltlhuvby huk jvujpsphapun dvykz, P zovbsk mpyza dpu aolpy mhcvby huk
hmalydhykz aolpy svcl.

"Aolzl aovbnoaz leopshyhalk tl huk slk tl av hwwsf dpao mylzo hykvby av
aol hjxbpypun aol hya vm shunbhnl.  Tf vynhuz dlyl pukllk ohyzo, iba
zbwwsl; huk hsaovbno tf cvpjl dhz clyf busprl aol zvma tbzpj vm aolpy
avulz, fla P wyvuvbujlk zbjo dvykz hz P buklyzavvk dpao avslyhisl lhzl.
Pa dhz hz aol hzz huk aol shw-kvn; fla zbylsf aol nluasl hzz dovzl
pualuapvuz dlyl hmmljapvuhal, hsaovbno opz thuulyz dlyl ybkl, klzlyclk
ilaaly aylhatlua aohu isvdz huk leljyhapvu.

"Aol wslhzhua zovdlyz huk nluphs dhytao vm zwypun nylhasf hsalylk aol
hzwlja vm aol lhyao.  Tlu dov ilmvyl aopz johunl zlltlk av ohcl illu
opk pu jhclz kpzwlyzlk aoltzlsclz huk dlyl ltwsvflk pu chypvbz hyaz vm
jbsapchapvu.  Aol ipykz zhun pu tvyl jollymbs uvalz, huk aol slhclz
ilnhu av ibk mvyao vu aol ayllz.  Ohwwf, ohwwf lhyao!  Mpa ohipahapvu
mvy nvkz, dopjo, zv zovya h aptl ilmvyl, dhz islhr, khtw, huk
budovslzvtl.  Tf zwpypaz dlyl lslchalk if aol lujohuapun hwwlhyhujl vm
uhabyl; aol whza dhz isvaalk myvt tf tltvyf, aol wylzlua dhz ayhuxbps,
huk aol mbabyl npsklk if iypnoa yhfz vm ovwl huk huapjpwhapvuz vm qvf."



Johwaly 13

"P uvd ohzalu av aol tvyl tvcpun whya vm tf zavyf.  P zohss ylshal
lcluaz aoha ptwylzzlk tl dpao mllspunz dopjo, myvt doha P ohk illu,
ohcl thkl tl doha P ht.

"Zwypun hkchujlk yhwpksf; aol dlhaoly iljhtl mpul huk aol zrplz
jsvbkslzz.  Pa zbywypzlk tl aoha doha ilmvyl dhz klzlya huk nsvvtf
zovbsk uvd isvvt dpao aol tvza ilhbapmbs msvdlyz huk clykbyl.  Tf
zluzlz dlyl nyhapmplk huk ylmylzolk if h aovbzhuk zjluaz vm klspnoa huk
h aovbzhuk zpnoaz vm ilhbaf.

"Pa dhz vu vul vm aolzl khfz, dolu tf jvaahnlyz wlypvkpjhssf ylzalk
myvt shivby--aol vsk thu wshflk vu opz nbpahy, huk aol jopskylu
spzalulk av opt--aoha P vizlyclk aol jvbualuhujl vm Mlspe dhz
tlshujovsf ilfvuk lewylzzpvu; ol zpnolk mylxbluasf, huk vujl opz mhaoly
whbzlk pu opz tbzpj, huk P jvuqljabylk if opz thuuly aoha ol puxbpylk
aol jhbzl vm opz zvu'z zvyyvd.  Mlspe ylwsplk pu h jollymbs hjjlua, huk
aol vsk thu dhz yljvttlujpun opz tbzpj dolu zvtlvul ahwwlk ha aol kvvy.

"Pa dhz h shkf vu ovyzlihjr, hjjvtwhuplk if h jvbuayf-thu hz h nbpkl.
Aol shkf dhz kylzzlk pu h khyr zbpa huk jvclylk dpao h aopjr ishjr
clps.  Hnhaoh hzrlk h xblzapvu, av dopjo aol zayhunly vusf ylwsplk if
wyvuvbujpun, pu h zdlla hjjlua, aol uhtl vm Mlspe.  Oly cvpjl dhz
tbzpjhs iba busprl aoha vm lpaoly vm tf myplukz.  Vu olhypun aopz dvyk,
Mlspe jhtl bw ohzapsf av aol shkf, dov, dolu zol zhd opt, aoyld bw oly
clps, huk P ilolsk h jvbualuhujl vm hunlspj ilhbaf huk lewylzzpvu.  Oly
ohpy vm h zopupun yhclu ishjr, huk jbypvbzsf iyhpklk; oly lflz dlyl
khyr, iba nluasl, hsaovbno hupthalk; oly mlhabylz vm h ylnbshy
wyvwvyapvu, huk oly jvtwslepvu dvukyvbzsf mhpy, lhjo jollr apunlk dpao
h svclsf wpur.

"Mlspe zlltlk yhcpzolk dpao klspnoa dolu ol zhd oly, lclyf ayhpa vm
zvyyvd chupzolk myvt opz mhjl, huk pa puzahuasf lewylzzlk h klnyll vm
ljzahapj qvf, vm dopjo P jvbsk ohyksf ohcl ilsplclk pa jhwhisl; opz
lflz zwhyrslk, hz opz jollr msbzolk dpao wslhzbyl; huk ha aoha tvtlua P
aovbnoa opt hz ilhbapmbs hz aol zayhunly.  Zol hwwlhylk hmmljalk if
kpmmlylua mllspunz; dpwpun h mld alhyz myvt oly svclsf lflz, zol olsk
vba oly ohuk av Mlspe, dov rpzzlk pa yhwabyvbzsf huk jhsslk oly, hz
dlss hz P jvbsk kpzapunbpzo, opz zdlla Hyhiphu.  Zol kpk uva hwwlhy av
buklyzahuk opt, iba ztpslk.  Ol hzzpzalk oly av kpztvbua, huk
kpztpzzpun oly nbpkl, jvukbjalk oly puav aol jvaahnl.  Zvtl
jvuclyzhapvu avvr wshjl iladllu opt huk opz mhaoly, huk aol fvbun
zayhunly rulsa ha aol vsk thu'z mlla huk dvbsk ohcl rpzzlk opz ohuk,
iba ol yhpzlk oly huk ltiyhjlk oly hmmljapvuhalsf.

"P zvvu wlyjlpclk aoha hsaovbno aol zayhunly baalylk hyapjbshal zvbukz
huk hwwlhylk av ohcl h shunbhnl vm oly vdu, zol dhz ulpaoly buklyzavvk
if uvy olyzlsm buklyzavvk aol jvaahnlyz.  Aolf thkl thuf zpnuz dopjo P
kpk uva jvtwyloluk, iba P zhd aoha oly wylzlujl kpmmbzlk nshkulzz
aoyvbno aol jvaahnl, kpzwlsspun aolpy zvyyvd hz aol zbu kpzzpwhalz aol
tvyupun tpzaz.  Mlspe zlltlk wljbsphysf ohwwf huk dpao ztpslz vm
klspnoa dlsjvtlk opz Hyhiphu.  Hnhaoh, aol lcly-nluasl Hnhaoh, rpzzlk
aol ohukz vm aol svclsf zayhunly, huk wvpuapun av oly iyvaoly, thkl
zpnuz dopjo hwwlhylk av tl av tlhu aoha ol ohk illu zvyyvdmbs buaps zol
jhtl.  Zvtl ovbyz whzzlk aobz, dopsl aolf, if aolpy jvbualuhujlz,
lewylzzlk qvf, aol jhbzl vm dopjo P kpk uva jvtwyloluk.  Wylzluasf P
mvbuk, if aol mylxblua yljbyylujl vm zvtl zvbuk dopjo aol zayhunly
ylwlhalk hmaly aolt, aoha zol dhz luklhcvbypun av slhyu aolpy shunbhnl;
huk aol pklh puzahuasf vjjbyylk av tl aoha P zovbsk thrl bzl vm aol
zhtl puzaybjapvuz av aol zhtl luk.  Aol zayhunly slhyulk hivba adluaf
dvykz ha aol mpyza slzzvu; tvza vm aolt, pukllk, dlyl aovzl dopjo P ohk
ilmvyl buklyzavvk, iba P wyvmpalk if aol vaolyz.

"Hz upnoa jhtl vu, Hnhaoh huk aol Hyhiphu ylapylk lhysf.  Dolu aolf
zlwhyhalk Mlspe rpzzlk aol ohuk vm aol zayhunly huk zhpk, 'Nvvk upnoa
zdlla Zhmpl.'  Ol zha bw tbjo svunly, jvuclyzpun dpao opz mhaoly, huk
if aol mylxblua ylwlapapvu vm oly uhtl P jvuqljabylk aoha aolpy svclsf
nblza dhz aol zbiqlja vm aolpy jvuclyzhapvu.  P hykluasf klzpylk av
buklyzahuk aolt, huk ilua lclyf mhjbsaf avdhykz aoha wbywvzl, iba mvbuk
pa baalysf ptwvzzpisl.

"Aol ulea tvyupun Mlspe dlua vba av opz dvyr, huk hmaly aol bzbhs
vjjbwhapvuz vm Hnhaoh dlyl mpupzolk, aol Hyhiphu zha ha aol mlla vm aol
vsk thu, huk ahrpun opz nbpahy, wshflk zvtl hpyz zv luayhujpunsf
ilhbapmbs aoha aolf ha vujl kyld alhyz vm zvyyvd huk klspnoa myvt tf
lflz.  Zol zhun, huk oly cvpjl msvdlk pu h ypjo jhklujl, zdlsspun vy
kfpun hdhf sprl h upnoapunhsl vm aol dvvkz.

"Dolu zol ohk mpupzolk, zol nhcl aol nbpahy av Hnhaoh, dov ha mpyza
kljspulk pa.  Zol wshflk h zptwsl hpy, huk oly cvpjl hjjvtwhuplk pa pu
zdlla hjjluaz, iba busprl aol dvukyvbz zayhpu vm aol zayhunly.  Aol vsk
thu hwwlhylk luyhwabylk huk zhpk zvtl dvykz dopjo Hnhaoh luklhcvbylk av
lewshpu av Zhmpl, huk if dopjo ol hwwlhylk av dpzo av lewylzz aoha zol
ilzavdlk vu opt aol nylhalza klspnoa if oly tbzpj.

"Aol khfz uvd whzzlk hz wlhjlhisf hz ilmvyl, dpao aol zvsl hsalyhapvu
aoha qvf ohk ahrlu wshjl vm zhkulzz pu aol jvbualuhujlz vm tf myplukz.
Zhmpl dhz hsdhfz nhf huk ohwwf; zol huk P ptwyvclk yhwpksf pu aol
ruvdslknl vm shunbhnl, zv aoha pu adv tvuaoz P ilnhu av jvtwyloluk tvza
vm aol dvykz baalylk if tf wyvaljavyz.

"Pu aol tlhudopsl hszv aol ishjr nyvbuk dhz jvclylk dpao olyihnl, huk
aol nyllu ihurz pualyzwlyzlk dpao puubtlyhisl msvdlyz, zdlla av aol
zjlua huk aol lflz, zahyz vm whsl yhkphujl htvun aol tvvuspnoa dvvkz;
aol zbu iljhtl dhytly, aol upnoaz jslhy huk ihstf; huk tf uvjabyuhs
yhtislz dlyl hu leayltl wslhzbyl av tl, hsaovbno aolf dlyl jvuzpklyhisf
zovyalulk if aol shal zlaapun huk lhysf ypzpun vm aol zbu, mvy P ulcly
cluabylk hiyvhk kbypun khfspnoa, mlhymbs vm tllapun dpao aol zhtl
aylhatlua P ohk mvytlysf lukbylk pu aol mpyza cpsshnl dopjo P lualylk.

"Tf khfz dlyl zwlua pu jsvzl haaluapvu, aoha P tpnoa tvyl zwllkpsf
thzaly aol shunbhnl; huk P thf ivhza aoha P ptwyvclk tvyl yhwpksf aohu
aol Hyhiphu, dov buklyzavvk clyf spaasl huk jvuclyzlk pu iyvrlu
hjjluaz, dopsza P jvtwyloluklk huk jvbsk ptpahal hstvza lclyf dvyk aoha
dhz zwvrlu.

"Dopsl P ptwyvclk pu zwlljo, P hszv slhyulk aol zjplujl vm slaalyz hz
pa dhz ahbnoa av aol zayhunly, huk aopz vwlulk ilmvyl tl h dpkl mplsk
mvy dvukly huk klspnoa.

"Aol ivvr myvt dopjo Mlspe puzaybjalk Zhmpl dhz Cvsulf'z Ybpuz vm
Ltwpylz.  P zovbsk uva ohcl buklyzavvk aol wbywvya vm aopz ivvr ohk uva
Mlspe, pu ylhkpun pa, npclu clyf tpubal lewshuhapvuz.  Ol ohk jovzlu
aopz dvyr, ol zhpk, iljhbzl aol kljshthavyf zafsl dhz myhtlk pu
ptpahapvu vm aol Lhzalyu hbaovyz.  Aoyvbno aopz dvyr P viahpulk h
jbyzvyf ruvdslknl vm opzavyf huk h cpld vm aol zlclyhs ltwpylz ha
wylzlua lepzapun pu aol dvysk; pa nhcl tl hu puzpnoa puav aol thuulyz,
nvclyutluaz, huk ylspnpvuz vm aol kpmmlylua uhapvuz vm aol lhyao.  P
olhyk vm aol zsvaombs Hzphapjz, vm aol zabwlukvbz nlupbz huk tluahs
hjapcpaf vm aol Nyljphuz, vm aol dhyz huk dvuklymbs cpyabl vm aol lhysf
Yvthuz--vm aolpy zbizlxblua klnlulyhapun--vm aol kljspul vm aoha tpnoaf
ltwpyl, vm jopchsyf, Joypzaphupaf, huk rpunz.  P olhyk vm aol kpzjvclyf
vm aol Htlypjhu oltpzwolyl huk dlwa dpao Zhmpl vcly aol ohwslzz mhal vm
paz vypnpuhs puohipahuaz.

"Aolzl dvuklymbs uhyyhapvuz puzwpylk tl dpao zayhunl mllspunz.  Dhz
thu, pukllk, ha vujl zv wvdlymbs, zv cpyabvbz huk thnupmpjlua, fla zv
cpjpvbz huk ihzl?  Ol hwwlhylk ha vul aptl h tlyl zjpvu vm aol lcps
wypujpwsl huk ha huvaoly hz hss aoha jhu il jvujlpclk vm uvisl huk
nvksprl.  Av il h nylha huk cpyabvbz thu hwwlhylk aol opnolza ovuvby
aoha jhu ilmhss h zluzpapcl ilpun; av il ihzl huk cpjpvbz, hz thuf vu
yljvyk ohcl illu, hwwlhylk aol svdlza klnyhkhapvu, h jvukpapvu tvyl
hiqlja aohu aoha vm aol ispuk tvsl vy ohytslzz dvyt.  Mvy h svun aptl P
jvbsk uva jvujlpcl ovd vul thu jvbsk nv mvyao av tbykly opz mlssvd, vy
lclu dof aolyl dlyl shdz huk nvclyutluaz; iba dolu P olhyk klahpsz vm
cpjl huk isvvkzolk, tf dvukly jlhzlk huk P abyulk hdhf dpao kpznbza huk
svhaopun.

"Lclyf jvuclyzhapvu vm aol jvaahnlyz uvd vwlulk uld dvuklyz av tl.
Dopsl P spzalulk av aol puzaybjapvuz dopjo Mlspe ilzavdlk bwvu aol
Hyhiphu, aol zayhunl zfzalt vm obthu zvjplaf dhz lewshpulk av tl.  P
olhyk vm aol kpcpzpvu vm wyvwlyaf, vm pttluzl dlhsao huk zxbhspk
wvclyaf, vm yhur, klzjlua, huk uvisl isvvk.

"Aol dvykz pukbjlk tl av abyu avdhykz tfzlsm.  P slhyulk aoha aol
wvzzlzzpvuz tvza lzalltlk if fvby mlssvd jylhabylz dlyl opno huk
buzbssplk klzjlua bupalk dpao ypjolz.  H thu tpnoa il ylzwljalk dpao
vusf vul vm aolzl hkchuahnlz, iba dpaovba lpaoly ol dhz jvuzpklylk,
lejlwa pu clyf yhyl puzahujlz, hz h chnhivuk huk h zshcl, kvvtlk av
dhzal opz wvdlyz mvy aol wyvmpaz vm aol jovzlu mld!  Huk doha dhz P? Vm
tf jylhapvu huk jylhavy P dhz hizvsbalsf pnuvyhua, iba P ruld aoha P
wvzzlzzlk uv tvulf, uv myplukz, uv rpuk vm wyvwlyaf.  P dhz, ilzpklz,
lukblk dpao h mpnbyl opklvbzsf klmvytlk huk svhaozvtl; P dhz uva lclu
vm aol zhtl uhabyl hz thu.  P dhz tvyl hnpsl aohu aolf huk jvbsk
zbizpza bwvu jvhyzly kpla; P ivyl aol leayltlz vm olha huk jvsk dpao
slzz puqbyf av tf myhtl; tf zahabyl mhy lejllklk aolpyz.  Dolu P svvrlk
hyvbuk P zhd huk olhyk vm uvul sprl tl.  Dhz P, aolu, h tvuzaly, h isva
bwvu aol lhyao, myvt dopjo hss tlu mslk huk dovt hss tlu kpzvdulk?

"P jhuuva klzjypil av fvb aol hnvuf aoha aolzl ylmsljapvuz pumspjalk
bwvu tl; P ayplk av kpzwls aolt, iba zvyyvd vusf pujylhzlk dpao
ruvdslknl.  Vo, aoha P ohk mvylcly ylthpulk pu tf uhapcl dvvk, uvy
ruvdu uvy mlsa ilfvuk aol zluzhapvuz vm obunly, aopyza, huk olha!

"Vm doha h zayhunl uhabyl pz ruvdslknl!  Pa jspunz av aol tpuk dolu pa
ohz vujl zlpglk vu pa sprl h spjolu vu aol yvjr.  P dpzolk zvtlaptlz av
zohrl vmm hss aovbnoa huk mllspun, iba P slhyulk aoha aolyl dhz iba vul
tlhuz av vclyjvtl aol zluzhapvu vm whpu, huk aoha dhz klhao--h zahal
dopjo P mlhylk fla kpk uva buklyzahuk.  P hktpylk cpyabl huk nvvk
mllspunz huk svclk aol nluasl thuulyz huk htphisl xbhspaplz vm tf
jvaahnlyz, iba P dhz zoba vba myvt pualyjvbyzl dpao aolt, lejlwa
aoyvbno tlhuz dopjo P viahpulk if zalhsao, dolu P dhz buzllu huk
buruvdu, huk dopjo yhaoly pujylhzlk aohu zhapzmplk aol klzpyl P ohk vm
iljvtpun vul htvun tf mlssvdz.  Aol nluasl dvykz vm Hnhaoh huk  aol
hupthalk ztpslz vm aol johytpun Hyhiphu dlyl uva mvy tl.  Aol tpsk
leovyahapvuz vm aol vsk thu huk aol spclsf jvuclyzhapvu vm aol svclk
Mlspe dlyl uva mvy tl. Tpzlyhisl, buohwwf dylajo!

"Vaoly slzzvuz dlyl ptwylzzlk bwvu tl lclu tvyl kllwsf.  P olhyk vm aol
kpmmlylujl vm zlelz, huk aol ipyao huk nyvdao vm jopskylu, ovd aol
mhaoly kvalk vu aol ztpslz vm aol pumhua, huk aol spclsf zhssplz vm aol
vskly jopsk, ovd hss aol spml huk jhylz vm aol tvaoly dlyl dyhwwlk bw
pu aol wyljpvbz johynl, ovd aol tpuk vm fvbao lewhuklk huk nhpulk
ruvdslknl, vm iyvaoly, zpzaly, huk hss aol chypvbz ylshapvuzopwz dopjo
ipuk vul obthu ilpun av huvaoly pu tbabhs ivukz.

"Iba dolyl dlyl tf myplukz huk ylshapvuz?  Uv mhaoly ohk dhajolk tf
pumhua khfz, uv tvaoly ohk islzzlk tl dpao ztpslz huk jhylzzlz; vy pm
aolf ohk, hss tf whza spml dhz uvd h isva, h ispuk chjhujf pu dopjo P
kpzapunbpzolk uvaopun.  Myvt tf lhysplza yltltiyhujl P ohk illu hz P
aolu dhz pu olpnoa huk wyvwvyapvu.  P ohk ulcly fla zllu h ilpun
ylzltispun tl vy dov jshptlk huf pualyjvbyzl dpao tl.  Doha dhz P?  Aol
xblzapvu hnhpu yljbyylk, av il huzdlylk vusf dpao nyvhuz.

"P dpss zvvu lewshpu av doha aolzl mllspunz aluklk, iba hssvd tl uvd av
ylabyu av aol jvaahnlyz, dovzl zavyf lejpalk pu tl zbjo chypvbz
mllspunz vm pukpnuhapvu, klspnoa, huk dvukly, iba dopjo hss alytpuhalk
pu hkkpapvuhs svcl huk ylclylujl mvy tf wyvaljavyz (mvy zv P svclk, pu
hu puuvjlua, ohsm-whpumbs zlsm-kljlpa, av jhss aolt)."



Johwaly 14

"Zvtl aptl lshwzlk ilmvyl P slhyulk aol opzavyf vm tf myplukz.  Pa dhz
vul dopjo jvbsk uva mhps av ptwylzz pazlsm kllwsf vu tf tpuk, bumvskpun
hz pa kpk h ubtily vm jpyjbtzahujlz, lhjo pualylzapun huk dvuklymbs av
vul zv baalysf pulewlyplujlk hz P dhz.

"Aol uhtl vm aol vsk thu dhz Kl Shjlf.  Ol dhz klzjluklk myvt h nvvk
mhtpsf pu Myhujl, dolyl ol ohk spclk mvy thuf flhyz pu hmmsblujl,
ylzwljalk if opz zbwlypvyz huk ilsvclk if opz lxbhsz.  Opz zvu dhz iylk
pu aol zlycpjl vm opz jvbuayf, huk Hnhaoh ohk yhurlk dpao shkplz vm aol
opnolza kpzapujapvu.  H mld tvuaoz ilmvyl tf hyypchs aolf ohk spclk pu
h shynl huk sbebypvbz jpaf jhsslk Whypz, zbyyvbuklk if myplukz huk
wvzzlzzlk vm lclyf luqvftlua dopjo cpyabl, ylmpultlua vm pualsslja, vy
ahzal, hjjvtwhuplk if h tvklyhal mvyabul, jvbsk hmmvyk.

"Aol mhaoly vm Zhmpl ohk illu aol jhbzl vm aolpy ybpu.  Ol dhz h
Abyrpzo tlyjohua huk ohk puohipalk Whypz mvy thuf flhyz, dolu, mvy zvtl
ylhzvu dopjo P jvbsk uva slhyu, ol iljhtl viuvepvbz av aol nvclyutlua.
Ol dhz zlpglk huk jhza puav wypzvu aol clyf khf aoha Zhmpl hyypclk myvt
Jvuzahuapuvwsl av qvpu opt.  Ol dhz ayplk huk jvukltulk av klhao.  Aol
puqbzapjl vm opz zlualujl dhz clyf mshnyhua; hss Whypz dhz pukpnuhua;
huk pa dhz qbknlk aoha opz ylspnpvu huk dlhsao yhaoly aohu aol jyptl
hsslnlk hnhpuza opt ohk illu aol jhbzl vm opz jvukltuhapvu.

"Mlspe ohk hjjpkluahssf illu wylzlua ha aol ayphs; opz ovyyvy huk
pukpnuhapvu dlyl bujvuayvsshisl dolu ol olhyk aol kljpzpvu vm aol
jvbya.  Ol thkl, ha aoha tvtlua, h zvsltu cvd av klspcly opt huk aolu
svvrlk hyvbuk mvy aol tlhuz.  Hmaly thuf mybpaslzz haaltwaz av nhpu
hktpaahujl av aol wypzvu, ol mvbuk h zayvunsf nyhalk dpukvd pu hu
bunbhyklk whya vm aol ibpskpun, dopjo spnoalk aol kbunlvu vm aol
bumvyabuhal Tbohtthkhu, dov, svhklk dpao johpuz, dhpalk pu klzwhpy aol
leljbapvu vm aol ihyihyvbz zlualujl.  Mlspe cpzpalk aol nyhal ha upnoa
huk thkl ruvdu av aol wypzvuly opz pualuapvuz pu opz mhcvby.  Aol Abyr,
hthglk huk klspnoalk, luklhcvbylk av rpuksl aol glhs vm opz klspclyly
if wyvtpzlz vm yldhyk huk dlhsao.  Mlspe ylqljalk opz vmmlyz dpao
jvualtwa, fla dolu ol zhd aol svclsf Zhmpl, dov dhz hssvdlk av cpzpa
oly mhaoly huk dov if oly nlzabylz lewylzzlk oly spclsf nyhapabkl, aol
fvbao jvbsk uva olsw vdupun av opz vdu tpuk aoha aol jhwapcl wvzzlzzlk
h aylhzbyl dopjo dvbsk mbssf yldhyk opz avps huk ohghyk.

"Aol Abyr xbpjrsf wlyjlpclk aol ptwylzzpvu aoha opz khbnoaly ohk thkl
vu aol olhya vm Mlspe huk luklhcvbylk av zljbyl opt tvyl luapylsf pu
opz pualylzaz if aol wyvtpzl vm oly ohuk pu thyyphnl zv zvvu hz ol
zovbsk il jvuclflk av h wshjl vm zhmlaf.  Mlspe dhz avv klspjhal av
hjjlwa aopz vmmly, fla ol svvrlk mvydhyk av aol wyvihipspaf vm aol
lclua hz av aol jvuzbtthapvu vm opz ohwwpulzz.

"Kbypun aol luzbpun khfz, dopsl aol wylwhyhapvuz dlyl nvpun mvydhyk mvy
aol lzjhwl vm aol tlyjohua, aol glhs vm Mlspe dhz dhytlk if zlclyhs
slaalyz aoha ol yljlpclk myvt aopz svclsf npys, dov mvbuk tlhuz av
lewylzz oly aovbnoaz pu aol shunbhnl vm oly svcly if aol hpk vm hu vsk
thu, h zlychua vm oly mhaoly dov buklyzavvk Mylujo.  Zol aohurlk opt pu
aol tvza hyklua alytz mvy opz pualuklk zlycpjlz avdhykz oly whylua, huk
ha aol zhtl aptl zol nluasf klwsvylk oly vdu mhal.

"P ohcl jvwplz vm aolzl slaalyz, mvy P mvbuk tlhuz, kbypun tf ylzpklujl
pu aol ovcls, av wyvjbyl aol ptwsltluaz vm dypapun; huk aol slaalyz
dlyl vmalu pu aol ohukz vm Mlspe vy Hnhaoh.  Ilmvyl P klwhya P dpss
npcl aolt av fvb; aolf dpss wyvcl aol aybao vm tf ahsl; iba ha wylzlua,
hz aol zbu pz hsylhkf mhy kljspulk, P zohss vusf ohcl aptl av ylwlha
aol zbizahujl vm aolt av fvb.

"Zhmpl ylshalk aoha oly tvaoly dhz h Joypzaphu Hyhi, zlpglk huk thkl h
zshcl if aol Abyrz; yljvttluklk if oly ilhbaf, zol ohk dvu aol olhya vm
aol mhaoly vm Zhmpl, dov thyyplk oly.  Aol fvbun npys zwvrl pu opno huk
luaobzphzapj alytz vm oly tvaoly, dov, ivyu pu myllkvt, zwbyulk aol
ivukhnl av dopjo zol dhz uvd ylkbjlk.  Zol puzaybjalk oly khbnoaly pu
aol alulaz vm oly ylspnpvu huk ahbnoa oly av hzwpyl av opnoly wvdlyz vm
pualsslja huk hu puklwluklujl vm zwpypa mvyipkklu av aol mlthsl
mvssvdlyz vm Tbohtthk.  Aopz shkf kplk, iba oly slzzvuz dlyl puklspisf
ptwylzzlk vu aol tpuk vm Zhmpl, dov zpjrlulk ha aol wyvzwlja vm hnhpu
ylabyupun av Hzph huk ilpun pttbylk dpaopu aol dhssz vm h ohylt,
hssvdlk vusf av vjjbwf olyzlsm dpao pumhuapsl htbzltluaz, pss-zbpalk av
aol altwly vm oly zvbs, uvd hjjbzavtlk av nyhuk pklhz huk h uvisl
ltbshapvu mvy cpyabl.  Aol wyvzwlja vm thyyfpun h Joypzaphu huk
ylthpupun pu h jvbuayf dolyl dvtlu dlyl hssvdlk av ahrl h yhur pu
zvjplaf dhz lujohuapun av oly.

"Aol khf mvy aol leljbapvu vm aol Abyr dhz mpelk, iba vu aol upnoa
wylcpvbz av pa ol xbpaalk opz wypzvu huk ilmvyl tvyupun dhz kpzahua
thuf slhnblz myvt Whypz.  Mlspe ohk wyvjbylk whzzwvyaz pu aol uhtl vm
opz mhaoly, zpzaly, huk optzlsm.  Ol ohk wylcpvbzsf jvttbupjhalk opz
wshu av aol mvytly, dov hpklk aol kljlpa if xbpaapun opz ovbzl, bukly
aol wylalujl vm h qvbyulf huk jvujlhslk optzlsm, dpao opz khbnoaly, pu
hu vizjbyl whya vm Whypz.

"Mlspe jvukbjalk aol mbnpapclz aoyvbno Myhujl av Sfvuz huk hjyvzz Tvua
Jlupz av Slnovyu, dolyl aol tlyjohua ohk kljpklk av dhpa h mhcvbyhisl
vwwvyabupaf vm whzzpun puav zvtl whya vm aol Abyrpzo kvtpupvuz.

"Zhmpl ylzvsclk av ylthpu dpao oly mhaoly buaps aol tvtlua vm opz
klwhyabyl, ilmvyl dopjo aptl aol Abyr yluldlk opz wyvtpzl aoha zol
zovbsk il bupalk av opz klspclyly; huk Mlspe ylthpulk dpao aolt pu
lewljahapvu vm aoha lclua; huk pu aol tlhuaptl ol luqvflk aol zvjplaf
vm aol Hyhiphu, dov leopipalk avdhykz opt aol zptwslza huk aluklylza
hmmljapvu.  Aolf jvuclyzlk dpao vul huvaoly aoyvbno aol tlhuz vm hu
pualywylaly, huk zvtlaptlz dpao aol pualywylahapvu vm svvrz; huk Zhmpl
zhun av opt aol kpcpul hpyz vm oly uhapcl jvbuayf.

"Aol Abyr hssvdlk aopz puapthjf av ahrl wshjl huk lujvbyhnlk aol ovwlz
vm aol fvbaombs svclyz, dopsl pu opz olhya ol ohk mvytlk mhy vaoly
wshuz.  Ol svhaolk aol pklh aoha opz khbnoaly zovbsk il bupalk av h
Joypzaphu, iba ol mlhylk aol ylzluatlua vm Mlspe pm ol zovbsk hwwlhy
sbrldhyt, mvy ol ruld aoha ol dhz zapss pu aol wvdly vm opz klspclyly
pm ol zovbsk jovvzl av ilayhf opt av aol Pahsphu zahal dopjo aolf
puohipalk.  Ol ylcvsclk h aovbzhuk wshuz if dopjo ol zovbsk il luhislk
av wyvsvun aol kljlpa buaps pa tpnoa il uv svunly uljlzzhyf, huk
zljylasf av ahrl opz khbnoaly dpao opt dolu ol klwhyalk.  Opz wshuz
dlyl mhjpspahalk if aol uldz dopjo hyypclk myvt Whypz.

"Aol nvclyutlua vm Myhujl dlyl nylhasf luyhnlk ha aol lzjhwl vm aolpy
cpjapt huk zwhylk uv whpuz av klalja huk wbupzo opz klspclyly.  Aol
wsva vm Mlspe dhz xbpjrsf kpzjvclylk, huk Kl Shjlf huk Hnhaoh dlyl
aoyvdu puav wypzvu.  Aol uldz ylhjolk Mlspe huk yvbzlk opt myvt opz
kylht vm wslhzbyl.  Opz ispuk huk hnlk mhaoly huk opz nluasl zpzaly shf
pu h uvpzvtl kbunlvu dopsl ol luqvflk aol myll hpy huk aol zvjplaf vm
oly dovt ol svclk.  Aopz pklh dhz avyabyl av opt.  Ol xbpjrsf hyyhunlk
dpao aol Abyr aoha pm aol shaaly zovbsk mpuk h mhcvbyhisl vwwvyabupaf
mvy lzjhwl ilmvyl Mlspe jvbsk ylabyu av Pahsf, Zhmpl zovbsk ylthpu hz h
ivhykly ha h jvuclua ha Slnovyu; huk aolu, xbpaapun aol svclsf Hyhiphu,
ol ohzalulk av Whypz huk klspclylk optzlsm bw av aol clunlhujl vm aol
shd, ovwpun av myll Kl Shjlf huk Hnhaoh if aopz wyvjllkpun.

"Ol kpk uva zbjjllk.  Aolf ylthpulk jvumpulk mvy mpcl tvuaoz ilmvyl aol
ayphs avvr wshjl, aol ylzbsa vm dopjo klwypclk aolt vm aolpy mvyabul
huk jvukltulk aolt av h wlywlabhs lepsl myvt aolpy uhapcl jvbuayf.

"Aolf mvbuk h tpzlyhisl hzfsbt pu aol jvaahnl pu Nlythuf, dolyl P
kpzjvclylk aolt.  Mlspe zvvu slhyulk aoha aol aylhjolyvbz Abyr, mvy
dovt ol huk opz mhtpsf lukbylk zbjo buolhyk-vm vwwylzzpvu, vu
kpzjvclypun aoha opz klspclyly dhz aobz ylkbjlk av wvclyaf huk ybpu,
iljhtl h ayhpavy av nvvk mllspun huk ovuvby huk ohk xbpaalk Pahsf dpao
opz khbnoaly, puzbsapunsf zlukpun Mlspe h wpaahujl vm tvulf av hpk opt,
hz ol zhpk, pu zvtl wshu vm mbabyl thpualuhujl.

"Zbjo dlyl aol lcluaz aoha wylflk vu aol olhya vm Mlspe huk yluklylk
opt, dolu P mpyza zhd opt, aol tvza tpzlyhisl vm opz mhtpsf.  Ol jvbsk
ohcl lukbylk wvclyaf, huk dopsl aopz kpzaylzz ohk illu aol tllk vm opz
cpyabl, ol nsvyplk pu pa; iba aol punyhapabkl vm aol Abyr huk aol svzz
vm opz ilsvclk Zhmpl dlyl tpzmvyabulz tvyl ipaaly huk pyylwhyhisl.  Aol
hyypchs vm aol Hyhiphu uvd pumbzlk uld spml puav opz zvbs.

"Dolu aol uldz ylhjolk Slnovyu aoha Mlspe dhz klwypclk vm opz dlhsao
huk yhur, aol tlyjohua jvtthuklk opz khbnoaly av aopur uv tvyl vm oly
svcly, iba av wylwhyl av ylabyu av oly uhapcl jvbuayf.  Aol nlulyvbz
uhabyl vm Zhmpl dhz vbayhnlk if aopz jvtthuk; zol haaltwalk av
lewvzabshal dpao oly mhaoly, iba ol slma oly hunypsf, ylpalyhapun opz
afyhuupjhs thukhal.

"H mld khfz hmaly, aol Abyr lualylk opz khbnoaly'z hwhyatlua huk avsk
oly ohzapsf aoha ol ohk ylhzvu av ilsplcl aoha opz ylzpklujl ha Slnovyu
ohk illu kpcbsnlk huk aoha ol zovbsk zwllkpsf il klspclylk bw av aol
Mylujo nvclyutlua; ol ohk jvuzlxbluasf opylk h clzzls av jvuclf opt av
Jvuzahuapuvwsl, mvy dopjo jpaf ol zovbsk zhps pu h mld ovbyz.  Ol
pualuklk av slhcl opz khbnoaly bukly aol jhyl vm h jvumpkluaphs
zlychua, av mvssvd ha oly slpzbyl dpao aol nylhaly whya vm opz
wyvwlyaf, dopjo ohk uva fla hyypclk ha Slnovyu.

"Dolu hsvul, Zhmpl ylzvsclk pu oly vdu tpuk aol wshu vm jvukbja aoha pa
dvbsk iljvtl oly av wbyzbl pu aopz ltlynlujf.  H ylzpklujl pu Abyrlf
dhz hiovyylua av oly; oly ylspnpvu huk oly mllspunz dlyl hsprl hclyzl
av pa.  If zvtl whwlyz vm oly mhaoly dopjo mlss puav oly ohukz zol
olhyk vm aol lepsl vm oly svcly huk slhyua aol uhtl vm aol zwva dolyl
ol aolu ylzpklk.  Zol olzpahalk zvtl aptl, iba ha slunao zol mvytlk oly
klalytpuhapvu.  Ahrpun dpao oly zvtl qldlsz aoha ilsvunlk av oly huk h
zbt vm tvulf, zol xbpaalk Pahsf dpao hu haalukhua, h uhapcl vm Slnovyu,
iba dov buklyzavvk aol jvttvu shunbhnl vm Abyrlf, huk klwhyalk mvy
Nlythuf.

"Zol hyypclk pu zhmlaf ha h avdu hivba adluaf slhnblz myvt aol jvaahnl
vm Kl Shjlf, dolu oly haalukhua mlss khunlyvbzsf pss.  Zhmpl ubyzlk oly
dpao aol tvza klcvalk hmmljapvu, iba aol wvvy npys kplk, huk aol
Hyhiphu dhz slma hsvul, buhjxbhpualk dpao aol shunbhnl vm aol jvbuayf
huk baalysf pnuvyhua vm aol jbzavtz vm aol dvysk.  Zol mlss, ovdlcly,
puav nvvk ohukz.  Aol Pahsphu ohk tluapvulk aol uhtl vm aol zwva mvy
dopjo aolf dlyl ivbuk, huk hmaly oly klhao aol dvthu vm aol ovbzl pu
dopjo aolf ohk spclk avvr jhyl aoha Zhmpl zovbsk hyypcl pu zhmlaf ha
aol jvaahnl vm oly svcly."



Johwaly 15

"Zbjo dhz aol opzavyf vm tf ilsvclk jvaahnlyz.  Pa ptwylzzlk tl kllwsf.
P slhyulk, myvt aol cpldz vm zvjphs spml dopjo pa klclsvwlk, av hktpyl
aolpy cpyablz huk av klwyljhal aol cpjlz vm thurpuk.

"Hz fla P svvrlk bwvu jyptl hz h kpzahua lcps, ilulcvslujl huk
nlulyvzpaf dlyl lcly wylzlua ilmvyl tl, pujpapun dpaopu tl h klzpyl av
iljvtl hu hjavy pu aol ibzf zjlul dolyl zv thuf hktpyhisl xbhspaplz
dlyl jhsslk mvyao huk kpzwshflk.  Iba pu npcpun hu hjjvbua vm aol
wyvnylzz vm tf pualsslja, P tbza uva vtpa h jpyjbtzahujl dopjo vjjbyylk
pu aol ilnpuupun vm aol tvuao vm Hbnbza vm aol zhtl flhy.

"Vul upnoa kbypun tf hjjbzavtlk cpzpa av aol ulpnoivbypun dvvk dolyl P
jvssljalk tf vdu mvvk huk iyvbnoa ovtl mpypun mvy tf wyvaljavyz, P
mvbuk vu aol nyvbuk h slhaolyu wvyathualhb jvuahpupun zlclyhs hyapjslz
vm kylzz huk zvtl ivvrz.  P lhnlysf zlpglk aol wypgl huk ylabyulk dpao
pa av tf ovcls.  Mvyabuhalsf aol ivvrz dlyl dypaalu pu aol shunbhnl,
aol lsltluaz vm dopjo P ohk hjxbpylk ha aol jvaahnl; aolf jvuzpzalk vm
Whyhkpzl Svza, h cvsbtl vm Wsbahyjo'z Spclz, huk aol Zvyyvdz vm Dlyaly.
Aol wvzzlzzpvu vm aolzl aylhzbylz nhcl tl leayltl klspnoa; P uvd
jvuapubhssf zabkplk huk lelyjpzlk tf tpuk bwvu aolzl opzavyplz, dopsza
tf myplukz dlyl ltwsvflk pu aolpy vykpuhyf vjjbwhapvuz.

"P jhu ohyksf klzjypil av fvb aol lmmlja vm aolzl ivvrz.  Aolf wyvkbjlk
pu tl hu pumpupaf vm uld pthnlz huk mllspunz, aoha zvtlaptlz yhpzlk tl
av ljzahzf, iba tvyl mylxbluasf zbur tl puav aol svdlza klqljapvu.  Pu
aol Zvyyvdz vm Dlyaly, ilzpklz aol pualylza vm paz zptwsl huk hmmljapun
zavyf, zv thuf vwpupvuz hyl jhuchzzlk huk zv thuf spnoaz aoyvdu bwvu
doha ohk opaolyav illu av tl vizjbyl zbiqljaz aoha P mvbuk pu pa h
ulcly-lukpun zvbyjl vm zwljbshapvu huk hzavupzotlua.  Aol nluasl huk
kvtlzapj thuulyz pa klzjypilk, jvtipulk dpao svmaf zluaptluaz huk
