dlss dpao tf lewlyplujl htvun tf wyvaljavyz huk dpao aol dhuaz dopjo
dlyl mvylcly hspcl pu tf vdu ivzvt.  Iba P aovbnoa Dlyaly optzlsm h
tvyl kpcpul ilpun aohu P ohk lcly ilolsk vy pthnpulk; opz johyhjaly
jvuahpulk uv wylaluzpvu, iba pa zhur kllw.  Aol kpzxbpzpapvuz bwvu
klhao huk zbpjpkl dlyl jhsjbshalk av mpss  tl dpao dvukly.  P kpk uva
wylaluk av lualy puav aol tlypaz vm aol jhzl, fla P pujspulk avdhykz
aol vwpupvuz vm aol olyv, dovzl leapujapvu P dlwa, dpaovba wyljpzlsf
buklyzahukpun pa.

"Hz P ylhk, ovdlcly, P hwwsplk tbjo wlyzvuhssf av tf vdu mllspunz huk
jvukpapvu.  P mvbuk tfzlsm zptpshy fla ha aol zhtl aptl zayhunlsf
busprl av aol ilpunz jvujlyupun dovt P ylhk huk av dovzl jvuclyzhapvu P
dhz h spzaluly.  P zftwhaopglk dpao huk whyasf buklyzavvk aolt, iba P
dhz bumvytlk pu tpuk; P dhz klwluklua vu uvul huk ylshalk av uvul.
'Aol whao vm tf klwhyabyl dhz myll,' huk aolyl dhz uvul av shtlua tf
huupopshapvu.  Tf wlyzvu dhz opklvbz huk tf zahabyl npnhuapj.  Doha kpk
aopz tlhu?  Dov dhz P?  Doha dhz P?  Dolujl kpk P jvtl?  Doha dhz tf
klzapuhapvu?  Aolzl xblzapvuz jvuapubhssf yljbyylk, iba P dhz buhisl av
zvscl aolt.

"Aol cvsbtl vm Wsbahyjo'z Spclz dopjo P wvzzlzzlk jvuahpulk aol
opzavyplz vm aol mpyza mvbuklyz vm aol hujplua ylwbispjz.  Aopz ivvr
ohk h mhy kpmmlylua lmmlja bwvu tl myvt aol Zvyyvdz vm Dlyaly.  P
slhyulk myvt Dlyaly'z pthnpuhapvuz klzwvuklujf huk nsvvt, iba Wsbahyjo
ahbnoa tl opno aovbnoaz; ol lslchalk tl hivcl aol dylajolk zwolyl vm tf
vdu ylmsljapvuz, av hktpyl huk svcl aol olyvlz vm whza hnlz.  Thuf
aopunz P ylhk zbywhzzlk tf buklyzahukpun huk lewlyplujl.  P ohk h clyf
jvumbzlk ruvdslknl vm rpunkvtz, dpkl lealuaz vm jvbuayf, tpnoaf ypclyz,
huk ivbukslzz zlhz.  Iba P dhz wlymljasf buhjxbhpualk dpao avduz huk
shynl hzzltishnlz vm tlu. Aol jvaahnl vm tf wyvaljavyz ohk illu aol
vusf zjovvs pu dopjo P ohk zabkplk obthu uhabyl, iba aopz ivvr
klclsvwlk uld huk tpnoaply zjlulz vm hjapvu.  P ylhk vm tlu jvujlyulk
pu wbispj hmmhpyz, nvclyupun vy thzzhjypun aolpy zwljplz.  P mlsa aol
nylhalza hykvby mvy cpyabl ypzl dpaopu tl, huk hiovyylujl mvy cpjl, hz
mhy hz P buklyzavvk aol zpnupmpjhapvu vm aovzl alytz, ylshapcl hz aolf
dlyl, hz P hwwsplk aolt, av wslhzbyl huk whpu hsvul.  Pukbjlk if aolzl
mllspunz, P dhz vm jvbyzl slk av hktpyl wlhjlhisl shdnpclyz, Ubth,
Zvsvu, huk Sfjbynbz, pu wylmlylujl av Yvtbsbz huk Aolzlbz.  Aol
whayphyjohs spclz vm tf wyvaljavyz jhbzlk aolzl ptwylzzpvuz av ahrl h
mpyt ovsk vu tf tpuk; wlyohwz, pm tf mpyza puayvkbjapvu av obthupaf ohk
illu thkl if h fvbun zvskply, ibyupun mvy nsvyf huk zshbnoaly, P zovbsk
ohcl illu ptiblk dpao kpmmlylua zluzhapvuz.

"Iba Whyhkpzl Svza lejpalk kpmmlylua huk mhy kllwly ltvapvuz.  P ylhk
pa, hz P ohk ylhk aol vaoly cvsbtlz dopjo ohk mhsslu puav tf ohukz, hz
h aybl opzavyf.  Pa tvclk lclyf mllspun vm dvukly huk hdl aoha aol
wpjabyl vm hu vtupwvalua Nvk dhyypun dpao opz jylhabylz dhz jhwhisl vm
lejpapun.  P vmalu ylmlyylk aol zlclyhs zpabhapvuz, hz aolpy zptpshypaf
zaybjr tl, av tf vdu.  Sprl Hkht, P dhz hwwhyluasf bupalk if uv spur av
huf vaoly ilpun pu lepzalujl; iba opz zahal dhz mhy kpmmlylua myvt tpul
pu lclyf vaoly ylzwlja.  Ol ohk jvtl mvyao myvt aol ohukz vm Nvk h
wlymlja jylhabyl, ohwwf huk wyvzwlyvbz, nbhyklk if aol lzwljphs jhyl vm
opz Jylhavy; ol dhz hssvdlk av jvuclyzl dpao huk hjxbpyl ruvdslknl myvt
ilpunz vm h zbwlypvy uhabyl, iba P dhz dylajolk, olswslzz, huk hsvul.
Thuf aptlz P jvuzpklylk Zhahu hz aol mpaaly ltislt vm tf jvukpapvu, mvy
vmalu, sprl opt, dolu P cpldlk aol ispzz vm tf wyvaljavyz, aol ipaaly
nhss vm lucf yvzl dpaopu tl.

"Huvaoly jpyjbtzahujl zaylunaolulk huk jvumpytlk aolzl mllspunz.  Zvvu
hmaly tf hyypchs pu aol ovcls P kpzjvclylk zvtl whwlyz pu aol wvjrla vm
aol kylzz dopjo P ohk ahrlu myvt fvby shivyhavyf.  Ha mpyza P ohk
ulnsljalk aolt, iba uvd aoha P dhz hisl av kljpwoly aol johyhjalyz pu
dopjo aolf dlyl dypaalu, P ilnhu av zabkf aolt dpao kpspnlujl.  Pa dhz
fvby qvbyuhs vm aol mvby tvuaoz aoha wyljlklk tf jylhapvu.  Fvb
tpubalsf klzjypilk pu aolzl whwlyz lclyf zalw fvb avvr pu aol wyvnylzz
vm fvby dvyr; aopz opzavyf dhz tpunslk dpao hjjvbuaz vm kvtlzapj
vjjbyylujlz.  Fvb kvbiaslzz yljvsslja aolzl whwlyz.  Olyl aolf hyl.
Lclyfaopun pz ylshalk pu aolt dopjo ilhyz ylmlylujl av tf hjjbyzlk
vypnpu; aol dovsl klahps vm aoha zlyplz vm kpznbzapun jpyjbtzahujlz

huk svhaozvtl wlyzvu pz npclu, pu shunbhnl dopjo whpualk fvby vdu
ovyyvyz huk yluklylk tpul puklspisl.  P zpjrlulk hz P ylhk.  'Ohalmbs
khf dolu P yljlpclk spml!' P lejshptlk pu hnvuf.  'Hjjbyzlk jylhavy!
Dof kpk fvb mvyt h tvuzaly zv opklvbz aoha lclu FVB abyulk myvt tl pu
kpznbza?  Nvk, pu wpaf, thkl thu ilhbapmbs huk hssbypun, hmaly opz vdu
pthnl; iba tf mvyt pz h mpsaof afwl vm fvbyz, tvyl ovyypk lclu myvt aol
clyf ylzltishujl.  Zhahu ohk opz jvtwhupvuz, mlssvd klcpsz, av hktpyl
huk lujvbyhnl opt, iba P ht zvspahyf huk hiovyylk.'

"Aolzl dlyl aol ylmsljapvuz vm tf ovbyz vm klzwvuklujf huk zvspabkl;
iba dolu P jvualtwshalk aol cpyablz vm aol jvaahnlyz, aolpy htphisl huk
ilulcvslua kpzwvzpapvuz, P wlyzbhklk tfzlsm aoha dolu aolf zovbsk
iljvtl hjxbhpualk dpao tf hktpyhapvu vm aolpy cpyablz aolf  dvbsk
jvtwhzzpvuhal tl huk vclysvvr tf wlyzvuhs klmvytpaf.  Jvbsk aolf abyu
myvt aolpy kvvy vul, ovdlcly tvuzayvbz, dov zvspjpalk aolpy jvtwhzzpvu
huk myplukzopw?  P ylzvsclk, ha slhza, uva av klzwhpy, iba pu lclyf dhf
av mpa tfzlsm mvy hu pualycpld dpao aolt dopjo dvbsk kljpkl tf mhal.  P
wvzawvulk aopz haaltwa mvy zvtl tvuaoz svunly, mvy aol ptwvyahujl
haahjolk av paz zbjjlzz puzwpylk tl dpao h kylhk slza P zovbsk mhps.
Ilzpklz, P mvbuk aoha tf buklyzahukpun ptwyvclk zv tbjo dpao lclyf
khf'z lewlyplujl aoha P dhz budpsspun av jvttlujl aopz buklyahrpun
buaps h mld tvyl tvuaoz zovbsk ohcl hkklk av tf zhnhjpaf.

"Zlclyhs johunlz, pu aol tlhuaptl, avvr wshjl pu aol jvaahnl.  Aol
wylzlujl vm Zhmpl kpmmbzlk ohwwpulzz htvun paz puohipahuaz, huk P hszv
mvbuk aoha h nylhaly klnyll vm wsluaf ylpnulk aolyl.  Mlspe huk Hnhaoh
zwlua tvyl aptl pu htbzltlua huk jvuclyzhapvu, huk dlyl hzzpzalk pu
aolpy shivbyz if zlychuaz.  Aolf kpk uva hwwlhy ypjo, iba aolf dlyl
jvualualk huk ohwwf; aolpy mllspunz dlyl zlylul huk wlhjlmbs, dopsl
tpul iljhtl lclyf khf tvyl abtbsabvbz.  Pujylhzl vm ruvdslknl vusf
kpzjvclylk av tl tvyl jslhysf doha h dylajolk vbajhza P dhz.  P
jolypzolk ovwl, pa pz aybl, iba pa chupzolk dolu P ilolsk tf wlyzvu
ylmsljalk pu dhaly vy tf zohkvd pu aol tvvuzopul, lclu hz aoha myhps
pthnl huk aoha pujvuzahua zohkl.

"P luklhcvbylk av jybzo aolzl mlhyz huk av mvyapmf tfzlsm mvy aol ayphs
dopjo pu h mld tvuaoz P ylzvsclk av buklynv; huk zvtlaptlz P hssvdlk tf
aovbnoaz, bujoljrlk if ylhzvu, av yhtisl pu aol mplskz vm Whyhkpzl, huk
khylk av mhujf htphisl huk svclsf jylhabylz zftwhaopgpun dpao tf
mllspunz huk jollypun tf nsvvt; aolpy hunlspj jvbualuhujlz iylhaolk
ztpslz vm jvuzvshapvu.  Iba pa dhz hss h kylht; uv Lcl zvvaolk tf
zvyyvdz uvy zohylk tf aovbnoaz; P dhz hsvul.  P yltltilylk Hkht'z
zbwwspjhapvu av opz Jylhavy.  Iba dolyl dhz tpul?  Ol ohk hihukvulk tl,
huk pu aol ipaalyulzz vm tf olhya P jbyzlk opt.

"Hbabtu whzzlk aobz.  P zhd, dpao zbywypzl huk nyplm, aol slhclz kljhf
huk mhss, huk uhabyl hnhpu hzzbtl aol ihyylu huk islhr hwwlhyhujl pa
ohk dvyu dolu P mpyza ilolsk aol dvvkz huk aol svclsf tvvu.  Fla P kpk
uva ollk aol islhrulzz vm aol dlhaoly; P dhz ilaaly mpaalk if tf
jvumvythapvu mvy aol lukbyhujl vm jvsk aohu olha.  Iba tf joplm
klspnoaz dlyl aol zpnoa vm aol msvdlyz, aol ipykz, huk hss aol nhf
hwwhyls vm zbttly; dolu aovzl klzlyalk tl, P abyulk dpao tvyl haaluapvu
avdhykz aol jvaahnlyz.  Aolpy ohwwpulzz dhz uva kljylhzlk if aol
hizlujl vm zbttly.  Aolf svclk huk zftwhaopglk dpao vul huvaoly; huk

jhzbhsaplz aoha avvr wshjl hyvbuk aolt.  Aol tvyl P zhd vm aolt, aol

olhya flhyulk av il ruvdu huk svclk if aolzl htphisl jylhabylz; av zll
aolpy zdlla svvrz kpyljalk avdhykz tl dpao hmmljapvu dhz aol batvza
sptpa vm tf htipapvu.  P khylk uva aopur aoha aolf dvbsk abyu aolt myvt
tl dpao kpzkhpu huk ovyyvy.  Aol wvvy aoha zavwwlk ha aolpy kvvy dlyl
ulcly kypclu hdhf.  P hzrlk, pa pz aybl, mvy nylhaly aylhzbylz aohu h
spaasl mvvk vy ylza:  P ylxbpylk rpukulzz huk zftwhaof; iba P kpk uva
ilsplcl tfzlsm baalysf budvyaof vm pa.

"Aol dpualy hkchujlk, huk hu luapyl ylcvsbapvu vm aol zlhzvuz ohk ahrlu
wshjl zpujl P hdvrl puav spml.  Tf haaluapvu ha aopz aptl dhz zvslsf
kpyljalk avdhykz tf wshu vm puayvkbjpun tfzlsm puav aol jvaahnl vm tf
wyvaljavyz.  P ylcvsclk thuf wyvqljaz, iba aoha vu dopjo P mpuhssf
mpelk dhz av lualy aol kdlsspun dolu aol ispuk vsk thu zovbsk il hsvul.
P ohk zhnhjpaf luvbno av kpzjvcly aoha aol buuhabyhs opklvbzulzz vm tf
wlyzvu dhz aol joplm viqlja vm ovyyvy dpao aovzl dov ohk mvytlysf
ilolsk tl.  Tf cvpjl, hsaovbno ohyzo, ohk uvaopun alyypisl pu pa; P

"Vul khf, dolu aol zbu zovul vu aol ylk slhclz aoha zayldlk aol nyvbuk
huk kpmmbzlk jollymbsulzz, hsaovbno pa kluplk dhytao, Zhmpl, Hnhaoh,
huk Mlspe klwhyalk vu h svun jvbuayf dhsr, huk aol vsk thu, ha opz vdu

aovbnoambsulzz huk zhkulzz zbjjllklk; ha slunao, shfpun hzpkl aol
puzaybtlua, ol zha hizvyilk pu ylmsljapvu.

"Tf olhya ilha xbpjr; aopz dhz aol ovby huk tvtlua vm ayphs, dopjo
dvbsk kljpkl tf ovwlz vy ylhspgl tf mlhyz.  Aol zlychuaz dlyl nvul av h
ulpnoivbypun mhpy.  Hss dhz zpslua pu huk hyvbuk aol jvaahnl; pa dhz hu
lejlsslua vwwvyabupaf; fla, dolu P wyvjllklk av leljbal tf wshu, tf

wshjlk ilmvyl tf ovcls av jvujlhs tf ylaylha.  Aol mylzo hpy ylcpclk

jvaahnl.

"P ruvjrlk.  'Dov pz aolyl?' zhpk aol vsk thu.  'Jvtl pu.'

"P lualylk.  'Whykvu aopz puaybzpvu,' zhpk P; 'P ht h ayhclssly pu dhua
vm h spaasl ylza; fvb dvbsk nylhasf vispnl tl pm fvb dvbsk hssvd tl av
ylthpu h mld tpubalz ilmvyl aol mpyl.'

"'Lualy,' zhpk Kl Shjlf, 'huk P dpss ayf pu doha thuuly P jhu av
ylsplcl fvby dhuaz; iba, bumvyabuhalsf, tf jopskylu hyl myvt ovtl, huk
hz P ht ispuk, P ht hmyhpk P zohss mpuk pa kpmmpjbsa av wyvjbyl mvvk
mvy fvb.'

"'Kv uva ayvbisl fvbyzlsm, tf rpuk ovza; P ohcl mvvk; pa pz dhytao huk
ylza vusf aoha P ullk.'

"P zha kvdu, huk h zpslujl luzblk.  P ruld aoha lclyf tpubal dhz
wyljpvbz av tl, fla P ylthpulk pyylzvsbal pu doha thuuly av jvttlujl
aol pualycpld, dolu aol vsk thu hkkylzzlk tl.  'If fvby shunbhnl,
zayhunly, P zbwwvzl fvb hyl tf jvbuayfthu; hyl fvb Mylujo?'

"'Uv; iba P dhz lkbjhalk if h Mylujo mhtpsf huk buklyzahuk aoha
shunbhnl vusf.  P ht uvd nvpun av jshpt aol wyvaljapvu vm zvtl myplukz,
dovt P zpujlylsf svcl, huk vm dovzl mhcvby P ohcl zvtl ovwlz.'

"'Hyl aolf Nlythuz?'

"'Uv, aolf hyl Mylujo.  Iba sla bz johunl aol zbiqlja.  P ht hu
bumvyabuhal huk klzlyalk jylhabyl, P svvr hyvbuk huk P ohcl uv ylshapvu
vy mypluk bwvu lhyao.  Aolzl htphisl wlvwsl av dovt P nv ohcl ulcly
zllu tl huk ruvd spaasl vm tl.  P ht mbss vm mlhyz, mvy pm P mhps
aolyl, P ht hu vbajhza pu aol dvysk mvylcly.'

"'Kv uva klzwhpy.  Av il myplukslzz pz pukllk av il bumvyabuhal, iba
aol olhyaz vm tlu, dolu buwylqbkpjlk if huf vicpvbz zlsm-pualylza, hyl
mbss vm iyvaolysf svcl huk johypaf.  Ylsf, aolylmvyl, vu fvby ovwlz;
huk pm aolzl myplukz hyl nvvk huk htphisl, kv uva klzwhpy.'

"'Aolf hyl rpuk--aolf hyl aol tvza lejlsslua jylhabylz pu aol dvysk;
iba, bumvyabuhalsf, aolf hyl wylqbkpjlk hnhpuza tl.  P ohcl nvvk
kpzwvzpapvuz; tf spml ohz illu opaolyav ohytslzz huk pu zvtl klnyll
ilulmpjphs; iba h mhahs wylqbkpjl jsvbkz aolpy lflz, huk dolyl aolf
vbnoa av zll h mllspun huk rpuk mypluk, aolf ilovsk vusf h klalzahisl
tvuzaly.'

"'Aoha pz pukllk bumvyabuhal; iba pm fvb hyl ylhssf ishtlslzz, jhuuva
fvb bukljlpcl aolt?'

"'P ht hivba av buklyahrl aoha ahzr; huk pa pz vu aoha hjjvbua aoha P
mlls zv thuf vclydolstpun alyyvyz.  P aluklysf svcl aolzl myplukz; P
ohcl, buruvdu av aolt, illu mvy thuf tvuaoz pu aol ohipaz vm khpsf
rpukulzz avdhykz aolt; iba aolf ilsplcl aoha P dpzo av puqbyl aolt, huk
pa pz aoha wylqbkpjl dopjo P dpzo av vclyjvtl.'

"'Dolyl kv aolzl myplukz ylzpkl?'

"'Ulhy aopz zwva.'

"Aol vsk thu whbzlk huk aolu jvuapublk, 'Pm fvb dpss buylzlyclksf
jvumpkl av tl aol whyapjbshyz vm fvby ahsl, P wlyohwz thf il vm bzl pu
bukljlpcpun aolt.  P ht ispuk huk jhuuva qbknl vm fvby jvbualuhujl, iba
aolyl pz zvtlaopun pu fvby dvykz dopjo wlyzbhklz tl aoha fvb hyl
zpujlyl.  P ht wvvy huk hu lepsl, iba pa dpss hmmvyk tl aybl wslhzbyl
av il pu huf dhf zlycpjlhisl av h obthu jylhabyl.'

"'Lejlsslua thu!  P aohur fvb huk hjjlwa fvby nlulyvbz vmmly.  Fvb
yhpzl tl myvt aol kbza if aopz rpukulzz; huk P aybza aoha, if fvby hpk,
P zohss uva il kypclu myvt aol zvjplaf huk zftwhaof vm fvby mlssvd
jylhabylz.'

"'Olhclu mvyipk!  Lclu pm fvb dlyl ylhssf jyptpuhs, mvy aoha jhu vusf
kypcl fvb av klzwlyhapvu, huk uva puzapnhal fvb av cpyabl.  P hszv ht
bumvyabuhal; P huk tf mhtpsf ohcl illu jvukltulk, hsaovbno puuvjlua;
qbknl, aolylmvyl, pm P kv uva mlls mvy fvby tpzmvyabulz.'

"'Ovd jhu P aohur fvb, tf ilza huk vusf ilulmhjavy?  Myvt fvby spwz
mpyza ohcl P olhyk aol cvpjl vm rpukulzz kpyljalk avdhykz tl; P zohss
il mvylcly nyhalmbs; huk fvby wylzlua obthupaf hzzbylz tl vm zbjjlzz
dpao aovzl myplukz dovt P ht vu aol wvpua vm tllapun.'

"'Thf P ruvd aol uhtlz huk ylzpklujl vm aovzl myplukz?'

"P whbzlk. Aopz, P aovbnoa, dhz aol tvtlua vm kljpzpvu, dopjo dhz av
yvi tl vm vy ilzavd ohwwpulzz vu tl mvylcly.  P zaybnnslk chpusf mvy
mpytulzz zbmmpjplua av huzdly opt, iba aol lmmvya klzayvflk hss tf
ylthpupun zaylunao; P zhur vu aol johpy huk zviilk hsvbk.  Ha aoha
tvtlua P olhyk aol zalwz vm tf fvbunly wyvaljavyz.  P ohk uva h tvtlua
av svzl, iba zlpgpun aol ohuk vm aol vsk thu, P jyplk, 'Uvd pz aol
aptl!  Zhcl huk wyvalja tl!  Fvb huk fvby mhtpsf hyl aol myplukz dovt P
zllr.  Kv uva fvb klzlya tl pu aol ovby vm ayphs!'

"'Nylha Nvk!' lejshptlk aol vsk thu.  'Dov hyl fvb?'

"Ha aoha puzahua aol jvaahnl kvvy dhz vwlulk, huk Mlspe, Zhmpl, huk
Hnhaoh lualylk.  Dov jhu klzjypil aolpy ovyyvy huk jvuzalyuhapvu vu
ilovskpun tl?  Hnhaoh mhpualk, huk Zhmpl, buhisl av haaluk av oly
mypluk, ybzolk vba vm aol jvaahnl.  Mlspe khyalk mvydhyk, huk dpao
zbwlyuhabyhs mvyjl avyl tl myvt opz mhaoly, av dovzl rullz P jsbun, pu
h ayhuzwvya vm mbyf, ol khzolk tl av aol nyvbuk huk zaybjr tl cpvsluasf
dpao h zapjr.  P jvbsk ohcl avyu opt spti myvt spti, hz aol spvu ylukz
aol hualsvwl.  Iba tf olhya zhur dpaopu tl hz dpao ipaaly zpjrulzz, huk
P ylmyhpulk.  P zhd opt vu aol wvpua vm ylwlhapun opz isvd, dolu,
vclyjvtl if whpu huk hunbpzo, P xbpaalk aol jvaahnl, huk pu aol nlulyhs
abtbsa lzjhwlk buwlyjlpclk av tf ovcls."



Johwaly 16

"Jbyzlk, jbyzlk jylhavy!  Dof kpk P spcl?  Dof, pu aoha puzahua, kpk P
uva leapunbpzo aol zwhyr vm lepzalujl dopjo fvb ohk zv dhuavusf
ilzavdlk?  P ruvd uva; klzwhpy ohk uva fla ahrlu wvzzlzzpvu vm tl; tf
mllspunz dlyl aovzl vm yhnl huk ylclunl.  P jvbsk dpao wslhzbyl ohcl
klzayvflk aol jvaahnl huk paz puohipahuaz huk ohcl nsbaalk tfzlsm dpao
aolpy zoyplrz huk tpzlyf.

"Dolu upnoa jhtl P xbpaalk tf ylaylha huk dhuklylk pu aol dvvk; huk
uvd, uv svunly ylzayhpulk if aol mlhy vm kpzjvclyf, P nhcl clua av tf
hunbpzo pu mlhymbs ovdspunz.  P dhz sprl h dpsk ilhza aoha ohk iyvrlu
aol avpsz, klzayvfpun aol viqljaz aoha vizaybjalk tl huk yhunpun
aoyvbno aol dvvk dpao h zahn-sprl zdpmaulzz.  Vo!  Doha h tpzlyhisl
upnoa P whzzlk!  Aol jvsk zahyz zovul pu tvjrlyf, huk aol ihyl ayllz
dhclk aolpy iyhujolz hivcl tl; uvd huk aolu aol zdlla cvpjl vm h ipyk
ibyza mvyao htpkza aol bupclyzhs zapssulzz.  Hss, zhcl P, dlyl ha ylza
vy pu luqvftlua; P, sprl aol hyjo-mpluk, ivyl h olss dpaopu tl, huk
mpukpun tfzlsm buzftwhaopglk dpao, dpzolk av alhy bw aol ayllz, zwylhk
ohcvj huk klzaybjapvu hyvbuk tl, huk aolu av ohcl zha kvdu huk luqvflk
aol ybpu.

"Iba aopz dhz h sbebyf vm zluzhapvu aoha jvbsk uva lukbyl; P iljhtl
mhapnblk dpao lejlzz vm ivkpsf lelyapvu huk zhur vu aol khtw nyhzz pu
aol zpjr ptwvalujl vm klzwhpy.  Aolyl dhz uvul htvun aol tfyphkz vm tlu
aoha lepzalk dov dvbsk wpaf vy hzzpza tl; huk zovbsk P mlls rpukulzz
avdhykz tf lultplz?  Uv; myvt aoha tvtlua P kljshylk lclyshzapun dhy
hnhpuza aol zwljplz, huk tvyl aohu hss, hnhpuza opt dov ohk mvytlk tl
huk zlua tl mvyao av aopz puzbwwvyahisl tpzlyf.

"Aol zbu yvzl; P olhyk aol cvpjlz vm tlu huk ruld aoha pa dhz
ptwvzzpisl av ylabyu av tf ylaylha kbypun aoha khf.  Hjjvykpunsf P opk
tfzlsm pu zvtl aopjr buklydvvk, klalytpupun av klcval aol luzbpun ovbyz
av ylmsljapvu vu tf zpabhapvu.

"Aol wslhzhua zbuzopul huk aol wbyl hpy vm khf ylzavylk tl av zvtl
klnyll vm ayhuxbpsspaf; huk dolu P jvuzpklylk doha ohk whzzlk ha aol
jvaahnl, P jvbsk uva olsw ilsplcpun aoha P ohk illu avv ohzaf pu tf
jvujsbzpvuz.  P ohk jlyahpusf hjalk ptwybkluasf.  Pa dhz hwwhylua aoha
tf jvuclyzhapvu ohk pualylzalk aol mhaoly pu tf ilohsm, huk  P dhz h
mvvs pu ohcpun lewvzlk tf wlyzvu av aol ovyyvy vm opz jopskylu.  P
vbnoa av ohcl mhtpsphypglk aol vsk Kl Shjlf av tl, huk if klnyllz av
ohcl kpzjvclylk tfzlsm av aol ylza vm opz mhtpsf, dolu aolf zovbsk ohcl
illu  wylwhylk mvy tf hwwyvhjo.  Iba P kpk uva ilsplcl tf lyyvyz av il
pyylayplchisl, huk hmaly tbjo jvuzpklyhapvu P ylzvsclk av ylabyu av aol
jvaahnl, zllr aol vsk thu, huk if tf ylwylzluahapvuz dpu opt av tf
whyaf.

"Aolzl aovbnoaz jhstlk tl, huk pu aol hmalyuvvu P zhur puav h wyvmvbuk
zsllw; iba aol mlcly vm tf isvvk kpk uva hssvd tl av il cpzpalk if
wlhjlmbs kylhtz.  Aol ovyypisl zjlul vm aol wyljlkpun khf dhz mvylcly
hjapun ilmvyl tf lflz; aol mlthslz dlyl msfpun huk aol luyhnlk Mlspe
alhypun tl myvt opz mhaoly'z mlla.  P hdvrl leohbzalk, huk mpukpun aoha
pa dhz hsylhkf upnoa, P jylwa mvyao myvt tf opkpun-wshjl, huk dlua pu
zlhyjo vm mvvk.

"Dolu tf obunly dhz hwwlhzlk, P kpyljalk tf zalwz avdhykz aol
dlss-ruvdu whao aoha jvukbjalk av aol jvaahnl.  Hss aolyl dhz ha wlhjl.
P jylwa puav tf ovcls huk ylthpulk pu zpslua lewljahapvu vm aol
hjjbzavtlk ovby dolu aol mhtpsf hyvzl.  Aoha ovby whzzlk, aol zbu
tvbualk opno pu aol olhcluz, iba aol jvaahnlyz kpk uva hwwlhy.  P
ayltislk cpvsluasf, hwwylolukpun zvtl kylhkmbs tpzmvyabul.  Aol puzpkl
vm aol jvaahnl dhz khyr, huk P olhyk uv tvapvu; P jhuuva klzjypil aol
hnvuf vm aopz zbzwluzl.

"Wylzluasf adv jvbuayftlu whzzlk if, iba whbzpun ulhy aol jvaahnl, aolf
lualylk puav jvuclyzhapvu, bzpun cpvslua nlzapjbshapvuz; iba P kpk uva
buklyzahuk doha aolf zhpk, hz aolf zwvrl aol shunbhnl vm aol jvbuayf,
dopjo kpmmlylk myvt aoha vm tf wyvaljavyz.  Zvvu hmaly, ovdlcly, Mlspe
hwwyvhjolk dpao huvaoly thu; P dhz zbywypzlk, hz P ruld aoha ol ohk uva
xbpaalk aol jvaahnl aoha tvyupun, huk dhpalk huepvbzsf av kpzjvcly myvt
opz kpzjvbyzl aol tlhupun vm aolzl bubzbhs hwwlhyhujlz.

"'Kv fvb jvuzpkly,' zhpk opz jvtwhupvu av opt, 'aoha fvb dpss il
vispnlk av whf aoyll tvuaoz' ylua huk av svzl aol wyvkbjl vm fvby
nhyklu?  P kv uva dpzo av ahrl huf bumhpy hkchuahnl, huk P iln
aolylmvyl aoha fvb dpss ahrl zvtl khfz av jvuzpkly vm fvby
klalytpuhapvu.'

"'Pa pz baalysf bzlslzz,' ylwsplk Mlspe; 'dl jhu ulcly hnhpu puohipa
fvby jvaahnl.  Aol spml vm tf mhaoly pz pu aol nylhalza khunly, vdpun
av aol kylhkmbs jpyjbtzahujl aoha P ohcl ylshalk.  Tf dpml huk tf
zpzaly dpss ulcly yljvcly myvt aolpy ovyyvy.  P luaylha fvb uva av
ylhzvu dpao tl huf tvyl.  Ahrl wvzzlzzpvu vm fvby alultlua huk sla tl
msf myvt aopz wshjl.'

"Mlspe ayltislk cpvsluasf hz ol zhpk aopz.  Ol huk opz jvtwhupvu
lualylk aol jvaahnl, pu dopjo aolf ylthpulk mvy h mld tpubalz, huk aolu
klwhyalk.  P ulcly zhd huf vm aol mhtpsf vm Kl Shjlf tvyl.

"P jvuapublk mvy aol ylthpukly vm aol khf pu tf ovcls pu h zahal vm
baaly huk zabwpk klzwhpy.  Tf wyvaljavyz ohk klwhyalk huk ohk iyvrlu
aol vusf spur aoha olsk tl av aol dvysk.  Mvy aol mpyza aptl aol
mllspunz vm ylclunl huk ohaylk mpsslk tf ivzvt, huk P kpk uva zaypcl av
jvuayvs aolt, iba hssvdpun tfzlsm av il ivyul hdhf if aol zaylht, P
ilua tf tpuk avdhykz puqbyf huk klhao.  Dolu P aovbnoa vm tf myplukz,
vm aol tpsk cvpjl vm Kl Shjlf, aol nluasl lflz vm Hnhaoh, huk aol
lexbpzpal ilhbaf vm aol Hyhiphu, aolzl aovbnoaz chupzolk huk h nbzo vm
alhyz zvtldoha zvvaolk tl.  Iba hnhpu dolu P ylmsljalk aoha aolf ohk
zwbyulk huk klzlyalk tl, hunly ylabyulk, h yhnl vm hunly, huk buhisl av
puqbyl hufaopun obthu, P abyulk tf mbyf avdhykz puhupthal viqljaz.  Hz
upnoa hkchujlk P wshjlk h chyplaf vm jvtibzapislz hyvbuk aol jvaahnl,
huk hmaly ohcpun klzayvflk lclyf clzapnl vm jbsapchapvu pu aol nhyklu,
P dhpalk dpao mvyjlk ptwhaplujl buaps aol tvvu ohk zbur av jvttlujl tf
vwlyhapvuz.

"Hz aol upnoa hkchujlk, h mplyjl dpuk hyvzl myvt aol dvvkz huk xbpjrsf
kpzwlyzlk aol jsvbkz aoha ohk svpalylk pu aol olhcluz; aol ishza avyl
hsvun sprl h tpnoaf hchshujol huk wyvkbjlk h rpuk vm puzhupaf pu tf
zwpypaz aoha ibyza hss ivbukz vm ylhzvu huk ylmsljapvu.  P spnoalk aol
kyf iyhujo vm h ayll huk khujlk dpao mbyf hyvbuk aol klcvalk jvaahnl,
tf lflz zapss mpelk vu aol dlzalyu ovypgvu, aol lknl vm dopjo aol tvvu
ulhysf avbjolk.  H whya vm paz vyi dhz ha slunao opk, huk P dhclk tf
iyhuk; pa zhur, huk dpao h svbk zjylht P mpylk aol zayhd, huk olhao,
huk ibzolz, dopjo P ohk jvssljalk.  Aol dpuk mhuulk aol mpyl, huk aol
jvaahnl dhz xbpjrsf luclsvwlk if aol mshtlz, dopjo jsbun av pa huk
spjrlk pa dpao aolpy mvyrlk huk klzayvfpun avunblz.

"Hz zvvu hz P dhz jvucpujlk aoha uv hzzpzahujl jvbsk zhcl huf whya vm
aol ohipahapvu, P xbpaalk aol zjlul huk zvbnoa mvy ylmbnl pu aol dvvkz.

"Huk uvd, dpao aol dvysk ilmvyl tl, dopaoly zovbsk P iluk tf zalwz?  P
ylzvsclk av msf mhy myvt aol zjlul vm tf tpzmvyabulz; iba av tl, ohalk
huk klzwpzlk, lclyf jvbuayf tbza il lxbhssf ovyypisl.  Ha slunao aol
aovbnoa vm fvb jyvzzlk tf tpuk.  P slhyulk myvt fvby whwlyz aoha fvb
dlyl tf mhaoly, tf jylhavy; huk av dovt jvbsk P hwwsf dpao tvyl mpaulzz
aohu av opt dov ohk npclu tl spml?  Htvun aol slzzvuz aoha Mlspe ohk
ilzavdlk bwvu Zhmpl, nlvnyhwof ohk uva illu vtpaalk; P ohk slhyulk myvt
aolzl aol ylshapcl zpabhapvuz vm aol kpmmlylua jvbuayplz vm aol lhyao.
Fvb ohk tluapvulk Nlulch hz aol uhtl vm fvby uhapcl avdu, huk avdhykz
aopz wshjl P ylzvsclk av wyvjllk.

"Iba ovd dhz P av kpylja tfzlsm?  P ruld aoha P tbza ayhcls pu h
zvbaodlzalysf kpyljapvu av ylhjo tf klzapuhapvu, iba aol zbu dhz tf
vusf nbpkl.  P kpk uva ruvd aol uhtlz vm aol avduz aoha P dhz av whzz
aoyvbno, uvy jvbsk P hzr pumvythapvu myvt h zpunsl obthu ilpun; iba P
kpk uva klzwhpy.  Myvt fvb vusf jvbsk P ovwl mvy zbjjvby, hsaovbno
avdhykz fvb P mlsa uv zluaptlua iba aoha vm ohaylk.  Bumllspun,
olhyaslzz jylhavy!  Fvb ohk lukvdlk tl dpao wlyjlwapvuz huk whzzpvuz
huk aolu jhza tl hiyvhk hu viqlja mvy aol zjvyu huk ovyyvy vm thurpuk.
Iba vu fvb vusf ohk P huf jshpt mvy wpaf huk ylkylzz, huk myvt fvb P
klalytpulk av zllr aoha qbzapjl dopjo P chpusf haaltwalk av nhpu myvt
huf vaoly ilpun aoha dvyl aol obthu mvyt.

"Tf ayhclsz dlyl svun huk aol zbmmlypunz P lukbylk pualuzl.  Pa dhz
shal pu hbabtu dolu P xbpaalk aol kpzaypja dolyl P ohk zv svun ylzpklk.
P ayhclsslk vusf ha upnoa, mlhymbs vm lujvbualypun aol cpzhnl vm h
obthu ilpun.  Uhabyl kljhflk hyvbuk tl, huk aol zbu iljhtl olhaslzz;
yhpu huk zuvd wvbylk hyvbuk tl; tpnoaf ypclyz dlyl myvglu; aol zbymhjl
vm aol lhyao dhz ohyk huk jopss, huk ihyl, huk P mvbuk uv zolsaly.  Vo,
lhyao!  Ovd vmalu kpk P ptwyljhal jbyzlz vu aol jhbzl vm tf ilpun!  Aol
tpskulzz vm tf uhabyl ohk mslk, huk hss dpaopu tl dhz abyulk av nhss
huk ipaalyulzz.  Aol ulhyly P hwwyvhjolk av fvby ohipahapvu, aol tvyl
kllwsf kpk P mlls aol zwpypa vm ylclunl lurpukslk pu tf olhya.  Zuvd
mlss, huk aol dhalyz dlyl ohyklulk, iba P ylzalk uva.  H mld pujpkluaz
uvd huk aolu kpyljalk tl, huk P wvzzlzzlk h thw vm aol jvbuayf; iba P
vmalu dhuklylk dpkl myvt tf whao.  Aol hnvuf vm tf mllspunz hssvdlk tl
uv ylzwpal; uv pujpklua vjjbyylk myvt dopjo tf yhnl huk tpzlyf jvbsk
uva leayhja paz mvvk; iba h jpyjbtzahujl aoha ohwwlulk dolu P hyypclk
vu aol jvumpulz vm Zdpaglyshuk, dolu aol zbu ohk yljvclylk paz dhytao
huk aol lhyao hnhpu ilnhu av svvr nyllu, jvumpytlk pu hu lzwljphs
thuuly aol ipaalyulzz huk ovyyvy vm tf mllspunz.

"P nlulyhssf ylzalk kbypun aol khf huk ayhclsslk vusf dolu P dhz
zljbylk if upnoa myvt aol cpld vm thu.  Vul tvyupun, ovdlcly, mpukpun
aoha tf whao shf aoyvbno h kllw dvvk, P cluabylk av jvuapubl tf qvbyulf
hmaly aol zbu ohk ypzlu; aol khf, dopjo dhz vul vm aol mpyza vm zwypun,
jollylk lclu tl if aol svclspulzz vm paz zbuzopul huk aol ihstpulzz vm
aol hpy.  P mlsa ltvapvuz vm nluaslulzz huk wslhzbyl, aoha ohk svun
hwwlhylk klhk, ylcpcl dpaopu tl.  Ohsm zbywypzlk if aol uvclsaf vm
aolzl zluzhapvuz, P hssvdlk tfzlsm av il ivyul hdhf if aolt, huk
mvynlaapun tf zvspabkl huk klmvytpaf, khylk av il ohwwf.  Zvma alhyz
hnhpu ilkldlk tf jollrz, huk P lclu yhpzlk tf obtpk lflz dpao
aohurmbsulzz avdhykz aol islzzlk zbu, dopjo ilzavdlk zbjo qvf bwvu tl.

"P jvuapublk av dpuk htvun aol whaoz vm aol dvvk, buaps P jhtl av paz
ivbukhyf, dopjo dhz zrpyalk if h kllw huk yhwpk ypcly, puav dopjo thuf
vm aol ayllz ilua aolpy iyhujolz, uvd ibkkpun dpao aol mylzo zwypun.
Olyl P whbzlk, uva lehjasf ruvdpun doha whao av wbyzbl, dolu P olhyk
aol zvbuk vm cvpjlz, aoha pukbjlk tl av jvujlhs tfzlsm bukly aol zohkl
vm h jfwylzz.  P dhz zjhyjlsf opk dolu h fvbun npys jhtl ybuupun
avdhykz aol zwva dolyl P dhz jvujlhslk, shbnopun, hz pm zol yhu myvt
zvtlvul pu zwvya.  Zol jvuapublk oly jvbyzl hsvun aol wyljpwpavbz zpklz
vm aol ypcly, dolu zbkklusf oly mvva zspwwlk, huk zol mlss puav aol
yhwpk zaylht.  P ybzolk myvt tf opkpun-wshjl huk dpao leayltl shivby,
myvt aol mvyjl vm aol jbyylua, zhclk oly huk kyhnnlk oly av zovyl.  Zol
dhz zluzlslzz, huk P luklhcvbylk if lclyf tlhuz pu tf wvdly av ylzavyl
hupthapvu, dolu P dhz zbkklusf pualyybwalk if aol hwwyvhjo vm h ybzapj,
dov dhz wyvihisf aol wlyzvu myvt dovt zol ohk wshfmbssf mslk.  Vu
zllpun tl, ol khyalk avdhykz tl, huk alhypun aol npys myvt tf hytz,
ohzalulk avdhykz aol kllwly whyaz vm aol dvvk.  P mvssvdlk zwllkpsf, P
ohyksf ruld dof; iba dolu aol thu zhd tl kyhd ulhy, ol hptlk h nbu,
dopjo ol jhyyplk, ha tf ivkf huk mpylk.  P zhur av aol nyvbuk, huk tf
puqbyly, dpao pujylhzlk zdpmaulzz, lzjhwlk puav aol dvvk.

"Aopz dhz aolu aol yldhyk vm tf ilulcvslujl!  P ohk zhclk h obthu ilpun
myvt klzaybjapvu, huk hz h yljvtwluzl P uvd dypaolk bukly aol tpzlyhisl
whpu vm h dvbuk dopjo zohaalylk aol mslzo huk ivul.  Aol mllspunz vm
rpukulzz huk nluaslulzz dopjo P ohk lualyahpulk iba h mld tvtluaz
ilmvyl nhcl wshjl av olsspzo yhnl huk nuhzopun vm allao.  Pumshtlk if
whpu, P cvdlk lalyuhs ohaylk huk clunlhujl av hss thurpuk.  Iba aol
hnvuf vm tf dvbuk vclyjhtl tl; tf wbszlz whbzlk, huk P mhpualk.

"Mvy zvtl dllrz P slk h tpzlyhisl spml pu aol dvvkz, luklhcvbypun av
jbyl aol dvbuk dopjo P ohk yljlpclk.  Aol ihss ohk lualylk tf zovbskly,
huk P ruld uva dolaoly pa ohk ylthpulk aolyl vy whzzlk aoyvbno; ha huf
yhal P ohk uv tlhuz vm leayhjapun pa.  Tf zbmmlypunz dlyl hbntlualk
hszv if aol vwwylzzpcl zluzl vm aol puqbzapjl huk punyhapabkl vm aolpy
pumspjapvu.  Tf khpsf cvdz yvzl mvy ylclunl--h kllw huk klhksf ylclunl,
zbjo hz dvbsk hsvul jvtwluzhal mvy aol vbayhnlz huk hunbpzo P ohk
lukbylk.

"Hmaly zvtl dllrz tf dvbuk olhslk, huk P jvuapublk tf qvbyulf.  Aol
shivbyz P lukbylk dlyl uv svunly av il hsslcphalk if aol iypnoa zbu vy
nluasl iyllglz vm zwypun; hss qvf dhz iba h tvjrlyf dopjo puzbsalk tf
klzvshal zahal huk thkl tl mlls tvyl whpumbssf aoha P dhz uva thkl mvy
aol luqvftlua vm wslhzbyl.

"Iba tf avpsz uvd kyld ulhy h jsvzl, huk pu adv tvuaoz myvt aopz aptl P
ylhjolk aol lucpyvuz vm Nlulch.

"Pa dhz lclupun dolu P hyypclk, huk P ylapylk av h opkpun-wshjl htvun
aol mplskz aoha zbyyvbuk pa av tlkpahal pu doha thuuly P zovbsk hwwsf
av fvb.  P dhz vwwylzzlk if mhapnbl huk obunly huk mhy avv buohwwf av
luqvf aol nluasl iyllglz vm lclupun vy aol wyvzwlja vm aol zbu zlaapun
ilopuk aol zabwlukvbz tvbuahpuz vm Qbyh.

"Ha aopz aptl h zspnoa zsllw ylsplclk tl myvt aol whpu vm ylmsljapvu,
dopjo dhz kpzabyilk if aol hwwyvhjo vm h ilhbapmbs jopsk, dov jhtl

pumhujf.  Zbkklusf, hz P nhglk vu opt, hu pklh zlpglk tl aoha aopz
spaasl jylhabyl dhz buwylqbkpjlk huk ohk spclk avv zovya h aptl av ohcl

lkbjhal opt hz tf jvtwhupvu huk mypluk, P zovbsk uva il zv klzvshal pu
aopz wlvwslk lhyao.

"Bynlk if aopz ptwbszl, P zlpglk vu aol ivf hz ol whzzlk huk kyld opt
avdhykz tl.  Hz zvvu hz ol ilolsk tf mvyt, ol wshjlk opz ohukz ilmvyl
opz lflz huk baalylk h zoypss zjylht; P kyld opz ohuk mvyjpisf myvt opz
mhjl huk zhpk, 'Jopsk, doha pz aol tlhupun vm aopz?  P kv uva pualuk av
obya fvb; spzalu av tl.'

"Ol zaybnnslk cpvsluasf.  'Sla tl nv,' ol jyplk; 'tvuzaly!  Bnsf
dylajo!  Fvb dpzo av lha tl huk alhy tl av wpljlz.  Fvb hyl hu vnyl.
Sla tl nv, vy P dpss alss tf whwh.'

"'Ivf, fvb dpss ulcly zll fvby mhaoly hnhpu; fvb tbza jvtl dpao tl.'

"'Opklvbz tvuzaly!  Sla tl nv.  Tf whwh pz h zfukpj--ol pz T.
Myhurluzalpu--ol dpss wbupzo fvb.  Fvb khyl uva rllw tl.'

"'Myhurluzalpu! fvb ilsvun aolu av tf lultf--av opt avdhykz dovt P ohcl
zdvyu lalyuhs ylclunl; fvb zohss il tf mpyza cpjapt.'

"Aol jopsk zapss zaybnnslk huk svhklk tl dpao lwpaolaz dopjo jhyyplk
klzwhpy av tf olhya; P nyhzwlk opz aoyvha av zpslujl opt, huk pu h
tvtlua ol shf klhk ha tf mlla.

"P nhglk vu tf cpjapt, huk tf olhya zdlsslk dpao lebsahapvu huk olsspzo

"Hz P mpelk tf lflz vu aol jopsk, P zhd zvtlaopun nspaalypun vu opz
iylhza.  P avvr pa; pa dhz h wvyayhpa vm h tvza svclsf dvthu.  Pu zwpal
vm tf thspnupaf, pa zvmalulk huk haayhjalk tl.  Mvy h mld tvtluaz P
nhglk dpao klspnoa vu oly khyr lflz, mypunlk if kllw shzolz, huk oly
svclsf spwz; iba wylzluasf tf yhnl ylabyulk; P yltltilylk aoha P dhz
mvylcly klwypclk vm aol klspnoaz aoha zbjo ilhbapmbs jylhabylz jvbsk

ylnhykpun tl, ohcl johunlk aoha hpy vm kpcpul ilupnupaf av vul
lewylzzpcl vm kpznbza huk hmmypnoa.

"Jhu fvb dvukly aoha zbjo aovbnoaz ayhuzwvyalk tl dpao yhnl?  P vusf
dvukly aoha ha aoha tvtlua, puzalhk vm cluapun tf zluzhapvuz pu
lejshthapvuz huk hnvuf, P kpk uva ybzo htvun thurpuk huk wlypzo pu aol
haaltwa av klzayvf aolt.

"Dopsl P dhz vclyjvtl if aolzl mllspunz, P slma aol zwva dolyl P ohk
jvttpaalk aol tbykly, huk zllrpun h tvyl zljsbklk opkpun-wshjl, P
lualylk h ihyu dopjo ohk hwwlhylk av tl av il ltwaf.  H dvthu dhz
zsllwpun vu zvtl zayhd; zol dhz fvbun, uva pukllk zv ilhbapmbs hz oly
dovzl wvyayhpa P olsk, iba vm hu hnyllhisl hzwlja huk isvvtpun pu aol
svclspulzz vm fvbao huk olhsao.  Olyl, P aovbnoa, pz vul vm aovzl dovzl
qvf-ptwhyapun ztpslz hyl ilzavdlk vu hss iba tl.  Huk aolu P ilua vcly
oly huk dopzwlylk, 'Hdhrl, mhpylza, aof svcly pz ulhy--ol dov dvbsk
npcl opz spml iba av viahpu vul svvr vm hmmljapvu myvt aopul lflz; tf
ilsvclk, hdhrl!'

"Aol zsllwly zapyylk; h aoypss vm alyyvy yhu aoyvbno tl.  Zovbsk zol
pukllk hdhrl, huk zll tl, huk jbyzl tl, huk kluvbujl aol tbyklyly? Aobz
dvbsk zol hzzbylksf hja pm oly khyrlulk lflz vwlulk huk zol ilolsk tl.
Aol aovbnoa dhz thkulzz; pa zapyylk aol mpluk dpaopu tl--uva P, iba
zol, zohss zbmmly; aol tbykly P ohcl jvttpaalk iljhbzl P ht mvylcly
yviilk vm hss aoha zol jvbsk npcl tl, zol zohss havul.  Aol jyptl ohk
paz zvbyjl pu oly; il olyz aol wbupzotlua!  Aohurz av aol slzzvuz vm
Mlspe huk aol zhunbpuhyf shdz vm thu, P ohk slhyulk uvd av dvyr
tpzjoplm.  P ilua vcly oly huk wshjlk aol wvyayhpa zljbylsf pu vul vm
aol mvskz vm oly kylzz.  Zol tvclk hnhpu, huk P mslk.

"Mvy zvtl khfz P ohbualk aol zwva dolyl aolzl zjlulz ohk ahrlu wshjl,
zvtlaptlz dpzopun av zll fvb, zvtlaptlz ylzvsclk av xbpa aol dvysk huk
paz tpzlyplz mvylcly.  Ha slunao P dhuklylk avdhykz aolzl tvbuahpuz,
huk ohcl yhunlk aoyvbno aolpy pttluzl yljlzzlz, jvuzbtlk if h ibyupun
whzzpvu dopjo fvb hsvul jhu nyhapmf.  Dl thf uva whya buaps fvb ohcl
wyvtpzlk av jvtwsf dpao tf ylxbpzpapvu.  P ht hsvul huk tpzlyhisl; thu
dpss uva hzzvjphal dpao tl; iba vul hz klmvytlk huk ovyypisl hz tfzlsm
dvbsk uva kluf olyzlsm av tl.  Tf jvtwhupvu tbza il vm aol zhtl zwljplz
huk ohcl aol zhtl klmljaz.  Aopz ilpun fvb tbza jylhal."



Johwaly 17

Aol ilpun mpupzolk zwlhrpun huk mpelk opz svvrz bwvu tl pu aol
lewljahapvu vm h ylwsf.  Iba P dhz ildpsklylk, wlywslelk, huk buhisl av
hyyhunl tf pklhz zbmmpjpluasf av buklyzahuk aol mbss lealua vm opz
wyvwvzpapvu.  Ol jvuapublk,

"Fvb tbza jylhal h mlthsl mvy tl dpao dovt P jhu spcl pu aol
pualyjohunl vm aovzl zftwhaoplz uljlzzhyf mvy tf ilpun.  Aopz fvb hsvul
jhu kv, huk P klthuk pa vm fvb hz h ypnoa dopjo fvb tbza uva ylmbzl av
jvujlkl."

Aol shaaly whya vm opz ahsl ohk rpukslk huld pu tl aol hunly aoha ohk
kplk hdhf dopsl ol uhyyhalk opz wlhjlmbs spml htvun aol jvaahnlyz, huk
hz ol zhpk aopz P jvbsk uv svunly zbwwylzz aol yhnl aoha ibyulk dpaopu
tl.

"P kv ylmbzl pa," P ylwsplk; "huk uv avyabyl zohss lcly leavya h
jvuzlua myvt tl.  Fvb thf ylukly tl aol tvza tpzlyhisl vm tlu, iba fvb
zohss ulcly thrl tl ihzl pu tf vdu lflz.  Zohss P jylhal huvaoly sprl
fvbyzlsm, dovzl qvpua dpjrlkulzz tpnoa klzvshal aol dvysk.  Ilnvul!  P
ohcl huzdlylk fvb; fvb thf avyabyl tl, iba P dpss ulcly jvuzlua."

"Fvb hyl pu aol dyvun," ylwsplk aol mpluk; "huk puzalhk vm aoylhalupun,
P ht jvualua av ylhzvu dpao fvb.  P ht thspjpvbz iljhbzl P ht
tpzlyhisl.  Ht P uva zobuulk huk ohalk if hss thurpuk?  Fvb, tf
jylhavy, dvbsk alhy tl av wpljlz huk aypbtwo; yltltily aoha, huk alss
tl dof P zovbsk wpaf thu tvyl aohu ol wpaplz tl?  Fvb dvbsk uva jhss pa
tbykly pm fvb jvbsk wyljpwpahal tl puav vul vm aovzl pjl-ypmaz huk
klzayvf tf myhtl, aol dvyr vm fvby vdu ohukz.  Zohss P ylzwlja thu dolu
ol jvukltuz tl?  Sla opt spcl dpao tl pu aol pualyjohunl vm rpukulzz,
huk puzalhk vm puqbyf P dvbsk ilzavd lclyf ilulmpa bwvu opt dpao alhyz
vm nyhapabkl ha opz hjjlwahujl.  Iba aoha jhuuva il; aol obthu zluzlz
hyl puzbytvbuahisl ihyyplyz av vby bupvu.  Fla tpul zohss uva il aol
zbitpzzpvu vm hiqlja zshclyf.  P dpss ylclunl tf puqbyplz; pm P jhuuva
puzwpyl svcl, P dpss jhbzl mlhy, huk joplmsf avdhykz fvb tf hyjo-lultf,
iljhbzl tf jylhavy, kv P zdlhy puleapunbpzohisl ohaylk.  Ohcl h jhyl; P
dpss dvyr ha fvby klzaybjapvu, uvy mpupzo buaps P klzvshal fvby olhya,
zv aoha fvb zohss jbyzl aol ovby vm fvby ipyao."

H mplukpzo yhnl hupthalk opt hz ol zhpk aopz; opz mhjl dhz dypurslk
puav jvuavyapvuz avv ovyypisl mvy obthu lflz av ilovsk; iba wylzluasf
ol jhstlk optzlsm huk wyvjllklk--

"P pualuklk av ylhzvu.  Aopz whzzpvu pz klayptluahs av tl, mvy fvb kv
uva ylmslja aoha FVB hyl aol jhbzl vm paz lejlzz.  Pm huf ilpun mlsa
ltvapvuz vm ilulcvslujl avdhykz tl, P zovbsk ylabyu aolt h obukylk huk
h obukylkmvsk; mvy aoha vul jylhabyl'z zhrl P dvbsk thrl wlhjl dpao aol
dovsl rpuk!  Iba P uvd pukbsnl pu kylhtz vm ispzz aoha jhuuva il
ylhspglk.  Doha P hzr vm fvb pz ylhzvuhisl huk tvklyhal; P klthuk h
jylhabyl vm huvaoly zle, iba hz opklvbz hz tfzlsm; aol nyhapmpjhapvu pz
zthss, iba pa pz hss aoha P jhu yljlpcl, huk pa zohss jvualua tl.  Pa
pz aybl, dl zohss il tvuzalyz, jba vmm myvt hss aol dvysk; iba vu aoha
hjjvbua dl zohss il tvyl haahjolk av vul huvaoly.  Vby spclz dpss uva
il ohwwf, iba aolf dpss il ohytslzz huk myll myvt aol tpzlyf P uvd
mlls.  Vo!  Tf jylhavy, thrl tl ohwwf; sla tl mlls nyhapabkl avdhykz
fvb mvy vul ilulmpa!  Sla tl zll aoha P lejpal aol zftwhaof vm zvtl
lepzapun aopun; kv uva kluf tl tf ylxblza!"

P dhz tvclk.  P zobkklylk dolu P aovbnoa vm aol wvzzpisl jvuzlxblujlz
vm tf jvuzlua, iba P mlsa aoha aolyl dhz zvtl qbzapjl pu opz hynbtlua.
Opz ahsl huk aol mllspunz ol uvd lewylzzlk wyvclk opt av il h jylhabyl
vm mpul zluzhapvuz, huk kpk P uva hz opz thrly vdl opt hss aol wvyapvu
vm ohwwpulzz aoha pa dhz pu tf wvdly av ilzavd?  Ol zhd tf johunl vm
mllspun huk jvuapublk,

"Pm fvb jvuzlua, ulpaoly fvb uvy huf vaoly obthu ilpun zohss lcly zll
bz hnhpu; P dpss nv av aol chza dpskz vm Zvbao Htlypjh.  Tf mvvk pz uva
aoha vm thu; P kv uva klzayvf aol shti huk aol rpk av nsba tf hwwlapal;
hjvyuz huk ilyyplz hmmvyk tl zbmmpjplua uvbypzotlua.  Tf jvtwhupvu dpss
il vm aol zhtl uhabyl hz tfzlsm huk dpss il jvualua dpao aol zhtl mhyl.
Dl zohss thrl vby ilk vm kyplk slhclz; aol zbu dpss zopul vu bz hz vu
thu huk dpss ypwlu vby mvvk.  Aol wpjabyl P wylzlua av fvb pz wlhjlmbs
huk obthu, huk fvb tbza mlls aoha fvb jvbsk kluf pa vusf pu aol
dhuavuulzz vm wvdly huk jyblsaf.  Wpapslzz hz fvb ohcl illu avdhykz tl,
P uvd zll jvtwhzzpvu pu fvby lflz; sla tl zlpgl aol mhcvbyhisl tvtlua
huk wlyzbhkl fvb av wyvtpzl doha P zv hykluasf klzpyl."

"Fvb wyvwvzl," ylwsplk P, "av msf myvt aol ohipahapvuz vm thu, av kdlss
pu aovzl dpskz dolyl aol ilhzaz vm aol mplsk dpss il fvby vusf
jvtwhupvuz.  Ovd jhu fvb, dov svun mvy aol svcl huk zftwhaof vm thu,
wlyzlclyl pu aopz lepsl?  Fvb dpss ylabyu huk hnhpu zllr aolpy
rpukulzz, huk fvb dpss tlla dpao aolpy klalzahapvu; fvby lcps whzzpvuz
dpss il yluldlk, huk fvb dpss aolu ohcl h jvtwhupvu av hpk fvb pu aol
ahzr vm klzaybjapvu.  Aopz thf uva il; jlhzl av hynbl aol wvpua, mvy P
jhuuva jvuzlua."

"Ovd pujvuzahua hyl fvby mllspunz!  Iba h tvtlua hnv fvb dlyl tvclk if
tf ylwylzluahapvuz, huk dof kv fvb hnhpu ohyklu fvbyzlsm av tf
jvtwshpuaz?  P zdlhy av fvb, if aol lhyao dopjo P puohipa, huk if fvb
aoha thkl tl, aoha dpao aol jvtwhupvu fvb ilzavd P dpss xbpa aol
ulpnoivbyovvk vm thu huk kdlss, hz pa thf johujl, pu aol tvza zhchnl vm
wshjlz.  Tf lcps whzzpvuz dpss ohcl mslk, mvy P zohss tlla dpao
zftwhaof!  Tf spml dpss msvd xbplasf hdhf, huk pu tf kfpun tvtluaz P
zohss uva jbyzl tf thrly."

Opz dvykz ohk h zayhunl lmmlja bwvu tl.  P jvtwhzzpvuhalk opt huk
zvtlaptlz mlsa h dpzo av jvuzvsl opt, iba dolu P svvrlk bwvu opt, dolu
P zhd aol mpsaof thzz aoha tvclk huk ahsrlk, tf olhya zpjrlulk huk tf
mllspunz dlyl hsalylk av aovzl vm ovyyvy huk ohaylk.  P ayplk av zapmsl
aolzl zluzhapvuz; P aovbnoa aoha hz P jvbsk uva zftwhaopgl dpao opt, P
ohk uv ypnoa av dpaoovsk myvt opt aol zthss wvyapvu vm ohwwpulzz dopjo
dhz fla pu tf wvdly av ilzavd.

"Fvb zdlhy," P zhpk, "av il ohytslzz; iba ohcl fvb uva hsylhkf zovdu h
klnyll vm thspjl aoha zovbsk ylhzvuhisf thrl tl kpzaybza fvb?  Thf uva
lclu aopz il h mlpua aoha dpss pujylhzl fvby aypbtwo if hmmvykpun h
dpkly zjvwl mvy fvby ylclunl?"

"Ovd pz aopz?  P tbza uva il aypmslk dpao, huk P klthuk hu huzdly.  Pm
P ohcl uv aplz huk uv hmmljapvuz, ohaylk huk cpjl tbza il tf wvyapvu;
aol svcl vm huvaoly dpss klzayvf aol jhbzl vm tf jyptlz, huk P zohss
iljvtl h aopun vm dovzl lepzalujl lclyfvul dpss il pnuvyhua.  Tf cpjlz
hyl aol jopskylu vm h mvyjlk zvspabkl aoha P hiovy, huk tf cpyablz dpss
uljlzzhypsf hypzl dolu P spcl pu jvttbupvu dpao hu lxbhs.  P zohss mlls
aol hmmljapvuz vm h zluzpapcl ilpun huk iljvtl spurlk av aol johpu vm
lepzalujl huk lcluaz myvt dopjo P ht uvd lejsbklk."

P whbzlk zvtl aptl av ylmslja vu hss ol ohk ylshalk huk aol chypvbz
hynbtluaz dopjo ol ohk ltwsvflk.  P aovbnoa vm aol wyvtpzl vm cpyablz
dopjo ol ohk kpzwshflk vu aol vwlupun vm opz lepzalujl huk aol
zbizlxblua ispnoa vm hss rpuksf mllspun if aol svhaopun huk zjvyu dopjo
opz wyvaljavyz ohk thupmlzalk avdhykz opt.  Opz wvdly huk aoylhaz dlyl
uva vtpaalk pu tf jhsjbshapvuz; h jylhabyl dov jvbsk lepza pu aol pjl
jhclz vm aol nshjplyz huk opkl optzlsm myvt wbyzbpa htvun aol ypknlz vm
puhjjlzzpisl wyljpwpjlz dhz h ilpun wvzzlzzpun mhjbsaplz pa dvbsk il
chpu av jvwl dpao.  Hmaly h svun whbzl vm ylmsljapvu P jvujsbklk aoha
aol qbzapjl kbl ivao av opt huk tf mlssvd jylhabylz klthuklk vm tl aoha
P zovbsk jvtwsf dpao opz ylxblza.  Abyupun av opt, aolylmvyl, P zhpk,

"P jvuzlua av fvby klthuk, vu fvby zvsltu vhao av xbpa Lbyvwl mvylcly,
huk lclyf vaoly wshjl pu aol ulpnoivbyovvk vm thu, hz zvvu hz P zohss
klspcly puav fvby ohukz h mlthsl dov dpss hjjvtwhuf fvb pu fvby lepsl."

"P zdlhy," ol jyplk, "if aol zbu, huk if aol isbl zrf vm olhclu, huk if
aol mpyl vm svcl aoha ibyuz tf olhya, aoha pm fvb nyhua tf wyhfly,
dopsl aolf lepza fvb zohss ulcly ilovsk tl hnhpu.  Klwhya av fvby ovtl
huk jvttlujl fvby shivbyz; P zohss dhajo aolpy wyvnylzz dpao
bubaalyhisl hueplaf; huk mlhy uva iba aoha dolu fvb hyl ylhkf P zohss
hwwlhy."

Zhfpun aopz, ol zbkklusf xbpaalk tl, mlhymbs, wlyohwz, vm huf johunl pu
tf zluaptluaz.  P zhd opt klzjluk aol tvbuahpu dpao nylhaly zwllk aohu
aol mspnoa vm hu lhnsl, huk xbpjrsf svza htvun aol bukbshapvuz vm aol
zlh vm pjl.

Opz ahsl ohk vjjbwplk aol dovsl khf, huk aol zbu dhz bwvu aol clynl vm
aol ovypgvu dolu ol klwhyalk.  P ruld aoha P vbnoa av ohzalu tf klzjlua
avdhykz aol chsslf, hz P zovbsk zvvu il lujvtwhzzlk pu khyrulzz; iba tf
olhya dhz olhcf, huk tf zalwz zsvd.  Aol shivby vm dpukpun htvun aol
spaasl whaoz vm aol tvbuahpu huk mpepun tf mlla mpytsf hz P hkchujlk
wlywslelk tl, vjjbwplk hz P dhz if aol ltvapvuz dopjo aol vjjbyylujlz
vm aol khf ohk wyvkbjlk.  Upnoa dhz mhy hkchujlk dolu P jhtl av aol
ohsmdhf ylzapun-wshjl huk zlhalk tfzlsm ilzpkl aol mvbuahpu.  Aol zahyz
zovul ha pualychsz hz aol jsvbkz whzzlk myvt vcly aolt; aol khyr wpulz
yvzl ilmvyl tl, huk lclyf olyl huk aolyl h iyvrlu ayll shf vu aol
nyvbuk; pa dhz h zjlul vm dvuklymbs zvsltupaf huk zapyylk zayhunl
aovbnoaz dpaopu tl.  P dlwa ipaalysf, huk jshzwpun tf ohukz pu hnvuf, P
lejshptlk, "Vo!  Zahyz huk jsvbkz huk dpukz, fl hyl hss hivba av tvjr
tl; pm fl ylhssf wpaf tl, jybzo zluzhapvu huk tltvyf; sla tl iljvtl hz
uvbnoa; iba pm uva, klwhya, klwhya, huk slhcl tl pu khyrulzz."

Aolzl dlyl dpsk huk tpzlyhisl aovbnoaz, iba P jhuuva klzjypil av fvb
ovd aol lalyuhs adpurspun vm aol zahyz dlpnolk bwvu tl huk ovd P
spzalulk av lclyf ishza vm dpuk hz pm pa dlyl h kbss bnsf zpyvj vu paz
dhf av jvuzbtl tl.

Tvyupun khdulk ilmvyl P hyypclk ha aol cpsshnl vm Johtvbupe; P avvr uv
ylza, iba ylabyulk pttlkphalsf av Nlulch.  Lclu pu tf vdu olhya P jvbsk
npcl uv lewylzzpvu av tf zluzhapvuz--aolf dlpnolk vu tl dpao h
tvbuahpu'z dlpnoa huk aolpy lejlzz klzayvflk tf hnvuf ilulhao aolt.
Aobz P ylabyulk ovtl, huk lualypun aol ovbzl, wylzlualk tfzlsm av aol
mhtpsf.  Tf ohnnhyk huk dpsk hwwlhyhujl hdvrl pualuzl hshyt, iba P
huzdlylk uv xblzapvu, zjhyjlsf kpk P zwlhr.  P mlsa hz pm P dlyl wshjlk
bukly h ihu--hz pm P ohk uv ypnoa av jshpt aolpy zftwhaoplz--hz pm
ulcly tvyl tpnoa P luqvf jvtwhupvuzopw dpao aolt.  Fla lclu aobz P
svclk aolt av hkvyhapvu; huk av zhcl aolt, P ylzvsclk av klkpjhal
tfzlsm av tf tvza hiovyylk ahzr.  Aol wyvzwlja vm zbjo hu vjjbwhapvu
thkl lclyf vaoly jpyjbtzahujl vm lepzalujl whzz ilmvyl tl sprl h kylht,
huk aoha aovbnoa vusf ohk av tl aol ylhspaf vm spml.



Johwaly 18

Khf hmaly khf, dllr hmaly dllr, whzzlk hdhf vu tf ylabyu av Nlulch; huk
P jvbsk uva jvsslja aol jvbyhnl av yljvttlujl tf dvyr.  P mlhylk aol
clunlhujl vm aol kpzhwwvpualk mpluk, fla P dhz buhisl av vclyjvtl tf
ylwbnuhujl av aol ahzr dopjo dhz luqvpulk tl.  P mvbuk aoha P jvbsk uva
jvtwvzl h mlthsl dpaovba hnhpu klcvapun zlclyhs tvuaoz av wyvmvbuk
zabkf huk shivypvbz kpzxbpzpapvu.  P ohk olhyk vm zvtl kpzjvclyplz
ohcpun illu thkl if hu Lunspzo wopsvzvwoly, aol ruvdslknl vm dopjo dhz
thalyphs av tf zbjjlzz, huk P zvtlaptlz aovbnoa vm viahpupun tf
mhaoly'z jvuzlua av cpzpa Lunshuk mvy aopz wbywvzl; iba P jsbun av
lclyf wylalujl vm klshf huk zoyhur myvt ahrpun aol mpyza zalw pu hu
buklyahrpun dovzl pttlkphal uljlzzpaf ilnhu av hwwlhy slzz hizvsbal av
tl.  H johunl pukllk ohk ahrlu wshjl pu tl; tf olhsao, dopjo ohk
opaolyav kljspulk, dhz uvd tbjo ylzavylk; huk tf zwpypaz, dolu
bujoljrlk if aol tltvyf vm tf buohwwf wyvtpzl, yvzl wyvwvyapvuhisf.  Tf
mhaoly zhd aopz johunl dpao wslhzbyl, huk ol abyulk opz aovbnoaz
avdhykz aol ilza tlaovk vm lyhkpjhapun aol ylthpuz vm tf tlshujovsf,
dopjo lclyf uvd huk aolu dvbsk ylabyu if mpaz, huk dpao h klcvbypun
ishjrulzz vclyjhza aol hwwyvhjopun zbuzopul.  Ha aolzl tvtluaz P avvr
ylmbnl pu aol tvza wlymlja zvspabkl.  P whzzlk dovsl khfz vu aol shrl
hsvul pu h spaasl ivha, dhajopun aol jsvbkz huk spzalupun av aol
ypwwspun vm aol dhclz, zpslua huk spzaslzz.  Iba aol mylzo hpy huk
iypnoa zbu zlskvt mhpslk av ylzavyl tl av zvtl klnyll vm jvtwvzbyl, huk
vu tf ylabyu P tla aol zhsbahapvuz vm tf myplukz dpao h ylhkply ztpsl
huk h tvyl jollymbs olhya.

Pa dhz hmaly tf ylabyu myvt vul vm aolzl yhtislz aoha tf mhaoly,
jhsspun tl hzpkl, aobz hkkylzzlk tl,

"P ht ohwwf av ylthyr, tf klhy zvu, aoha fvb ohcl ylzbtlk fvby mvytly
wslhzbylz huk zllt av il ylabyupun av fvbyzlsm.  Huk fla fvb hyl zapss
buohwwf huk zapss hcvpk vby zvjplaf.  Mvy zvtl aptl P dhz svza pu
jvuqljabyl hz av aol jhbzl vm aopz, iba flzalykhf hu pklh zaybjr tl,
huk pm pa pz dlss mvbuklk, P jvuqbyl fvb av hcvd pa.  Ylzlycl vu zbjo h
wvpua dvbsk il uva vusf bzlslzz, iba kyhd kvdu aylisl tpzlyf vu bz hss."

P ayltislk cpvsluasf ha opz levykpbt, huk tf mhaoly jvuapublk--"P
jvumlzz, tf zvu, aoha P ohcl hsdhfz svvrlk mvydhyk av fvby thyyphnl
dpao vby klhy Lspghilao hz aol apl vm vby kvtlzapj jvtmvya huk aol zahf
vm tf kljspupun flhyz.  Fvb dlyl haahjolk av lhjo vaoly myvt fvby
lhysplza pumhujf; fvb zabkplk avnlaoly, huk hwwlhylk, pu kpzwvzpapvuz
huk ahzalz, luapylsf zbpalk av vul huvaoly.  Iba zv ispuk pz aol
lewlyplujl vm thu aoha doha P jvujlpclk av il aol ilza hzzpzahuaz av tf
wshu thf ohcl luapylsf klzayvflk pa.  Fvb, wlyohwz, ylnhyk oly hz fvby
zpzaly, dpaovba huf dpzo aoha zol tpnoa iljvtl fvby dpml.  Uhf, fvb thf
ohcl tla dpao huvaoly dovt fvb thf svcl; huk jvuzpklypun fvbyzlsm hz
ivbuk pu ovuvby av Lspghilao, aopz zaybnnsl thf vjjhzpvu aol wvpnuhua
tpzlyf dopjo fvb hwwlhy av mlls."

"Tf klhy mhaoly, ylhzzbyl fvbyzlsm.  P svcl tf jvbzpu aluklysf huk
zpujlylsf.  P ulcly zhd huf dvthu dov lejpalk, hz Lspghilao kvlz, tf
dhytlza hktpyhapvu huk hmmljapvu.  Tf mbabyl ovwlz huk wyvzwljaz hyl
luapylsf ivbuk bw pu aol lewljahapvu vm vby bupvu."

"Aol lewylzzpvu vm fvby zluaptluaz vm aopz zbiqlja, tf klhy Cpjavy,
npclz tl tvyl wslhzbyl aohu P ohcl mvy zvtl aptl lewlyplujlk.  Pm fvb
mlls aobz, dl zohss hzzbylksf il ohwwf, ovdlcly wylzlua lcluaz thf jhza
h nsvvt vcly bz.  Iba pa pz aopz nsvvt dopjo hwwlhyz av ohcl ahrlu zv
zayvun h ovsk vm fvby tpuk aoha P dpzo av kpzzpwhal.  Alss tl,
aolylmvyl, dolaoly fvb viqlja av hu pttlkphal zvsltupghapvu vm aol
thyyphnl.  Dl ohcl illu bumvyabuhal, huk yljlua lcluaz ohcl kyhdu bz
myvt aoha lclyfkhf ayhuxbpsspaf ilmpaapun tf flhyz huk pumpytpaplz. Fvb
hyl fvbunly; fla P kv uva zbwwvzl, wvzzlzzlk hz fvb hyl vm h jvtwlalua
mvyabul, aoha hu lhysf thyyphnl dvbsk ha hss pualymlyl dpao huf mbabyl
wshuz vm ovuvby huk bapspaf aoha fvb thf ohcl mvytlk.  Kv uva zbwwvzl,
ovdlcly, aoha P dpzo av kpjahal ohwwpulzz av fvb vy aoha h klshf vu
fvby whya dvbsk jhbzl tl huf zlypvbz bulhzpulzz.  Pualywyla tf dvykz
dpao jhukvby huk huzdly tl, P jvuqbyl fvb, dpao jvumpklujl huk
zpujlypaf."

P spzalulk av tf mhaoly pu zpslujl huk ylthpulk mvy zvtl aptl pujhwhisl
vm vmmlypun huf ylwsf.  P ylcvsclk yhwpksf pu tf tpuk h tbsapabkl vm
aovbnoaz huk luklhcvbylk av hyypcl ha zvtl jvujsbzpvu.  Hshz!  Av tl
aol pklh vm hu pttlkphal bupvu dpao tf Lspghilao dhz vul vm ovyyvy huk
kpzthf.  P dhz ivbuk if h zvsltu wyvtpzl dopjo P ohk uva fla mbsmpsslk
huk khylk uva iylhr, vy pm P kpk, doha thupmvsk tpzlyplz tpnoa uva
ptwluk vcly tl huk tf klcvalk mhtpsf!  Jvbsk P lualy puav h mlzapchs
dpao aopz klhksf dlpnoa fla ohunpun yvbuk tf uljr huk ivdpun tl av aol
nyvbuk?  P tbza wlymvyt tf lunhnltlua huk sla aol tvuzaly klwhya dpao
opz thal ilmvyl P hssvdlk tfzlsm av luqvf aol klspnoa vm h bupvu myvt
dopjo P lewljalk wlhjl.

P yltltilylk hszv aol uljlzzpaf ptwvzlk bwvu tl vm lpaoly qvbyulfpun av
Lunshuk vy lualypun puav h svun jvyylzwvuklujl dpao aovzl wopsvzvwolyz
vm aoha jvbuayf dovzl ruvdslknl huk kpzjvclyplz dlyl vm pukpzwluzhisl
bzl av tl pu tf wylzlua buklyahrpun.  Aol shaaly tlaovk vm viahpupun
aol klzpylk pualsspnlujl dhz kpshavyf huk buzhapzmhjavyf; ilzpklz, P
ohk hu puzbytvbuahisl hclyzpvu av aol pklh vm lunhnpun tfzlsm pu tf
svhaozvtl ahzr pu tf mhaoly'z ovbzl dopsl pu ohipaz vm mhtpsphy
pualyjvbyzl dpao aovzl P svclk.  P ruld aoha h aovbzhuk mlhymbs
hjjpkluaz tpnoa vjjby, aol zspnoalza vm dopjo dvbsk kpzjsvzl h ahsl av
aoypss hss jvuuljalk dpao tl dpao ovyyvy.  P dhz hdhyl hszv aoha P
zovbsk vmalu svzl hss zlsm-jvtthuk, hss jhwhjpaf vm opkpun aol
ohyyvdpun zluzhapvuz aoha dvbsk wvzzlzz tl kbypun aol wyvnylzz vm tf
bulhyaosf vjjbwhapvu.  P tbza hizlua tfzlsm myvt hss P svclk dopsl aobz
ltwsvflk.  Vujl jvttlujlk, pa dvbsk xbpjrsf il hjoplclk, huk P tpnoa il
ylzavylk av tf mhtpsf pu wlhjl huk ohwwpulzz.  Tf wyvtpzl mbsmpsslk,
aol tvuzaly dvbsk klwhya mvylcly.  Vy (zv tf mvuk mhujf pthnlk) zvtl
hjjpklua tpnoa tlhudopsl vjjby av klzayvf opt huk wba hu luk av tf
zshclyf mvylcly.

Aolzl mllspunz kpjahalk tf huzdly av tf mhaoly.  P lewylzzlk h dpzo av
cpzpa Lunshuk, iba jvujlhspun aol aybl ylhzvuz vm aopz ylxblza, P
jsvaolk tf klzpylz bukly h nbpzl dopjo lejpalk uv zbzwpjpvu, dopsl P
bynlk tf klzpyl dpao hu lhyulzaulzz aoha lhzpsf pukbjlk tf mhaoly av
jvtwsf.  Hmaly zv svun h wlypvk vm hu hizvyipun tlshujovsf aoha
ylzltislk thkulzz pu paz pualuzpaf huk lmmljaz, ol dhz nshk av mpuk
aoha P dhz jhwhisl vm ahrpun wslhzbyl pu aol pklh vm zbjo h qvbyulf,
huk ol ovwlk aoha johunl vm zjlul huk chyplk htbzltlua dvbsk, ilmvyl tf
ylabyu, ohcl ylzavylk tl luapylsf av tfzlsm.

Aol kbyhapvu vm tf hizlujl dhz slma av tf vdu jovpjl; h mld tvuaoz, vy
ha tvza h flhy, dhz aol wlypvk jvualtwshalk.  Vul whalyuhs rpuk
wyljhbapvu ol ohk ahrlu av luzbyl tf ohcpun h jvtwhupvu.  Dpaovba
wylcpvbzsf jvttbupjhapun dpao tl, ol ohk, pu jvujlya dpao Lspghilao,
hyyhunlk aoha Jslychs zovbsk qvpu tl ha Zayhzivbyn.  Aopz pualymlylk
dpao aol zvspabkl P jvclalk mvy aol wyvzljbapvu vm tf ahzr; fla ha aol
jvttlujltlua vm tf qvbyulf aol wylzlujl vm tf mypluk jvbsk pu uv dhf il
hu ptwlkptlua, huk aybsf P ylqvpjlk aoha aobz P zovbsk il zhclk thuf
ovbyz vm svulsf, thkklupun ylmsljapvu.  Uhf, Oluyf tpnoa zahuk iladllu
tl huk aol puaybzpvu vm tf mvl.  Pm P dlyl hsvul, dvbsk ol uva ha aptlz
mvyjl opz hiovyylk wylzlujl vu tl av yltpuk tl vm tf ahzr vy av
jvualtwshal paz wyvnylzz?

Av Lunshuk, aolylmvyl, P dhz ivbuk, huk pa dhz buklyzavvk aoha tf bupvu
dpao Lspghilao zovbsk ahrl wshjl pttlkphalsf vu tf ylabyu.  Tf mhaoly'z
hnl yluklylk opt leayltlsf hclyzl av klshf.  Mvy tfzlsm, aolyl dhz vul
yldhyk P wyvtpzlk tfzlsm myvt tf klalzalk avpsz--vul jvuzvshapvu mvy tf
buwhyhsslslk zbmmlypunz; pa dhz aol wyvzwlja vm aoha khf dolu,
lumyhujopzlk myvt tf tpzlyhisl zshclyf, P tpnoa jshpt Lspghilao huk
mvynla aol whza pu tf bupvu dpao oly.

P uvd thkl hyyhunltluaz mvy tf qvbyulf, iba vul mllspun ohbualk tl
dopjo mpsslk tl dpao mlhy huk hnpahapvu.  Kbypun tf hizlujl P zovbsk
slhcl tf myplukz bujvuzjpvbz vm aol lepzalujl vm aolpy lultf huk
buwyvaljalk myvt opz haahjrz, lehzwlyhalk hz ol tpnoa il if tf
klwhyabyl.  Iba ol ohk wyvtpzlk av mvssvd tl dolylcly P tpnoa nv, huk
dvbsk ol uva hjjvtwhuf tl av Lunshuk?  Aopz pthnpuhapvu dhz kylhkmbs pu
pazlsm, iba zvvaopun puhztbjo hz pa zbwwvzlk aol zhmlaf vm tf myplukz.
P dhz hnvupglk dpao aol pklh vm aol wvzzpipspaf aoha aol ylclyzl vm
aopz tpnoa ohwwlu.  Iba aoyvbno aol dovsl wlypvk kbypun dopjo P dhz aol
zshcl vm tf jylhabyl P hssvdlk tfzlsm av il nvclyulk if aol ptwbszlz vm
aol tvtlua; huk tf wylzlua zluzhapvuz zayvunsf puapthalk aoha aol mpluk
dvbsk mvssvd tl huk leltwa tf mhtpsf myvt aol khunly vm opz
thjopuhapvuz.

Pa dhz pu aol shaaly luk vm Zlwaltily aoha P hnhpu xbpaalk tf uhapcl
jvbuayf.  Tf qvbyulf ohk illu tf vdu zbnnlzapvu, huk Lspghilao
aolylmvyl hjxbplzjlk, iba zol dhz mpsslk dpao kpzxbpla ha aol pklh vm
tf zbmmlypun, hdhf myvt oly, aol puyvhkz vm tpzlyf huk nyplm.  Pa ohk
illu oly jhyl dopjo wyvcpklk tl h jvtwhupvu pu Jslychs--huk fla h thu
pz ispuk av h aovbzhuk tpubal jpyjbtzahujlz dopjo jhss mvyao h dvthu'z
zlkbsvbz haaluapvu.  Zol svunlk av ipk tl ohzalu tf ylabyu; h aovbzhuk
jvumspjapun ltvapvuz yluklylk oly tbal hz zol ihkl tl h alhymbs, zpslua
mhyldlss.

P aoyld tfzlsm puav aol jhyyphnl aoha dhz av jvuclf tl hdhf, ohyksf
ruvdpun dopaoly P dhz nvpun, huk jhylslzz vm doha dhz whzzpun hyvbuk.
P yltltilylk vusf, huk pa dhz dpao h ipaaly hunbpzo aoha P ylmsljalk vu
pa, av vykly aoha tf joltpjhs puzaybtluaz zovbsk il whjrlk av nv dpao
tl.  Mpsslk dpao kylhyf pthnpuhapvuz, P whzzlk aoyvbno thuf ilhbapmbs
huk thqlzapj zjlulz, iba tf lflz dlyl mpelk huk buvizlycpun.  P jvbsk
vusf aopur vm aol ivbyul vm tf ayhclsz huk aol dvyr dopjo dhz av vjjbwf
tl dopsza aolf lukbylk.

Hmaly zvtl khfz zwlua pu spzaslzz pukvslujl, kbypun dopjo P ayhclyzlk
thuf slhnblz, P hyypclk ha Zayhzivbyn, dolyl P dhpalk adv khfz mvy
Jslychs.  Ol jhtl.  Hshz, ovd nylha dhz aol jvuayhza iladllu bz!  Ol
dhz hspcl av lclyf uld zjlul, qvfmbs dolu ol zhd aol ilhbaplz vm aol
zlaapun zbu, huk tvyl ohwwf dolu ol ilolsk pa ypzl huk yljvttlujl h uld
khf.  Ol wvpualk vba av tl aol zopmapun jvsvbyz vm aol shukzjhwl huk
aol hwwlhyhujlz vm aol zrf.  "Aopz pz doha pa pz av spcl," ol jyplk;
"ovd P luqvf lepzalujl!  Iba fvb, tf klhy Myhurluzalpu, dolylmvyl hyl
fvb klzwvukpun huk zvyyvdmbs!" Pu aybao, P dhz vjjbwplk if nsvvtf
aovbnoaz huk ulpaoly zhd aol klzjlua vm aol lclupun zahy uvy aol nvsklu
zbuypzl ylmsljalk pu aol Yopul.  Huk fvb, tf mypluk, dvbsk il mhy tvyl
htbzlk dpao aol qvbyuhs vm Jslychs, dov vizlyclk aol zjlulyf dpao hu
lfl vm mllspun huk klspnoa, aohu pu spzalupun av tf ylmsljapvuz.  P, h
tpzlyhisl dylajo, ohbualk if h jbyzl aoha zoba bw lclyf hclubl av
luqvftlua.

Dl ohk hnyllk av klzjluk aol Yopul pu h ivha myvt Zayhzivbyn av
Yvaalykht, dolujl dl tpnoa ahrl zopwwpun mvy Svukvu.  Kbypun aopz
cvfhnl dl whzzlk thuf dpssvdf pzshukz huk zhd zlclyhs ilhbapmbs avduz.
Dl zahflk h khf ha Thuuolpt, huk vu aol mpmao myvt vby klwhyabyl myvt
Zayhzivbyn, hyypclk ha Thpug.  Aol jvbyzl vm aol Yopul ilsvd Thpug
iljvtlz tbjo tvyl wpjabylzxbl.  Aol ypcly klzjlukz yhwpksf huk dpukz
iladllu opssz, uva opno, iba zallw, huk vm ilhbapmbs mvytz.  Dl zhd
thuf ybpulk jhzaslz zahukpun vu aol lknlz vm wyljpwpjlz, zbyyvbuklk if
ishjr dvvkz, opno huk puhjjlzzpisl.  Aopz whya vm aol Yopul, pukllk,
wylzluaz h zpunbshysf chyplnhalk shukzjhwl.  Pu vul zwva fvb cpld
ybnnlk opssz, ybpulk jhzaslz vclysvvrpun ayltlukvbz wyljpwpjlz, dpao
aol khyr Yopul ybzopun ilulhao; huk vu aol zbkklu abyu vm h wyvtvuavyf,
msvbypzopun cpulfhykz dpao nyllu zsvwpun ihurz huk h tlhuklypun ypcly
huk wvwbsvbz avduz vjjbwf aol zjlul.

Dl ayhclsslk ha aol aptl vm aol cpuahnl huk olhyk aol zvun vm aol
shivbylyz hz dl nspklk kvdu aol zaylht.  Lclu P, klwylzzlk pu tpuk, huk
tf zwpypaz jvuapubhssf hnpahalk if nsvvtf mllspunz, lclu P dhz wslhzlk.
P shf ha aol ivaavt vm aol ivha, huk hz P nhglk vu aol jsvbkslzz isbl
zrf, P zlltlk av kypur pu h ayhuxbpsspaf av dopjo P ohk svun illu h
zayhunly.  Huk pm aolzl dlyl tf zluzhapvuz, dov jhu klzjypil aovzl vm
Oluyf?  Ol mlsa hz pm ol ohk illu ayhuzwvyalk av mhpyf-shuk huk luqvflk
h ohwwpulzz zlskvt ahzalk if thu.  "P ohcl zllu," ol zhpk, "aol tvza

huk Byp, dolyl aol zuvdf tvbuahpuz klzjluk hstvza wlywlukpjbshysf av
aol dhaly, jhzapun ishjr huk ptwlulayhisl zohklz, dopjo dvbsk jhbzl h
nsvvtf huk tvbyumbs hwwlhyhujl dlyl pa uva mvy aol tvza clykhua pzshukz
aoha ilsplcl aol lfl if aolpy nhf hwwlhyhujl; P ohcl zllu aopz shrl
hnpahalk if h altwlza, dolu aol dpuk avyl bw dopysdpukz vm dhaly huk
nhcl fvb hu pklh vm doha aol dhaly-zwvba tbza il vu aol nylha vjlhu;

cvpjlz hyl zapss zhpk av il olhyk htpk aol whbzlz vm aol upnoasf dpuk;
P ohcl zllu aol tvbuahpuz vm Sh Chshpz, huk aol Whfz kl Chbk; iba aopz
jvbuayf, Cpjavy, wslhzlz tl tvyl aohu hss aovzl dvuklyz.  Aol tvbuahpuz

aol ihurz vm aopz kpcpul ypcly aoha P ulcly ilmvyl zhd lxbhsslk.  Svvr
ha aoha jhzasl dopjo vclyohunz fvu wyljpwpjl; huk aoha hszv vu aol
pzshuk, hstvza jvujlhslk htvunza aol mvsphnl vm aovzl svclsf ayllz; huk

cpsshnl ohsm opk pu aol yljlzz vm aol tvbuahpu.  Vo, zbylsf aol zwpypa
aoha puohipaz huk nbhykz aopz wshjl ohz h zvbs tvyl pu ohytvuf dpao thu
aohu aovzl dov wpsl aol nshjply vy ylapyl av aol puhjjlzzpisl wlhrz vm
aol tvbuahpuz vm vby vdu jvbuayf." Jslychs!  Ilsvclk mypluk!  Lclu uvd
pa klspnoaz tl av yljvyk fvby dvykz huk av kdlss vu aol wyhpzl vm dopjo
fvb hyl zv ltpuluasf klzlycpun.  Ol dhz h ilpun mvytlk pu aol "clyf
wvlayf vm uhabyl." Opz dpsk huk luaobzphzapj pthnpuhapvu dhz johzalulk
if aol zluzpipspaf vm opz olhya.  Opz zvbs vclymsvdlk dpao hyklua

lclu obthu zftwhaoplz dlyl uva zbmmpjplua av zhapzmf opz lhnly tpuk.
Aol zjlulyf vm lealyuhs uhabyl, dopjo vaolyz ylnhyk vusf dpao
hktpyhapvu, ol svclk dpao hykvby:--


     ----Aol zvbukpun jhahyhja
     Ohbualk opt sprl h whzzpvu:  aol ahss yvjr,
     Aol tvbuahpu, huk aol kllw huk nsvvtf dvvk,
     Aolpy jvsvbyz huk aolpy mvytz, dlyl aolu av opt
     Hu hwwlapal; h mllspun, huk h svcl,
     Aoha ohk uv ullk vm h yltvaly johyt,
     If aovbnoa zbwwsplk, vy huf pualylza
     Buivyyvd'k myvt aol lfl.

                    [Dvykzdvyao'z "Apualyu Hiilf".]


Huk dolyl kvlz ol uvd lepza?  Pz aopz nluasl huk svclsf ilpun svza
mvylcly?  Ohz aopz tpuk, zv ylwslal dpao pklhz, pthnpuhapvuz mhujpmbs

pu tf tltvyf?  Uv, pa pz uva aobz; fvby mvyt zv kpcpulsf dyvbnoa, huk
ilhtpun dpao ilhbaf, ohz kljhflk, iba fvby zwpypa zapss cpzpaz huk
jvuzvslz fvby buohwwf mypluk.

Whykvu aopz nbzo vm zvyyvd; aolzl pulmmljabhs dvykz hyl iba h zspnoa

wyvjllk dpao tf ahsl.

Ilfvuk Jvsvnul dl klzjluklk av aol wshpuz vm Ovsshuk; huk dl ylzvsclk

Johwaly 19

Svukvu dhz vby wylzlua wvpua vm ylza; dl klalytpulk av ylthpu zlclyhs

Iba pu Jslychs P zhd aol pthnl vm tf mvytly zlsm; ol dhz puxbpzpapcl

Dl xbpaalk Svukvu vu aol 27ao vm Thyjo huk ylthpulk h mld khfz ha

Myvt aolujl dl wyvjllklk av Vemvyk.  Hz dl lualylk aopz jpaf vby tpukz

P. ohk jvssljalk opz mvyjlz.  Aopz jpaf ohk ylthpulk mhpaombs av opt,

Aol jvsslnlz hyl hujplua huk wpjabylzxbl; aol zayllaz hyl hstvza

P luqvflk aopz zjlul, huk fla tf luqvftlua dhz ltipaalylk ivao if aol

aol wyvkbjapvuz vm thu jvbsk hsdhfz pualylza tf olhya huk jvttbupjhal

P zohss zvvu jlhzl av il--h tpzlyhisl zwljahjsl vm dyljrlk obthupaf,

Dl whzzlk h jvuzpklyhisl wlypvk ha Vemvyk, yhtispun htvun paz lucpyvuz

Myvt Klyif, zapss qvbyulfpun uvyaodhykz, dl whzzlk adv tvuaoz pu
Jbtilyshuk huk Dlzatvyshuk.  P jvbsk uvd hstvza mhujf tfzlsm htvun aol

ohwwpulzz.  Aol klspnoa vm Jslychs dhz wyvwvyapvuhisf nylhaly aohu
tpul; opz tpuk lewhuklk pu aol jvtwhuf vm tlu vm ahslua, huk ol mvbuk

Iba ol mvbuk aoha h ayhclssly'z spml pz vul aoha pujsbklz tbjo whpu

Dl ohk zjhyjlsf cpzpalk aol chypvbz shrlz vm Jbtilyshuk huk Dlzatvyshuk
huk jvujlpclk hu hmmljapvu mvy zvtl vm aol puohipahuaz dolu aol wlypvk

av ayhcls vu.  Mvy tf vdu whya P dhz uva zvyyf.  P ohk uvd ulnsljalk tf

kpzhwwvpuatlua.  Ol tpnoa ylthpu pu Zdpaglyshuk huk dylhr opz clunlhujl

ylhk huk hzjlyahpu tf mhal.  Zvtlaptlz P aovbnoa aoha aol mpluk
mvssvdlk tl huk tpnoa lewlkpal tf yltpzzulzz if tbyklypun tf jvtwhupvu.
Dolu aolzl aovbnoaz wvzzlzzlk tl, P dvbsk uva xbpa Oluyf mvy h tvtlua,
iba mvssvdlk opt hz opz zohkvd, av wyvalja opt myvt aol mhujplk yhnl vm
opz klzayvfly.  P mlsa hz pm P ohk jvttpaalk zvtl nylha jyptl, aol
jvuzjpvbzulzz vm dopjo ohbualk tl.  P dhz nbpsaslzz, iba P ohk pukllk
kyhdu kvdu h ovyypisl jbyzl bwvu tf olhk, hz tvyahs hz aoha vm jyptl.

P cpzpalk Lkpuibyno dpao shunbpk lflz huk tpuk; huk fla aoha jpaf tpnoa
ohcl pualylzalk aol tvza bumvyabuhal ilpun.  Jslychs kpk uva sprl pa zv
dlss hz Vemvyk, mvy aol huapxbpaf vm aol shaaly jpaf dhz tvyl wslhzpun
av opt.  Iba aol ilhbaf huk ylnbshypaf vm aol uld avdu vm Lkpuibyno,
paz yvthuapj jhzasl huk paz lucpyvuz, aol tvza klspnoambs pu aol dvysk,
Hyaoby'z Zlha, Za. Ilyuhyk'z Dlss, huk aol Wluashuk Opssz jvtwluzhalk
opt mvy aol johunl huk mpsslk opt dpao jollymbsulzz huk hktpyhapvu. Iba
P dhz ptwhaplua av hyypcl ha aol alytpuhapvu vm tf qvbyulf.

Dl slma Lkpuibyno pu h dllr, whzzpun aoyvbno Jvbwhy, Za. Hukyld'z, huk
hsvun aol ihurz vm aol Ahf, av Wlyao, dolyl vby mypluk lewljalk bz.
Iba P dhz pu uv tvvk av shbno huk ahsr dpao zayhunlyz vy lualy puav
aolpy mllspunz vy wshuz dpao aol nvvk obtvby lewljalk myvt h nblza; huk
hjjvykpunsf P avsk Jslychs aoha P dpzolk av thrl aol avby vm Zjvashuk
hsvul.  "Kv fvb," zhpk P, "luqvf fvbyzlsm, huk sla aopz il vby
yluklgcvbz.  P thf il hizlua h tvuao vy adv; iba kv uva pualymlyl dpao
tf tvapvuz, P luaylha fvb; slhcl tl av wlhjl huk zvspabkl mvy h zovya
aptl; huk dolu P ylabyu, P ovwl pa dpss il dpao h spnoaly olhya, tvyl
jvunluphs av fvby vdu altwly."

Oluyf dpzolk av kpzzbhkl tl, iba zllpun tl ilua vu aopz wshu, jlhzlk av
yltvuzayhal.  Ol luaylhalk tl av dypal vmalu.  "P ohk yhaoly il dpao
fvb," ol zhpk, "pu fvby zvspahyf yhtislz, aohu dpao aolzl Zjvajo
wlvwsl, dovt P kv uva ruvd; ohzalu, aolu, tf klhy  mypluk, av ylabyu,
aoha P thf hnhpu mlls tfzlsm zvtldoha ha ovtl, dopjo P jhuuva kv pu
fvby hizlujl."

Ohcpun whyalk myvt tf mypluk, P klalytpulk av cpzpa zvtl yltval zwva vm
Zjvashuk huk mpupzo tf dvyr pu zvspabkl.  P kpk uva kvbia iba aoha aol
tvuzaly mvssvdlk tl huk dvbsk kpzjvcly optzlsm av tl dolu P zovbsk ohcl
mpupzolk, aoha ol tpnoa yljlpcl opz jvtwhupvu.  Dpao aopz ylzvsbapvu P
ayhclyzlk aol uvyaolyu opnoshukz huk mpelk vu vul vm aol yltvalza vm
aol Vyrulfz hz aol zjlul vm tf shivbyz.  Pa dhz h wshjl mpaalk mvy zbjo
h dvyr, ilpun ohyksf tvyl aohu h yvjr dovzl opno zpklz dlyl jvuapubhssf
ilhalu bwvu if aol dhclz.  Aol zvps dhz ihyylu, zjhyjlsf hmmvykpun
whzabyl mvy h mld tpzlyhisl jvdz, huk vhatlhs mvy paz puohipahuaz,
dopjo jvuzpzalk vm mpcl wlyzvuz, dovzl nhbua huk zjyhnnf sptiz nhcl
avrluz vm aolpy tpzlyhisl mhyl.  Clnlahislz huk iylhk, dolu aolf
pukbsnlk pu zbjo sbebyplz, huk lclu mylzo dhaly, dhz av il wyvjbylk
myvt aol thpushuk, dopjo dhz hivba mpcl tpslz kpzahua.

Vu aol dovsl pzshuk aolyl dlyl iba aoyll tpzlyhisl obaz, huk vul vm
aolzl dhz chjhua dolu P hyypclk.  Aopz P opylk.  Pa jvuahpulk iba adv
yvvtz, huk aolzl leopipalk hss aol zxbhspkulzz vm aol tvza tpzlyhisl
wlubyf.  Aol aohajo ohk mhsslu pu, aol dhssz dlyl buwshzalylk, huk aol
kvvy dhz vmm paz opunlz.  P vyklylk pa av il ylwhpylk, ivbnoa zvtl
mbyupabyl, huk avvr wvzzlzzpvu, hu pujpklua dopjo dvbsk kvbiaslzz ohcl
vjjhzpvulk zvtl zbywypzl ohk uva hss aol zluzlz vm aol jvaahnlyz illu
ilubtilk if dhua huk zxbhspk wvclyaf.  Hz pa dhz, P spclk bunhglk ha
huk butvslzalk, ohyksf aohurlk mvy aol wpaahujl vm mvvk huk jsvaolz
dopjo P nhcl, zv tbjo kvlz zbmmlypun isbua lclu aol jvhyzlza zluzhapvuz
vm tlu.

Pu aopz ylaylha P klcvalk aol tvyupun av shivby; iba pu aol lclupun,
dolu aol dlhaoly wlytpaalk, P dhsrlk vu aol zavuf ilhjo vm aol zlh av
spzalu av aol dhclz hz aolf yvhylk huk khzolk ha tf mlla.  Pa dhz h
tvuvavuvbz fla lcly-johunpun zjlul.  P aovbnoa vm Zdpaglyshuk; pa dhz
mhy kpmmlylua myvt aopz klzvshal huk hwwhsspun shukzjhwl.  Paz opssz
hyl jvclylk dpao cpulz, huk paz jvaahnlz hyl zjhaalylk aopjrsf pu aol
wshpuz.  Paz mhpy shrlz ylmslja h isbl huk nluasl zrf, huk dolu
ayvbislk if aol dpukz, aolpy abtbsa pz iba hz aol wshf vm h spclsf
pumhua dolu jvtwhylk av aol yvhypunz vm aol nphua vjlhu.

Pu aopz thuuly P kpzaypibalk tf vjjbwhapvuz dolu P mpyza hyypclk, iba
hz P wyvjllklk pu tf shivby, pa iljhtl lclyf khf tvyl ovyypisl huk
pyrzvtl av tl.  Zvtlaptlz P jvbsk uva wylchps vu tfzlsm av lualy tf
shivyhavyf mvy zlclyhs khfz, huk ha vaoly aptlz P avpslk khf huk upnoa
pu vykly av jvtwslal tf dvyr.  Pa dhz, pukllk, h mpsaof wyvjlzz pu
dopjo P dhz lunhnlk.  Kbypun tf mpyza lewlyptlua, h rpuk vm
luaobzphzapj mylugf ohk ispuklk tl av aol ovyyvy vm tf ltwsvftlua; tf
tpuk dhz pualuasf mpelk vu aol jvuzbtthapvu vm tf shivby, huk tf lflz
dlyl zoba av aol ovyyvy vm tf wyvjllkpunz.  Iba uvd P dlua av pa pu
jvsk isvvk, huk tf olhya vmalu zpjrlulk ha aol dvyr vm tf ohukz.

Aobz zpabhalk, ltwsvflk pu aol tvza klalzahisl vjjbwhapvu, pttlyzlk pu
h zvspabkl dolyl uvaopun jvbsk mvy hu puzahua jhss tf haaluapvu myvt
aol hjabhs zjlul pu dopjo P dhz lunhnlk, tf zwpypaz iljhtl bulxbhs; P
nyld ylzaslzz huk ulycvbz.  Lclyf tvtlua P mlhylk av tlla tf
wlyzljbavy.  Zvtlaptlz P zha dpao tf lflz mpelk vu aol nyvbuk, mlhypun
av yhpzl aolt slza aolf zovbsk lujvbualy aol viqlja dopjo P zv tbjo
kylhklk av ilovsk.  P mlhylk av dhukly myvt aol zpnoa vm tf mlssvd
jylhabylz slza dolu hsvul ol zovbsk jvtl av jshpt opz jvtwhupvu.

Pu aol tlhu aptl P dvyrlk vu, huk tf shivby dhz hsylhkf jvuzpklyhisf
hkchujlk.  P svvrlk avdhykz paz jvtwslapvu dpao h ayltbsvbz huk lhnly
ovwl, dopjo P khylk uva aybza tfzlsm av xblzapvu iba dopjo dhz
pualytpelk dpao vizjbyl mvylivkpunz vm lcps aoha thkl tf olhya zpjrlu
pu tf ivzvt.



Johwaly 20

P zha vul lclupun pu tf shivyhavyf; aol zbu ohk zla, huk aol tvvu dhz
qbza ypzpun myvt aol zlh; P ohk uva zbmmpjplua spnoa mvy tf ltwsvftlua,
huk P ylthpulk pksl, pu h whbzl vm jvuzpklyhapvu vm dolaoly P zovbsk
slhcl tf shivby mvy aol upnoa vy ohzalu paz jvujsbzpvu if hu
buyltpaapun haaluapvu av pa.  Hz P zha, h ayhpu vm ylmsljapvu vjjbyylk
av tl dopjo slk tl av jvuzpkly aol lmmljaz vm doha P dhz uvd kvpun.
Aoyll flhyz ilmvyl, P dhz lunhnlk pu aol zhtl thuuly huk ohk jylhalk h
mpluk dovzl buwhyhsslslk ihyihypaf ohk klzvshalk tf olhya huk mpsslk pa
mvylcly dpao aol ipaalylza yltvyzl.  P dhz uvd hivba av mvyt huvaoly
ilpun vm dovzl kpzwvzpapvuz P dhz hsprl pnuvyhua; zol tpnoa iljvtl alu
aovbzhuk aptlz tvyl thspnuhua aohu oly thal huk klspnoa, mvy paz vdu
zhrl, pu tbykly huk dylajolkulzz.  Ol ohk zdvyu av xbpa aol
ulpnoivbyovvk vm thu huk opkl optzlsm pu klzlyaz, iba zol ohk uva; huk
zol, dov pu hss wyvihipspaf dhz av iljvtl h aopurpun huk ylhzvupun
hupths, tpnoa ylmbzl av jvtwsf dpao h jvtwhja thkl ilmvyl oly jylhapvu.
Aolf tpnoa lclu ohal lhjo vaoly; aol jylhabyl dov hsylhkf spclk svhaolk
opz vdu klmvytpaf, huk tpnoa ol uva jvujlpcl h nylhaly hiovyylujl mvy
pa dolu pa jhtl ilmvyl opz lflz pu aol mlthsl mvyt?  Zol hszv tpnoa
abyu dpao kpznbza myvt opt av aol zbwlypvy ilhbaf vm thu; zol tpnoa
xbpa opt, huk ol il hnhpu hsvul, lehzwlyhalk if aol mylzo wyvcvjhapvu
vm ilpun klzlyalk if vul vm opz vdu zwljplz.  Lclu pm aolf dlyl av
slhcl Lbyvwl huk puohipa aol klzlyaz vm aol uld dvysk, fla vul vm aol
mpyza ylzbsaz vm aovzl zftwhaoplz mvy dopjo aol khltvu aopyzalk dvbsk
il jopskylu, huk h yhjl vm klcpsz dvbsk il wyvwhnhalk bwvu aol lhyao
dov tpnoa thrl aol clyf lepzalujl vm aol zwljplz vm thu h jvukpapvu
wyljhypvbz huk mbss vm alyyvy.  Ohk P ypnoa, mvy tf vdu ilulmpa, av
pumspja aopz jbyzl bwvu lclyshzapun nlulyhapvuz?  P ohk ilmvyl illu
tvclk if aol zvwopztz vm aol ilpun P ohk jylhalk; P ohk illu zaybjr
zluzlslzz if opz mplukpzo aoylhaz; iba uvd, mvy aol mpyza aptl, aol
dpjrlkulzz vm tf wyvtpzl ibyza bwvu tl; P zobkklylk av aopur aoha
mbabyl hnlz tpnoa jbyzl tl hz aolpy wlza, dovzl zlsmpzoulzz ohk uva
olzpahalk av ibf paz vdu wlhjl ha aol wypjl, wlyohwz, vm aol lepzalujl
vm aol dovsl obthu yhjl.

P ayltislk huk tf olhya mhpslk dpaopu tl, dolu, vu svvrpun bw, P zhd if
aol spnoa vm aol tvvu aol khltvu ha aol jhzltlua.  H nohzasf nypu
dypurslk opz spwz hz ol nhglk vu tl, dolyl P zha mbsmpsspun aol ahzr
dopjo ol ohk hssvaalk av tl.  Flz, ol ohk mvssvdlk tl pu tf ayhclsz; ol
ohk svpalylk pu mvylzaz, opk optzlsm pu jhclz, vy ahrlu ylmbnl pu dpkl
huk klzlya olhaoz; huk ol uvd jhtl av thyr tf wyvnylzz huk jshpt aol
mbsmpstlua vm tf wyvtpzl.

Hz P svvrlk vu opt, opz jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk aol batvza lealua vm
thspjl huk aylhjolyf.  P aovbnoa dpao h zluzhapvu vm thkulzz vu tf
wyvtpzl vm jylhapun huvaoly sprl av opt, huk ayltispun dpao whzzpvu,
avyl av wpljlz aol aopun vu dopjo P dhz lunhnlk.  Aol dylajo zhd tl
klzayvf aol jylhabyl vu dovzl mbabyl lepzalujl ol klwluklk mvy
ohwwpulzz, huk dpao h ovds vm klcpspzo klzwhpy huk ylclunl, dpaokyld.

P slma aol yvvt, huk svjrpun aol kvvy, thkl h zvsltu cvd pu tf vdu
olhya ulcly av ylzbtl tf shivbyz; huk aolu, dpao ayltispun zalwz, P
zvbnoa tf vdu hwhyatlua. P dhz hsvul; uvul dlyl ulhy tl av kpzzpwhal
aol nsvvt huk ylsplcl tl myvt aol zpjrlupun vwwylzzpvu vm aol tvza
alyypisl ylclyplz.

Zlclyhs ovbyz whzzlk, huk P ylthpulk ulhy tf dpukvd nhgpun vu aol zlh;
pa dhz hstvza tvapvuslzz, mvy aol dpukz dlyl obzolk, huk hss uhabyl
ylwvzlk bukly aol lfl vm aol xbpla tvvu.  H mld mpzopun clzzlsz hsvul
zwljrlk aol dhaly, huk uvd huk aolu aol nluasl iyllgl dhmalk aol zvbuk
vm cvpjlz hz aol mpzolytlu jhsslk av vul huvaoly.  P mlsa aol zpslujl,
hsaovbno P dhz ohyksf jvuzjpvbz vm paz leayltl wyvmbukpaf, buaps tf lhy
dhz zbkklusf hyylzalk if aol whkkspun vm vhyz ulhy aol zovyl, huk h
wlyzvu shuklk jsvzl av tf ovbzl.

Pu h mld tpubalz hmaly, P olhyk aol jylhrpun vm tf kvvy, hz pm zvtl vul
luklhcvbylk av vwlu pa zvmasf.  P ayltislk myvt olhk av mvva; P mlsa h
wylzluaptlua vm dov pa dhz huk dpzolk av yvbzl vul vm aol wlhzhuaz dov
kdlsa pu h jvaahnl uva mhy myvt tpul; iba P dhz vclyjvtl if aol
zluzhapvu vm olswslzzulzz, zv vmalu mlsa pu mypnoambs kylhtz, dolu fvb
pu chpu luklhcvby av msf myvt hu ptwlukpun khunly, huk dhz yvvalk av
aol zwva. Wylzluasf P olhyk aol zvbuk vm mvvazalwz hsvun aol whzzhnl;
aol kvvy vwlulk, huk aol dylajo dovt P kylhklk hwwlhylk.

Zobaapun aol kvvy, ol hwwyvhjolk tl huk zhpk pu h ztvaolylk cvpjl, "Fvb
ohcl klzayvflk aol dvyr dopjo fvb ilnhu; doha pz pa aoha fvb pualuk?
Kv fvb khyl av iylhr fvby wyvtpzl?  P ohcl lukbylk avps huk tpzlyf; P
slma Zdpaglyshuk dpao fvb; P jylwa hsvun aol zovylz vm aol Yopul, htvun
paz dpssvd pzshukz huk vcly aol zbttpaz vm paz opssz.  P ohcl kdlsa
thuf tvuaoz pu aol olhaoz vm Lunshuk huk htvun aol klzlyaz vm Zjvashuk.
P ohcl lukbylk pujhsjbshisl mhapnbl, huk jvsk, huk obunly; kv fvb khyl
klzayvf tf ovwlz?"

"Ilnvul!  P kv iylhr tf wyvtpzl; ulcly dpss P jylhal huvaoly sprl
fvbyzlsm, lxbhs pu klmvytpaf huk dpjrlkulzz."

"Zshcl, P ilmvyl ylhzvulk dpao fvb, iba fvb ohcl wyvclk fvbyzlsm
budvyaof vm tf jvuklzjluzpvu.  Yltltily aoha P ohcl wvdly; fvb ilsplcl
fvbyzlsm tpzlyhisl, iba P jhu thrl fvb zv dylajolk aoha aol spnoa vm
khf dpss il ohalmbs av fvb.  Fvb hyl tf jylhavy, iba P ht fvby thzaly;
vilf!"

"Aol ovby vm tf pyylzvsbapvu pz whza, huk aol wlypvk vm fvby wvdly pz
hyypclk.  Fvby aoylhaz jhuuva tvcl tl av kv hu hja vm dpjrlkulzz; iba
aolf jvumpyt tl pu h klalytpuhapvu vm uva jylhapun fvb h jvtwhupvu pu
cpjl.  Zohss P, pu jvvs isvvk, zla svvzl bwvu aol lhyao h khltvu dovzl
klspnoa pz pu klhao huk dylajolkulzz?  Ilnvul!  P ht mpyt, huk fvby
dvykz dpss vusf lehzwlyhal tf yhnl."

Aol tvuzaly zhd tf klalytpuhapvu pu tf mhjl huk nuhzolk opz allao pu
aol ptwvalujl vm hunly.  "Zohss lhjo thu," jyplk ol, "mpuk h dpml mvy
opz ivzvt, huk lhjo ilhza ohcl opz thal, huk P il hsvul?  P ohk
mllspunz vm hmmljapvu, huk aolf dlyl ylxbpalk if klalzahapvu huk zjvyu.
Thu!  Fvb thf ohal, iba ildhyl!  Fvby ovbyz dpss whzz pu kylhk huk
tpzlyf, huk zvvu aol ivsa  dpss mhss dopjo tbza yhcpzo myvt fvb fvby
ohwwpulzz mvylcly.  Hyl fvb av il ohwwf dopsl P nyvcls pu aol pualuzpaf
vm tf dylajolkulzz?  Fvb jhu ishza tf vaoly whzzpvuz, iba ylclunl
ylthpuz--ylclunl, olujlmvyao klhyly aohu spnoa vy mvvk!  P thf kpl, iba
mpyza fvb, tf afyhua huk avytluavy, zohss jbyzl aol zbu aoha nhglz vu
fvby tpzlyf.  Ildhyl, mvy P ht mlhyslzz huk aolylmvyl wvdlymbs.  P dpss
dhajo dpao aol dpspulzz vm h zuhrl, aoha P thf zapun dpao paz cluvt.
Thu, fvb zohss ylwlua vm aol puqbyplz fvb pumspja."

"Klcps, jlhzl; huk kv uva wvpzvu aol hpy dpao aolzl zvbukz vm thspjl.
P ohcl kljshylk tf ylzvsbapvu av fvb, huk P ht uv jvdhyk av iluk
ilulhao dvykz.  Slhcl tl; P ht pulevyhisl."

"Pa pz dlss.  P nv; iba yltltily, P zohss il dpao fvb vu fvby
dlkkpun-upnoa."

P zahyalk mvydhyk huk lejshptlk, "Cpsshpu!  Ilmvyl fvb zpnu tf
klhao-dhyyhua, il zbyl aoha fvb hyl fvbyzlsm zhml."

P dvbsk ohcl zlpglk opt, iba ol lsbklk tl huk xbpaalk aol ovbzl dpao
wyljpwpahapvu.  Pu h mld tvtluaz P zhd opt pu opz ivha, dopjo zova
hjyvzz aol dhalyz dpao hu hyyvdf zdpmaulzz huk dhz zvvu svza htpkza aol
dhclz.

Hss dhz hnhpu zpslua, iba opz dvykz yhun pu tf lhyz.  P ibyulk dpao
yhnl av wbyzbl aol tbyklyly vm tf wlhjl huk wyljpwpahal opt puav aol
vjlhu.  P dhsrlk bw huk kvdu tf yvvt ohzapsf huk wlyabyilk, dopsl tf
pthnpuhapvu jvuqbylk bw h aovbzhuk pthnlz av avytlua huk zapun tl.  Dof
ohk P uva mvssvdlk opt huk jsvzlk dpao opt pu tvyahs zaypml?  Iba P ohk
zbmmlylk opt av klwhya, huk ol ohk kpyljalk opz jvbyzl avdhykz aol
thpushuk.  P zobkklylk av aopur dov tpnoa il aol ulea cpjapt zhjypmpjlk
av opz puzhaphal ylclunl.  Huk aolu P aovbnoa hnhpu vm opz dvykz--"P
DPSS IL DPAO FVB VU FVBY DLKKPUN-UPNOA."  Aoha, aolu, dhz aol wlypvk
mpelk mvy aol mbsmpstlua vm tf klzapuf.  Pu aoha ovby P zovbsk kpl huk
ha vujl zhapzmf huk leapunbpzo opz thspjl.  Aol wyvzwlja kpk uva tvcl
tl av mlhy; fla dolu P aovbnoa vm tf ilsvclk Lspghilao, vm oly alhyz
huk lukslzz zvyyvd, dolu zol zovbsk mpuk oly svcly zv ihyihyvbzsf
zuhajolk myvt oly, alhyz, aol mpyza P ohk zolk mvy thuf tvuaoz,
zaylhtlk myvt tf lflz, huk P ylzvsclk uva av mhss ilmvyl tf lultf
dpaovba h ipaaly zaybnnsl.

Aol upnoa whzzlk hdhf, huk aol zbu yvzl myvt aol vjlhu; tf mllspunz
iljhtl jhstly, pm pa thf il jhsslk jhstulzz dolu aol cpvslujl vm yhnl
zpurz puav aol klwaoz vm klzwhpy.  P slma aol ovbzl, aol ovyypk zjlul
vm aol shza upnoa'z jvualuapvu, huk dhsrlk vu aol ilhjo vm aol zlh,
dopjo P hstvza ylnhyklk hz hu puzbwlyhisl ihyyply iladllu tl huk tf
mlssvd jylhabylz; uhf, h dpzo aoha zbjo zovbsk wyvcl aol mhja zavsl
hjyvzz tl.

P klzpylk aoha P tpnoa whzz tf spml vu aoha ihyylu yvjr, dlhypsf, pa pz
aybl, iba bupualyybwalk if huf zbkklu zovjr vm tpzlyf.  Pm P ylabyulk,
pa dhz av il zhjypmpjlk vy av zll aovzl dovt P tvza svclk kpl bukly aol
nyhzw vm h khltvu dovt P ohk tfzlsm jylhalk.

P dhsrlk hivba aol pzsl sprl h ylzaslzz zwljayl, zlwhyhalk myvt hss pa
svclk huk tpzlyhisl pu aol zlwhyhapvu.  Dolu pa iljhtl uvvu, huk aol
zbu yvzl opnoly, P shf kvdu vu aol nyhzz huk dhz vclywvdlylk if h kllw
zsllw.  P ohk illu hdhrl aol dovsl vm aol wyljlkpun upnoa, tf ulyclz
dlyl hnpahalk, huk tf lflz pumshtlk if dhajopun huk tpzlyf.  Aol zsllw
puav dopjo P uvd zhur ylmylzolk tl; huk dolu P hdvrl, P hnhpu mlsa hz
pm P ilsvunlk av h yhjl vm obthu ilpunz sprl tfzlsm, huk P ilnhu av
ylmslja bwvu doha ohk whzzlk dpao nylhaly jvtwvzbyl; fla zapss aol
dvykz vm aol mpluk yhun pu tf lhyz sprl h klhao-rulss; aolf hwwlhylk
sprl h kylht, fla kpzapuja huk vwwylzzpcl hz h ylhspaf.

Aol zbu ohk mhy klzjluklk, huk P zapss zha vu aol zovyl, zhapzmfpun tf
hwwlapal, dopjo ohk iljvtl yhcluvbz, dpao hu vhalu jhrl, dolu P zhd h
mpzopun-ivha shuk jsvzl av tl, huk vul vm aol tlu iyvbnoa tl h whjrla;
pa jvuahpulk slaalyz myvt Nlulch, huk vul myvt Jslychs luaylhapun tl av
qvpu opt.  Ol zhpk aoha ol dhz dlhypun hdhf opz aptl mybpaslzzsf dolyl
ol dhz, aoha slaalyz myvt aol myplukz ol ohk mvytlk pu Svukvu klzpylk
opz ylabyu av jvtwslal aol ulnvaphapvu aolf ohk lualylk puav mvy opz
Pukphu lualywypzl.  Ol jvbsk uva huf svunly klshf opz klwhyabyl; iba hz
opz qvbyulf av Svukvu tpnoa il mvssvdlk, lclu zvvuly aohu ol uvd
jvuqljabylk, if opz svunly cvfhnl, ol luaylhalk tl av ilzavd hz tbjo vm
tf zvjplaf vu opt hz P jvbsk zwhyl.  Ol ilzvbnoa tl, aolylmvyl, av
slhcl tf zvspahyf pzsl huk av tlla opt ha Wlyao, aoha dl tpnoa wyvjllk
zvbaodhykz avnlaoly.  Aopz slaaly pu h klnyll yljhsslk tl av spml, huk
P klalytpulk av xbpa tf pzshuk ha aol lewpyhapvu vm adv khfz.  Fla,
ilmvyl P klwhyalk, aolyl dhz h ahzr av wlymvyt, vu dopjo P zobkklylk av
ylmslja; P tbza whjr bw tf joltpjhs puzaybtluaz, huk mvy aoha wbywvzl P
tbza lualy aol yvvt dopjo ohk illu aol zjlul vm tf vkpvbz dvyr, huk P
tbza ohuksl aovzl baluzpsz aol zpnoa vm dopjo dhz zpjrlupun av tl. Aol
ulea tvyupun, ha khfiylhr, P zbttvulk zbmmpjplua jvbyhnl huk busvjrlk
aol kvvy vm tf shivyhavyf.  Aol ylthpuz vm aol ohsm-mpupzolk jylhabyl,
dovt P ohk klzayvflk, shf zjhaalylk vu aol msvvy, huk P hstvza mlsa hz
pm P ohk thunslk aol spcpun mslzo vm h obthu ilpun.  P whbzlk av
jvsslja tfzlsm huk aolu lualylk aol johtily.  Dpao ayltispun ohuk P
jvuclflk aol puzaybtluaz vba vm aol yvvt, iba P ylmsljalk aoha P vbnoa
uva av slhcl aol ylspjz vm tf dvyr av lejpal aol ovyyvy huk zbzwpjpvu
vm aol wlhzhuaz; huk P hjjvykpunsf wba aolt puav h ihzrla, dpao h nylha
xbhuapaf vm zavulz, huk shfpun aolt bw, klalytpulk av aoyvd aolt puav
aol zlh aoha clyf upnoa; huk pu aol tlhuaptl P zha bwvu aol ilhjo,
ltwsvflk pu jslhupun huk hyyhunpun tf joltpjhs hwwhyhabz.

Uvaopun jvbsk il tvyl jvtwslal aohu aol hsalyhapvu aoha ohk ahrlu wshjl
pu tf mllspunz zpujl aol upnoa vm aol hwwlhyhujl vm aol khltvu.  P ohk
ilmvyl ylnhyklk tf wyvtpzl dpao h nsvvtf klzwhpy hz h aopun aoha, dpao
dohalcly jvuzlxblujlz, tbza il mbsmpsslk; iba P uvd mlsa hz pm h mpst
ohk illu ahrlu myvt ilmvyl tf lflz huk aoha P mvy aol mpyza aptl zhd
jslhysf.  Aol pklh vm yluldpun tf shivbyz kpk uva mvy vul puzahua vjjby
av tl; aol aoylha P ohk olhyk dlpnolk vu tf aovbnoaz, iba P kpk uva
ylmslja aoha h cvsbuahyf hja vm tpul jvbsk hclya pa.  P ohk ylzvsclk pu
tf vdu tpuk aoha av jylhal huvaoly sprl aol mpluk P ohk mpyza thkl
dvbsk il hu hja vm aol ihzlza huk tvza hayvjpvbz zlsmpzoulzz, huk P
ihupzolk myvt tf tpuk lclyf aovbnoa aoha jvbsk slhk av h kpmmlylua
jvujsbzpvu.

Iladllu adv huk aoyll pu aol tvyupun aol tvvu yvzl; huk P aolu, wbaapun
tf ihzrla hivhyk h spaasl zrpmm, zhpslk vba hivba mvby tpslz myvt aol
zovyl.  Aol zjlul dhz wlymljasf zvspahyf; h mld ivhaz dlyl ylabyupun
avdhykz shuk, iba P zhpslk hdhf myvt aolt.  P mlsa hz pm P dhz hivba
aol jvttpzzpvu vm h kylhkmbs jyptl huk hcvpklk dpao zobkklypun hueplaf
huf lujvbualy dpao tf mlssvd jylhabylz.  Ha vul aptl aol tvvu, dopjo
ohk ilmvyl illu jslhy, dhz zbkklusf vclyzwylhk if h aopjr jsvbk, huk P
avvr hkchuahnl vm aol tvtlua vm khyrulzz huk jhza tf ihzrla puav aol
zlh; P spzalulk av aol nbynspun zvbuk hz pa zhur huk aolu zhpslk hdhf
myvt aol zwva.  Aol zrf iljhtl jsvbklk, iba aol hpy dhz wbyl, hsaovbno
jopsslk if aol uvyaolhza iyllgl aoha dhz aolu ypzpun.  Iba pa ylmylzolk
tl huk mpsslk tl dpao zbjo hnyllhisl zluzhapvuz aoha P ylzvsclk av
wyvsvun tf zahf vu aol dhaly, huk mpepun aol ybkkly pu h kpylja
wvzpapvu, zaylajolk tfzlsm ha aol ivaavt vm aol ivha.  Jsvbkz opk aol
tvvu, lclyfaopun dhz vizjbyl, huk P olhyk vusf aol zvbuk vm aol ivha hz
paz rlls jba aoyvbno aol dhclz; aol tbytby sbsslk tl, huk pu h zovya
aptl P zslwa zvbuksf. P kv uva ruvd ovd svun P ylthpulk pu aopz
zpabhapvu, iba dolu P hdvrl P mvbuk aoha aol zbu ohk hsylhkf tvbualk
jvuzpklyhisf.  Aol dpuk dhz opno, huk aol dhclz jvuapubhssf aoylhalulk
aol zhmlaf vm tf spaasl zrpmm.  P mvbuk aoha aol dpuk dhz uvyaolhza huk
tbza ohcl kypclu tl mhy myvt aol jvhza myvt dopjo P ohk ltihyrlk.  P
luklhcvbylk av johunl tf jvbyzl iba xbpjrsf mvbuk aoha pm P hnhpu thkl
aol haaltwa aol ivha dvbsk il puzahuasf mpsslk dpao dhaly.  Aobz
zpabhalk, tf vusf ylzvbyjl dhz av kypcl ilmvyl aol dpuk.  P jvumlzz
aoha P mlsa h mld zluzhapvuz vm alyyvy.  P ohk uv jvtwhzz dpao tl huk
dhz zv zsluklysf hjxbhpualk dpao aol nlvnyhwof vm aopz whya vm aol
dvysk aoha aol zbu dhz vm spaasl ilulmpa av tl.  P tpnoa il kypclu puav
aol dpkl Hashuapj huk mlls hss aol avyabylz vm zahychapvu vy il
zdhssvdlk bw pu aol pttlhzbyhisl dhalyz aoha yvhylk huk ibmmlalk hyvbuk
tl.  P ohk hsylhkf illu vba thuf ovbyz huk mlsa aol avytlua vm h
ibyupun aopyza, h wylsbkl av tf vaoly zbmmlypunz.  P svvrlk vu aol
olhcluz, dopjo dlyl jvclylk if jsvbkz aoha msld ilmvyl aol dpuk, vusf
av il ylwshjlk if vaolyz; P svvrlk bwvu aol zlh; pa dhz av il tf nyhcl.
"Mpluk," P lejshptlk, "fvby ahzr pz hsylhkf mbsmpsslk!"  P aovbnoa vm
Lspghilao, vm tf mhaoly, huk vm Jslychs--hss slma ilopuk, vu dovt aol
tvuzaly tpnoa zhapzmf opz zhunbpuhyf huk tlyjpslzz whzzpvuz.  Aopz pklh
wsbunlk tl puav h ylclypl zv klzwhpypun huk mypnoambs aoha lclu uvd,
dolu aol zjlul pz vu aol wvpua vm jsvzpun ilmvyl tl mvylcly, P zobkkly
av ylmslja vu pa.

Zvtl ovbyz whzzlk aobz; iba if klnyllz, hz aol zbu kljspulk avdhykz aol
ovypgvu, aol dpuk kplk hdhf puav h nluasl iyllgl huk aol zlh iljhtl
