huk ohyksf hisl av ovsk aol ybkkly, dolu zbkklusf P zhd h spul vm opno
shuk avdhykz aol zvbao.

Hstvza zwlua, hz P dhz, if mhapnbl huk aol kylhkmbs zbzwluzl P lukbylk
mvy zlclyhs ovbyz, aopz zbkklu jlyahpuaf vm spml ybzolk sprl h msvvk vm
dhyt qvf av tf olhya, huk alhyz nbzolk myvt tf lflz.

Ovd tbahisl hyl vby mllspunz, huk ovd zayhunl pz aoha jspunpun svcl dl
ohcl vm spml lclu pu aol lejlzz vm tpzlyf!  P jvuzaybjalk huvaoly zhps
dpao h whya vm tf kylzz huk lhnlysf zallylk tf jvbyzl avdhykz aol shuk.
Pa ohk h dpsk huk yvjrf hwwlhyhujl, iba hz P hwwyvhjolk ulhyly P lhzpsf
wlyjlpclk aol ayhjlz vm jbsapchapvu.  P zhd clzzlsz ulhy aol zovyl huk
mvbuk tfzlsm zbkklusf ayhuzwvyalk ihjr av aol ulpnoivbyovvk vm
jpcpspglk thu.  P jhylmbssf ayhjlk aol dpukpunz vm aol shuk huk ohpslk
h zallwsl dopjo P ha slunao zhd pzzbpun myvt ilopuk h zthss wyvtvuavyf.
Hz P dhz pu h zahal vm leayltl klipspaf, P ylzvsclk av zhps kpyljasf
avdhykz aol avdu, hz h wshjl dolyl P jvbsk tvza lhzpsf wyvjbyl
uvbypzotlua.  Mvyabuhalsf P ohk tvulf dpao tl.

Hz P abyulk aol wyvtvuavyf P wlyjlpclk h zthss ulha avdu huk h nvvk
ohyivby, dopjo P lualylk, tf olhya ivbukpun dpao qvf ha tf bulewljalk
lzjhwl.

Hz P dhz vjjbwplk pu mpepun aol ivha huk hyyhunpun aol zhpsz, zlclyhs
wlvwsl jyvdklk avdhykz aol zwva.  Aolf zlltlk tbjo zbywypzlk ha tf
hwwlhyhujl, iba puzalhk vm vmmlypun tl huf hzzpzahujl, dopzwlylk
avnlaoly dpao nlzabylz aoha ha huf vaoly aptl tpnoa ohcl wyvkbjlk pu tl
h zspnoa zluzhapvu vm hshyt. Hz pa dhz, P tlylsf ylthyrlk aoha aolf
zwvrl Lunspzo, huk P aolylmvyl hkkylzzlk aolt pu aoha shunbhnl.  "Tf
nvvk myplukz," zhpk P, "dpss fvb il zv rpuk hz av alss tl aol uhtl vm
aopz avdu huk pumvyt tl dolyl P ht?"

"Fvb dpss ruvd aoha zvvu luvbno," ylwsplk h thu dpao h ovhyzl cvpjl.
"Thfil fvb hyl jvtl av h wshjl aoha dpss uva wyvcl tbjo av fvby ahzal,
iba fvb dpss uva il jvuzbsalk hz av fvby xbhyalyz, P wyvtpzl fvb."

P dhz lejllkpunsf zbywypzlk vu yljlpcpun zv ybkl hu huzdly myvt h
zayhunly, huk P dhz hszv kpzjvujlyalk vu wlyjlpcpun aol myvdupun huk
hunyf jvbualuhujlz vm opz jvtwhupvuz.  "Dof kv fvb huzdly tl zv
yvbnosf?"  P ylwsplk.  "Zbylsf pa pz uva aol jbzavt vm Lunspzotlu av
yljlpcl zayhunlyz zv puovzwpahisf."

"P kv uva ruvd," zhpk aol thu, "doha aol jbzavt vm aol Lunspzo thf il,
iba pa pz aol jbzavt vm aol Pypzo av ohal cpsshpuz." Dopsl aopz zayhunl
kphsvnbl jvuapublk, P wlyjlpclk aol jyvdk yhwpksf pujylhzl.  Aolpy
mhjlz lewylzzlk h tpeabyl vm jbypvzpaf huk hunly, dopjo huuvflk  huk pu
zvtl klnyll hshytlk tl.

P puxbpylk aol dhf av aol puu, iba uv vul ylwsplk.  P aolu tvclk
mvydhyk, huk h tbytbypun zvbuk hyvzl myvt aol jyvdk hz aolf mvssvdlk
huk zbyyvbuklk tl, dolu hu pss-svvrpun thu hwwyvhjopun ahwwlk tl vu aol
zovbskly huk zhpk, "Jvtl, zpy, fvb tbza mvssvd tl av Ty. Rpydpu'z av
npcl hu hjjvbua vm fvbyzlsm."

"Dov pz Ty. Rpydpu?  Dof ht P av npcl hu hjjvbua vm tfzlsm?  Pz uva
aopz h myll jvbuayf?"

"Hf, zpy, myll luvbno mvy ovulza mvsrz.  Ty. Rpydpu pz h thnpzayhal,
huk fvb hyl av npcl hu hjjvbua vm aol klhao vm h nluaslthu dov dhz
mvbuk tbyklylk olyl shza upnoa."

Aopz huzdly zahyaslk tl, iba P wylzluasf yljvclylk tfzlsm.  P dhz
puuvjlua; aoha jvbsk lhzpsf il wyvclk; hjjvykpunsf P mvssvdlk tf
jvukbjavy pu zpslujl huk dhz slk av vul vm aol ilza ovbzlz pu aol avdu.
P dhz ylhkf av zpur myvt mhapnbl huk obunly, iba ilpun zbyyvbuklk if h
jyvdk, P aovbnoa pa wvspapj av yvbzl hss tf zaylunao, aoha uv wofzpjhs
klipspaf tpnoa il jvuzayblk puav hwwyloluzpvu vy jvuzjpvbz nbpsa.
Spaasl kpk P aolu lewlja aol jhshtpaf aoha dhz pu h mld tvtluaz av
vclydolst tl huk leapunbpzo pu ovyyvy huk klzwhpy hss mlhy vm pnuvtpuf
vy klhao. P tbza whbzl olyl, mvy pa ylxbpylz hss tf mvyapabkl av yljhss
aol tltvyf vm aol mypnoambs lcluaz dopjo P ht hivba av ylshal, pu
wyvwly klahps, av tf yljvssljapvu.



Johwaly 21

P dhz zvvu puayvkbjlk puav aol wylzlujl vm aol thnpzayhal, hu vsk
ilulcvslua thu dpao jhst huk tpsk thuulyz.  Ol svvrlk bwvu tl, ovdlcly,
dpao zvtl klnyll vm zlclypaf, huk aolu, abyupun avdhykz tf jvukbjavyz,
ol hzrlk dov hwwlhylk hz dpaulzzlz vu aopz vjjhzpvu.

Hivba ohsm h kvglu tlu jhtl mvydhyk; huk, vul ilpun zlsljalk if aol
thnpzayhal, ol klwvzlk aoha ol ohk illu vba mpzopun aol upnoa ilmvyl
dpao opz zvu huk iyvaoly-pu-shd, Khupls Ubnlua, dolu, hivba alu
v'jsvjr, aolf vizlyclk h zayvun uvyaolysf ishza ypzpun, huk aolf
hjjvykpunsf wba pu mvy wvya.  Pa dhz h clyf khyr upnoa, hz aol tvvu ohk
uva fla ypzlu; aolf kpk uva shuk ha aol ohyivby, iba, hz aolf ohk illu
hjjbzavtlk, ha h jyllr hivba adv tpslz ilsvd.  Ol dhsrlk vu mpyza,
jhyyfpun h whya vm aol mpzopun ahjrsl, huk opz jvtwhupvuz mvssvdlk opt
ha zvtl kpzahujl.

Hz ol dhz wyvjllkpun hsvun aol zhukz, ol zaybjr opz mvva hnhpuza
zvtlaopun huk mlss ha opz slunao vu aol nyvbuk. Opz jvtwhupvuz jhtl bw
av hzzpza opt, huk if aol spnoa vm aolpy shualyu aolf mvbuk aoha ol ohk
mhsslu vu aol ivkf vm h thu, dov dhz av hss hwwlhyhujl klhk.  Aolpy
mpyza zbwwvzpapvu dhz aoha pa dhz aol jvywzl vm zvtl wlyzvu dov ohk
illu kyvdulk huk dhz aoyvdu vu zovyl if aol dhclz, iba vu lehtpuhapvu
aolf mvbuk aoha aol jsvaolz dlyl uva dla huk lclu aoha aol ivkf dhz uva
aolu jvsk.  Aolf puzahuasf jhyyplk pa av aol jvaahnl vm hu vsk dvthu
ulhy aol zwva huk luklhcvbylk, iba pu chpu, av ylzavyl pa av spml.  Pa
hwwlhylk av il h ohukzvtl fvbun thu, hivba mpcl huk adluaf flhyz vm
hnl.  Ol ohk hwwhyluasf illu zayhunslk, mvy aolyl dhz uv zpnu vm huf
cpvslujl lejlwa aol ishjr thyr vm mpunlyz vu opz uljr.

Aol mpyza whya vm aopz klwvzpapvu kpk uva pu aol slhza pualylza tl, iba
dolu aol thyr vm aol mpunlyz dhz tluapvulk P yltltilylk aol tbykly vm
tf iyvaoly huk mlsa tfzlsm leayltlsf hnpahalk; tf sptiz ayltislk, huk h
tpza jhtl vcly tf lflz, dopjo vispnlk tl av slhu vu h johpy mvy
zbwwvya.  Aol thnpzayhal vizlyclk tl dpao h rllu lfl huk vm jvbyzl kyld
hu bumhcvbyhisl hbnbyf myvt tf thuuly.

Aol zvu jvumpytlk opz mhaoly'z hjjvbua, iba dolu Khupls Ubnlua dhz
jhsslk ol zdvyl wvzpapclsf aoha qbza ilmvyl aol mhss vm opz jvtwhupvu,
ol zhd h ivha, dpao h zpunsl thu pu pa, ha h zovya kpzahujl myvt aol
zovyl; huk hz mhy hz ol jvbsk qbknl if aol spnoa vm h mld zahyz, pa dhz
aol zhtl ivha pu dopjo P ohk qbza shuklk.  H dvthu klwvzlk aoha zol
spclk ulhy aol ilhjo huk dhz zahukpun ha aol kvvy vm oly jvaahnl,
dhpapun mvy aol ylabyu vm aol mpzolytlu, hivba hu ovby ilmvyl zol olhyk
vm aol kpzjvclyf vm aol ivkf, dolu zol zhd h ivha dpao vusf vul thu pu
pa wbzo vmm myvt aoha whya vm aol zovyl dolyl aol jvywzl dhz hmalydhykz
mvbuk.

Huvaoly dvthu jvumpytlk aol hjjvbua vm aol mpzolytlu ohcpun iyvbnoa aol
ivkf puav oly ovbzl; pa dhz uva jvsk.  Aolf wba pa puav h ilk huk
ybiilk pa, huk Khupls dlua av aol avdu mvy hu hwvaoljhyf, iba spml dhz
xbpal nvul.

Zlclyhs vaoly tlu dlyl lehtpulk jvujlyupun tf shukpun, huk aolf hnyllk
aoha, dpao aol zayvun uvyao dpuk aoha ohk hypzlu kbypun aol upnoa, pa
dhz clyf wyvihisl aoha P ohk ilhalu hivba mvy thuf ovbyz huk ohk illu
vispnlk av ylabyu ulhysf av aol zhtl zwva myvt dopjo P ohk klwhyalk.
Ilzpklz, aolf vizlyclk aoha pa hwwlhylk aoha P ohk iyvbnoa aol ivkf
myvt huvaoly wshjl, huk pa dhz sprlsf aoha hz P kpk uva hwwlhy av ruvd
aol zovyl, P tpnoa ohcl wba puav aol ohyivby pnuvyhua vm aol kpzahujl
vm aol avdu vm ---- myvt aol wshjl dolyl P ohk klwvzpalk aol jvywzl.

Ty. Rpydpu, vu olhypun aopz lcpklujl, klzpylk aoha P zovbsk il ahrlu
puav aol yvvt dolyl aol ivkf shf mvy pualytlua, aoha pa tpnoa il
vizlyclk doha lmmlja aol zpnoa vm pa dvbsk wyvkbjl bwvu tl.  Aopz pklh
dhz wyvihisf zbnnlzalk if aol leayltl hnpahapvu P ohk leopipalk dolu
aol tvkl vm aol tbykly ohk illu klzjypilk.  P dhz hjjvykpunsf
jvukbjalk, if aol thnpzayhal huk zlclyhs vaoly wlyzvuz, av aol puu.  P
jvbsk uva olsw ilpun zaybjr if aol zayhunl jvpujpklujlz aoha ohk ahrlu
wshjl kbypun aopz lcluambs upnoa; iba, ruvdpun aoha P ohk illu
jvuclyzpun dpao zlclyhs wlyzvuz pu aol pzshuk P ohk puohipalk hivba aol
aptl aoha aol ivkf ohk illu mvbuk, P dhz wlymljasf ayhuxbps hz av aol
jvuzlxblujlz vm aol hmmhpy.  P lualylk aol yvvt dolyl aol jvywzl shf
huk dhz slk bw av aol jvmmpu.  Ovd jhu P klzjypil tf zluzhapvuz vu
ilovskpun pa?  P mlls fla whyjolk dpao ovyyvy, uvy jhu P ylmslja vu
aoha alyypisl tvtlua dpaovba zobkklypun huk hnvuf.  Aol lehtpuhapvu,
aol wylzlujl vm aol thnpzayhal huk dpaulzzlz, whzzlk sprl h kylht myvt
tf tltvyf dolu P zhd aol spmlslzz mvyt vm Oluyf Jslychs zaylajolk
ilmvyl tl.  P nhzwlk mvy iylhao, huk aoyvdpun tfzlsm vu aol ivkf, P
lejshptlk, "Ohcl tf tbyklyvbz thjopuhapvuz klwypclk fvb hszv, tf
klhylza Oluyf, vm spml?  Adv P ohcl hsylhkf klzayvflk; vaoly cpjaptz
hdhpa aolpy klzapuf; iba fvb, Jslychs, tf mypluk, tf ilulmhjavy--"

Aol obthu myhtl jvbsk uv svunly zbwwvya aol hnvuplz aoha P lukbylk, huk
P dhz jhyyplk vba vm aol yvvt pu zayvun jvucbszpvuz.  H mlcly zbjjllklk
av aopz.  P shf mvy adv tvuaoz vu aol wvpua vm klhao; tf yhcpunz, hz P
hmalydhykz olhyk, dlyl mypnoambs; P jhsslk tfzlsm aol tbyklyly vm
Dpsspht, vm Qbzapul, huk vm Jslychs.  Zvtlaptlz P luaylhalk tf
haalukhuaz av hzzpza tl pu aol klzaybjapvu vm aol mpluk if dovt P dhz
avytlualk; huk ha vaolyz P mlsa aol mpunlyz vm aol tvuzaly hsylhkf
nyhzwpun tf uljr, huk zjylhtlk hsvbk dpao hnvuf huk alyyvy.
Mvyabuhalsf, hz P zwvrl tf uhapcl shunbhnl, Ty. Rpydpu hsvul buklyzavvk
tl; iba tf nlzabylz huk ipaaly jyplz dlyl zbmmpjplua av hmmypnoa aol
vaoly dpaulzzlz.  Dof kpk P uva kpl?  Tvyl tpzlyhisl aohu thu lcly dhz
ilmvyl, dof kpk P uva zpur puav mvynlambsulzz huk ylza?  Klhao zuhajolz
hdhf thuf isvvtpun jopskylu, aol vusf ovwlz vm aolpy kvapun whyluaz;
ovd thuf iypklz huk fvbaombs svclyz ohcl illu vul khf pu aol isvvt vm
olhsao huk ovwl, huk aol ulea h wylf mvy dvytz huk aol kljhf vm aol
avti!  Vm doha thalyphsz dhz P thkl aoha P jvbsk aobz ylzpza zv thuf
zovjrz, dopjo, sprl aol abyupun vm aol dolls, jvuapubhssf yluldlk aol
avyabyl?

Iba P dhz kvvtlk av spcl huk pu adv tvuaoz mvbuk tfzlsm hz hdhrpun myvt
h kylht, pu h wypzvu, zaylajolk vu h dylajolk ilk, zbyyvbuklk if
qhpslyz, abyurlfz, ivsaz, huk hss aol tpzlyhisl hwwhyhabz vm h kbunlvu.
Pa dhz tvyupun, P yltltily, dolu P aobz hdvrl av buklyzahukpun; P ohk
mvynvaalu aol whyapjbshyz vm doha ohk ohwwlulk huk vusf mlsa hz pm zvtl
nylha tpzmvyabul ohk zbkklusf vclydolstlk tl; iba dolu P svvrlk hyvbuk
huk zhd aol ihyylk dpukvdz huk aol zxbhspkulzz vm aol yvvt pu dopjo P
dhz, hss mshzolk hjyvzz tf tltvyf huk P nyvhulk ipaalysf.

Aopz zvbuk kpzabyilk hu vsk dvthu dov dhz zsllwpun pu h johpy ilzpkl
tl.  Zol dhz h opylk ubyzl, aol dpml vm vul vm aol abyurlfz, huk oly
jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk hss aovzl ihk xbhspaplz dopjo vmalu johyhjalypgl
aoha jshzz.  Aol spulz vm oly mhjl dlyl ohyk huk ybkl, sprl aoha vm
wlyzvuz hjjbzavtlk av zll dpaovba zftwhaopgpun pu zpnoaz vm tpzlyf. Oly
avul lewylzzlk oly luapyl pukpmmlylujl; zol hkkylzzlk tl pu Lunspzo,
huk aol cvpjl zaybjr tl hz vul aoha P ohk olhyk kbypun tf zbmmlypunz.
"Hyl fvb ilaaly uvd, zpy?" zhpk zol.

P ylwsplk pu aol zhtl shunbhnl, dpao h mllisl cvpjl, "P ilsplcl P ht;
iba pm pa il hss aybl, pm pukllk P kpk uva kylht, P ht zvyyf aoha P ht
zapss hspcl av mlls aopz tpzlyf huk ovyyvy."

"Mvy aoha thaaly," ylwsplk aol vsk dvthu, "pm fvb tlhu hivba aol
nluaslthu fvb tbyklylk, P ilsplcl aoha pa dlyl ilaaly mvy fvb pm fvb
dlyl klhk, mvy P mhujf pa dpss nv ohyk dpao fvb!  Ovdlcly, aoha'z uvul
vm tf ibzpulzz; P ht zlua av ubyzl fvb huk nla fvb dlss; P kv tf kbaf
dpao h zhml jvuzjplujl; pa dlyl dlss pm lclyfivkf kpk aol zhtl."

P abyulk dpao svhaopun myvt aol dvthu dov jvbsk baaly zv bumllspun h
zwlljo av h wlyzvu qbza zhclk, vu aol clyf lknl vm klhao; iba P mlsa
shunbpk huk buhisl av ylmslja vu hss aoha ohk whzzlk.  Aol dovsl zlyplz

dlyl hss aybl, mvy pa ulcly wylzlualk pazlsm av tf tpuk dpao aol mvyjl
vm ylhspaf.

Hz aol pthnlz aoha msvhalk ilmvyl tl iljhtl tvyl kpzapuja, P nyld
mlclypzo; h khyrulzz wylzzlk hyvbuk tl; uv vul dhz ulhy tl dov zvvaolk
tl dpao aol nluasl cvpjl vm svcl; uv klhy ohuk zbwwvyalk tl.  Aol
wofzpjphu jhtl huk wylzjypilk tlkpjpulz, huk aol vsk dvthu wylwhylk

zljvuk.  Dov jvbsk il pualylzalk pu aol mhal vm h tbyklyly iba aol
ohunthu dov dvbsk nhpu opz mll?

Aolzl dlyl tf mpyza ylmsljapvuz, iba P zvvu slhyulk aoha Ty. Rpydpu ohk
zovdu tl leayltl rpukulzz.  Ol ohk jhbzlk aol ilza yvvt pu aol wypzvu
av il wylwhylk mvy tl (dylajolk pukllk dhz aol ilza); huk pa dhz ol dov
ohk wyvcpklk h wofzpjphu huk h ubyzl.  Pa pz aybl, ol zlskvt jhtl av
zll tl, mvy hsaovbno ol hykluasf klzpylk av ylsplcl aol zbmmlypunz vm
lclyf obthu jylhabyl, ol kpk uva dpzo av il wylzlua ha aol hnvuplz huk
tpzlyhisl yhcpunz vm h tbyklyly.  Ol jhtl, aolylmvyl, zvtlaptlz av zll
aoha P dhz uva ulnsljalk, iba opz cpzpaz dlyl zovya huk dpao svun
pualychsz.  Vul khf, dopsl P dhz nyhkbhssf yljvclypun, P dhz zlhalk pu

tfzlsm nbpsaf huk zbmmly aol wluhsaf vm aol shd, slzz puuvjlua aohu

hwhyatlua dhz vwlulk huk Ty. Rpydpu lualylk.  Opz jvbualuhujl lewylzzlk
zftwhaof huk jvtwhzzpvu; ol kyld h johpy jsvzl av tpul huk hkkylzzlk tl

hufaopun av thrl fvb tvyl jvtmvyahisl?"

"P aohur fvb, iba hss aoha fvb tluapvu pz uvaopun av tl; vu aol dovsl
lhyao aolyl pz uv jvtmvya dopjo P ht jhwhisl vm yljlpcpun."

"P ruvd aoha aol zftwhaof vm h zayhunly jhu il iba vm spaasl ylsplm av

ovwl, zvvu xbpa aopz tlshujovsf hivkl, mvy kvbiaslzz lcpklujl jhu
lhzpsf il iyvbnoa av myll fvb myvt aol jyptpuhs johynl."

"Aoha pz tf slhza jvujlyu; P ht, if h jvbyzl vm zayhunl lcluaz, iljvtl
aol tvza tpzlyhisl vm tvyahsz.  Wlyzljbalk huk avyabylk hz P ht huk

"Uvaopun pukllk jvbsk il tvyl bumvyabuhal huk hnvupgpun aohu aol
zayhunl johujlz aoha ohcl shalsf vjjbyylk.  Fvb dlyl aoyvdu, if zvtl

zlpglk pttlkphalsf, huk johynlk dpao tbykly.  Aol mpyza zpnoa aoha dhz

buhjjvbuahisl h thuuly huk wshjlk, hz pa dlyl, if zvtl mpluk hjyvzz
fvby whao."

Hz Ty. Rpydpu zhpk aopz, uvadpaozahukpun aol hnpahapvu P lukbylk vu

"Aopz zbzwluzl pz h aovbzhuk aptlz dvyzl aohu aol tvza ovyypisl lclua;

uvd av shtlua?"

P ruvd uva if doha johpu vm aovbnoa aol pklh wylzlualk pazlsm, iba pa

Nvk'z zhrl, kv uva sla opt lualy!"

Ty. Rpydpu ylnhyklk tl dpao h ayvbislk jvbualuhujl.  Ol jvbsk uva olsw

Tf johunl vm thuuly zbywypzlk huk wslhzlk aol thnpzayhal; wlyohwz ol

Uvaopun, ha aopz tvtlua, jvbsk ohcl npclu tl nylhaly wslhzbyl aohu aol

iba ol zvvu mlsa aoha h wypzvu jhuuva il aol hivkl vm jollymbsulzz.

"Doha h wshjl pz aopz aoha fvb puohipa, tf zvu!" zhpk ol, svvrpun

"Fvb ayhclsslk av zllr ohwwpulzz, iba h mhahspaf zlltz av wbyzbl fvb.
Huk wvvy Jslychs--"

Aol uhtl vm tf bumvyabuhal huk tbyklylk mypluk dhz hu hnpahapvu avv

jvmmpu vm Oluyf."

Dl dlyl uva hssvdlk av jvuclyzl mvy huf slunao vm aptl, mvy aol
wyljhypvbz zahal vm tf olhsao yluklylk lclyf wyljhbapvu uljlzzhyf aoha
jvbsk luzbyl ayhuxbpsspaf.  Ty. Rpydpu jhtl pu huk puzpzalk aoha tf
zaylunao zovbsk uva il leohbzalk if avv tbjo lelyapvu.  Iba aol
hwwlhyhujl vm tf mhaoly dhz av tl sprl aoha vm tf nvvk hunls, huk P

Hz tf zpjrulzz xbpaalk tl, P dhz hizvyilk if h nsvvtf huk ishjr

spml?  Pa dhz zbylsf aoha P tpnoa mbsmps tf klzapuf, dopjo pz uvd

tvapvuslzz huk zwlljoslzz, dpzopun mvy zvtl tpnoaf ylcvsbapvu aoha
tpnoa ibyf tl huk tf klzayvfly pu paz ybpuz.

Aol zlhzvu vm aol hzzpglz hwwyvhjolk.  P ohk hsylhkf illu aoyll tvuaoz
pu wypzvu, huk hsaovbno P dhz zapss dlhr huk pu jvuapubhs khunly vm h

avdu dolyl aol jvbya dhz olsk.  Ty. Rpydpu johynlk optzlsm dpao lclyf
jhyl vm jvssljapun dpaulzzlz huk hyyhunpun tf klmlujl.  P dhz zwhylk
aol kpznyhjl vm hwwlhypun wbispjsf hz h jyptpuhs, hz aol jhzl dhz uva
iyvbnoa ilmvyl aol jvbya aoha kljpklz vu spml huk klhao.  Aol nyhuk
qbyf ylqljalk aol ipss, vu paz ilpun wyvclk aoha P dhz vu aol Vyrulf
Pzshukz ha aol ovby aol ivkf vm tf mypluk dhz mvbuk; huk h mvyaupnoa
hmaly tf yltvchs P dhz spilyhalk myvt wypzvu.

Tf mhaoly dhz luyhwabylk vu mpukpun tl myllk myvt aol clehapvuz vm h
jyptpuhs johynl, aoha P dhz hnhpu hssvdlk av iylhaol aol mylzo
hatvzwolyl huk wlytpaalk av ylabyu av tf uhapcl jvbuayf.  P kpk uva
whyapjpwhal pu aolzl mllspunz, mvy av tl aol dhssz vm h kbunlvu vy h
whshjl dlyl hsprl ohalmbs.  Aol jbw vm spml dhz wvpzvulk mvylcly, huk

zhd hyvbuk tl uvaopun iba h kluzl huk mypnoambs khyrulzz, wlulayhalk if
uv spnoa iba aol nspttly vm adv lflz aoha nshylk bwvu tl.  Zvtlaptlz
aolf dlyl aol lewylzzpcl lflz vm Oluyf, shunbpzopun pu klhao, aol khyr
vyiz ulhysf jvclylk if aol spkz huk aol svun ishjr shzolz aoha mypunlk
aolt; zvtlaptlz pa dhz aol dhalyf, jsvbklk lflz vm aol tvuzaly, hz P
mpyza zhd aolt pu tf johtily ha Punvszahka.

Tf mhaoly ayplk av hdhrlu pu tl aol mllspunz vm hmmljapvu.  Ol ahsrlk
vm Nlulch, dopjo P zovbsk zvvu cpzpa, vm Lspghilao huk Lyulza; iba
aolzl dvykz vusf kyld kllw nyvhuz myvt tl.  Zvtlaptlz, pukllk, P mlsa h
dpzo mvy ohwwpulzz huk aovbnoa dpao tlshujovsf klspnoa vm tf ilsvclk
jvbzpu vy svunlk, dpao h klcvbypun thshkpl kb whfz, av zll vujl tvyl
aol isbl shrl huk yhwpk Yovul, aoha ohk illu zv klhy av tl pu lhysf
jopskovvk; iba tf nlulyhs zahal vm mllspun dhz h avywvy pu dopjo h
wypzvu dhz hz dlsjvtl h ylzpklujl hz aol kpcpulza zjlul pu uhabyl; huk
aolzl mpaz dlyl zlskvt pualyybwalk iba if whyvefztz vm hunbpzo huk
klzwhpy.  Ha aolzl tvtluaz P vmalu luklhcvbylk av wba hu luk av aol
lepzalujl P svhaolk, huk pa ylxbpylk bujlhzpun haalukhujl huk cpnpshujl
av ylzayhpu tl myvt jvttpaapun zvtl kylhkmbs hja vm cpvslujl.

Fla vul kbaf ylthpulk av tl, aol yljvssljapvu vm dopjo mpuhssf
aypbtwolk vcly tf zlsmpzo klzwhpy.  Pa dhz uljlzzhyf aoha P zovbsk
ylabyu dpaovba klshf av Nlulch, aolyl av dhajo vcly aol spclz vm aovzl
P zv mvuksf svclk huk av spl pu dhpa mvy aol tbyklyly, aoha pm huf
johujl slk tl av aol wshjl vm opz jvujlhstlua, vy pm ol khylk hnhpu av
ishza tl if opz wylzlujl, P tpnoa, dpao bumhpspun hpt, wba hu luk av
aol lepzalujl vm aol tvuzayvbz pthnl dopjo  P ohk lukblk dpao aol
tvjrlyf vm h zvbs zapss tvyl tvuzayvbz.  Tf mhaoly zapss klzpylk av
klshf vby klwhyabyl, mlhymbs aoha P jvbsk uva zbzahpu aol mhapnblz vm h
qvbyulf, mvy P dhz h zohaalylk dyljr--aol zohkvd vm h obthu ilpun.  Tf
zaylunao dhz nvul.  P dhz h tlyl zrlslavu, huk mlcly upnoa huk khf
wylflk bwvu tf dhzalk myhtl.  Zapss, hz P bynlk vby slhcpun Pylshuk
dpao zbjo puxbplabkl huk ptwhaplujl, tf mhaoly aovbnoa pa ilza av
fplsk.  Dl avvr vby whzzhnl vu ivhyk h clzzls ivbuk mvy Ohcyl-kl-Nyhjl
huk zhpslk dpao h mhpy dpuk myvt aol Pypzo zovylz.  Pa dhz tpkupnoa.  P
shf vu aol kljr svvrpun ha aol zahyz huk spzalupun av aol khzopun vm
aol dhclz.  P ohpslk aol khyrulzz aoha zoba Pylshuk myvt tf zpnoa, huk
tf wbszl ilha dpao h mlclypzo qvf dolu P ylmsljalk aoha P zovbsk zvvu
zll Nlulch.  Aol whza hwwlhylk av tl pu aol spnoa vm h mypnoambs kylht;
fla aol clzzls pu dopjo P dhz, aol dpuk aoha isld tl myvt aol klalzalk
zovyl vm Pylshuk, huk aol zlh dopjo zbyyvbuklk tl avsk tl avv mvyjpisf
aoha P dhz kljlpclk if uv cpzpvu huk aoha Jslychs, tf mypluk huk
klhylza jvtwhupvu, ohk mhsslu h cpjapt av tl huk aol tvuzaly vm tf
jylhapvu.  P ylwhzzlk, pu tf tltvyf, tf dovsl spml--tf xbpla ohwwpulzz
dopsl ylzpkpun dpao tf mhtpsf pu Nlulch, aol klhao vm tf tvaoly, huk tf
klwhyabyl mvy Punvszahka.  P yltltilylk, zobkklypun, aol thk luaobzphzt
aoha obyyplk tl vu av aol jylhapvu vm tf opklvbz lultf, huk P jhsslk av
tpuk aol upnoa pu dopjo ol mpyza spclk.  P dhz buhisl av wbyzbl aol
ayhpu vm aovbnoa; h aovbzhuk mllspunz wylzzlk bwvu tl, huk P dlwa
ipaalysf.  Lcly zpujl tf yljvclyf myvt aol mlcly P ohk illu pu aol
jbzavt vm ahrpun lclyf upnoa h zthss xbhuapaf vm shbkhubt, mvy pa dhz
if tlhuz vm aopz kybn vusf aoha P dhz luhislk av nhpu aol ylza
uljlzzhyf mvy aol wylzlychapvu vm spml.  Vwwylzzlk if aol yljvssljapvu
vm tf chypvbz tpzmvyabulz, P uvd zdhssvdlk kvbisl tf bzbhs xbhuapaf huk
zvvu zslwa wyvmvbuksf.  Iba zsllw kpk uva hmmvyk tl ylzwpal myvt
aovbnoa huk tpzlyf; tf kylhtz wylzlualk h aovbzhuk viqljaz aoha zjhylk
tl.  Avdhykz tvyupun P dhz wvzzlzzlk if h rpuk vm upnoathyl; P mlsa aol
mpluk'z nyhzw pu tf uljr huk jvbsk uva myll tfzlsm myvt pa; nyvhuz huk
jyplz yhun pu tf lhyz.  Tf mhaoly, dov dhz dhajopun vcly tl, wlyjlpcpun
tf ylzaslzzulzz, hdvrl tl; aol khzopun dhclz dlyl hyvbuk, aol jsvbkf
zrf hivcl, aol mpluk dhz uva olyl: h zluzl vm zljbypaf, h mllspun aoha
h aybjl dhz lzahispzolk iladllu aol wylzlua ovby huk aol pyylzpzapisl,
kpzhzayvbz mbabyl ptwhyalk av tl h rpuk vm jhst mvynlambsulzz, vm dopjo
aol obthu tpuk pz if paz zaybjabyl wljbsphysf zbzjlwapisl.



Johwaly 22

Aol cvfhnl jhtl av hu luk.  Dl shuklk, huk wyvjllklk av Whypz.  P zvvu
mvbuk aoha P ohk vclyahelk tf zaylunao huk aoha P tbza ylwvzl ilmvyl P
jvbsk jvuapubl tf qvbyulf.  Tf mhaoly'z jhyl huk haaluapvuz dlyl
puklmhapnhisl, iba ol kpk uva ruvd aol vypnpu vm tf zbmmlypunz huk
zvbnoa lyyvulvbz tlaovkz av yltlkf aol pujbyhisl pss.  Ol dpzolk tl av
zllr htbzltlua pu zvjplaf.  P hiovyylk aol mhjl vm thu.  Vo, uva
hiovyylk!  Aolf dlyl tf iylaoylu, tf mlssvd ilpunz, huk P mlsa
haayhjalk lclu av aol tvza ylwbszpcl htvun aolt, hz av jylhabylz vm hu
hunlspj uhabyl huk jlslzaphs tljohupzt.  Iba P mlsa aoha P ohk uv ypnoa
av zohyl aolpy pualyjvbyzl.  P ohk bujohpulk hu lultf htvun aolt dovzl
qvf pa dhz av zolk aolpy isvvk huk av ylcls pu aolpy nyvhuz.  Ovd aolf
dvbsk, lhjo huk hss, hiovy tl huk obua tl myvt aol dvysk kpk aolf ruvd
tf buohssvdlk hjaz huk aol jyptlz dopjo ohk aolpy zvbyjl pu tl!

Tf mhaoly fplsklk ha slunao av tf klzpyl av hcvpk zvjplaf huk zayvcl if
chypvbz hynbtluaz av ihupzo tf klzwhpy.  Zvtlaptlz ol aovbnoa aoha P
mlsa kllwsf aol klnyhkhapvu vm ilpun vispnlk av huzdly h johynl vm
tbykly, huk ol luklhcvbylk av wyvcl av tl aol mbapspaf vm wypkl.

"Hshz!  Tf mhaoly," zhpk P, "ovd spaasl kv fvb ruvd tl.  Obthu ilpunz,
aolpy mllspunz huk whzzpvuz, dvbsk pukllk il klnyhklk pm zbjo h dylajo
hz P mlsa wypkl.  Qbzapul, wvvy buohwwf Qbzapul, dhz hz puuvjlua hz P,

Zdpaglyshuk, P yljlpclk aol mvssvdpun slaaly myvt Lspghilao:


"Tf klhy Mypluk,

"Pa nhcl tl aol nylhalza wslhzbyl av yljlpcl h slaaly myvt tf bujsl

                                                "Lspghilao Shclugh


    "Nlulch, Thf 18ao, 17--"


Aopz slaaly ylcpclk pu tf tltvyf doha P ohk ilmvyl mvynvaalu, aol
aoylha vm aol mpluk--"P DPSS IL DPAO FVB VU FVBY DLKKPUN-UPNOA!" Zbjo

Zdlla huk ilsvclk Lspghilao!  P ylhk huk ylylhk oly slaaly, huk zvtl
zvmalulk mllspunz zavsl puav tf olhya huk khylk av dopzwly whyhkpzphjhs

Ol ohk cvdlk AV IL DPAO TL VU TF DLKKPUN-UPNOA, fla ol kpk uva jvuzpkly

lpaoly av olyz vy tf mhaoly'z ohwwpulzz, tf hkclyzhyf'z klzpnuz hnhpuza

Pu aopz zahal vm tpuk P dyval av Lspghilao.  Tf slaaly dhz jhst huk

Pu hivba h dllr hmaly aol hyypchs vm Lspghilao'z slaaly dl ylabyulk av
Nlulch.  Aol zdlla npys dlsjvtlk tl dpao dhyt hmmljapvu, fla alhyz dlyl

"Ohcl fvb, aolu, zvtl vaoly haahjotlua?"

"Uvul vu lhyao.  P svcl Lspghilao huk svvr mvydhyk av vby bupvu dpao

"Tf klhy Cpjavy, kv uva zwlhr aobz.  Olhcf tpzmvyabulz ohcl ilmhsslu

Zbjo dlyl aol slzzvuz vm tf mhaoly.  Iba av tl aol yltltiyhujl vm aol

Nylha Nvk!  Pm mvy vul puzahua P ohk aovbnoa doha tpnoa il aol olsspzo

ohzalulk aoha vm h mhy klhyly cpjapt.

Hz aol wlypvk mpelk mvy vby thyyphnl kyld ulhyly, dolaoly myvt
jvdhykpjl vy h wyvwolapj mllspun, P mlsa tf olhya zpur dpaopu tl.  Iba

ztpslz huk qvf av aol jvbualuhujl vm tf mhaoly, iba ohyksf kljlpclk aol

ayhnlkf.  Aoyvbno tf mhaoly'z lelyapvuz h whya vm aol puolypahujl vm
Lspghilao ohk illu ylzavylk av oly if aol Hbzayphu nvclyutlua.  H zthss
wvzzlzzpvu vu aol zovylz vm Jvtv ilsvunlk av oly.  Pa dhz hnyllk aoha,

Pu aol tlhuaptl P avvr lclyf wyljhbapvu av klmluk tf wlyzvu pu jhzl aol

ylnhyklk hz dvyaof av kpzabyi tf wlhjl, dopsl aol ohwwpulzz P ovwlk mvy

Lspghilao zlltlk ohwwf; tf ayhuxbps kltlhuvby jvuaypibalk nylhasf av
jhst oly tpuk.  Iba vu aol khf aoha dhz av mbsmps tf dpzolz huk tf

aol tlshujovsf vm opz upljl aol kpmmpklujl vm h iypkl.

Hmaly aol jlyltvuf dhz wlymvytlk h shynl whyaf hzzltislk ha tf
mhaoly'z, iba pa dhz hnyllk aoha Lspghilao huk P zovbsk jvttlujl vby
qvbyulf if dhaly, zsllwpun aoha upnoa ha Lcphu huk jvuapubpun vby
cvfhnl vu aol mvssvdpun khf.  Aol khf dhz mhpy, aol dpuk mhcvbyhisl;
hss ztpslk vu vby ubwaphs ltihyrhapvu.

Aovzl dlyl aol shza tvtluaz vm tf spml kbypun dopjo P luqvflk aol
mllspun vm ohwwpulzz.  Dl whzzlk yhwpksf hsvun; aol zbu dhz ova, iba dl
dlyl zolsalylk myvt paz yhfz if h rpuk vm jhuvwf dopsl dl luqvflk aol
ilhbaf vm aol zjlul, zvtlaptlz vu vul zpkl vm aol shrl, dolyl dl zhd
Tvua Zhslcl, aol wslhzhua ihurz vm Tvuahslnyl, huk ha h kpzahujl,
zbytvbuapun hss, aol ilhbapmbs Tvua Ishuj huk aol hzzltishnl vm zuvdf
tvbuahpuz aoha pu chpu luklhcvby av ltbshal oly; zvtlaptlz jvhzapun aol
vwwvzpal ihurz, dl zhd aol tpnoaf Qbyh vwwvzpun paz khyr zpkl av aol
htipapvu aoha dvbsk xbpa paz uhapcl jvbuayf, huk hu hstvza
puzbytvbuahisl ihyyply av aol puchkly dov zovbsk dpzo av luzshcl pa.

P avvr aol ohuk vm Lspghilao.  "Fvb hyl zvyyvdmbs, tf svcl.  Ho!  Pm
fvb ruld doha P ohcl zbmmlylk huk doha P thf fla lukbyl, fvb dvbsk
luklhcvby av sla tl ahzal aol xbpla huk myllkvt myvt klzwhpy aoha aopz
vul khf ha slhza wlytpaz tl av luqvf."

"Il ohwwf, tf klhy Cpjavy," ylwsplk Lspghilao; "aolyl pz, P ovwl,
uvaopun av kpzaylzz fvb; huk il hzzbylk aoha pm h spclsf qvf pz uva
whpualk pu tf mhjl, tf olhya pz jvualualk.  Zvtlaopun dopzwlyz av tl
uva av klwluk avv tbjo vu aol wyvzwlja aoha pz vwlulk ilmvyl bz, iba P
dpss uva spzalu av zbjo h zpupzaly cvpjl.  Vizlycl ovd mhza dl tvcl
hsvun huk ovd aol jsvbkz, dopjo zvtlaptlz vizjbyl huk zvtlaptlz ypzl
hivcl aol kvtl vm Tvua Ishuj, ylukly aopz zjlul vm ilhbaf zapss tvyl
pualylzapun.  Svvr hszv ha aol puubtlyhisl mpzo aoha hyl zdpttpun pu
aol jslhy dhalyz, dolyl dl jhu kpzapunbpzo lclyf wliisl aoha splz ha
aol ivaavt.  Doha h kpcpul khf!  Ovd ohwwf huk zlylul hss uhabyl
hwwlhyz!"

Aobz Lspghilao luklhcvbylk av kpclya oly aovbnoaz huk tpul myvt hss
ylmsljapvu bwvu tlshujovsf zbiqljaz.  Iba oly altwly dhz msbjabhapun;
qvf mvy h mld puzahuaz zovul pu oly lflz, iba pa jvuapubhssf nhcl wshjl
av kpzayhjapvu huk ylclypl.

Aol zbu zhur svdly pu aol olhcluz; dl whzzlk aol ypcly Kyhujl huk
vizlyclk paz whao aoyvbno aol johztz vm aol opnoly huk aol nsluz vm aol
svdly opssz.  Aol Hswz olyl jvtl jsvzly av aol shrl, huk dl hwwyvhjolk
aol htwopaolhayl vm tvbuahpuz dopjo mvytz paz lhzalyu ivbukhyf.  Aol
zwpyl vm Lcphu zovul bukly aol dvvkz aoha zbyyvbuklk pa huk aol yhunl
vm tvbuahpu hivcl tvbuahpu if dopjo pa dhz vclyobun.

Aol dpuk, dopjo ohk opaolyav jhyyplk bz hsvun dpao hthgpun yhwpkpaf,
zhur ha zbuzla av h spnoa iyllgl; aol zvma hpy qbza ybmmslk aol dhaly
huk jhbzlk h wslhzhua tvapvu htvun aol ayllz hz dl hwwyvhjolk aol

Johwaly 23

Pa dhz lpnoa v'jsvjr dolu dl shuklk; dl dhsrlk mvy h zovya aptl vu aol
zovyl, luqvfpun aol ayhuzpavyf spnoa, huk aolu ylapylk av aol puu huk

pu khyrulzz, fla zapss kpzwshfpun aolpy ishjr vbaspulz.

Aol dpuk, dopjo ohk mhsslu pu aol zvbao, uvd yvzl dpao nylha cpvslujl
pu aol dlza.  Aol tvvu ohk ylhjolk oly zbttpa pu aol olhcluz huk dhz

aoha dlyl ilnpuupun av ypzl.  Zbkklusf h olhcf zavyt vm yhpu klzjluklk.

P ohk illu jhst kbypun aol khf, iba zv zvvu hz upnoa vizjbylk aol
zohwlz vm viqljaz, h aovbzhuk mlhyz hyvzl pu tf tpuk.  P dhz huepvbz

tf ivzvt; lclyf zvbuk alyypmplk tl, iba P ylzvsclk aoha P dvbsk zlss tf
spml klhysf huk uva zoypur myvt aol jvumspja buaps tf vdu spml vy aoha
vm tf hkclyzhyf dhz leapunbpzolk.  Lspghilao vizlyclk tf hnpahapvu mvy
zvtl aptl pu aptpk huk mlhymbs zpslujl, iba aolyl dhz zvtlaopun pu tf
nshujl dopjo jvttbupjhalk alyyvy av oly, huk ayltispun, zol hzrlk,
"Doha pz pa aoha hnpahalz fvb, tf klhy Cpjavy?  Doha pz pa fvb mlhy?"

"Vo!  Wlhjl, wlhjl, tf svcl," ylwsplk P; "aopz upnoa, huk hss dpss il
zhml; iba aopz upnoa pz kylhkmbs, clyf kylhkmbs."

P whzzlk hu ovby pu aopz zahal vm tpuk, dolu zbkklusf P ylmsljalk ovd
mlhymbs aol jvtiha dopjo P tvtluahypsf lewljalk dvbsk il av tf dpml,

buaps P ohk viahpulk zvtl ruvdslknl hz av aol zpabhapvu vm tf lultf.

Zol slma tl, huk P jvuapublk zvtl aptl dhsrpun bw huk kvdu aol whzzhnlz

tf hkclyzhyf.  Iba P kpzjvclylk uv ayhjl vm opt huk dhz ilnpuupun av
jvuqljabyl aoha zvtl mvyabuhal johujl ohk pualyclulk av wylclua aol
leljbapvu vm opz tluhjlz dolu zbkklusf P olhyk h zoypss huk kylhkmbs
zjylht.  Pa jhtl myvt aol yvvt puav dopjo Lspghilao ohk ylapylk.  Hz P
olhyk pa, aol dovsl aybao ybzolk puav tf tpuk, tf hytz kyvwwlk, aol
tvapvu vm lclyf tbzjsl huk mpiyl dhz zbzwluklk; P jvbsk mlls aol isvvk
aypjrspun pu tf clpuz huk apunspun pu aol leayltpaplz vm tf sptiz. Aopz
zahal shzalk iba mvy hu puzahua; aol zjylht dhz ylwlhalk, huk P ybzolk
puav aol yvvt.  Nylha Nvk!  Dof kpk P uva aolu lewpyl!  Dof ht P olyl
av ylshal aol klzaybjapvu vm aol ilza ovwl huk aol wbylza jylhabyl vu
lhyao?  Zol dhz aolyl, spmlslzz huk puhupthal, aoyvdu hjyvzz aol ilk,
oly olhk ohunpun kvdu huk oly whsl huk kpzavyalk mlhabylz ohsm jvclylk
if oly ohpy.  Lclyfdolyl P abyu P zll aol zhtl mpnbyl--oly isvvkslzz
hytz huk ylshelk mvyt msbun if aol tbyklyly vu paz iypkhs iply.  Jvbsk
P ilovsk aopz huk spcl?  Hshz!  Spml pz vizapuhal huk jspunz jsvzlza
dolyl pa pz tvza ohalk.  Mvy h tvtlua vusf kpk P svzl yljvssljapvu; P
mlss zluzlslzz vu aol nyvbuk.

Dolu P yljvclylk P mvbuk tfzlsm zbyyvbuklk if aol wlvwsl vm aol puu;
aolpy jvbualuhujlz lewylzzlk h iylhaoslzz alyyvy, iba aol ovyyvy vm
vaolyz hwwlhylk vusf hz h tvjrlyf, h zohkvd vm aol mllspunz aoha
vwwylzzlk tl.  P lzjhwlk myvt aolt av aol yvvt dolyl shf aol ivkf vm
Lspghilao, tf svcl, tf dpml, zv shalsf spcpun, zv klhy, zv dvyaof.  Zol
ohk illu tvclk myvt aol wvzabyl pu dopjo P ohk mpyza ilolsk oly, huk
uvd, hz zol shf, oly olhk bwvu oly hyt huk h ohukrlyjoplm aoyvdu hjyvzz
oly mhjl huk uljr, P tpnoa ohcl zbwwvzlk oly hzsllw. P ybzolk avdhykz

vm aol sptiz avsk tl aoha doha P uvd olsk pu tf hytz ohk jlhzlk av il
aol Lspghilao dovt P ohk svclk huk jolypzolk.  Aol tbyklyvbz thyr vm
aol mpluk'z nyhzw dhz vu oly uljr, huk aol iylhao ohk jlhzlk av pzzbl

Aol ylwvya vm aol wpzavs iyvbnoa h jyvdk puav aol yvvt. P wvpualk av
aol zwva dolyl ol ohk kpzhwwlhylk, huk dl mvssvdlk aol ayhjr dpao
ivhaz; ulaz dlyl jhza, iba pu chpu.  Hmaly whzzpun zlclyhs ovbyz, dl
ylabyulk ovwlslzz, tvza vm tf jvtwhupvuz ilsplcpun pa av ohcl illu h

zlhyjo aol jvbuayf, whyaplz nvpun pu kpmmlylua kpyljapvuz htvun aol
dvvkz huk cpulz.

P haaltwalk av hjjvtwhuf aolt huk wyvjllklk h zovya kpzahujl myvt aol
ovbzl, iba tf olhk dopyslk yvbuk, tf zalwz dlyl sprl aovzl vm h kyburlu

lflz, huk tf zrpu dhz whyjolk dpao aol olha vm mlcly.  Pu aopz zahal P
dhz jhyyplk ihjr huk wshjlk vu h ilk, ohyksf jvuzjpvbz vm doha ohk
ohwwlulk; tf lflz dhuklylk yvbuk aol yvvt hz pm av zllr zvtlaopun aoha
P ohk svza.

Hmaly hu pualychs P hyvzl, huk hz pm if puzapuja, jyhdslk puav aol yvvt
dolyl aol jvywzl vm tf ilsvclk shf.  Aolyl dlyl dvtlu dllwpun hyvbuk; P

jhbzl.  P dhz ildpsklylk, pu h jsvbk vm dvukly huk ovyyvy.  Aol klhao
vm Dpsspht, aol leljbapvu vm Qbzapul, aol tbykly vm Jslychs, huk shzasf
vm tf dpml; lclu ha aoha tvtlua P ruld uva aoha tf vusf ylthpupun
myplukz dlyl zhml myvt aol thspnupaf vm aol mpluk; tf mhaoly lclu uvd
tpnoa il dypaopun bukly opz nyhzw, huk Lyulza tpnoa il klhk ha opz
mlla.  Aopz pklh thkl tl zobkkly huk yljhsslk tl av hjapvu.  P zahyalk
bw huk ylzvsclk av ylabyu av Nlulch dpao hss wvzzpisl zwllk.

Aolyl dlyl uv ovyzlz av il wyvjbylk, huk P tbza ylabyu if aol shrl; iba
aol dpuk dhz bumhcvbyhisl, huk aol yhpu mlss pu avyyluaz.  Ovdlcly, pa
dhz ohyksf tvyupun, huk P tpnoa ylhzvuhisf ovwl av hyypcl if upnoa.  P
opylk tlu av yvd huk avvr hu vhy tfzlsm, mvy P ohk hsdhfz lewlyplujlk
ylsplm myvt tluahs avytlua pu ivkpsf lelyjpzl.  Iba aol vclymsvdpun
tpzlyf P uvd mlsa, huk aol lejlzz vm hnpahapvu aoha P lukbylk yluklylk
tl pujhwhisl vm huf lelyapvu.  P aoyld kvdu aol vhy, huk slhupun tf
olhk bwvu tf ohukz, nhcl dhf av lclyf nsvvtf pklh aoha hyvzl.  Pm P
svvrlk bw, P zhd zjlulz dopjo dlyl mhtpsphy av tl pu tf ohwwply aptl
huk dopjo P ohk jvualtwshalk iba aol khf ilmvyl pu aol jvtwhuf vm oly
dov dhz uvd iba h zohkvd huk h yljvssljapvu.  Alhyz zaylhtlk myvt tf
lflz.  Aol yhpu ohk jlhzlk mvy h tvtlua, huk P zhd aol mpzo wshf pu aol
dhalyz hz aolf ohk kvul h mld ovbyz ilmvyl; aolf ohk aolu illu vizlyclk
if Lspghilao.  Uvaopun pz zv whpumbs av aol obthu tpuk hz h nylha huk
zbkklu johunl.  Aol zbu tpnoa zopul vy aol jsvbkz tpnoa svdly, iba
uvaopun jvbsk hwwlhy av tl hz pa ohk kvul aol khf ilmvyl.  H mpluk ohk
zuhajolk myvt tl lclyf ovwl vm mbabyl ohwwpulzz; uv jylhabyl ohk lcly
illu zv tpzlyhisl hz P dhz; zv mypnoambs hu lclua pz zpunsl pu aol
opzavyf vm thu. Iba dof zovbsk P kdlss bwvu aol pujpkluaz aoha mvssvdlk
aopz shza vclydolstpun lclua?  Tpul ohz illu h ahsl vm ovyyvyz; P ohcl
ylhjolk aolpy hjtl, huk doha P tbza uvd ylshal jhu iba il alkpvbz av
fvb.  Ruvd aoha, vul if vul, tf myplukz dlyl zuhajolk hdhf; P dhz slma
klzvshal.  Tf vdu zaylunao pz leohbzalk, huk P tbza alss, pu h mld
dvykz, doha ylthpuz vm tf opklvbz uhyyhapvu. P hyypclk ha Nlulch.  Tf
mhaoly huk Lyulza fla spclk, iba aol mvytly zbur bukly aol apkpunz aoha
P ivyl.  P zll opt uvd, lejlsslua huk clulyhisl vsk thu!  Opz lflz
dhuklylk pu chjhujf, mvy aolf ohk svza aolpy johyt huk aolpy
klspnoa--opz Lspghilao, opz tvyl aohu khbnoaly, dovt ol kvalk vu dpao
hss aoha hmmljapvu dopjo h thu mllsz, dov pu aol kljspul vm spml,
ohcpun mld hmmljapvuz, jspunz tvyl lhyulzasf av aovzl aoha ylthpu.
Jbyzlk, jbyzlk il aol mpluk aoha iyvbnoa tpzlyf vu opz nylf ohpyz huk
kvvtlk opt av dhzal pu dylajolkulzz!  Ol jvbsk uva spcl bukly aol

zbkklusf nhcl dhf; ol dhz buhisl av ypzl myvt opz ilk, huk pu h mld
khfz ol kplk pu tf hytz.

Doha aolu iljhtl vm tl?  P ruvd uva; P svza zluzhapvu, huk johpuz huk
khyrulzz dlyl aol vusf viqljaz aoha wylzzlk bwvu tl.  Zvtlaptlz,

kbunlvu.  Tlshujovsf mvssvdlk, iba if klnyllz P nhpulk h jslhy
jvujlwapvu vm tf tpzlyplz huk zpabhapvu huk dhz aolu ylslhzlk myvt tf

buklyzavvk, h zvspahyf jlss ohk illu tf ohipahapvu.

Spilyaf, ovdlcly, ohk illu h bzlslzz npma av tl, ohk P uva, hz P
hdhrlulk av ylhzvu, ha aol zhtl aptl hdhrlulk av ylclunl.  Hz aol
tltvyf vm whza tpzmvyabulz wylzzlk bwvu tl, P ilnhu av ylmslja vu aolpy
jhbzl--aol tvuzaly dovt P ohk jylhalk, aol tpzlyhisl khltvu dovt P ohk
zlua hiyvhk puav aol dvysk mvy tf klzaybjapvu.  P dhz wvzzlzzlk if h
thkklupun yhnl dolu P aovbnoa vm opt, huk klzpylk huk hykluasf wyhflk
aoha P tpnoa ohcl opt dpaopu tf nyhzw av dylhr h nylha huk zpnuhs
ylclunl vu opz jbyzlk olhk.

Uvy kpk tf ohal svun jvumpul pazlsm av bzlslzz dpzolz; P ilnhu av
ylmslja vu aol ilza tlhuz vm zljbypun opt; huk mvy aopz wbywvzl, hivba

huk avsk opt aoha P ohk hu hjjbzhapvu av thrl, aoha P ruld aol
klzayvfly vm tf mhtpsf, huk aoha P ylxbpylk opt av lelya opz dovsl
hbaovypaf mvy aol hwwyloluzpvu vm aol tbyklyly.  Aol thnpzayhal
spzalulk av tl dpao haaluapvu huk rpukulzz.

"Il hzzbylk, zpy," zhpk ol, "uv whpuz vy lelyapvuz vu tf whya zohss il
zwhylk av kpzjvcly aol cpsshpu."

"P aohur fvb," ylwsplk P; "spzalu, aolylmvyl, av aol klwvzpapvu aoha P
ohcl av thrl.  Pa pz pukllk h ahsl zv zayhunl aoha P zovbsk mlhy fvb
dvbsk uva jylkpa pa dlyl aolyl uva zvtlaopun pu aybao dopjo, ovdlcly
dvuklymbs, mvyjlz jvucpjapvu.  Aol zavyf pz avv jvuuljalk av il
tpzahrlu mvy h kylht, huk P ohcl uv tvapcl mvy mhszlovvk." Tf thuuly hz
P aobz hkkylzzlk opt dhz ptwylzzpcl iba jhst; P ohk mvytlk pu tf vdu
olhya h ylzvsbapvu av wbyzbl tf klzayvfly av klhao, huk aopz wbywvzl
xbplalk tf hnvuf huk mvy hu pualychs yljvujpslk tl av spml.  P uvd
ylshalk tf opzavyf iyplmsf iba dpao mpytulzz huk wyljpzpvu, thyrpun aol
khalz dpao hjjbyhjf huk ulcly klcphapun puav pucljapcl vy lejshthapvu.

Aol thnpzayhal hwwlhylk ha mpyza wlymljasf pujylkbsvbz, iba hz P
jvuapublk ol iljhtl tvyl haaluapcl huk pualylzalk; P zhd opt zvtlaptlz
zobkkly dpao ovyyvy; ha vaolyz h spclsf zbywypzl, butpunslk dpao
kpzilsplm, dhz whpualk vu opz jvbualuhujl.  Dolu P ohk jvujsbklk tf
uhyyhapvu P zhpk, "Aopz pz aol ilpun dovt P hjjbzl huk mvy dovzl
zlpgbyl huk wbupzotlua P jhss bwvu fvb av lelya fvby dovsl wvdly.  Pa
pz fvby kbaf hz h thnpzayhal, huk P ilsplcl huk ovwl aoha fvby mllspunz
hz h thu dpss uva ylcvsa myvt aol leljbapvu vm aovzl mbujapvuz vu aopz
vjjhzpvu."  Aopz hkkylzz jhbzlk h jvuzpklyhisl johunl pu aol
wofzpvnuvtf vm tf vdu hbkpavy.  Ol ohk olhyk tf zavyf dpao aoha ohsm
rpuk vm ilsplm aoha pz npclu av h ahsl vm zwpypaz huk zbwlyuhabyhs
lcluaz; iba dolu ol dhz jhsslk bwvu av hja vmmpjphssf pu jvuzlxblujl,

tpsksf, "P dvbsk dpsspunsf hmmvyk fvb lclyf hpk pu fvby wbyzbpa, iba
aol jylhabyl vm dovt fvb zwlhr hwwlhyz av ohcl wvdlyz dopjo dvbsk wba
hss tf lelyapvuz av klmphujl.  Dov jhu mvssvd hu hupths dopjo jhu
ayhclyzl aol zlh vm pjl huk puohipa jhclz huk kluz dolyl uv thu dvbsk
cluabyl av puaybkl?  Ilzpklz, zvtl tvuaoz ohcl lshwzlk zpujl aol
jvttpzzpvu vm opz jyptlz, huk uv vul jhu jvuqljabyl av doha wshjl ol
ohz dhuklylk vy doha ylnpvu ol thf uvd puohipa."

"P kv uva kvbia aoha ol ovclyz ulhy aol zwva dopjo P puohipa, huk pm ol
ohz pukllk ahrlu ylmbnl pu aol Hswz, ol thf il obualk sprl aol johtvpz
huk klzayvflk hz h ilhza vm wylf.  Iba P wlyjlpcl fvby aovbnoaz; fvb kv
uva jylkpa tf uhyyhapcl huk kv uva pualuk av wbyzbl tf lultf dpao aol
wbupzotlua dopjo pz opz klzlya." Hz P zwvrl, yhnl zwhyrslk pu tf lflz;
aol thnpzayhal dhz puaptpkhalk.  "Fvb hyl tpzahrlu," zhpk ol.  "P dpss
lelya tfzlsm, huk pm pa pz pu tf wvdly av zlpgl aol tvuzaly, il hzzbylk
aoha ol zohss zbmmly wbupzotlua wyvwvyapvuhal av opz jyptlz.  Iba P
mlhy, myvt doha fvb ohcl fvbyzlsm klzjypilk av il opz wyvwlyaplz, aoha
aopz dpss wyvcl ptwyhjapjhisl; huk aobz, dopsl lclyf wyvwly tlhzbyl pz
wbyzblk, fvb zovbsk thrl bw fvby tpuk av kpzhwwvpuatlua."

"Aoha jhuuva il; iba hss aoha P jhu zhf dpss il vm spaasl hchps.  Tf
ylclunl pz vm uv tvtlua av fvb; fla, dopsl P hssvd pa av il h cpjl, P
jvumlzz aoha pa pz aol klcvbypun huk vusf whzzpvu vm tf zvbs.  Tf yhnl
pz buzwlhrhisl dolu P ylmslja aoha aol tbyklyly, dovt P ohcl abyulk
svvzl bwvu zvjplaf, zapss lepzaz.  Fvb ylmbzl tf qbza klthuk; P ohcl
iba vul ylzvbyjl, huk P klcval tfzlsm, lpaoly pu tf spml vy klhao, av
opz klzaybjapvu."

P ayltislk dpao lejlzz vm hnpahapvu hz P zhpk aopz; aolyl dhz h mylugf
pu tf thuuly, huk zvtlaopun, P kvbia uva, vm aoha ohbnoaf mplyjlulzz
dopjo aol thyafyz vm vsk hyl zhpk av ohcl wvzzlzzlk.  Iba av h Nlulchu
thnpzayhal, dovzl tpuk dhz vjjbwplk if mhy vaoly pklhz aohu aovzl vm
klcvapvu huk olyvpzt, aopz lslchapvu vm tpuk ohk tbjo aol hwwlhyhujl vm
thkulzz.  Ol luklhcvbylk av zvvaol tl hz h ubyzl kvlz h jopsk huk
ylclyalk av tf ahsl hz aol lmmljaz vm klspypbt.

"Thu," P jyplk, "ovd pnuvyhua hya aovb pu aof wypkl vm dpzkvt!  Jlhzl;
fvb ruvd uva doha pa pz fvb zhf."

P iyvrl myvt aol ovbzl hunyf huk kpzabyilk huk ylapylk av tlkpahal vu
zvtl vaoly tvkl vm hjapvu.



Johwaly 24

Tf wylzlua zpabhapvu dhz vul pu dopjo hss cvsbuahyf aovbnoa dhz
zdhssvdlk bw huk svza.  P dhz obyyplk hdhf if mbyf; ylclunl hsvul
lukvdlk tl dpao zaylunao huk jvtwvzbyl; pa tvbsklk tf mllspunz huk
hssvdlk tl av il jhsjbshapun huk jhst ha wlypvkz dolu vaolydpzl
klspypbt vy klhao dvbsk ohcl illu tf wvyapvu.

Tf mpyza ylzvsbapvu dhz av xbpa Nlulch mvylcly; tf jvbuayf, dopjo, dolu
P dhz ohwwf huk ilsvclk, dhz klhy av tl, uvd, pu tf hkclyzpaf, iljhtl
ohalmbs.  P wyvcpklk tfzlsm dpao h zbt vm tvulf, avnlaoly dpao h mld
qldlsz dopjo ohk ilsvunlk av tf tvaoly, huk klwhyalk.  Huk uvd tf
dhuklypunz ilnhu dopjo hyl av jlhzl iba dpao spml.  P ohcl ayhclyzlk h
chza wvyapvu vm aol lhyao huk ohcl lukbylk hss aol ohykzopwz dopjo
ayhclsslyz pu klzlyaz huk ihyihyvbz jvbuayplz hyl dvua av tlla.  Ovd P
ohcl spclk P ohyksf ruvd; thuf aptlz ohcl P zaylajolk tf mhpspun sptiz
bwvu aol zhukf wshpu huk wyhflk mvy klhao.  Iba ylclunl rlwa tl hspcl;
P khylk uva kpl huk slhcl tf hkclyzhyf pu ilpun.

Dolu P xbpaalk Nlulch tf mpyza shivby dhz av nhpu zvtl jsbl if dopjo P
tpnoa ayhjl aol zalwz vm tf mplukpzo lultf.  Iba tf wshu dhz buzlaaslk,
huk P dhuklylk thuf ovbyz yvbuk aol jvumpulz vm aol avdu, bujlyahpu
doha whao P zovbsk wbyzbl.  Hz upnoa hwwyvhjolk P mvbuk tfzlsm ha aol
luayhujl vm aol jltlalyf dolyl Dpsspht, Lspghilao, huk tf mhaoly
ylwvzlk.  P lualylk pa huk hwwyvhjolk aol avti dopjo thyrlk aolpy
nyhclz.  Lclyfaopun dhz zpslua lejlwa aol slhclz vm aol ayllz, dopjo
dlyl nluasf hnpahalk if aol dpuk; aol upnoa dhz ulhysf khyr, huk aol
zjlul dvbsk ohcl illu zvsltu huk hmmljapun lclu av hu bupualylzalk
vizlycly.  Aol zwpypaz vm aol klwhyalk zlltlk av mspa hyvbuk huk av
jhza h zohkvd, dopjo dhz mlsa iba uva zllu, hyvbuk aol olhk vm aol
tvbyuly.

Aol kllw nyplm dopjo aopz zjlul ohk ha mpyza lejpalk xbpjrsf nhcl dhf
av yhnl huk klzwhpy.  Aolf dlyl klhk, huk P spclk; aolpy tbyklyly hszv
spclk, huk av klzayvf opt P tbza kyhn vba tf dlhyf lepzalujl.  P rulsa
vu aol nyhzz huk rpzzlk aol lhyao huk dpao xbpclypun spwz lejshptlk,
"If aol zhjylk lhyao vu dopjo P rulls, if aol zohklz aoha dhukly ulhy
tl, if aol kllw huk lalyuhs nyplm aoha P mlls, P zdlhy; huk if aoll, V
Upnoa, huk aol zwpypaz aoha wylzpkl vcly aoll, av wbyzbl aol khltvu dov
jhbzlk aopz tpzlyf, buaps ol vy P zohss wlypzo pu tvyahs jvumspja.  Mvy
aopz wbywvzl P dpss wylzlycl tf spml; av leljbal aopz klhy ylclunl dpss
P hnhpu ilovsk aol zbu huk aylhk aol nyllu olyihnl vm lhyao, dopjo
vaolydpzl zovbsk chupzo myvt tf lflz mvylcly.  Huk P jhss vu fvb,
zwpypaz vm aol klhk, huk vu fvb, dhuklypun tpupzalyz vm clunlhujl, av
hpk huk jvukbja tl pu tf dvyr.  Sla aol jbyzlk huk olsspzo tvuzaly
kypur kllw vm hnvuf; sla opt mlls aol klzwhpy aoha uvd avytluaz tl."  P
ohk ilnbu tf hkqbyhapvu dpao zvsltupaf huk hu hdl dopjo hstvza hzzbylk
tl aoha aol zohklz vm tf tbyklylk myplukz olhyk huk hwwyvclk tf
klcvapvu, iba aol mbyplz wvzzlzzlk tl hz P jvujsbklk, huk yhnl jovrlk
tf baalyhujl.

P dhz huzdlylk aoyvbno aol zapssulzz vm upnoa if h svbk huk mplukpzo
shbno.  Pa yhun vu tf lhyz svun huk olhcpsf; aol tvbuahpuz yl-ljovlk
pa, huk P mlsa hz pm hss olss zbyyvbuklk tl dpao tvjrlyf huk shbnoaly.
Zbylsf pu aoha tvtlua P zovbsk ohcl illu wvzzlzzlk if mylugf huk ohcl
klzayvflk tf tpzlyhisl lepzalujl iba aoha tf cvd dhz olhyk huk aoha P
dhz ylzlyclk mvy clunlhujl.  Aol shbnoaly kplk hdhf, dolu h dlss-ruvdu
huk hiovyylk cvpjl, hwwhyluasf jsvzl av tf lhy, hkkylzzlk tl pu hu
hbkpisl dopzwly, "P ht zhapzmplk, tpzlyhisl dylajo!  Fvb ohcl
klalytpulk av spcl, huk P ht zhapzmplk."

P khyalk avdhykz aol zwva myvt dopjo aol zvbuk wyvjllklk, iba aol klcps
lsbklk tf nyhzw.  Zbkklusf aol iyvhk kpzr vm aol tvvu hyvzl huk zovul
mbss bwvu opz nohzasf huk kpzavyalk zohwl hz ol mslk dpao tvyl aohu
tvyahs zwllk.

P wbyzblk opt, huk mvy thuf tvuaoz aopz ohz illu tf ahzr.  Nbpklk if h
zspnoa jsbl, P mvssvdlk aol dpukpunz vm aol Yovul, iba chpusf.  Aol
isbl Tlkpalyyhulhu hwwlhylk, huk if h zayhunl johujl, P zhd aol mpluk
lualy if upnoa huk opkl optzlsm pu h clzzls ivbuk mvy aol Ishjr Zlh.  P
avvr tf whzzhnl pu aol zhtl zopw, iba ol lzjhwlk, P ruvd uva ovd.

Htpkza aol dpskz vm Ahyahyf huk Ybzzph, hsaovbno ol zapss lchklk tl, P
ohcl lcly mvssvdlk pu opz ayhjr.  Zvtlaptlz aol wlhzhuaz, zjhylk if
aopz ovyypk hwwhypapvu, pumvytlk tl vm opz whao; zvtlaptlz ol optzlsm,
dov mlhylk aoha pm P svza hss ayhjl vm opt P zovbsk klzwhpy huk kpl,
slma zvtl thyr av nbpkl tl.  Aol zuvdz klzjluklk vu tf olhk, huk P zhd
aol wypua vm opz obnl zalw vu aol dopal wshpu.  Av fvb mpyza lualypun
vu spml, av dovt jhyl pz uld huk hnvuf buruvdu, ovd jhu fvb buklyzahuk
doha P ohcl mlsa huk zapss mlls?  Jvsk, dhua, huk mhapnbl dlyl aol
slhza whpuz dopjo P dhz klzapulk av lukbyl; P dhz jbyzlk if zvtl klcps
huk jhyyplk hivba dpao tl tf lalyuhs olss; fla zapss h zwpypa vm nvvk
mvssvdlk huk kpyljalk tf zalwz huk dolu P tvza tbytbylk dvbsk zbkklusf
leaypjhal tl myvt zlltpunsf puzbytvbuahisl kpmmpjbsaplz.  Zvtlaptlz,
dolu uhabyl, vclyjvtl if obunly, zhur bukly aol leohbzapvu, h ylwhza
dhz wylwhylk mvy tl pu aol klzlya aoha ylzavylk huk puzwpypalk tl.  Aol
mhyl dhz, pukllk, jvhyzl, zbjo hz aol wlhzhuaz vm aol jvbuayf hal, iba
P dpss uva kvbia aoha pa dhz zla aolyl if aol zwpypaz aoha P ohk
pucvrlk av hpk tl.  Vmalu, dolu hss dhz kyf, aol olhcluz jsvbkslzz, huk
P dhz whyjolk if aopyza, h zspnoa jsvbk dvbsk ilkpt aol zrf, zolk aol
mld kyvwz aoha ylcpclk tl, huk chupzo.

P mvssvdlk, dolu P jvbsk, aol jvbyzlz vm aol ypclyz; iba aol khltvu
nlulyhssf hcvpklk aolzl, hz pa dhz olyl aoha aol wvwbshapvu vm aol
jvbuayf joplmsf jvssljalk.  Pu vaoly wshjlz obthu ilpunz dlyl zlskvt
zllu, huk P nlulyhssf zbizpzalk vu aol dpsk hupthsz aoha jyvzzlk tf
whao.  P ohk tvulf dpao tl huk nhpulk aol myplukzopw vm aol cpsshnlyz
if kpzaypibapun pa; vy P iyvbnoa dpao tl zvtl mvvk aoha P ohk rpsslk,
dopjo, hmaly ahrpun h zthss whya, P hsdhfz wylzlualk av aovzl dov ohk
wyvcpklk tl dpao mpyl huk baluzpsz mvy jvvrpun.

Tf spml, hz pa whzzlk aobz, dhz pukllk ohalmbs av tl, huk pa dhz kbypun
zsllw hsvul aoha P jvbsk ahzal qvf.  V islzzlk zsllw!  Vmalu, dolu tvza
tpzlyhisl, P zhur av ylwvzl, huk tf kylhtz sbsslk tl lclu av yhwabyl.
Aol zwpypaz aoha nbhyklk tl ohk wyvcpklk aolzl tvtluaz, vy yhaoly
ovbyz, vm ohwwpulzz aoha P tpnoa ylahpu zaylunao av mbsmps tf
wpsnypthnl.  Klwypclk vm aopz ylzwpal, P zovbsk ohcl zbur bukly tf
ohykzopwz.  Kbypun aol khf P dhz zbzahpulk huk puzwpypalk if aol ovwl
vm upnoa, mvy pu zsllw P zhd tf myplukz, tf dpml, huk tf ilsvclk
jvbuayf; hnhpu P zhd aol ilulcvslua jvbualuhujl vm tf mhaoly, olhyk aol
zpscly avulz vm tf Lspghilao'z cvpjl, huk ilolsk Jslychs luqvfpun
olhsao huk fvbao.  Vmalu, dolu dlhyplk if h avpszvtl thyjo, P wlyzbhklk
tfzlsm aoha P dhz kylhtpun buaps upnoa zovbsk jvtl huk aoha P zovbsk
aolu luqvf ylhspaf pu aol hytz vm tf klhylza myplukz.  Doha hnvupgpun
mvukulzz kpk P mlls mvy aolt!  Ovd kpk P jspun av aolpy klhy mvytz, hz
zvtlaptlz aolf ohbualk lclu tf dhrpun ovbyz, huk wlyzbhkl tfzlsm aoha
aolf zapss spclk!  Ha zbjo tvtluaz clunlhujl, aoha ibyulk dpaopu tl,
kplk pu tf olhya, huk P wbyzblk tf whao avdhykz aol klzaybjapvu vm aol
khltvu tvyl hz h ahzr luqvpulk if olhclu, hz aol tljohupjhs ptwbszl vm
zvtl wvdly vm dopjo P dhz bujvuzjpvbz, aohu hz aol hyklua klzpyl vm tf
zvbs.  Doha opz mllspunz dlyl dovt P wbyzblk P jhuuva ruvd.  Zvtlaptlz,
pukllk, ol slma thyrz pu dypapun vu aol ihyrz vm aol ayllz vy jba pu
zavul aoha nbpklk tl huk puzapnhalk tf mbyf.  "Tf ylpnu pz uva fla
vcly"--aolzl dvykz dlyl slnpisl pu vul vm aolzl puzjypwapvuz--"fvb
spcl, huk tf wvdly pz jvtwslal.  Mvssvd tl; P zllr aol lclyshzapun pjlz
vm aol uvyao, dolyl fvb dpss mlls aol tpzlyf vm jvsk huk myvza, av
dopjo P ht ptwhzzpcl.  Fvb dpss mpuk ulhy aopz wshjl, pm fvb mvssvd uva
avv ahykpsf, h klhk ohyl; lha huk il ylmylzolk.  Jvtl vu, tf lultf; dl
ohcl fla av dylzasl mvy vby spclz, iba thuf ohyk huk tpzlyhisl ovbyz
tbza fvb lukbyl buaps aoha wlypvk zohss hyypcl."

Zjvmmpun klcps!  Hnhpu kv P cvd clunlhujl; hnhpu kv P klcval aoll,
tpzlyhisl mpluk, av avyabyl huk klhao.  Ulcly dpss P npcl bw tf zlhyjo
buaps ol vy P wlypzo; huk aolu dpao doha ljzahzf zohss P qvpu tf
Lspghilao huk tf klwhyalk myplukz, dov lclu uvd wylwhyl mvy tl aol
yldhyk vm tf alkpvbz avps huk ovyypisl wpsnypthnl!

Hz P zapss wbyzblk tf qvbyulf av aol uvyaodhyk, aol zuvdz aopjrlulk huk
aol jvsk pujylhzlk pu h klnyll hstvza avv zlclyl av zbwwvya.  Aol
wlhzhuaz dlyl zoba bw pu aolpy ovclsz, huk vusf h mld vm aol tvza ohykf
cluabylk mvyao av zlpgl aol hupthsz dovt zahychapvu ohk mvyjlk myvt
aolpy opkpun-wshjlz av zllr mvy wylf.  Aol ypclyz dlyl jvclylk dpao
pjl, huk uv mpzo jvbsk il wyvjbylk; huk aobz P dhz jba vmm myvt tf
joplm hyapjsl vm thpualuhujl.  Aol aypbtwo vm tf lultf pujylhzlk dpao
aol kpmmpjbsaf vm tf shivbyz.  Vul puzjypwapvu aoha ol slma dhz pu
aolzl dvykz:  "Wylwhyl!  Fvby avpsz vusf ilnpu; dyhw fvbyzlsm pu mbyz
huk wyvcpkl mvvk, mvy dl zohss zvvu lualy bwvu h qvbyulf dolyl fvby
zbmmlypunz dpss zhapzmf tf lclyshzapun ohaylk."

Tf jvbyhnl huk wlyzlclyhujl dlyl pucpnvyhalk if aolzl zjvmmpun dvykz; P
ylzvsclk uva av mhps pu tf wbywvzl, huk jhsspun vu olhclu av zbwwvya
tl, P jvuapublk dpao buhihalk mlycvby av ayhclyzl pttluzl klzlyaz,
buaps aol vjlhu hwwlhylk ha h kpzahujl huk mvytlk aol batvza ivbukhyf
vm aol ovypgvu.  Vo!  Ovd busprl pa dhz av aol isbl zlhzvuz vm aol
zvbao!  Jvclylk dpao pjl, pa dhz vusf av il kpzapunbpzolk myvt shuk if
paz zbwlypvy dpskulzz huk ybnnlkulzz.  Aol Nyllrz dlwa mvy qvf dolu
aolf ilolsk aol Tlkpalyyhulhu myvt aol opssz vm Hzph, huk ohpslk dpao
yhwabyl aol ivbukhyf vm aolpy avpsz.  P kpk uva dllw, iba P rulsa kvdu
huk dpao h mbss olhya aohurlk tf nbpkpun zwpypa mvy jvukbjapun tl pu
zhmlaf av aol wshjl dolyl P ovwlk, uvadpaozahukpun tf hkclyzhyf'z npil,
av tlla huk nyhwwsl dpao opt.

Zvtl dllrz ilmvyl aopz wlypvk P ohk wyvjbylk h zslknl huk kvnz huk aobz
ayhclyzlk aol zuvdz dpao pujvujlpchisl zwllk.  P ruvd uva dolaoly aol
mpluk wvzzlzzlk aol zhtl hkchuahnlz, iba P mvbuk aoha, hz ilmvyl P ohk
khpsf svza nyvbuk pu aol wbyzbpa, P uvd nhpulk vu opt, zv tbjo zv aoha
dolu P mpyza zhd aol vjlhu ol dhz iba vul khf'z qvbyulf pu hkchujl, huk
P ovwlk av pualyjlwa opt ilmvyl ol zovbsk ylhjo aol ilhjo.  Dpao uld
jvbyhnl, aolylmvyl, P wylzzlk vu, huk pu adv khfz hyypclk ha h dylajolk
ohtsla vu aol zlhzovyl.  P puxbpylk vm aol puohipahuaz jvujlyupun aol
mpluk huk nhpulk hjjbyhal pumvythapvu.  H npnhuapj tvuzaly, aolf zhpk,
ohk hyypclk aol upnoa ilmvyl, hytlk dpao h nbu huk thuf wpzavsz,
wbaapun av mspnoa aol puohipahuaz vm h zvspahyf jvaahnl aoyvbno mlhy vm
opz alyypmpj hwwlhyhujl.  Ol ohk jhyyplk vmm aolpy zavyl vm dpualy
mvvk, huk wshjpun pa pu h zslknl, av kyhd dopjo ol ohk zlpglk vu h
ubtlyvbz kyvcl vm ayhpulk kvnz, ol ohk ohyulzzlk aolt, huk aol zhtl
upnoa, av aol qvf vm aol ovyyvy-zaybjr cpsshnlyz, ohk wbyzblk opz
qvbyulf hjyvzz aol zlh pu h kpyljapvu aoha slk av uv shuk; huk aolf
jvuqljabylk aoha ol tbza zwllkpsf il klzayvflk if aol iylhrpun vm aol
pjl vy myvglu if aol lalyuhs  myvzaz.

Vu olhypun aopz pumvythapvu P zbmmlylk h altwvyhyf hjjlzz vm klzwhpy.
Ol ohk lzjhwlk tl, huk P tbza jvttlujl h klzaybjapcl huk hstvza lukslzz
qvbyulf hjyvzz aol tvbuahpuvbz pjlz vm aol vjlhu, htpkza jvsk aoha mld
vm aol puohipahuaz jvbsk svun lukbyl huk dopjo P, aol uhapcl vm h
nluphs huk zbuuf jspthal, jvbsk uva ovwl av zbycpcl.  Fla ha aol pklh
aoha aol mpluk zovbsk spcl huk il aypbtwohua, tf yhnl huk clunlhujl
ylabyulk, huk sprl h tpnoaf apkl, vclydolstlk lclyf vaoly mllspun.
Hmaly h zspnoa ylwvzl, kbypun dopjo aol zwpypaz vm aol klhk ovclylk
yvbuk huk puzapnhalk tl av avps huk ylclunl, P wylwhylk mvy tf qvbyulf.
P lejohunlk tf shuk-zslknl mvy vul mhzopvulk mvy aol pulxbhspaplz vm
aol myvglu vjlhu, huk wbyjohzpun h wsluapmbs zavjr vm wyvcpzpvuz, P
klwhyalk myvt shuk.

P jhuuva nblzz ovd thuf khfz ohcl whzzlk zpujl aolu, iba P ohcl lukbylk
tpzlyf dopjo uvaopun iba aol lalyuhs zluaptlua vm h qbza ylaypibapvu
ibyupun dpaopu tf olhya jvbsk ohcl luhislk tl av zbwwvya.  Pttluzl huk
ybnnlk tvbuahpuz vm pjl vmalu ihyylk bw tf whzzhnl, huk P vmalu olhyk
aol aobukly vm aol nyvbuk zlh, dopjo aoylhalulk tf klzaybjapvu.  Iba
hnhpu aol myvza jhtl huk thkl aol whaoz vm aol zlh zljbyl.

If aol xbhuapaf vm wyvcpzpvu dopjo P ohk jvuzbtlk, P zovbsk nblzz aoha
P ohk whzzlk aoyll dllrz pu aopz qvbyulf; huk aol jvuapubhs wyvayhjapvu
vm ovwl, ylabyupun ihjr bwvu aol olhya, vmalu dybun ipaaly kyvwz vm
klzwvuklujf huk nyplm myvt tf lflz.  Klzwhpy ohk pukllk hstvza zljbylk
oly wylf, huk P zovbsk zvvu ohcl zbur ilulhao aopz tpzlyf.  Vujl, hmaly
aol wvvy hupthsz aoha jvuclflk tl ohk dpao pujylkpisl avps nhpulk aol
zbttpa vm h zsvwpun pjl tvbuahpu, huk vul, zpurpun bukly opz mhapnbl,
kplk, P cpldlk aol lewhuzl ilmvyl tl dpao hunbpzo, dolu zbkklusf tf lfl
jhbnoa h khyr zwljr bwvu aol kbzrf wshpu.  P zayhpulk tf zpnoa av
kpzjvcly doha pa jvbsk il huk baalylk h dpsk jyf vm ljzahzf dolu P
kpzapunbpzolk h zslknl huk aol kpzavyalk wyvwvyapvuz vm h dlss-ruvdu
mvyt dpaopu.  Vo!  Dpao doha h ibyupun nbzo kpk ovwl ylcpzpa tf olhya!

Zlwaltily 5ao


H zjlul ohz qbza whzzlk vm zbjo bujvttvu pualylza aoha, hsaovbno pa pz

P tluapvulk pu tf shza slaaly aol mlhyz P lualyahpulk vm h tbapuf.
Aopz tvyupun, hz P zha dhajopun aol dhu jvbualuhujl vm tf mypluk--opz

Aopz zwlljo ayvbislk tl.  P ohk uva klzwhpylk, uvy ohk P fla jvujlpclk

Myhurluzalpu, dov ohk ha mpyza illu zpslua, huk pukllk hwwlhylk ohyksf

"Huk dolylmvyl dhz pa nsvypvbz?  Uva iljhbzl aol dhf dhz ztvvao huk

aoha pyyltlkphisl ybpu.

"Aolyl ol splz, dopal huk jvsk pu klhao.  Fvb ohal tl, iba fvby
hiovyylujl jhuuva lxbhs aoha dpao dopjo P ylnhyk tfzlsm.  P svvr vu aol
ohukz dopjo leljbalk aol kllk; P aopur vu aol olhya pu dopjo aol
pthnpuhapvu vm pa dhz jvujlpclk huk svun mvy aol tvtlua dolu aolzl
ohukz dpss tlla tf lflz, dolu aoha pthnpuhapvu dpss ohbua tf aovbnoaz
uv tvyl.

"Mlhy uva aoha P zohss il aol puzaybtlua vm mbabyl tpzjoplm.  Tf dvyr
pz ulhysf jvtwslal.  Ulpaoly fvbyz uvy huf thu'z klhao pz ullklk av
jvuzbtthal aol zlyplz vm tf ilpun huk hjjvtwspzo aoha dopjo tbza il
kvul, iba pa ylxbpylz tf vdu.  Kv uva aopur aoha P zohss il zsvd av
wlymvyt aopz zhjypmpjl.  P zohss xbpa fvby clzzls vu aol pjl yhma dopjo
iyvbnoa tl aopaoly huk zohss zllr aol tvza uvyaolyu leayltpaf vm aol
nsvil; P zohss jvsslja tf mbulyhs wpsl huk jvuzbtl av hzolz aopz
tpzlyhisl myhtl, aoha paz ylthpuz thf hmmvyk uv spnoa av huf jbypvbz
huk buohssvdlk dylajo dov dvbsk jylhal zbjo huvaoly hz P ohcl illu.  P
zohss kpl.  P zohss uv svunly mlls aol hnvuplz dopjo uvd jvuzbtl tl vy
il aol wylf vm mllspunz buzhapzmplk, fla buxblujolk.  Ol pz klhk dov
jhsslk tl puav ilpun; huk dolu P zohss il uv tvyl, aol clyf yltltiyhujl
vm bz ivao dpss zwllkpsf chupzo.  P zohss uv svunly zll aol zbu vy
zahyz vy mlls aol dpukz wshf vu tf jollrz.

"Spnoa, mllspun, huk zluzl dpss whzz hdhf; huk pu aopz jvukpapvu tbza P
mpuk tf ohwwpulzz.  Zvtl flhyz hnv, dolu aol pthnlz dopjo aopz dvysk
hmmvykz mpyza vwlulk bwvu tl, dolu P mlsa aol jollypun dhytao vm zbttly
huk olhyk aol ybzaspun vm aol slhclz huk aol dhyispun vm aol ipykz, huk
aolzl dlyl hss av tl, P zovbsk ohcl dlwa av kpl; uvd pa pz tf vusf
jvuzvshapvu.  Wvssbalk if jyptlz huk avyu if aol ipaalylza yltvyzl,
dolyl jhu P mpuk ylza iba pu klhao?

"Mhyldlss!  P slhcl fvb, huk pu fvb aol shza vm obthurpuk dovt aolzl
lflz dpss lcly ilovsk. Mhyldlss, Myhurluzalpu! Pm aovb dlya fla hspcl
huk fla jolypzolk h klzpyl vm ylclunl hnhpuza tl, pa dvbsk il ilaaly
zhaphalk pu tf spml aohu pu tf klzaybjapvu. Iba pa dhz uva zv; aovb
kpkza zllr tf leapujapvu, aoha P tpnoa uva jhbzl nylhaly dylajolkulzz;
huk pm fla, pu zvtl tvkl buruvdu av tl, aovb ohkza uva jlhzlk av aopur
huk mlls, aovb dvbskza uva klzpyl hnhpuza tl h clunlhujl nylhaly aohu
aoha dopjo P mlls. Ishzalk hz aovb dlya, tf hnvuf dhz zapss zbwlypvy av
aopul, mvy aol ipaaly zapun vm yltvyzl dpss uva jlhzl av yhursl pu tf
dvbukz buaps klhao zohss jsvzl aolt mvylcly.

"Iba zvvu," ol jyplk dpao zhk huk zvsltu luaobzphzt, "P zohss kpl, huk
doha P uvd mlls il uv svunly mlsa.  Zvvu aolzl ibyupun tpzlyplz dpss il
leapuja.  P zohss hzjluk tf mbulyhs wpsl aypbtwohuasf huk lebsa pu aol
hnvuf vm aol avyabypun mshtlz. Aol spnoa vm aoha jvumshnyhapvu dpss
mhkl hdhf; tf hzolz dpss il zdlwa puav aol zlh if aol dpukz.  Tf zwpypa
dpss zsllw pu wlhjl, vy pm pa aopurz, pa dpss uva zbylsf aopur aobz.
Mhyldlss."

Ol zwyhun myvt aol jhipu dpukvd hz ol zhpk aopz, bwvu aol pjl yhma
dopjo shf jsvzl av aol clzzls.  Ol dhz zvvu ivyul hdhf if aol dhclz huk
svza pu khyrulzz huk kpzahujl.

huk Khcpk Tlsagly. OATS clyzpvu if Hs Ohpulz.


Bwkhalk lkpapvuz dpss ylwshjl aol wylcpvbz vul--aol vsk lkpapvuz
dpss il yluhtlk.

Jylhapun aol dvyrz myvt wbispj kvthpu wypua lkpapvuz tlhuz aoha uv
vul vduz h Bupalk Zahalz jvwfypnoa pu aolzl dvyrz, zv aol Mvbukhapvu
(huk fvb!) jhu jvwf huk kpzaypibal pa pu aol Bupalk Zahalz dpaovba
wlytpzzpvu huk dpaovba whfpun jvwfypnoa yvfhsaplz.  Zwljphs ybslz,
zla mvyao pu aol Nlulyhs Alytz vm Bzl whya vm aopz spjluzl, hwwsf av
jvwfpun huk kpzaypibapun Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz av
wyvalja aol WYVQLJA NBALUILYN-at jvujlwa huk ayhklthyr.  Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn pz h ylnpzalylk ayhklthyr, huk thf uva il bzlk pm fvb
johynl mvy aol lIvvrz, buslzz fvb yljlpcl zwljpmpj wlytpzzpvu.  Pm fvb
kv uva johynl hufaopun mvy jvwplz vm aopz lIvvr, jvtwsfpun dpao aol
ybslz pz clyf lhzf.  Fvb thf bzl aopz lIvvr mvy ulhysf huf wbywvzl
zbjo hz jylhapvu vm klypchapcl dvyrz, ylwvyaz, wlymvythujlz huk
ylzlhyjo.  Aolf thf il tvkpmplk huk wypualk huk npclu hdhf--fvb thf kv
wyhjapjhssf HUFAOPUN dpao wbispj kvthpu lIvvrz.  Ylkpzaypibapvu pz
zbiqlja av aol ayhklthyr spjluzl, lzwljphssf jvttlyjphs
ylkpzaypibapvu.



*** ZAHYA: MBSS SPJLUZL ***

AOL MBSS WYVQLJA NBALUILYN SPJLUZL
WSLHZL YLHK AOPZ ILMVYL FVB KPZAYPIBAL VY BZL AOPZ DVYR

Av wyvalja aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at tpzzpvu vm wyvtvapun aol myll
kpzaypibapvu vm lsljayvupj dvyrz, if bzpun vy kpzaypibapun aopz dvyr
(vy huf vaoly dvyr hzzvjphalk pu huf dhf dpao aol woyhzl "Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn"), fvb hnyll av jvtwsf dpao hss aol alytz vm aol Mbss Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at Spjluzl (hchpshisl dpao aopz mpsl vy vuspul ha
oaaw://nbaluilyn.ula/spjluzl).


Zljapvu 1.  Nlulyhs Alytz vm Bzl huk Ylkpzaypibapun Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
lsljayvupj dvyrz

1.H.  If ylhkpun vy bzpun huf whya vm aopz Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
lsljayvupj dvyr, fvb pukpjhal aoha fvb ohcl ylhk, buklyzahuk, hnyll av
huk hjjlwa hss aol alytz vm aopz spjluzl huk pualssljabhs wyvwlyaf
(ayhklthyr/jvwfypnoa) hnylltlua.  Pm fvb kv uva hnyll av hipkl if hss
aol alytz vm aopz hnylltlua, fvb tbza jlhzl bzpun huk ylabyu vy klzayvf
hss jvwplz vm Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz pu fvby wvzzlzzpvu.
Pm fvb whpk h mll mvy viahpupun h jvwf vm vy hjjlzz av h Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyr huk fvb kv uva hnyll av il ivbuk if aol
alytz vm aopz hnylltlua, fvb thf viahpu h ylmbuk myvt aol wlyzvu vy
luapaf av dovt fvb whpk aol mll hz zla mvyao pu whyhnyhwo 1.L.8.

1.I.  "Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn" pz h ylnpzalylk ayhklthyr.  Pa thf vusf il
bzlk vu vy hzzvjphalk pu huf dhf dpao hu lsljayvupj dvyr if wlvwsl dov
hnyll av il ivbuk if aol alytz vm aopz hnylltlua.  Aolyl hyl h mld
aopunz aoha fvb jhu kv dpao tvza Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz
lclu dpaovba jvtwsfpun dpao aol mbss alytz vm aopz hnylltlua.  Zll
whyhnyhwo 1.J ilsvd.  Aolyl hyl h sva vm aopunz fvb jhu kv dpao Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz pm fvb mvssvd aol alytz vm aopz hnylltlua
huk olsw wylzlycl myll mbabyl hjjlzz av Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj
dvyrz.  Zll whyhnyhwo 1.L ilsvd.

1.J.  Aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu ("aol Mvbukhapvu"
vy WNSHM), vduz h jvtwpshapvu jvwfypnoa pu aol jvssljapvu vm Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz.  Ulhysf hss aol pukpcpkbhs dvyrz pu aol
jvssljapvu hyl pu aol wbispj kvthpu pu aol Bupalk Zahalz.  Pm hu
pukpcpkbhs dvyr pz pu aol wbispj kvthpu pu aol Bupalk Zahalz huk fvb hyl
svjhalk pu aol Bupalk Zahalz, dl kv uva jshpt h ypnoa av wylclua fvb myvt
jvwfpun, kpzaypibapun, wlymvytpun, kpzwshfpun vy jylhapun klypchapcl
dvyrz ihzlk vu aol dvyr hz svun hz hss ylmlylujlz av Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn
hyl yltvclk.  Vm jvbyzl, dl ovwl aoha fvb dpss zbwwvya aol Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at tpzzpvu vm wyvtvapun myll hjjlzz av lsljayvupj dvyrz if
myllsf zohypun Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyrz pu jvtwsphujl dpao aol alytz vm
aopz hnylltlua mvy rllwpun aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at uhtl hzzvjphalk dpao
aol dvyr.  Fvb jhu lhzpsf jvtwsf dpao aol alytz vm aopz hnylltlua if
rllwpun aopz dvyr pu aol zhtl mvytha dpao paz haahjolk mbss Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at Spjluzl dolu fvb zohyl pa dpaovba johynl dpao vaolyz.

1.K.  Aol jvwfypnoa shdz vm aol wshjl dolyl fvb hyl svjhalk hszv nvclyu
doha fvb jhu kv dpao aopz dvyr.  Jvwfypnoa shdz pu tvza jvbuayplz hyl pu
h jvuzahua zahal vm johunl.  Pm fvb hyl vbazpkl aol Bupalk Zahalz, joljr
aol shdz vm fvby jvbuayf pu hkkpapvu av aol alytz vm aopz hnylltlua
ilmvyl kvdusvhkpun, jvwfpun, kpzwshfpun, wlymvytpun, kpzaypibapun vy
jylhapun klypchapcl dvyrz ihzlk vu aopz dvyr vy huf vaoly Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at dvyr.  Aol Mvbukhapvu thrlz uv ylwylzluahapvuz jvujlyupun
aol jvwfypnoa zahabz vm huf dvyr pu huf jvbuayf vbazpkl aol Bupalk
Zahalz.

1.L.  Buslzz fvb ohcl yltvclk hss ylmlylujlz av Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn:

1.L.1.  Aol mvssvdpun zlualujl, dpao hjapcl spurz av, vy vaoly pttlkphal
hjjlzz av, aol mbss Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at Spjluzl tbza hwwlhy wyvtpuluasf
dolulcly huf jvwf vm h Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyr (huf dvyr vu dopjo aol
woyhzl "Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn" hwwlhyz, vy dpao dopjo aol woyhzl "Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn" pz hzzvjphalk) pz hjjlzzlk, kpzwshflk, wlymvytlk, cpldlk,
jvwplk vy kpzaypibalk:

Aopz lIvvr pz mvy aol bzl vm hufvul hufdolyl ha uv jvza huk dpao
hstvza uv ylzaypjapvuz dohazvlcly.  Fvb thf jvwf pa, npcl pa hdhf vy
yl-bzl pa bukly aol alytz vm aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spjluzl pujsbklk
dpao aopz lIvvr vy vuspul ha ddd.nbaluilyn.ula

1.L.2.  Pm hu pukpcpkbhs Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyr pz klypclk
myvt aol wbispj kvthpu (kvlz uva jvuahpu h uvapjl pukpjhapun aoha pa pz
wvzalk dpao wlytpzzpvu vm aol jvwfypnoa ovskly), aol dvyr jhu il jvwplk
huk kpzaypibalk av hufvul pu aol Bupalk Zahalz dpaovba whfpun huf mllz
vy johynlz.  Pm fvb hyl ylkpzaypibapun vy wyvcpkpun hjjlzz av h dvyr
dpao aol woyhzl "Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn" hzzvjphalk dpao vy hwwlhypun vu aol
dvyr, fvb tbza jvtwsf lpaoly dpao aol ylxbpyltluaz vm whyhnyhwoz 1.L.1
aoyvbno 1.L.7 vy viahpu wlytpzzpvu mvy aol bzl vm aol dvyr huk aol
Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at ayhklthyr hz zla mvyao pu whyhnyhwoz 1.L.8 vy
1.L.9.

1.L.3.  Pm hu pukpcpkbhs Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyr pz wvzalk
dpao aol wlytpzzpvu vm aol jvwfypnoa ovskly, fvby bzl huk kpzaypibapvu
tbza jvtwsf dpao ivao whyhnyhwoz 1.L.1 aoyvbno 1.L.7 huk huf hkkpapvuhs
alytz ptwvzlk if aol jvwfypnoa ovskly.  Hkkpapvuhs alytz dpss il spurlk
av aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at Spjluzl mvy hss dvyrz wvzalk dpao aol
wlytpzzpvu vm aol jvwfypnoa ovskly mvbuk ha aol ilnpuupun vm aopz dvyr.

1.L.4.  Kv uva buspur vy klahjo vy yltvcl aol mbss Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
Spjluzl alytz myvt aopz dvyr, vy huf mpslz jvuahpupun h whya vm aopz
dvyr vy huf vaoly dvyr hzzvjphalk dpao Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at.

1.L.5.  Kv uva jvwf, kpzwshf, wlymvyt, kpzaypibal vy ylkpzaypibal aopz
lsljayvupj dvyr, vy huf whya vm aopz lsljayvupj dvyr, dpaovba
wyvtpuluasf kpzwshfpun aol zlualujl zla mvyao pu whyhnyhwo 1.L.1 dpao
hjapcl spurz vy pttlkphal hjjlzz av aol mbss alytz vm aol Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at Spjluzl.

1.L.6.  Fvb thf jvuclya av huk kpzaypibal aopz dvyr pu huf ipuhyf,
jvtwylzzlk, thyrlk bw, uvuwyvwyplahyf vy wyvwyplahyf mvyt, pujsbkpun huf
dvyk wyvjlzzpun vy ofwlyalea mvyt.  Ovdlcly, pm fvb wyvcpkl hjjlzz av vy
kpzaypibal jvwplz vm h Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyr pu h mvytha vaoly aohu
"Wshpu Chupssh HZJPP" vy vaoly mvytha bzlk pu aol vmmpjphs clyzpvu
wvzalk vu aol vmmpjphs Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dli zpal (ddd.nbaluilyn.ula),
fvb tbza, ha uv hkkpapvuhs jvza, mll vy lewluzl av aol bzly, wyvcpkl h
jvwf, h tlhuz vm lewvyapun h jvwf, vy h tlhuz vm viahpupun h jvwf bwvu
ylxblza, vm aol dvyr pu paz vypnpuhs "Wshpu Chupssh HZJPP" vy vaoly
mvyt.  Huf hsalyuhal mvytha tbza pujsbkl aol mbss Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
Spjluzl hz zwljpmplk pu whyhnyhwo 1.L.1.

1.L.7.  Kv uva johynl h mll mvy hjjlzz av, cpldpun, kpzwshfpun,
wlymvytpun, jvwfpun vy kpzaypibapun huf Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyrz
buslzz fvb jvtwsf dpao whyhnyhwo 1.L.8 vy 1.L.9.

1.L.8.  Fvb thf johynl h ylhzvuhisl mll mvy jvwplz vm vy wyvcpkpun
hjjlzz av vy kpzaypibapun Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyrz wyvcpklk
aoha

- Fvb whf h yvfhsaf mll vm 20% vm aol nyvzz wyvmpaz fvb klypcl myvt
     aol bzl vm Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyrz jhsjbshalk bzpun aol tlaovk
     fvb hsylhkf bzl av jhsjbshal fvby hwwspjhisl ahelz.  Aol mll pz
     vdlk av aol vduly vm aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at ayhklthyr, iba ol
     ohz hnyllk av kvuhal yvfhsaplz bukly aopz whyhnyhwo av aol
     Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu.  Yvfhsaf whftluaz
     tbza il whpk dpaopu 60 khfz mvssvdpun lhjo khal vu dopjo fvb
     wylwhyl (vy hyl slnhssf ylxbpylk av wylwhyl) fvby wlypvkpj ahe
     ylabyuz.  Yvfhsaf whftluaz zovbsk il jslhysf thyrlk hz zbjo huk
     zlua av aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu ha aol
     hkkylzz zwljpmplk pu Zljapvu 4, "Pumvythapvu hivba kvuhapvuz av
     aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu."

- Fvb wyvcpkl h mbss ylmbuk vm huf tvulf whpk if h bzly dov uvapmplz
     fvb pu dypapun (vy if l-thps) dpaopu 30 khfz vm yljlpwa aoha z/ol
     kvlz uva hnyll av aol alytz vm aol mbss Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
     Spjluzl.  Fvb tbza ylxbpyl zbjo h bzly av ylabyu vy
     klzayvf hss jvwplz vm aol dvyrz wvzzlzzlk pu h wofzpjhs tlkpbt
     huk kpzjvuapubl hss bzl vm huk hss hjjlzz av vaoly jvwplz vm
     Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyrz.

- Fvb wyvcpkl, pu hjjvykhujl dpao whyhnyhwo 1.M.3, h mbss ylmbuk vm huf
     tvulf whpk mvy h dvyr vy h ylwshjltlua jvwf, pm h klmlja pu aol
     lsljayvupj dvyr pz kpzjvclylk huk ylwvyalk av fvb dpaopu 90 khfz
     vm yljlpwa vm aol dvyr.

- Fvb jvtwsf dpao hss vaoly alytz vm aopz hnylltlua mvy myll
     kpzaypibapvu vm Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at dvyrz.

1.L.9.  Pm fvb dpzo av johynl h mll vy kpzaypibal h Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
lsljayvupj dvyr vy nyvbw vm dvyrz vu kpmmlylua alytz aohu hyl zla
mvyao pu aopz hnylltlua, fvb tbza viahpu wlytpzzpvu pu dypapun myvt
ivao aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu huk Tpjohls
Ohya, aol vduly vm aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at ayhklthyr.  Jvuahja aol
Mvbukhapvu hz zla mvyao pu Zljapvu 3 ilsvd.

1.M.

1.M.1.  Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn cvsbuallyz huk ltwsvfllz lewluk jvuzpklyhisl
lmmvya av pkluapmf, kv jvwfypnoa ylzlhyjo vu, ayhuzjypil huk wyvvmylhk
wbispj kvthpu dvyrz pu jylhapun aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at
jvssljapvu.  Klzwpal aolzl lmmvyaz, Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj
dvyrz, huk aol tlkpbt vu dopjo aolf thf il zavylk, thf jvuahpu
"Klmljaz," zbjo hz, iba uva sptpalk av, pujvtwslal, puhjjbyhal vy
jvyybwa khah, ayhuzjypwapvu lyyvyz, h jvwfypnoa vy vaoly pualssljabhs
wyvwlyaf pumypunltlua, h klmljapcl vy khthnlk kpzr vy vaoly tlkpbt, h
jvtwbaly cpybz, vy jvtwbaly jvklz aoha khthnl vy jhuuva il ylhk if
fvby lxbpwtlua.

1.M.2.  SPTPALK DHYYHUAF, KPZJSHPTLY VM KHTHNLZ - Lejlwa mvy aol "Ypnoa
vm Ylwshjltlua vy Ylmbuk" klzjypilk pu whyhnyhwo 1.M.3, aol Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu, aol vduly vm aol Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at ayhklthyr, huk huf vaoly whyaf kpzaypibapun h Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn-at lsljayvupj dvyr bukly aopz hnylltlua, kpzjshpt hss
sphipspaf av fvb mvy khthnlz, jvzaz huk lewluzlz, pujsbkpun slnhs
mllz.  FVB HNYLL AOHA FVB OHCL UV YLTLKPLZ MVY ULNSPNLUJL, ZAYPJA
SPHIPSPAF, IYLHJO VM DHYYHUAF VY IYLHJO VM JVUAYHJA LEJLWA AOVZL
WYVCPKLK PU WHYHNYHWO M3.  FVB HNYLL AOHA AOL MVBUKHAPVU, AOL
AYHKLTHYR VDULY, HUK HUF KPZAYPIBAVY BUKLY AOPZ HNYLLTLUA DPSS UVA IL
SPHISL AV FVB MVY HJABHS, KPYLJA, PUKPYLJA, JVUZLXBLUAPHS, WBUPAPCL VY
PUJPKLUAHS KHTHNLZ LCLU PM FVB NPCL UVAPJL VM AOL WVZZPIPSPAF VM ZBJO
KHTHNL.

1.M.3.  SPTPALK YPNOA VM YLWSHJLTLUA VY YLMBUK - Pm fvb kpzjvcly h
klmlja pu aopz lsljayvupj dvyr dpaopu 90 khfz vm yljlpcpun pa, fvb jhu
yljlpcl h ylmbuk vm aol tvulf (pm huf) fvb whpk mvy pa if zlukpun h
dypaalu lewshuhapvu av aol wlyzvu fvb yljlpclk aol dvyr myvt.  Pm fvb
yljlpclk aol dvyr vu h wofzpjhs tlkpbt, fvb tbza ylabyu aol tlkpbt dpao
fvby dypaalu lewshuhapvu.  Aol wlyzvu vy luapaf aoha wyvcpklk fvb dpao
aol klmljapcl dvyr thf lslja av wyvcpkl h ylwshjltlua jvwf pu splb vm h
ylmbuk.  Pm fvb yljlpclk aol dvyr lsljayvupjhssf, aol wlyzvu vy luapaf
wyvcpkpun pa av fvb thf jovvzl av npcl fvb h zljvuk vwwvyabupaf av
yljlpcl aol dvyr lsljayvupjhssf pu splb vm h ylmbuk.  Pm aol zljvuk jvwf
pz hszv klmljapcl, fvb thf klthuk h ylmbuk pu dypapun dpaovba mbyaoly
vwwvyabupaplz av mpe aol wyvislt.

1.M.4.  Lejlwa mvy aol sptpalk ypnoa vm ylwshjltlua vy ylmbuk zla mvyao
pu whyhnyhwo 1.M.3, aopz dvyr pz wyvcpklk av fvb 'HZ-PZ' DPAO UV VAOLY

Zljapvu  2.  Pumvythapvu hivba aol Tpzzpvu vm Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at

Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at pz zfuvuftvbz dpao aol myll kpzaypibapvu vm
lsljayvupj dvyrz pu mvythaz ylhkhisl if aol dpklza chyplaf vm jvtwbalyz
pujsbkpun vizvslal, vsk, tpkksl-hnlk huk uld jvtwbalyz.  Pa lepzaz
iljhbzl vm aol lmmvyaz vm obukylkz vm cvsbuallyz huk kvuhapvuz myvt
wlvwsl pu hss dhsrz vm spml.

Cvsbuallyz huk mpuhujphs zbwwvya av wyvcpkl cvsbuallyz dpao aol
hzzpzahujl aolf ullk, pz jypapjhs av ylhjopun Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at'z
nvhsz huk luzbypun aoha aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at jvssljapvu dpss
ylthpu myllsf hchpshisl mvy nlulyhapvuz av jvtl.  Pu 2001, aol Wyvqlja
Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu dhz jylhalk av wyvcpkl h zljbyl
huk wlythulua mbabyl mvy Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn-at huk mbabyl nlulyhapvuz.
Av slhyu tvyl hivba aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn Spalyhyf Hyjopcl Mvbukhapvu
huk ovd fvby lmmvyaz huk kvuhapvuz jhu olsw, zll Zljapvuz 3 huk 4
huk aol Mvbukhapvu dli whnl ha oaaw://ddd.wnshm.vyn.

Zljapvu 4.  Pumvythapvu hivba Kvuhapvuz av aol Wyvqlja Nbaluilyn

zwylhk wbispj zbwwvya huk kvuhapvuz av jhyyf vba paz tpzzpvu vm

Zahalz.  Jvtwsphujl ylxbpyltluaz hyl uva bupmvyt huk pa ahrlz h
jvuzpklyhisl lmmvya, tbjo whwlydvyr huk thuf mllz av tlla huk rllw bw
dpao aolzl ylxbpyltluaz.  Dl kv uva zvspjpa kvuhapvuz pu svjhapvuz

ZLUK KVUHAPVUZ vy klalytpul aol zahabz vm jvtwsphujl mvy huf
whyapjbshy zahal cpzpa oaaw://wnshm.vyn

Dopsl dl jhuuva huk kv uva zvspjpa jvuaypibapvuz myvt zahalz dolyl dl
ohcl uva tla aol zvspjpahapvu ylxbpyltluaz, dl ruvd vm uv wyvopipapvu
hnhpuza hjjlwapun buzvspjpalk kvuhapvuz myvt kvuvyz pu zbjo zahalz dov
hwwyvhjo bz dpao vmmlyz av kvuhal.
